Iŋuc mupie kiŋaŋ moteczi risierâ bomboŋ-ticne dâŋ binaŋ ecneme maname gâpârewec. Erâ kiŋaŋ motec-ticne šiŋuc muhuc âzâcne sorec ewec: `Go bâruŋ jaha bozene bozene jufârehuc ŋic roroc qaŋqaŋne â kike demba, šeke puriŋ â tiŋtuŋ rocjopatec warenšepieŋ. Ž
Eme kiŋaŋ motec e iŋuc erâ bomboŋ-ticne šiŋuc âzâcnewec: `Bomboŋ, go dâŋ mumec i epac, erâ fic ine fâfâoc fokac. Ž
Âzâcneme bomboŋzi šiŋuc muwec: `Irec go mocwâc rarâ haesoŋko ŋic juraŋgopieŋ fotarie-jaretec ware-jâmbâŋkerâ ficnane fusucmanšepieŋ.
Erâ ŋazape mananiŋ: Ŋic bâbâni hefârec-jopakicne jaŋe mâc jâmbâŋ ŋenšepieŋ. Ž ”
Eme ŋic guru sâko jâmbâŋ Jesu bâjâpepie fotikierâ šiŋuc jazawec:
“Moc e nohec juzo murâ neŋgoc mamac, ŋokac motec, hahac ɋa seŋ baŋec jaŋe mi qaisoc-jopaocmu, e motec jâmbâŋ-nane sâcne mi erâ juocmu.
Moc e jahacne maripoŋ mi hâpora bâjâpecnuocmu, e motec jâmbâŋ-nane sâcne mi erâ juocmu.
“Ŋoŋeraonec moczi wapafic sâko baocte qanaŋ furinere manarâ moneŋ-ticne wose biric erâ eene me mi eene irec fuŋne bataniŋkeocmu.
Me iŋuc mi ehuc onšoŋ jaha ficticne wiseme hume šaeckerâ moneŋ basarâ beheocmuo ine ŋic jaŋe hone manac erâ mu gâgâwi ecnehuc
šiŋuc muniŋmu: `Ŋic keci fazic erâ ficsâko wiseme hume eipierâ beheme ŋekac. Ž
Ŋicwofuŋ moczi ŋicwofuŋ âgo-ticne qaocte onšoŋ jaha râsi mi raocmu. E qanaŋ šiŋuc muocmu: `Nâŋe ši afecne juŋgopeneŋzi ocni bocjaha juŋgopieŋ jaŋe sâcne jopanaŋmu me mâcne? Ž
Iŋuc murâ e jahacne momorifâc jaŋere maname afeckeme rasi-ticne hae-ticnao juhame biac sahac taha-ticne râecnehuc muocmu, `Wama fuame junac. Ž
Eme ŋoŋeraonec moc e iŋuc jaha wiac-ticne sasawa mi qikiŋne-fârerâ weniŋuc motec-nane erâ juocmu.
“Hâwec i wiac aŋacne. Á nonocne eme ine weniŋuc ecnepene hâtâne-ticne mocwâc fuaocmu, i aricne i¡
Izi iŋuc me iŋuc eene mi fokac, i mâc hoŋkepene raocmu. Moc e hazec-ticneheczi dâŋ kecši manazejec.”
Takesi roro â sâqocne bapa Jesurao miti-ticne mananiŋte mâretec fisi jumbieŋ.
Epie farisaio â miti qaqazu jaŋe irec manapie sâqoreme Jesure šiŋuc mumbiŋ: “Ŋic e sâqocne bapa rocjoparâ iqic-joparâ jaŋehec nânâ nâekac.”
Eme irec Jesuzi dâŋ suŋsuŋne moc šiŋuc jazawec:
“Ŋoŋeraonec moc e lama 100 jucneniŋmu. Eme mocsâkoazi qâsorieme beheocmu me? Aricne, e gâcne sâko 99 tuhuo behec-joparâ qâsoriekicne basaocmu.
Basaku bâfuarâ bubiaŋ manahuc âsickerâ
haeo fisirâ âgofâcne wira-jarerâ muocmu: `Lama-nane qâsoriekicne bâfuakopacte šeri enaŋ. Ž
No ŋazape mananiŋ, ŋic tiŋne 99 maŋ bâbârisiere mi mumu-jarene jaŋere erâ sambâŋko šeri aafecne fuaha sâqocne bapa mocjaha maczi maŋne bârisieme ere erâ sambâŋko šeri fekicne fuaocmu.
“Ŋokac moczi siliwa moneŋ 10 bajuocmu. Bajuhame mocjaha wahame beheocmu me? Aricne, e waha qazerâ fic ofaŋne qâzuc ehuc basaocmu.
Basaku bâfuarâ ŋokac âgofâcne wira-jarerâ šiŋuc jazaocmu: `Moneŋ-nane sifuckejec i bâfuakopacte šeri enaŋ. Ž
Mupe mananiŋ, Anuture aŋelofâc jaŋe iŋuc jaha sâqocne bapa mocjahazi mac maŋne bârisieme bubiaŋ manaeŋgopieŋ.”
Jesuzi binaŋ moc šiŋuc bawec: “Ŋic moc ŋokâ jahec-ticne jajahec jupic.
Juku šâhec ŋokâzi mamac-ticne šiŋuc âzâcnewec: `Mamac, go moneŋ mafa nore biŋe qakicne i narec. Ž Mume moneŋ mafa bâtâc barâ jactewec.
Eme šâhec ŋokâ e gie bapa afecne jurâ mafa wiac-ticne bâmockerâ ame susuckerâ rawec. Erâ ocna sasec gie bahuc nânâ qowire nâ areŋ ehuc moneŋ mafa-ticne ititiŋke-fârewec.
Ititiŋke-fârerâ juhame mâreŋ ira roroc sâko fuawec. Eme motec e kitac qatac eku
mâreŋ rune moc erao ra qohotame eki mume susubecfâc-ticne soŋaŋ-jopawec.
Ehuc bec jaŋere nânâ nâocte ecnewec i wâc sakarecnembiŋ.
Iŋuc juku maŋnezi mumu hehec ecneme šiŋuc muwec: `Mamac-nanere kiŋaŋ qaqa wemo afecne juŋgopieŋ, eme jaŋe nânâ nâqiŋ qâqiŋ ehuc juhapie no ŋokâ-ticnezi šira rorocte sipirickezo ekopac.
Irec no hae-naneo rarâ mamac-nanerao fisirâ šiŋuc muhuc âzâcnezepac: Mamac, no sâqocne bape kiŋnanezi sambâŋko â gorao ŋemâckekac.
Irec wemocko ŋokâge mocwâc munarepie jupemu, go mâc kiŋaŋ motecge bacnutec juzepac. Ž
Iŋuc murâ šawierâ mamac-ticnerao rawec. Raku hae upeo fisihame mamac-ticnezi biac honerâ bune sâqoreme gasacke ra hâpo mumuduc ecnewec.
Eme motec e šiŋuc âzâcnewec: `Mamac, no sâqocne bape kiŋnanezi sambâŋko â gorao ŋemâckekac, irec wemocko ŋokâge mocwâc munarepie jupemu. Ž
Iŋuc mume mamac-ticnezi kiŋaŋ motec jazarâ muwec: `Ŋoŋe picpac jaha ŋaqi biaŋne jâmbâŋ moc baware hecnepie huoc, â megâŋ menao hecnepie feoc, â kikehuhu mâmâc râcneniŋ.
Erâ bulimakao motecne biuc sâko i hezu rikec epie nâhuc šeri enšepeneŋ.
Ŋokâ-nane e hâmoweczi mocwâc ɋârekac, erâ e qâsorieweczi mocwâc fuakac. Ž Iŋuc mume šeri embiŋ.
“Ehame mârâc ŋokâ e gieo juweczi risierâ hae râpeo domahuc gae â šeri mic šonšoŋ manarâ
kiŋaŋ motec moc ecneme fisime mu wioc ecnerâ muwec: `Wiac i wemocte? Ž
Eme eki muwec: `Ɋage ware fisikac. Eme sahac furu fisikacte mamac-ŋekiczi mume bulimakao motecne biuc sâko i qa rikec eŋgopeneŋ. Ž
Iŋuc âzâcneme mârâc ŋokâ e kimbeŋ qarâ haeo feocte qikiŋnewec. Eme mamac-ticnezi manarâ hae upeo hurâ mu bâmiriŋ ecnewec.
Ecneme mi mamana šiŋuc muwec: `Manakic, no jara wemo afecne kiŋaŋ qagarehuc juhuc dâŋge moc mi qatara-gareekopac. Eme go noniŋ motecne mac moc mi qikiŋne-naretec âgofâc-nane jaŋehec nâ šeri embeŋ.
Á šâhec ŋokâge e gore moneŋ mafa sasec gie bahuc sipiricke-fârewec, e iŋucnezi fisime mutec bulimakao motecne biuc sâko i hezu rikec ecneŋgopieŋ. Ž
Mume mamacnezi šiŋuc âzâcnewec: `Ŋokâ-mae, go dameŋ sâc nohec juwareekiczi wiac mi basaekic, wiac sasawa wirec-nâhec fokac.
Á ɋage e hâmoweczi mocwâc ɋârekac, erâ e qâsorieweczi mocwâc fuakac, irec šeri bubiaŋ epene sâckekac. Ž ”
Jesuzi motecfâc-ticne binaŋ moc šiŋuc bajarewec: “Ŋicbomboŋ sâko moc ere moneŋ mafa soŋaŋ moc juwec. Eme juku ere šiŋuc mupie manawec: `Soŋaŋ e mafa ro bâsifuc eekac. Ž
Iŋuc manarâ hefârerâ âzâcnewec: `No gore dâŋ weniŋuc mupie manapac? Go iŋucnezi soŋaŋ mocwâc mi jucmurâ mukopacte papiage bawaretec moneŋ mafare fuŋne bataniŋkezo. Ž
Mume soŋaŋ e maŋnezi šiŋuc muwec: `Ʒi bomboŋ-nanezi soŋaŋ gie nowac rome wenac epemu? Gie he sarac ezore takicnukac, qafec qawahac juzore mimiekopac.
Miŋecne manakopac, bomboŋ-nanezi jâpecnume ŋic âgofâc-nane hezu hefâroc enarepie ficjeŋicko ŋeŋe epemurâ wiac ejarezepac. Ž
Iŋuc murâ bomboŋ-ticnere tofa bajumbiŋ i jaŋe buc buc hefârec-jopawec. Ehuc moc wiocnerâ muwec, `Bomboŋ-nanere tofa gorao wezimuc fokac? Ž
Eme eki muwec, `Qowitiŋ 100. Ž Mume šiŋuc âzâcnewec: `Ajoc, papia ši rorâ 50 qâreŋkec. Ž
Iŋuc murâ moc wiocnewec, `Bomboŋ-nanere tofa gorao wezimuc fokac? Ž Eme eki muwec, `Padi târu 100. Ž Mume šiŋuc âzâcnewec: `Ajoc, papia ši rorâ 80 qâreŋkec. Ž
Iŋuc eme bomboŋ e manarâ soŋaŋ bâkiri bapa maŋfânâŋ-ticnere muteŋkewec. Miti tâmiric jaŋe âgofâc-jeŋic jaŋehec wiac eniŋte maŋfânâŋ-jeŋic kâcɋene fokac, mitihec ŋoŋe sâc iŋucne mi foŋarekac.
Irec mupe mananiŋ, ŋoŋe iŋuc jaha moneŋ mafa jawane ŋic qikiŋne-jarepie jaŋe âgo bacŋoparâ juku i babaju dameŋne tarame juju sanaŋ ficjeŋicko hefârec-ŋopapie junšepieŋ.
“Moc e wiac omane metâo sâcne soŋaŋkeocmu, eki wiac fârine iŋuc jaha metâo sâcne soŋaŋkeocmu. Á moc e wiac omane bâsifuckeocmu, eki wiac fârine iŋuc jaha bâsifuckeocmu.
Ŋoŋe moneŋ mafa jawane metâo sâcne mi bajupie wiac fârine mozi ŋareocmu?
Á wiac jaba ŋarekicne i sâcne mi bajupie ŋaŋacne biŋe i mozi ŋareocmu?
Motec mocjahazi jajahec jahere kiŋaŋ sâcne mi qaocmu. E moc âgo ecnehuc moc hone takireocmu, â moctao qohotahuc moc râpeckeocmu. Ŋoŋe iŋuc jaha Anuture gie mecne â moneŋ mafa qâqâhâc sâko irec gie mecne sâckoa sâcne mi bacjofaniŋmu.”
Jesu e dâŋ i mume farisaio jaŋe moneŋ mafare sasec embiŋzi manarâ dâŋticne surembiŋ.
Epie šiŋuc jazawec” “Ŋoŋe hâcne ŋic jaŋere maio tiŋne hawari juniŋte šoɋac eeŋgopieŋ. Anutuzi ine maŋŋeŋicte fuŋne manaekac. Ŋic jaŋe wiac honepie tiŋne hawari eekac, i Anutuzi honeme mamakâcne eekac.
Sâcmutâc dâŋqâhâc â porofete dâŋ irec hata fowareku Johanerao mickewec. Irec faicnao ine Anuture uucmaŋ irec Biŋebiaŋ haŋ barakac. Eme ɋicwânšâŋ eeŋgopieŋzi rašieŋgopieŋ.
Sambâŋ â mâreŋ jahe sirowezo murâ sirowenicmu, â sâcmutâc dâŋ irec huŋgaŋne mac moc mâc foku arictac eene ine mi fokac.
Ŋic moc e ŋonâŋ-ticne beherâ moc roocmu, e šušuhuc-jekic bâtâcnehuc kiŋsâko hureocmu. Á moc e ŋokac behekicne i roocmu, e iŋuc jaha šuhuc bâtâcte kiŋ hureocmu.
“Ŋicbomboŋ moc juwec e ŋaqi erinehec furi sâko sasawa rojuwec, erâ šoaŋne šoaŋne tiwa šepec nâ šeri ehuc juwec.
Ehame ŋic hapetac moc juwec, šâŋene Lazaro. E sahacne wic sasawa. Eme eki ŋicbomboŋte fic rurumaŋko fojujec.
Ehame ŋicbomboŋte fickonec nâkitâc wahame i nâocte aŋac focne jujec. Fohame qâto jaŋe fisirâ wicticne apurumbiŋ.
Eme juku hapetaczi hâmome aŋelo jaŋe jowa ferâ Abrahamte qicfuŋko râepie juwec Eme šâhec ŋicbomboŋ e wâc hâmome duckembiŋ.
Eme e hârâcko hurâ šâic fâro sâko manahuc fime feme Abrahamte qicfuŋko Lazaro honewec.
Honerâ wirahuc muwec: `Abraham mamac-nane, nore buge sâqoreme Lazaro soretec mebotâŋne sawa opâo âke uruckerâ ware nameŋ-naneo bame mâteŋkezejec. No šira šocbâruŋko šâic serereŋ sâqocne manahuc jukopac. Ž
Mume Abrahamzi muwec: `Ŋokâ-nane manakic, go mâreŋko aŋac faio jumeŋ i tarawec. Á Lazaro busâqoc faio juwec i iŋuc jaha tarawec. Eme irec e bubiaŋhec juekac â go ine šâichec juekic.
Erâ wâc ŋondeŋ-nâŋecko hârâc sâko domakac, irec šireczi ŋoŋerao wemocko hufâzo â ŋoŋeraoneczi šira wemocko wefuzo. Ž
Eme ŋicbomboŋzi muwec, `Mamac-nane, moc mupe mana-narec”
ocna nore haeo ɋafâc-nane memoc juŋgopieŋ, jaŋe šâic haeo šira warenšipiŋte Lazaro soretec ra uŋdâŋ hazec qâuŋ jazazejec. Ž
Mume Abrahamzi muwec, `Aricne, Mose â porofete jaŋere micdâŋ fokac i mananšepieŋ. Ž
Eme muwec, `Mamac-nane Abraham, iŋuc mâcne, hâmokicne moczi ra jazame maŋjeŋic sâcne bârisieniŋmu. Ž
Eme muwec, `Jaŋe Mose â porofete jaŋere dâŋ qikiŋneeŋgopieŋko hâmokicne moczi ra jazame iŋuc jaha qikiŋneniŋmu. Ž ”
Jesuzi motecfâcne dâŋ moc šiŋuc jazawec: “Sâqocnere suru jâiŋ fufua i fuaocmu. weniŋuc mâc foocmu. Á ŋic moc sâqocnere suru jâiŋ bâfuaocmu, jei, e ine wemo ecnezo¡
E ŋic hujukicne suru jâiŋ ejarezacte buse sâko upenao qonaŋkecnerâ hâwecko sârockepie hume muzac, izi wiac aafecne fuacnekac ezac.
Ŋoŋe soŋaŋ babac ehuc junšepieŋ. Âgoge moczi bahac bâfua-gareme tutuc qacnezemec. Tutuc qacnetec manarâ busâqoc bâfuame kiŋticne behecnezemec.
Erâ šoaŋ mocjahao bahac arecne 7 bâfua-gararâ arec 7 gorao fisirâ muocmu, `Âgo, iŋuc egarepacte bunane sâqorekac,Ʒ eme go irec sâc jaha wâc kiŋticne behecnehuc juzemec.”
Aposolo jaŋe Wofuŋ šiŋuc muhuc numucnembiŋ: “Go mamanasiŋ-nâŋec basawe-nârezemec.”
Mupie Wofuŋzi šiŋuc jazawec: “Mamanasiŋ fârine piicne mac, šocšu hândâŋ iŋucne mac foŋareme muzac, ine nemuja jâc kecocni, ŋeunuckerâ tararâ hâwecko huŋ domaocte âzâcnepie eki micŋeŋic reŋkerâ iŋuc ezac.
“Ŋoŋeraonec moc e kiŋaŋ motec-ticne gie baku me bulimakao soŋaŋ juku owâ ririŋte fisime šiŋuc sâcne âzâcneocmu me? `Go ficko wefu ŋehaŋte nânâ rike bâmoc egarepe. Ž
Aricne, e šiŋuc âzâcneocmu: `Ajoc, kambaŋ ɋaɋacne qarâ ŋafere nânâ rike ŋec enaretec nahape šâhec go gahacne rike nâc ezemec. Ž
Eme kiŋaŋ motec e gie mucnekicne i sawa bame bomboŋ-ticnezi mâc maname taraocmu, â muteŋ bâteŋ ine wemocko ecneocmu.
Eme ŋoŋere fuŋne ijaha fokac. ŋoŋe wiac muŋarekicne i efârerâ šiŋuc munšepieŋ: `Nâŋe kiŋaŋ motec ba bititicne, wiac munârekicne i Sawa mac epârâckeŋgopeneŋ. Ž ”
Jesu e Jerusalem haeo raocte Galilaia mâreŋ fotâcnerâ Samaria mâreŋ qaŋeŋnao fisiwec.
Fisirâ hae mocko fehame ŋic wicsanaŋ-jeŋichec 10 jaŋe honerâ taic domahuc
wira wâwâsic ecnehuc mumbiŋ: “O Qaqazu Jesu, go nâŋere mac buge sâqoreoc.”
Eme honec-joparâ šiŋuc jazawec: “Ŋoŋe rarâ sahac-ŋeŋic taha bapa jowatunšepieŋ.” Mume jaŋe raha rahapie sahac-jeŋic fâsâewec.
Eme jaŋeraonec mocsâkoazi sahacne fâsâeme honerâ risiewec. Risierâ hahaŋne bahuc Anutu muteŋkehuc
Jesure kikefuŋko fodaperâ daŋge âzâcnewec. Eme ŋic e Samaria mâreŋkonec
Eme Jesuzi šiŋuc muwec: “Ŋic 10 fâsâembieŋ, gâcne sâko 9 jaŋe weni?
Jaŋe risierâ Anutu daŋge âzâcneniŋte mi muhuc mâc qâoma erâ rahapie ŋic qâpuc keczi e mocjahazi warekac me?”
Iŋuc murâ ŋic e šiŋuc âzâcnewec: “Mamanasiŋgere biaŋkekomec, irec fahare rac.”
Farisaio jaŋe Jesu wiocnerâ mumbiŋ: “Anuture uucmaŋ wezimucko fua tâcneocmu?” Eme jazawec: “Anuture uucmaŋ tâtâc mi fuaocmu,
irec wemocko honerâ šiŋuc muzo: `O šira fuakac, o ocna fuakac. Ž Manaŋgopieŋ, Anuture uucmaŋ i ŋondeŋ-ŋeŋicko fuawec fokac.”
Erâ motecfâcne šiŋuc jazawec: “Juku dameŋ moc maickeocmu ira ŋic Fâri Wâtuŋne e šoaŋ mocjaha tâtâcko fuame honeniŋte eŋare-bipieha sifu mi honeniŋmu.
Dameŋ ira kecšiŋuc ŋazaniŋmu: `O šira nâŋerao fuakac, o ocna jaŋerao fuakac. Ž Mupie mi ranšepieŋ â manapie jâmbomac mi ezejec.
Bâbâric e sambâŋ ŋifec bâricneme ŋifec qâninipe-fâreekac, irec sâc ŋic Fâri Wâtuŋne ere fifisi fuazokac.
Qanaŋ ine ŋicguru ši jaŋe Ŋic Fâri Wâtuŋne râpeckepie šâic gie sâko baocte mucnekicne.
Noa juwec dameŋ ira ŋic jaŋe wiac embiŋ ijaha Ŋic Fâri Wâtuŋne ere fifisi dameŋ maickeha enšoŋgopieŋ.
Jaŋe nânâ qowi nâmbiŋ, huc šocšu nâmbiŋ, ŋokac nareŋ gareŋ embiŋ. Qâoma iŋuc hâcne ehuc juhapie Noa wokeo feme rumi sâkozi fisirâ šeŋgoma bârârâŋ-jopawec.
Á Loti juwec dameŋ ira iŋuc jaha embiŋ. Jaŋe nânâ qowi huc šocšu i nâmbiŋ, wiac nareŋ gareŋ i embiŋ, gie hesac qasarac i embiŋ, fic gie bapa i bambiŋ.
Iŋuc ehuc juhapie Loti e Sodom hae râpeckeme sambâŋkonec kâmbâc â šoc wahame ŋic šeŋgoma sipirickembiŋ.
Ŋic Fâri Wâtuŋne e juku fua taniŋkezokac dameŋ ira ŋic jaŋe sâc ijaha eniŋmu.
Eme ira moc e hae šoŋao juocmuzi ficmaŋ-ticnao mi risie ferâ mafa-ticne rozejec, â moc e gieo juocmuzi haeo mi risiezejec.
Ŋoŋe Loti ŋonâŋ-ticnere manasunšepieŋ.
Moc e juju-ticne ŋezickezo mume sifuckecneocmu, â moc e juju-ticne qikiŋneme e fuacneocmu.
No mupe mananiŋ, ŋafe ira ŋic jajahec fofo wirec fohapire moc rohuc moc qikiŋnezo.
Ŋokac jajahec nânâ sufiehuc ŋehapire moc rohuc moc qikiŋnezo. [
Ŋic jajahec gieo domahapire moc rohuc moc qikiŋnezo.]”
Jesu e dâŋ i mufâreme motec jaŋe wiocnerâ mumbiŋ: “Wofuŋ, i wena fuazokac?” Eme muwec, “Âsu gâreczi keŋwipe fârecjopame fisirâ tumaŋneeŋgopieŋ.”
Eme motecfâcne jaŋe mi rokawehuc šoaŋ gie bapa sâc numecnehuc juniŋte irec Jesuzi binaŋ moc kecšiŋuc bajarewec:
“Hae mocko kia moc juwec, eki Anutu mecne â ŋic mecne araŋ mi bajarewec.
Eme hae ijaha ŋokac hozec moc juwec, eki kia erao hâcne hati rarâ šiŋuc âzâcne jujec: `Go kisâ-nanere ŋezicnuc. Ž
Eme kia e hozecte dâŋ dameŋ šora mana takirehuc juwec. Juku maŋnezi šiŋuc muwec: `No Anutu mecne â ŋic mecne araŋ mi bajareekopac i jâmbomac,
erâ hozec e micneneŋ sâqocne enarehuc juekacte sifu bafickezepac, juku fisirâ nuzackohec. Ž ”
Wofuŋ e binaŋ i bafârerâ muwec, “Kia râŋgeŋnezi dâŋ muwec i manaŋgopieŋ me?
Eme Anuture weniŋuc mueŋgopieŋ, e fuŋfuŋfâc-ticne ŋafe furec wâsickehuc jaha jupie šika ŋondeŋkonec mi batarac-jopaocmu me? Muŋgopieŋ, mana takirehuc juocmu me?
Aricne, e jume mi šoraha batarac-jopaocmu. Ŋic Fâri Wâtuŋne e juku mocwâc fisirâ mâreŋko mamanasiŋ bâfuaocmu me?”
Ŋic gâcne jaŋacne manapie tiŋne eha âgofâc-jeŋic mana wahac-jopambiŋ jaŋere qâqiŋdâŋ moc šiŋuc muwec:
“Ŋic jajahec taha ufuŋko ferâ numupic. Moc e farisaio â moc e takesi roro.
Farisaio e hâŋ domahuc e jahacnere šiŋuc manasuhuc numuwec: `O Anutu, ŋic gâcne jaŋe šika qaeŋgopieŋ, fiuc serereŋ eeŋgopieŋ, sasec mamakâc eeŋgopieŋ. No jaŋe iŋucne mâcne, me takesi roro kecocni e iŋucne wâc mâcne. Eme no irec hâcne daŋge gazakopac.
No Sonda sâc irec gie bapa jajahec sowa juekopac â moneŋ mafa hurerâ teŋkonec wâŋte sâc mitire biŋe qaekopac. Ž
Takesi roro eki ine tuturuŋko domahuc fime feocte mimierâ menezi amecne bofackehuc šiŋuc numuwec: `O Anutu, ŋic sâqocne no mi mac behecnuzemec. Ž
Manaŋgopieŋ, takesi roro e Anutuzi kiŋticne behecne-fâreme ficticnao risiewec, farisaio e ine focnewec. Moc e jahacne maŋte feme Anutuzi bawahaocmu, â moc e jahacne maŋte wahame Anutuzi bafeocmu.”
Eme ŋic ŋokac jaŋe ɋiefâc-jeŋic Jesurao amec-jopa rarâ mezi bâuac-jopaocte mupie motec jaŋe hâhâwic hejarembiŋ.
Jesuzi ine hefârec-jopahuc muwec: “ŋoŋe behehapie naru motec norao wareniŋ, mi hecke-jareniŋ. Iŋucne jaŋe hâcne Anuture uucmaŋ biŋe qajarekicne.
No jâmbomac ŋazape: Moc e ɋie jaŋere sâc ehuc Anuture uucmaŋ mi biŋeckeocmu, e maŋnao mi rašiocmu.”
Eme soŋaŋ moczi Jesu wiocnerâ muwec: “Qaqazu biaŋ, no weniŋuc erâ juju sanaŋte biŋe epemu?”
Jesuzi muwec, “Biaŋne wemocte munarekomec? Biaŋne rune Anutu mocjaha.
Erâ go sâcmutâc dâŋ manaekic, kecšiŋuc: Ŋowe ŋonâŋ ŋohe bebehec mi ezepirec, go šika mi qazemec, go fiuc mi rozemec, go micko âkec mi ezemec, go neŋgoc mamac jahecge sâsec-jofazemec.”
Mume soŋaŋzi šiŋuc muwec: “I ɋieo fuŋkerâ reŋke warehuc juekopac.”
Mume Jesuzi manarâ šiŋuc âzâcnewec: “Mocjaha fokac, i ezemec, go rarâ moneŋ mafage ŋic hapetac qikiŋne-jarezemec, eme sambâŋko boreŋ šeŋaŋ fua-gareocmu. Erâ ware bâjâpecnuzemec.”
Eme ŋic e moneŋ mafa ɋâfoŋne focnewecte dâŋ i manarâ bune boc sâqorewec.
Iŋuc eme Jesuzi honerâ muwec, “Moneŋ mafa mâririheczi Anuture uucmaŋko rašiniŋte ququŋkenehec boc eekac.
Kamelizi buŋic hawecnao raraši i wiac afecne, â moneŋ mafa mâririheczi Anuture uucmaŋko raraši i wiac ŋemâcne.”
Mume manahuc domambiŋ ŋic i jaŋe mumbiŋ, “Hâc, eme mozi sambâŋko feocmu?”
Eme Jesuzi jazawec, “Wiac ŋiczi eniŋte quŋkeeŋgopieŋ i Anutuzi hatane bâfuaocte mi quŋkeekac.”
Eme Petorozi šiŋuc âzâcnewec: “Manakic, nâŋe wiac-nâŋec sasawa râpecke-fârerâ go bâjâpecgumbeŋ.”
Mume Jesuzi šiŋuc jazawec: “No jâmbomac ŋazape: Moc e hae-ticne me ŋokac motecfâcne, me hahac ɋa seŋ baŋecfâcne, me neŋgoc mamac jahecne Anuture uucmaŋte erâ behec-jopaocmu,
e irec okacne šira mâreŋko wiac fekicne tahackezo, â juku sambâŋko juju sanaŋ tahackezo.”
Jesu e motecfâcne hefârec-joparâ šiŋuc jazawec: “Manaŋgopieŋ, nâŋâc Jerusalem haeo feŋgopeneŋ. Eme porofete jaŋe Ŋic Fâri Wâtuŋne ere findaŋdâŋ qâreŋkembiŋ i sanaŋke-fâreocmu.
E ŋic qâpuc jaŋere meo feme jaŋe mu ruruc ecnerâ qa imac ecnehuc tâfeckeniŋmu,
erâ becsahac biriŋneheczi qa qâšâic ecnerâ qahâmoniŋmu. Eme šoaŋ jahec â moc eha hâmockonec ɋârerâ fahareocmu.”
Iŋuc mume jaŋe kâuc bambiŋ. Dâŋ i manapie quŋkeme fuŋne mananiŋte mana ririfirembiŋ.
Jesu e raku Jeriko hae bâqiŋkewec. Ehame hatamecko ŋic tiŋtuŋ moc nânâ moneŋte numuhuc ŋewec.
Eme ŋic guru sâko hata ira rapie kike fânâŋ-jeŋic manarâ fuŋnere wiojareme
mumbiŋ, “Jesu Nazarete haeonec warekac.”
Mupie manarâ hahaŋne bahuc wirarâ muwec, “Jesu go Dawidire ɋâriczi nore mac buge sâqoreoc me!”
Iŋuc eme ŋic bâniembiŋ jaŋe niniŋkerâ ŋeocte dâŋ mucnembiŋ. Eme eki dâŋjeŋic mana takirehuc fotarierâ wirawec, “Go Dawidire ɋâriczi nore mac buge sâqoreoc.”
Eme Jesuzi manarâ hatao domahuc muwec, “Ŋoŋe norao bawareniŋ.” Mume tiŋtuŋzi erao fisime wiocnerâ muwec,
“No wemo egarepemurâ mukic? `à Eme tiŋtuŋzi muwec, “Wofuŋ, no šâŋe fifihec epere enarekac.”
Mume Jesuzi šiŋuc âzâcnewec: “šâŋege fitâcneoc, mamanasiŋgere biaŋgukac.”
Muha izia šâŋe fifihec ewec. Erâ Jesu bâjâpehuc Anutu muteŋkewec. Á ŋic wiac i homembiŋzi iŋuc jaha Anutu muteŋkembiŋ.
Jesu e Jeriko haeo fisirâ fotâcnezo ewec.
Eme hae ira ŋic moc juwec, šâŋene Zakaio, e takesi roro jaŋere micne, erâ moneŋ mafa sâko-ticnehec juwec.
Eme ŋic eki Jesu hawari-ticne honeocte ecnewec. Erâ e ŋic bembeŋnere ŋicŋondeŋko domahuc tiŋtiŋne-bipiewec.
Iŋuc erâ gagasac jaha ŋic jowaru-fârerâ ra nemuja hahaŋko ferâ ŋehuc šiŋuc muwec: “Jesu šira ware rame honepe.”
Eme Jesu e ira fisirâ fime feme honerâ šiŋuc âzâcnewec: “Zakaio go picpac wahac, no miŋecgac ficgao iqicgupemu.”
Mume izia picpac jaha waharâ bubiaŋ manahuc ficticnao jowame fepic.
Eme ŋic sasawa jaŋe i honerâ mana sâqorerâ mumbiŋ, “E wemocte ŋic sâqocnere ficko fejec fokac.”
Zakaio eki ine Jesure maŋfuŋko rarâ muwec: “Manakic, Wofuŋ, moneŋ mafa-nane sâckoa bâtâc barâ tucne ŋic hapetac jarepemu, â ŋic gâcne moneŋ sâc jâuruhuc jowac ropo ine ropo sâc i fohame baferâ okacne bazu-jarepemu.”
Eme Jesuzi muwec: “Ŋic kecši Abrahamte ɋâric jaha, irec ere ficko miŋecgac miti fuame biaŋkekac.
Ŋic Fâri Wâtuŋne e ŋic sâqorekicne rocjoparâ bâpiaŋ-jopazore wahawec hâcne.”
Jesu e Jerusalem hae bâqiŋkeme ŋic dâŋticne manambiŋzi mumbiŋ, “Ʒi Anuture uucmaŋ fua taniŋkeocte dameŋne maickekac.”
Eme irec Jesuzi dâŋ suŋsuŋne moc šiŋuc jazawec: “Ŋicbomboŋ moczi, ŋicwofuŋ sâkorao ra mupe mâreŋ soŋaŋ âkendâŋnume risiezepac, muhuc mâreŋ wiwicko rawec.
Raocte kiŋaŋ motecfâcne 10 hefârec-joparâ moneŋfoŋ mocjaha mocjaha muhuc jarewec: `Ŋoŋe moneŋ ši kime kiŋ qahuc basawehuc juhapie risiezepac. Ž
Rahame ŋicfâcne ere takic-jopawecte ŋic kiŋaŋ sorec-jopapie šâhec rarâ ŋicwofuŋ sâko šiŋuc âzâcnembiŋ: `E mâreŋ soŋaŋ-nâŋec mi juocte muŋgopeneŋ. Ž
Eme ŋicwofuŋ sâko e sifu mâreŋ soŋaŋ âkendâŋneme risiewec. Risierâ kiŋaŋ motec moneŋ jarewec jaŋe šiŋuc muhuc hefârec-jopawec: `Moneŋ ŋarepo i giene bahuc hotâckekupie wezimuc fuawec? Ž
Hefârec-jopame kiŋaŋ motec moczi fisirâ muwec, `Bomboŋ, go moneŋfoŋ mocjaha naremeŋ izi furune 10 kime fuawec. Ž
Mume šiŋuc âzâcnewec: `Sowine kiŋaŋ motec biaŋne, go wiac omanere gie aimuŋ bameŋte noni hae 10 jaŋere soŋaŋ râecgupe juzemec. Ž
Iŋuc mume kiŋaŋ motec moczi fisirâ muwec, `Bomboŋ, go moneŋfoŋ mocjaha naremeŋ izi furune 5 kime fuawec. Ž
Mume šiŋuc âzâcnewec: `Sâcne, go hae 5 jaŋere soŋaŋ juzemec. Ž
Eme kiŋaŋ motec moczi fisirâ muwec, `Moneŋfoŋge ši, no qoruczi foŋkerâ aimuŋ râepe fowec.
Go ŋic gereŋ gereŋne, go gahac wiac mi hurehuc gâcnezi bâfuapie rozo muekic, â go gahac gie he sarac mi ehuc gâcnezi bapie fârine fuame nâzo muekic. Eme no irec araŋ bagarehuc moneŋge aimuŋ bajupo. Ž
Mume bomboŋzi šiŋuc âzâcnewec: `Kiŋaŋ motec sâqocne go, gahac dâŋ mumec ijaha bâtikie-garekopac” no ŋic gereŋ gereŋne, no nahac wiac mi hurehuc gâcnezi bâfuapie rozo muekopac, â no nahac gie mi he sarac ehuc gâcnezi bapie fârine fuame nâzo muekopac.
Go fuŋne-nane iŋuc manahuc moneŋ-nane moneŋŋic jaŋerao râetec jaŋe kime kiŋ qakupie sawehame risierâ rozapo. Ž
Iŋuc murâ ŋic domambiŋ jaŋe šiŋuc jazawec: `Ŋoŋe moneŋfoŋ-ticne jâoc rorâ 10 bajukac e râceniŋ. Ž
Eme jaŋe mumbiŋ, `Hâc, bomboŋ, e 10 bajukac i! Ž
Eme muwec, `No ŋazape mananiŋ, moc e wiac râcnekicne bajume kiqecnecnezo, â moc e wiac râcnekicne mi bajume jâoc rozo, eme mâc juzejec.
Râsifâc-nane ŋicwofuŋ-jeŋic mi jupere muŋgopieŋ, ine bacjopa warerâ honehape jopa mizieniŋ. Ž ”
Jesu e dâŋ i mufârerâ Jerusalem haeo fisiocte rawec.
Raku Oliwa tikio ferâ Betefage â Betania hae bâqiŋ-jofawec. Ehuc motecfâcne jaŋeraonec jajahec šiŋuc muhuc sorec-jofawec:
“Hae rajecko ŋekac ira ranic. Rarâ doŋgi motecne niŋgiŋko domakac i bâfuanicmu. Motecne i ŋiczi fainao mi ŋekicne furune. Eme i bâfuarâ firuerâ bareniŋ.
Firuepire ŋic moczi `wemocte rokopirec? Ž mume šiŋuc muhuc âzâcnenic: `Wofuŋzi irec mukac. Ž ”
Mume motec jahe rarâ muwec sâc bâfuapic.
Eme doŋgi firuepire rune jaŋe mumbiŋ, “Ŋohe wemocte goroŋkekopirec?”
Jahe mupic, “Wofuŋzi irec mume rokoperec.”
Iŋuc murâ Jesurao bararâ fainao ŋaqi-jeŋic râerâ Jesu sâsepie fewec.
Ferâ rame ŋaqi-jeŋic hatao rumacke rambiŋ.
Eme Oliwa tiki heâŋnao huhuctecne kikefuŋ gurufâc-ticne jaŋe mâsi-ticne fuŋne fuŋne honembiŋ irec manasurâ šeri ehuc Anutu mucne bacnembiŋ.
Ehuc fânâŋkehuc šiŋuc mumbiŋ: “Ŋicwofuŋ-nâŋec Wofuŋte micte warekac e mumbiaŋkenaŋ, faic sambâŋko wama bumâteŋ fokâc â hae faic micne ira šeri mumuteŋ fokac.”
Iŋuc muhuc fânâŋkepie farisaio moc moc ŋicŋondeŋko jumbiŋ jaŋe šiŋuc âzâcnembiŋ: “Qaqazu, qâjâpecfâcge qatara-jaretec beheniŋ.”
Mupie jazawec, “No ŋazape mananiŋ, jaŋe niniŋkeniŋmuo qânâzi owackeniŋmu.”
Eme rarâ Jesu e Jerusalem hae mai jaha ŋeme hone-fârerâ bune herickeme kiohuc muwec:
“Go akio juhâmocmurâ irec hatane dameŋ šiŋuczia hone taranšaŋ me¡ Go ine šâŋege hâpokicnere wiac mi šâŋitaekic.
Juku dameŋ moc maicgume râsi jaŋe fisirâ somâcgurâ ŋebâzicgupie nanamaŋ bititi erâ bâŋeŋkecmu.
Erâ fic šoŋ hae šoŋ egarehuc motecfâcge qâmiziec-jopapie raŋe siaeŋ foraniŋmu. Eme haege ŋetâ qâtâtieme sesucne fuarâ foocmu. Anutuzi maicguha râpeckemeŋ, irec wiac i fua-gareocmu.”
Dâŋ i mutararâ ra taha ufuŋko fewec. Ferâ wiac nareŋ gareŋ ehuc domambiŋ jaŋe šiŋuc muhuc jâpec-jopawec:
“Fic kecširec dâŋ šiŋuc mukic ne: Ficnane i nunumu fic ŋezejec, ŋoŋe ine epie fiuc sindaŋ jaŋere qânâuŋ-tinac ekac.”
Eme šoaŋne šoaŋne taha ufuŋko miti jaza qazuc ehuc juwec. Ehame taha bapa micne â miti qaqazu â micne bapa sasawa jaŋe ine qapie arictac eocte dâŋne mumbiŋ.
Erâ ŋic omane mâmâc sasawa miti-ticne manarâ erea boc ejarewecte quŋkembiŋ.
Ʒoaŋ gie bapa mocko Jesuzi taha ufuŋko ŋic miti jaza qazuc ehuc juhame taha bapa micne â miti qaqazu â soŋaŋ jaŋe erao rarâ
šiŋuc âzâcnembiŋ: Go nâzâc, šira wiac eekic, i more micte eekic? Mozi iŋuc ecmurâ mugareme eekomec?”
Mupie jazawec, “No iŋuc jaha dâŋ moc wio-ŋarepe nazaniŋ,
Johanere Miti Opâ gie i wenirec fuawec, sambâŋkonec me qickonec? Ž
Iŋuc jazame jaŋe jaŋackoaŋ šiŋuc muhuc nazaŋ gazaŋ embiŋ: “Nâŋâc `sambâŋkonec fuawec, iŋuc mupene muocmu, `Hâc, eme wemocte dâŋticne mi mana šakiembiŋ? Ž
Me `ŋickonec fuawec', iŋuc mupene ŋic sasawa jaŋe manarâ qânâzi hehâmoc-nâponiŋmu. Jaŋe Johanere manapie porofete fârine ekac i!”
Irec Jesu šiŋuc âzâcnembiŋ: “Hece, nâŋe Miti Opâ-ticnere fuŋne mi manaŋgopeneŋ.”
Mupie Jesuzi šiŋuc jazawec: “Wiac murâ sâcne, eme noni iŋuc jaha, more micte šira wiac eekopac, okacne wâc mi ŋazapemu.”
Jesu e ŋic dâŋ herâricne moc šiŋuc jazawec: “Ŋic moczi waiŋ gie sarawec. Sara-fârerâ soŋaŋ râec-joparâ mâreŋ wiwicko rarâ ira dameŋ šoricne juwec.
Juku fârine fufua dameŋ maickeme kiŋaŋ motec moc fârine tucne roocte soreme ra fisime soŋaŋ jaŋe qa imac ecnerâ jâpepie metariŋ risiewec.
Risieme runezi harierâ kiŋaŋ motec moc soreme rame iŋuc jaha wiac gâgâpâcne ecnerâ jâpepie metariŋ jaha risiewec.
Eme runezi harierâ kiŋaŋ motec moc soreme jaŋerao fisime šâpâ qarâ tuŋkembiŋ.
Iŋuc epie waiŋ gie runezi manarâ muwec: `Ʒi wenac epe? Joroc ŋokâ-nane sorepe rame araŋ bacneniŋmu mecne. Ž
Eme soŋaŋ jaŋe ine ŋokâ-ticne honerâ nazaŋ gazaŋ erâ mumbiŋ, `Eki hâcne juku gie ši rauckeocmu, murâ qapene gie ši nâŋâcne ezejec. Ž
Iŋuc murâ kâteo tuŋke tuŋke rarâ qâhâmombiŋ. Eme gie rune e soŋaŋ weniŋuc ejareocmu?
Manaŋgopieŋ, e warerâ soŋaŋ iŋucne jopa qâhâmoc ejarerâ gie-ticnao soŋaŋ furune râec-jopaocmu.” Eme jaŋe manarâ mumbiŋ, “Aricne, iŋuc mi ejâmbâŋkezo.”
Mupie Jesuzi hone dendeŋ-jopahuc muwec: “Miti dâŋɋâreŋ moc kecšiŋuc fokac i fuŋne weniŋucte? `Ficbapa ŋic jaŋe wâtuŋ surehuc behembiŋ, wâtuŋ izi mi jâmâ wâtuŋ ezejec i!'
Ŋic moczi jâmâ wâtuŋ ira herâ sahac-ticne imackeocmu, â wâtuŋzi ŋic mocte faio waha qaocmu ine qâgâreckeocmu.”
Iŋuc mume miti qaqazu â taha bapa micne jaŋe šoaŋ ijaha kâpâcwâru baniŋte mumbiŋ. Jesu e dâŋ suŋsuŋne jaŋere muwec, i mana tararâ iŋuc ecnezo murâ ŋic jaŋere hâwic-jopame behembiŋ.
Eme jaŋe Jesure ruc bahuc doc bapa ŋic erao sorec-jopapie rambiŋ. Eme ŋic izi hâcne miti hawari juhuc Jesu dâŋzi bitiŋ bacnepie kime kiarao râeniŋte
mu esâic ecnehuc mumbiŋ: “Qaqazu, nâŋe gore fuŋne manaŋgopeneŋ, go dâŋ sâcne nâza qazuc eekic, erâ fekicne fosâoc-jopahuc dâŋ mi muhasickeekic, ehuc Anuture hata jâmbomacko mutiŋne-nâreekic.
Irec mutec mananaŋ, Roma ŋicwofuŋ takesi moneŋ râcnepene sâckeekac me mâcne?”
Mupie eeatuc-jeŋicte fuŋne mana tararâ muwec,
“Ŋoŋe siliwa moneŋ moc bâfuarâ nowatupie honepe, ira more hawari â qâreŋ fokac?” Eme jaŋe mumbiŋ, “Roma ŋicwofuŋte.”
Eme jazarâ muwec: “Murâ ŋicwofuŋte biŋe i ŋicwofuŋ râcnenšepieŋ, â Anuture biŋe i Anutu râcnenšepieŋ,”
Iŋuc mume jaŋe dâŋticne batackerâ wemocko ŋic jaŋere maio qorickenšapiŋ. Irec mâc wareckerâ dâŋjeŋic fâsâewec.
Jaŋe rahapie sadukaio ŋic gâcne Jesurao fisimbiŋ. Ŋic i jaŋe, hâmockonec fafahare mi fokac, iŋuc muhuc jumbiŋ.
Jaŋe hâcne fisirâ Jesu dâŋ šiŋuc muhuc âzâcnembiŋ: “Qaqazu, Mose e dâŋ kecšiŋuc mutâcnewec, `ŋic moczi ŋokac rorâ ɋâric-ticne mi fuahame hâmome ɋanezi hozec-ticne rorâ hahac-ticnere biŋe ɋâric bâfuazejec. Ž
Eme hahac ɋa 7 jumbiŋ, ehuc mârâc hahac-jeŋic ŋokac rorâ ɋâric tâmiric jurâ hâmowec.
Hâmome ɋanezi hozec-ticne rorâ iŋuc jaha hâmowec.
Hâmome ɋaticne moczi hozec i jaha rowec. Iŋuczi iŋuc hahac ɋa 7 jaŋe ŋokac i jaha rorâ ɋâric tâmiric hâmo-fârembiŋ.
Eme šâhecko hozec-jeŋic iŋuc jaha wâc hâmowec.
Eme ŋic 7 jaŋe mâmâc sasawa ŋokac ijaha rombiŋte juku fafahare dameŋko more ŋonâŋ ezokac?”
Mupie Jesuzi šiŋuc jazawec: “Dameŋ šiŋuczia šira mâreŋko ŋic ŋokac roroc eeŋgopieŋ.
Juku dameŋ sâkoo Anutuzi mana-jareme sâckeha juju sanaŋte ɋârerâ faharenšoŋgopieŋ, ŋic ŋokac i jaŋe ine roroc mocwâc mi enšoŋgopieŋ.
Wemocte? Jaŋe hâmockonec faharerâ Anuture naru motecfâc ehuc aŋelo jaŋe iŋucne hâmo hetiric mi ehuc furu jaha junšoŋgopieŋ.
Hâmokicnezi ɋârerâ faharenšoŋgopieŋ, i Mosezi wâc šocbâruŋ jâc dutunao fuawec irec binaŋko mufuawec. E Wofuŋte šiŋuc qâreŋkewec: `E Abraham â Isaka â Jakobo jaŋere Anutu. Ž
Ine hâcne, e hâmokicne jaŋere Anutu mâcne, e ɋâricne juju jaŋere Anutu, eki maname mâmâc sasawa jujune eŋgopeneŋ ekac hâcne.”
Jesu e iŋuc muhuc jazame miti qaqazu gâcnezi mumbiŋ, “Qaqazu, go dâŋ mutecne biaŋkekac.”
Eme mocwâc mu esâic ecneniŋte manapie ŋemâckeme behembiŋ.
Eme Jesuzi šiŋuc muhuc esâic-jopawec: “Kristo e Dawidire ɋâric mueŋgopieŋ i weniŋucte?
Dawidi e jahac miti mânec ɋâreŋkehuc kecšiŋuc muwec: `Wofuŋ e nore Wofuŋ šiŋuc âzâcnewec: Go ware fâre-naneo ŋehaŋte
no râsifâcge kikefuŋgao guruc-jopape kikegere ââtesiŋ enšepieŋ. Ž
Dawidi e Wofuŋ-nane mucnewec izi weniŋuc erâ ɋâric-ticne ekac?”
Eme motecfâc-ticne ŋic maioa dâŋ decšiŋuc jazawec:
“Ŋoŋe miti qaqazu jaŋere juju mi junšepieŋ. Jaŋe ŋaqi šora rojuhuc hatao ŋic bâfuac-jopapie mu šeri ejareniŋte maŋjeŋic domaekac. Ehuc mitificko â tutumaŋ ficko ŋicbomboŋ ŋeŋeoa micne ŋeniŋte mueŋgopieŋ.
Iŋucnezi hozec jaŋere fic wiac kâŋgâc jowac roeŋgopieŋ, erâ nunumu šorazi hehesicjeŋic hefackeeŋgopieŋ. Ŋic i jaŋe juku okacne hâhâwicne ronšoŋgopieŋ.
Jesu e qâhâŋnerâ fime rame mafaŋiczi taha katapao moneŋ-jeŋic râepie hume honewec.
Ehame hozec moczi fisirâ toea jajahec sawa râeme huwec.
Iŋuc eme Jesuzi honerâ jazawec, “No jâmbomac ŋazape: Hozec hapetac kecizi râekac i gâcne sasawa jaŋere sâc jâurukac.
Gâcne jaŋe neŋgocne sâko fojarehame tucne sawa mac râembieŋ. Á hozec e hapetaczi ine focnejec sâc râe-fârerâ mâc jâmbâŋ jukac.”
Tucne jaŋe taha ufuŋ qânâ erineheczi â taha geroŋzi bapie kiseŋ qâseŋ kirâ fowec i honehuc mu warec epie Jesuzi jazawec,
“Fic honeriŋ qâriŋ ecneŋgopieŋ i boc mi ŋeocmu. Dameŋ moc maickeme râsi jaŋe heropiepie ŋetâ qâtâtieme sesucne fuarâ fozokac.”
Eme jaŋe mumbiŋ: “Qaqazu, mukic i wezimucko fuazokac â irec dameŋ bembeŋkeme sowi weniŋucne fuazokac?”
Eme Jesuzi dâŋ šiŋuc jazawec: “Maŋ bâsifuc eŋarenšipiŋte sawaŋ-ŋeŋic qahuc junšepieŋ. Ŋic bocjaha fuarâ nore šâŋe jaba bajuhuc muniŋmu: `No Kristo. Ž Á gâcnezi muniŋmu: `Dameŋ biac maickekac'. Eme ŋoŋe ŋic iŋucne jaŋere bâjâpecne mi junšepieŋ.
Erâ šika biŋe â râsi fânâŋ manarâ jajaŋ bibisac mi enšepieŋ. Wiac iŋucne hâcne qanaŋ fuaocte mukicne, erâ fuame sifu dameŋ biac mi taraocmu.”
Iŋuc murâ muwec: “Mâreŋne mâreŋne ŋic guru sâko guru pitic jaŋe rârâsi efârerâ ra qa ware qa ehuc qaqac ranšoŋgopieŋ.
Erâ homeŋ kâcɋene sâko samarierâ bazokac, erâ roroc â huc mimicne ra fua ware fua ezokac. Erâ sambâŋko sowi â wiac hâhâwicne fuazokac.
Wiac i mi fuahame jaŋe qanaŋ rocŋopaniŋmu â ŋopa jâpec eŋareniŋmu. Erâ wâc dâŋficko â kâpâcwâru ficko râec-ŋopaniŋmu â ŋicwofuŋ â kia jaŋerao bacŋopa raniŋmu, i ŋoŋe nore šâŋe bajuŋgopieŋte iŋuc eŋareniŋmu.
Eme ira fuŋne mumutaniŋ gie maic-ŋopaocmu.
Eme jaŋere maio domahuc dâŋ weniŋuc mupene sâckeocmu muhuc mana wosâc mi enšepieŋ.
No nahac mic â mamana baafecke-ŋarepe dâŋ mupie kisâfâc-ŋeŋic jaŋe dâŋŋeŋic bawaharâ qatara-ŋareniŋte eipieniŋmu.
Erâ omanezi sawa wiac mi eŋareniŋmu, neŋgoc mamac, hahac ɋa, seŋ sâme, âgo bago jaŋe wâc doc bacŋopaniŋmu. Eme ŋoŋeraonec gâcnezi šika kirâ hâmoniŋmu.
Eme ŋic mâmâc sasawa jaŋe šâŋe biŋe-nanere erâ ŋoŋere manapie aaricnehec eocmu.
Wiac iŋucne eŋarehapie noni ŋezic-ŋopape qizec susuc-ŋeŋic moc mi sifuckeocmu.
Dodocke tâmiric juraku juju-ŋeŋic bâfuaniŋmu.
Momori jaŋe fisirâ Jerusalem hae somâckepie honerâ munšepieŋ, Miti hae qizec-nâŋec tuhu eocte dameŋne maickekac à
Eme Judaia mâreŋko juniŋmuzi tiki mâreŋko wiserâ ranšepieŋ, â miti hae qizecko juniŋmuzi iŋuc jaha biac waha wise ranšepieŋ.
Dameŋ ira hâcne okacne babazu fuaocmu. ehuc mitio dâŋ mukicne i fideteŋ efâreocmu.
Jei, ŋokac kiwecheczi â susuonecheczi dameŋ ira weniŋuc enšoŋgopieŋ? Ŋicguru ši jaŋerao kiŋ babatara fuame bâŋeŋkerâ weaŋsicne nâniŋmu.
Eme râsi jaŋe ŋic gâcne šika mimicnezi jopa miziehuc gâcne mâreŋ sâc amec-jopa rapie kiŋaŋ qaqafâc-jeŋic erâ juniŋmu. Erâ qâpuc jaŋe Jerusalem haeo ima gie bahuc juhapie mâreŋ sâc ŋic qâpuc dameŋ-jeŋic hesackeocmu.
“Eme šâhecko šoaŋ mosa bâpiŋko wiac šâŋe furu fuazokac, â mâreŋko hâwec sirizi â temboŋzi fânâŋ sâko eme hazec furu-ŋeŋic fuazokac.
Erâ wâc sambâŋ qiriŋ qame tâpirine ŋeŋgoroŋkezokac. Eme ŋic jaŋe wiac fua taraocte woŋec juhuc hobu-jeŋic taŋtaŋ âeckehame nokafe tataeŋ erâ domanšoŋgopieŋ.
Ehame Ŋic Fâri Wâtuŋnezi karorac faio domahuc ɋuŋɋasaŋ bâric bâric-ticnehec fisime hone šâirenšoŋgopieŋ.
Wiac iŋucne hâcne fuame honerâ qâhâŋnerâ fie ruruckehuc šiŋuc munšepieŋ: `Roroc-nâpo dameŋ maickekac hâcne. Ž ”
Iŋuc murâ dâŋ suŋsuŋne moc šiŋuc šuhuckewec: “Ŋoŋe jâmiŋ â jâc gâcne gâcne honehuc fuŋne mananšepieŋ.
Jaŋe gitec herâ fiepie honerâ mueŋgopieŋ: `Ʒoaŋ dameŋ maickezo ekac. Ž
Eme wiac mukopac i fuame honerâ munšepieŋ: `Anuture uucmaŋ fua tâcnezo ekac. Ž
No jâmbomac ŋazape: ŋicguru ši jaŋe mi sirowehapie wiac mukicne i deŋke-fâreocmu.
Sambâŋ â mâreŋ jahe sirowezokopirec, â nore dâŋ ine mi sirowe-jâmbâŋkezokac.
“Ŋoŋe nâ areŋ ehuc wiac omanere kirâ utuckerâ juhapie maŋŋeŋic bâzickeme dameŋ sâkozi bitiŋko kiki tinac ututuŋ jâmbâŋ kicŋopazacte sawaŋ-ŋeŋic qahuc junšepieŋ.
Dameŋ sâko e mâreŋ sâc ŋic ŋoŋe sâcŋopa-fârerâ acmâc jaha fuaocmu.
Irec ŋoŋe maŋguŋ tâmiric erâ hati numuhuc juhapie wiac fuaocte mukicne izi riric-ŋopame Ŋic Fâri Wâtuŋne e fisime ere maio qiŋ herâ domanšepieŋ.”
Jesu e šoaŋko ŋic taha ufuŋko miti jaza qazuc ehuc juwec. Ehame hae owâeme hae beherâ Oliwa tikio ferâ ira fojujec.
Eme hae fure pârâckeme ŋic ŋokac sasawa jaŋe miti mume mananiŋte biac taha ufuŋko tumaŋne jumbieŋ.
Goreŋ sowa juhuc aakic hombaŋ ŋeŋe irec dameŋ bembeŋkewec.
Ehame taha bapa micne â miti qaqazu jaŋe ŋic araŋ bajarembiŋte Jesu weniŋuc ecnepene arictac ezejec muhuc hata basahuc jumbiŋ.
Iŋuc ehuc juhapie Sataŋzi Jesure motec moc šâŋene Juda Karioto haeonec ere maŋko hume
taha bapa micne â ufuŋte polismaŋ micne jaŋerao rarâ Jesu doc bame roniŋte dâŋ mumocke-jarewec.
Eme jaŋe manarâ bujeŋic biaŋkeme furine moneŋ râcneniŋte mujomirembiŋ.
Mupie dâŋjeŋic reŋkehuc ŋic jaŋe hone manac mi ehapie soŋsoŋko doc bame roniŋte hone qatarac ehuc juwec.
Ehame goreŋ sowa juhuc aakic lama hezuniŋte hombaŋ maickeme
Jesuzi Petoro â Johane šiŋuc muhuc sorec-jofawec: “Ŋohe rarâ aakic lama hezu rikec ehapire fâpene nânšepeŋeŋ.”
Mume jahe šiŋuc muhuc wiocnepic: “Fic wena hezu rikec ezeperec?”
Eme šiŋuc jasawec: “Mananic, ŋohe haeo ferâ ŋic moc opâ râqâchec bâfuarâ bâjâperâ, ficko feme fenic.
Ferâ fic rune šiŋuc âzâcneniŋ: `Qaqazuzi gore šiŋuc mukac, fic maŋne wena motecfâc-nane jaŋehec aakic lama nanaŋmu? Ž
Iŋuc âzâcnepire fic maŋne kâcɋene moc ŋeŋe fofo wiac rumacke emasaŋ ekicne ŋofatume ira aakic lama rike bâmoc ezepirec.”
Eme jahe rarâ wiac muwec sâc bâfuarâ aakic lama rike bâmoc epic.
Eme nâzo dameŋ maickeme motecfâcne gâcne rocjopame fisirâ nâmbiŋ.
Ehuc šiŋuc jazawec: “Ʒâic dameŋ-nanezi bâmbeŋnuhame aakic lama ši ŋoŋehec nâpemurâ boc enarejec.
No mupe mananiŋ: No aakic lama mocwâc mi nânâ juhape Anuture uucmaŋko fâri fideteŋ eocmu.”
Iŋuc murâ waiŋ râqâc rorâ daŋge murâ šiŋuc jazawec: “Ŋoŋe rorâ nâ nareŋ gareŋ eniŋ.
No ŋazape, waiŋ opâ mocwâc mi nânâ juhape Anuture uucmaŋ fua tâcnezokac.”
Dâŋ i murâ poroŋ rorâ daŋge murâ bazurâ šiŋuc muhuc jarewec: “Kecši fâri-nane, [i ŋoŋere erâ qikiŋnekicne. Nore manasuhuc iŋuc nânšepieŋ.”
Nânâ nâpie waiŋ râqâc rorâ iŋuc jaha jarehuc muwec: “Râqâc kecšira šâšâfic ɋâricnere socnane ŋekac. I ŋoŋere erâ qikiŋnekicne.Ý
Erâ manaŋgopieŋ, doc bacnuocmu eki nohec tebo šira wiac mâmâc ro nâc ehuc ŋekoperec.
Ŋic Fâri Wâtuŋne e hata mušâwecnekicne ijaha raocmu. Á doc baocmu e ine, jei okacne mo iŋucne roocmu.”
Iŋuc mume motec jaŋe guru-jeŋickonec mozi i eocmu muhuc wiwioc embiŋ.
Eku wâc motec jaŋe nâŋâcnaonec mozi femicne-nâŋec jukac muhuc hehefaric embiŋ.
Epie Jesuzi šiŋuc jazawec: “Mâreŋ ŋicwofuŋ jaŋe ŋiczi kiŋaŋ qajareeŋgopieŋ â fekicne sâko jaŋe omanezi mumbiaŋ-jopaeŋgopieŋ.
Ŋoŋerao ine iŋuc mi fuazejec. Ŋoŋerao kâcɋenezi piticnere sâc juzejec, â micnezi kiŋaŋ qaqare sâcko juzejec.
Me ŋoŋe muniŋ, wenimo izi fekicne? Nânâ mâc ŋehuc nâocmu eki fekicne, me rike bâmoc eocmu eki fekicne? Mâc ŋehuc nâocmuzi fekicne, i manaeŋgopieŋ. Noni ine ŋoŋere ŋondeŋko kiŋaŋ qaqa iŋucne erâ juekopac.
Ŋoŋe hâcne šârâ hâriŋ maŋko jupe jujufâc-nane jueŋgopieŋ.
Eme Mamac-nanezi guriŋ bapa gie munarewec iŋuc jaha noni ŋoŋe muŋarekopac,
ŋoŋe nore uucmaŋko tiwâ nâ šeri eniŋte â ŋicwofuŋ ŋeŋeo ŋehuc Israe ŋicguru 12 jaŋere dâŋ mutaraniŋte.
“Simoŋ, Simoŋ, padi saja bapie wosâeekac iŋuc jaha Sataŋzi ŋoŋe ere meo fepie saja bacŋopaocte mujec.
Eme noni ine mamanasiŋge omaezacte gore erâ numupac. Irec go miti hatao mocwâc risierâ qomâfâcge keteŋ-jopazemec.”
Mume Petorozi šiŋuc âzâcnewec: “Wofuŋ, go kâpâcwâruo me hâmocko fâtec fâpemu.”
Eme Jesuzi muwec, “Petoro, no gazape manac, qâqâczi miŋecgac ŋafeo mi dâŋehame goki jahec â moc micnucmu.”
Iŋuc murâ muwec, “Noni moneŋ tâmiric â he tâmiric â kikehuhu tâmiric sorec-ŋopape ra basac qasac moc embiŋ me?” Eme jaŋe mumbiŋ, “Iŋuc aricne jâmbâŋ.”
Mupie šiŋuc šuhuckewec: “Á dameŋ šiŋuczia ine moc e moneŋ focnekacko ro bajuzejec, â moc e hemotec focnekacko rupe juzejec, â moc e šika basahuc ŋaqi qikiŋneme moc kitâcnecnezejec.
No mupe mananiŋ, findaŋdâŋ moc šiŋuc qâreŋkekicne: `E šika qaqa jaŋere guruo râembiŋ', dâŋ i norao fârinehuc eocmu. Erâ nore dâŋ mukicne i mâmâc sasawa sanaŋke-fâreocte dameŋ maickekac hâcne.”
Mume motec jaŋe šiŋuc âzâcnembiŋ: “Wofuŋ honec, ši šika jajahec fokopirec.” Eme muwec: “Sâcne.”
Eme ŋeku Jesu e ŋafe sâc ejujec iŋuc erâ hae beherâ Oliwa tikio feme motec jaŋe bâjâpembiŋ.
Eme jujujecko fisirâ motecfâcne šiŋuc jazawec: “ŋoŋe eesâicko dockenšipiŋte numuniŋ.”
Iŋuc murâ qânâ wickepene raekac irec sâc rarâ dieŋzi herâ šiŋuc muhuc numuwec:
“Mamac, go manatec sâckeme mutec šâic guru šizi nowaruoc. Erâ nore dâŋ mâcne, gore dâŋ sanaŋkezejec.” [
Iŋuc muhame sambâŋkonec aŋelo moczi waharâ basanaŋkewec.
Eme maŋzi šâic hâhâwicne ecneha fotariehuc numuwec. Ehame fofoŋac-ticne soc šâmbâŋ iŋucne tâcnehuc mâreŋko wahawec.Ý
Numuku faharerâ motecfâcne jaŋerao rarâ honec-jopawec: Jaŋe busâqoczi bâdoc-jopame betaŋkerâ guŋ fombiŋ.
Fohapie jazarâ muwec: “Ŋoŋe wemocte guŋ foŋgopieŋ? Eesâicko dockenšipiŋte faharerâ numuniŋ me!”
Iŋuc muhuc domahame mi râsi guru ututuŋ fisinšepieŋ i¡ Eme motec jaŋere âgo moc šâŋene Juda, eki micne bajarehuc Jesurao rarâ muduckewec.
Muduckeme Jesuzi šiŋuc âzâcnewec: “Juda, go wemocte Ŋic Fâri Wâtuŋne e muduckehuc doc bakomec?”
Eme Jesure kikefuŋfâc jaŋe wiac fuazo eme honerâ mumbiŋ, “Wofuŋ, šikazi jopanaŋ me?”
Iŋuc murâ jaŋeraonec moczi taha bapa sâkore kiŋaŋ motec šikazi qaocte hazecne fâreopec i qatarawec.
Eme Jesuzi i honerâ muwec: “Ŋoŋe beheniŋ.” Iŋuc muhuc ŋic hazec-ticne bâuahuc bâsomiewec.
Erâ taha bapa micne â ufuŋte polismaî micne â soŋaŋ e roniŋte fisimbiŋ jaŋe šiŋuc jazawec: “Ŋoŋe nore manapie šika qaqa eme šika qaruc-ŋeŋichec fisirâ rocnuŋgopieŋ me?
No šoaŋne šoaŋne taha ufuŋko ŋoŋehec juekopac, ehame ŋoŋe ira mi rocnumbieŋ. Ʒi ine ŋoŋere dameŋ maickekac â dapâcte tâpiri fua tâcnekac.”
Eme jaŋe Jesu rorâ bararâ taha bapa sâkore ficko bafembiŋ. Ehame Petoro e fisi fâresuc ehuc šâhec rawec.
Eme momori jaŋe sacmaŋko raširâ šoc ruqerâ ruahuc ŋehapie Petoro e iŋuc jaha raširâ ŋondeŋ-jeŋicko ŋewec.
Ŋehame kiŋaŋ naru moczi fisirâ hone dedeŋnehuc muwec, “Ŋic keci ehec juekac wâc.”
Eme Petorozi mic bahuc muwec, “Ŋokac, no e mi honeekopac.”
Iŋuc murâ ŋeme mi šorahame ŋic moczi honerâ muwec, “Go hâcne jaŋere guruonec.” Eme Petorozi muwec, “ŋic go, no aricne.”
Eme šâhec ŋic moczi fisirâ musanaŋkehuc muwec: “Á ŋic kecši jâmbomac ehec juekac, e Galilaia ŋic jaha.”
Mume Petorozi muwec, “Ŋic go dâŋ mutec kâuc bakopac.” Muhame izia qâqâczi dâŋewec.
Eme Wofuŋzi forisierâ Petororao šâŋe fime Petoro e Wofuŋzi dâŋ šiŋuc âzâcnewec i manasuwec: “Qâqâczi mi dâŋehame go jahec â moc mic bacnucmu.”
Dâŋ i manasurâ bune herickeme ra kio sâqorewec.
Jesu soŋaŋkehuc domambiŋ ŋic i jaŋe mu šerec ecnehuc
šâŋe maine bâsoŋkerâ qahuc mumbiŋ, “Go porofete jukomeczi ŋic gukac ere šâŋe muc.”
Erâ âke sisic wiac gâcne mâmâc ecnembiŋ.
Ehapie hae fureme micne guru, taha bapa micne â miti qaqazu hâcne, jaŋe sasawa tumaŋne-fârerâ mupie Jesu guru-jeŋicko bafepie dâŋ šiŋuc âzâcnembiŋ:
“Go Kristo jukomecko mufua-nârec.” Mupie šiŋuc jazawec: “No ŋazape mi mananiŋmu,
me indiŋ-ŋopape ŋifecne sâcne wâc mi nazaniŋmu.
Ʒi ine ŋic Fâri Wâtuŋne e Anutu tâpiri rune fârenao ŋeocmurâ dameŋne maickekac.”
Mume manarâ mâmâc sasawa šiŋuc âzâcnembiŋ: “Eme go Anuture Ŋokâ ine hâcne?” Eme muwec, “Ine hâcne.”
Mume mumbiŋ: “Wemocte dâŋgie mocwâc banaŋmu, ši e jahacne mickonec wahame manaŋgopeneŋ.”
Eme jaŋe ŋeku mâmâc sasawa faharerâ Jesu Pilatorao barambiŋ.
Erao domahuc kecšiŋuc muhuc qorickembiŋ: “Ŋic kecširec fuŋne šiŋuc fokac, e ŋic mâmâc sasawa ɋâiŋ-jopaekac, ehuc Roma ŋicwofuŋte takesi moneŋ mi râeniŋte muac-jopaekac, erâ wâc e jahacnere šiŋuc muekac: No Kristo ŋicwofuŋ.
Eme Pilatozi wiocnerâ muwec: “Go Judaŋic jaŋere ŋicwofuŋ me?” Eme Jesuzi muwec: “Ine hâcne mukomec.”
Mume Pilatozi taha bapa micne â ŋic guru sâko mâmâc jazarâ muwec, “No ŋic širec kiŋ basakopac.”
Eme jaŋe fotarierâ mujâmbâŋkehuc mumbiŋ: “E jâmbomac ŋic qafeŋ-jopame dâŋticnezi mâreŋ-nâŋecko haŋ bafâreekac. E Galilaia mâreŋkonecteaŋ fuŋkerâ ewareku šira Judaia mâreŋko ijaha eekac.”
Iŋuc mupie Pilatozi wio-jarerâ muwec, “Ŋic e Galilaia mâreŋkonec me?”
Eme “ine hâcne” mupie Jesu e Herodere gie gaŋkonec, iŋuc manarâ mume Heroderao barambiŋ. Herode e dameŋ ira Jerusalem haeo juwec.
Herode e Jesu honerâ bune biaŋkewec. E Jesure biŋe gâbâ manahuc honeocte boc ecne jujec. Erâ wâc mâsi moc bame honeocte aŋac focnewec.
Eme Jesu dâŋ fuŋne fuŋne wiocneme okacne moc mi bâtikiecnewec.
Ehame taha bapa micne â miti qaqazu jaŋe qoricke sanaŋkehuc domambiŋ.
Eme Herode â momorifâcne jaŋe Jesu sâckehuc šoraŋ ecnembiŋ. Ehuc Herodezi mume Jesu ŋicbomboŋ ŋaqi moc hecnepie hume Pilatorao mocwâc bârisiembiŋ.
Eme šoaŋ gie bapa ira Pilato â Herode jahe ââgo epic, mârâc jaha ine kikisâ ehuc jupic.
Pilato e taha bapa micne â ŋic fekicne â ŋic omane jaŋe mâmâc hefârec-jopame fisimbiŋ.
Eme šiŋuc jazawec: “Ŋoŋe šiŋuc muhuc ŋic kecši norao barâ warembieŋ: `E ŋic qafeŋ-jopaekac. Ž Eme noni ŋoŋere maio fuŋne-ticne bataniŋkepe fâri tâmiric ejec.
Herodezi iŋuc jaha erâ mume mocwâc bârisierâ bawareŋgopieŋ. Manaŋgopieŋ, kiŋticnezi hâmocte sâc mi bâfuakac,
irec mupe momori jaŋe kâcbiŋzi qapie firuepemu.” [
Kia e hombaŋ dameŋko ŋic moc firue-jare jujec hâcne.Ý
Jaŋe ine micne mic sâc owackerâ mumbiŋ, “E arictac eoc, Baraba ine firue-nârec.”
Baraba eki ine ŋic gâcne jaŋehec šika qahuc ŋic moc qâhâmome kâpâcwâru ficko râembiŋ.
Eme Pilato e harierâ jazawec, “No Jesu firuepemu i!”
Mume jaŋe hahaŋne bahuc mumbiŋ, “Maripoŋko hâmooc, maripoŋko hâmooc!”
Eme Pilatozi qatara-jarehame jahec â moc eme jazawec, “Wemo sâqocne bawecte? No manape kiŋticne hâmocte sâc mi ekacte mupe kâcbiŋ sawa kirâ juzejec.”
Eme jaŋe fota qatarierâ micne mic šereŋ musereckerâ owackehuc mumbiŋ, “Maripoŋko hâmooc.” Murâ qâsifu sâko qarâ fetone fehuc kiare dâŋ bawahambiŋ.
Eme Pilatozi dâŋ mumbiŋ irec fârine fuaocte mutarawec.
Ehuc dâŋjeŋic reŋkerâ qaqafeŋte â šikare kâpâcwâruo râekicne ŋic e firue-jarewec â Jesu ine qikiŋne-jarewec.
Jaŋe Jesu baraku hatao ŋic moc bâfuambiŋ, šâŋene Simoŋ, Kirene hae mâreŋkonec. E gieonec wareme rorâ Jesure maripoŋ ɋawenao râepie hâporâ Jesure râpefuŋko rawec.
Erâ ŋic ŋokac guru sâkozi bâjâpembiŋ Ehuc ŋokac jaŋe kio wâwâsic â mu mamakuc ecnembiŋ.
Epie Jesuzi fotikierâ šiŋuc jazawec: “Jerusalemnec ŋokac bureŋ, ŋoŋe nore mi kioniŋ. Ŋoŋe â naru motecfâc-ŋeŋic ŋaŋacne kioniŋ.
Manaŋgopieŋ, juku dameŋ moc maickeme šiŋuc munšoŋgopieŋ: `Oi, ŋokac hufiŋne â me sawane jaŋe iŋucne junšapeŋ me! Ž
Eme dameŋ ira tiki jaŋere šiŋuc muniŋmu: `Ŋoŋe herickerâ waha ŋefac-nâponiŋ', â hârâc jaŋere muniŋmu, `Ŋoŋe fâuckerâ bârârâŋ-nâponiŋ'.
Wiac šiŋucne jâc ɋâricne ecneŋgopieŋko hâmocne weniŋuc ecnezo?”
Eme sâqocne bapa jajahec ehec mâmâc jopaniŋte bacjopa rambiŋ.
Eme raku mâreŋ moc šâŋene Utusiec ira fisirâ Jesu maripoŋko qambiŋ, â sâqocne bapa moc ŋifec â moc ŋifec mâmâc jofambiŋ.
Eme Jesuzi numuhuc muwec, “Mamac, jaŋe wiac eŋgopieŋ i fuŋne kâuc baŋgopieŋte kiŋjeŋic behec.” Momori jaŋe ine ŋaqi-ticnere jaŋaczia ɋâsâi qapie âke fuac-jopame sâc rauckembiŋ.
Ŋic ine wemo afecne ijaha domahuc wiac hone-fârembiŋ. Ehuc ŋic fekicne jaŋe sâke itic ecnehuc mumbiŋ, “Gâcne bafic-jopaweczi e jahacne sahac bafickeoc me¡ E Kristo Anuture joroc jukacko iŋuc eoc me!”
Momori jaŋe iŋuc jaha mu ruruc ecnembiŋ, ehuc waiŋ opâ šašacne sicnecnehuc mumbiŋ:
Go Judaŋic jaŋere ŋicwofuŋ jukomecko sahacge ŋezickec me!”
Eme Jesure qizec botâŋko dâŋqâreŋ šiŋuc râembiŋ: “Ʒi Judaŋic jaŋere ŋicwofuŋ.”
Eme sâqocne bapa moczi maripoŋko domahuc bafic-joparâ sâke kiki ecnerâ muwec, “Go iŋucnezi Kristo me? Murâ gahacne sahac batararâ nâhe mâmâc batarac-nâfoc.”
Iŋuc mume âgonezi dâŋ mucnehuc muwec, “Go šikare biŋe mâmâc ekicnezi Anuture mi hâwicguha iŋuc mukomec?
Nâhâc kiŋnâhecte sâcko wiac sâcne enâctekicne, ŋic kecšizi ine sindaŋ moc mi ewec.”
Iŋuc murâ muwec, “Jesu, go Wofuŋ tâpirigehec juku fisirâ nore manasuzemec.”
Mume Jesuzi šiŋuc âzâcnewec: “No jâmbomac gazape, miŋecgac jaha nohec Paradisio jucmu.”
Eme 12 kiloë ehame šoaŋ gâpâreme dapâc fuarâ mâreŋ sâckerâ fohame 3 kiloë ewec.
Ehame taha ufuŋko qoruc ââketâc sâko šâšâŋiŋ jaha hâŋ fâucke waharâ qatarawec.
Eme Jesu e wiwic jaha wirahuc muwec, “Mamac, megao maŋ qâqâtâc-nane râekopac.” Iŋuc murâ hâmowec.
Eme momori soŋaŋzi wiac i hone manac efârerâ Anutu mumbiaŋkehuc muwec, “Ŋic kecši e jâmbomac bahacmâc.”
Erâ ŋic gâcne sâko wiac hone aŋac eniŋte fisimbiŋ jaŋe wiac i sasawa hone manac erâ maŋjeŋiczi tutuc qajarehame risiembiŋ.
Jesu e jahacne wiacfâc â Galilaia mâreŋkonec ŋokac bâjâperâ warembiŋ jaŋe ine taicko domahuc wiac hone manac embiŋ.
Ŋic moc juwec, šâŋene Josefe” hae-ticne Judaia mâreŋko ŋewec, šâŋene Arimataia. Ŋic e micne sâko jumbiŋ jaŋere guruonec, erâ e ŋic wamane â tiŋne.
Âgofâcne jaŋe Jesu dâŋ qacnehuc šikao râepie maname mi sâckewec, erâ e Anuture uucmaŋ fua tâcneocte woŋec juwec hâcne.
Ŋic eki hâcne Pilatorao rarâ Jesu qâŋɋâŋ-ticnere âzâcnewec.
Eme manacneme ra maripoŋkonec batararâ qoruc qaŋqaŋzi râpâckerâ bararâ qânâ hâŋko hawec šâŋeruŋte biŋe gufukicne ira Jesure qâŋɋâŋ râewec. Hawec i furu fowec, ira mârâc jaha qâŋɋâŋ moc mi râekicne.
I šašawie dameŋte owâ gieo fuawec, sabata hombaŋ maickezo eha.
Ŋokac tucne Jesuhec Galilaia mâreŋkonec warembiŋ jaŋe Josefe bâjâpehuc honehapie Jesure qâŋɋâŋ šâŋeruŋko râewec.
Eme wiac hone-fârerâ haeo risierâ wokemaŋ âsu biaŋ â kâŋâ wiac bâmockembiŋ. Erâ sabata hombaŋko sâcmutâc dâŋ reŋkehuc ŋemanambiŋ.
Sonda uupicte hae fure pârâckezo ehame ŋokac jaŋe wiac âsu biaŋ bâmockembiŋ i šâŋeruŋko amecke rambiŋ.
Ra fisirâ honembiŋ: Qânâ sâko e rârieme hawec aaŋ fowec.
Eme šâŋeruŋ maŋko raširâ Wofuŋ Jesu qâŋɋâŋ-ticne basambiŋ.
Basarâ weaŋkerâ domahapie ŋic jajahec ŋaqi-jekic bâric bâricnekicne mi maŋfuŋ-jeŋicko fuarâ domazepirec i¡
Eme ŋokac jaŋe hâwic-jopame dunduŋ domahapie ŋic jahe šiŋuc jazapic: “ŋoŋe wemocte ɋârine jukac e hâmokicne jaŋerao basaŋgopieŋ?
E šira mi fokac, e ɋârerâ faharejec, Galilaia mâreŋko juhuc dâŋ kecšiŋuc ŋazawec i manasuniŋ:
`Mamac-nanezi ŋic Fâri Wâtuŋne e sâqocne bapa jaŋere meo râeme qapie hâmorâ šoaŋ jahec â moc eha ɋârerâ fahareocmu. Ž ”
Iŋuc mupire ŋokaŋ jaŋe dâŋ i manasuhuc
šâŋeruŋkonec risierâ haeo fisirâ motecfâcne 11 â ŋic ŋokac gâcne dâŋ binaŋ ejarembiŋ.
Ŋokac šâŋe-jeŋic Maria Madala haeonec â Johana â Maria Jakobore neŋgoc erâ âgofâc-jeŋic gâcne mâmâc jumbiŋ. Izi hâcne aposolo biŋedâŋ jazambiŋ.
Jazapie dâŋjeŋic manapie pacgoroŋ dâŋ eme mi mana šakiembiŋ.
Á Petoro e ine fahare šâŋeruŋko gasacke rarâ okarierâ fime rašime qoruc râpâ sawa honewec. Erâ wiac fuawec i mana warec ehuc haeo risie rawec.
Eme šoaŋ ijaha Jesure kikefuŋfâc jaŋeraonec ŋic jajahec Emausi haeo ranicte rapic. Hae i šoricko mi ŋewec, Judaŋic jaŋe qâqâtâc bembeŋkeme Jerusalem haeonec rârâ šoaŋ otewezo ehame fisi jumbieŋ.
Eme ŋic jahe hatao rahuc wiac fuawec irec muc manac epic.
Mu gufuc ehuc muc manac rahapire Jesu e jahac rarâ bâfuac-jofame mâmâc rambiŋ.
Eme šâŋe-jekic bâsâockekicnere mi hone tarapic.
Iŋuc ehapire wio-jacterâ muwec: “Ŋohe wemo wiacte nazaŋ gazaŋ ehuc jukopirec?” Mume jahe šâŋe mai-jekic sorondoŋ eha domapic.
Ehuc jaheraonec moc šâŋene Keleopa eki muwec, “Jerusalem haeo ŋic hombaŋte fisimbiŋ jaŋe dâŋ biŋe sâko hazec sâc mana-fârehapie go mocjahazi weniŋuc erâ hazec furu jukomec.”
Eme eki wio-jacterâ muwec, “Wemo wiac?” Mume jahe mupic, “Wiac Jesu Nazarete haeonec ere binaŋ. E porofete sâko juhuc Anuture maio â ŋicmaio wiac tâpiri jaha mu bac ehuc juwec.
Ehame taha bapa micne â fekicnefâc-nâŋec jaŋe hâmoocte mutaracnehuc kiarao râepie mume maripoŋko qambiŋ.
Nâŋe ine ere mamanac juhuc šiŋuc mumbeŋ: `Eki hâcne Israe ŋic nâŋâc niŋgiŋkonec firuec-nâpozejec. Ž Eme qapie hâmome juhapene biac šoaŋ gie bapa jahec â moc ekac.
Ehame miŋecgac nâŋeraonec ŋokac gâcne bu qâqânduc dâŋ nâzâmbieŋ. Jaŋe furicte šâŋeruŋko rarâ
qâŋɋâŋ-ticne basarâ risierâ šiŋuc mumbieŋ: `Aŋelo jajahec fua-nârehuc, Jesu ɋârerâ faharejec, iŋuc nâzâkopirec. Ž
Eme dâŋ i manarâ nâŋeraonec ŋic âgofâc-nâŋec tucnezi rarâ ŋokac mumbieŋ sâc bâfuambieŋ â e jahacne ine mi honembieŋ.”
Dâŋ iŋuc muhuc âzâcnepire eki muwec: “Porofete jaŋe dâŋ mu qâreŋ embiŋ i ŋoŋe wemocte mutuc â maŋ mâmâcne juhuc mi mana šakieeŋgopieŋ?
Kristo e wemocko hâmoc šâic tâmiric juku sambâŋ tatamac-ticnao rašizac?”
Iŋuc murâ Mose â porofete dâŋ erao iticnehuc qâreŋkembiŋ, irec fuŋne ritu-jacte-fârewec.
Eme raku Emausi hae bâqiŋkembiŋ. Ehuc eki hae fotâcnerâ raocte eme
jahe sakarehuc mupic, “Ʒoaŋ biac rifireha hae ŋafezo ekacte go nâhehec juc.” Eme jahehec juocte mana-jacteme ficko mâmâc fembiŋ.
Eme nânâ nâniŋte waha ŋerâ poroŋ rorâ jambuŋkehuc bazurâ jactewec.
Ehame šâŋe-jekic raruŋkeme hone tarapic. Hone tarapire izia sipuac ewec.
Eme jahe nazaŋ gazaŋ erâ kecšiŋuc mupic: “Hatao dâŋ nâsâhuc mitire fuŋne ritu-nâcteme bunâhec bâruŋkejec hâcne ine.”
Iŋuc murâ izia faharerâ Jerusalem haeo risie rapic. Ra fisirâ e jahacne motec 11 â âgofâc-jeŋic gâcne tumaŋnerâ ŋehapie bâfuac-jopapire
jaŋe biac šiŋuc jasambiŋ: “Wofuŋ e jâmbomac faharerâ Simoŋ fuacnejec.”
Eme jahe iŋuc jaha Wofuŋzi hatao bâfuac-jofarâ ficko poroŋ bazume šâŋitapic, irec dâŋ binaŋ ejarepic.
Motec jaŋe irec dâŋ binaŋ ehuc ŋehapie Jesu e jahac ŋondeŋ-jeŋicko fuarâ domawec.
Eme jaŋe honerâ fâfârerâ hâwic-jopame mumbiŋ, “Bawezi fuakac.”
Eme eki šiŋuc jazawec: “Ŋoŋe wemocte fâfârerâ maŋjahec eŋgopieŋ?
ši no nahac jâmbâŋ jukopac, ŋoŋe me kike-nane honeniŋ, ehuc ware bâuacnurâ hone-hâmocnuniŋ, no sahac biuc-nanehec, bawe jaŋe ijeŋichec aricne.”
Dâŋ iŋuc jazarâ, mejahecne â kike jahecne jowatuwec.
Eme jaŋe bujeŋic biaŋkeme dâŋticne mi mamana mâc wareckehuc ŋepie wio-jarerâ muwec:
“Nânâ-ŋeŋic moc fokac me?” Eme jaŋe opâ qowi šegoc šakicne moc râcnerâ
honehapie ro nâc ewec.
Erâ šiŋuc jazawec: “No ŋoŋehec juhuc kecšiŋuc ŋaza jupac: `Mosere sâcmutâc dâŋqâhâcko â porofete jaŋere papiao â miti mânecko nore findaŋdâŋ qâreŋkekicne, i fârinehec efâreocmu. Ž ”
Eme miti papiao dâŋqâreŋ fokac irec fuŋne ritu-jarekume maŋjeŋic uŋtowec.
Ehuc jazawec, “Kristore šiŋuc qâreŋkekicne: `E šâic manaku hâmorâ šoaŋ jahec â moc eha hâmockonec ɋârerâ fahareocmu. Ž
Á šâŋe biŋe-ticne ŋic mâreŋ sâc jaŋerao rame maŋ bâbârisie â sâqocne mumutâmire fua raocte mukicne. Gie i Jerusalem haeo fuŋkerâ barazo.
Wiac irec mumutaniŋ ŋic ŋoŋe hâcne.
Erâ manaŋgopieŋ, Mamac-nanezi wiac biŋe qaŋarewec i sorepe waha-ŋareocmu. Irec ŋoŋe hae ši mi behehuc mâc woŋec juhapie faic irec tâpiri heŋarepe huzejec.”
Eme haeonec jowac-jopa rarâ Betania hae mendâŋko fisirâ meticne sicnehuc jambuŋ-jopawec.
Jambuŋ-jopahuc behec-joparâ fewec.
Eme jaŋe bubiaŋ kâcɋene manahuc Jerusalem haeo risiembiŋ.
Risierâ taha ufuŋko hati jurâ ju ehuc Anutu muteŋkembiŋ.
Micdâŋ e fuŋnao fuŋkerâ juwarehuc juwec. Erâ Micdâŋ e juju-ticne Anuturao foha juhuc juwec. Erâ Micdâŋ e Anutu jaha wâc juwec.
E hâcne fuŋnao Anutuhec jurâ juwarewec.
Erâ Micdâŋ e Anuture me wâc ehuc wiac sasawa bâfua-fârewec, â wiac fuawec i e tâmiric moc mi fuawec.
Erâ juju irec rune erâ juwec. Á juju-ticnezi ŋic tamae-jarewec.
Eme tatamaczi dapâcko tamaeme dapâczi guriŋkeocte eipiewec.
Ŋic moc fuarâ juwec šâŋene Johane.
Eki tatamacte biŋedâŋ mufuame ŋic mâmâc sasawa jaŋe tatamac rune manasiŋkeniŋte Anutuzi sorewec.
Johane e jahacne tatamac rune mi juwec, e mâc tatamac runere biŋe muwec.
Tatamac rune ŋic mâreŋ sâc batamaec-jopaekac, eki hâcne dameŋ ira mâreŋko fuarâ juwec.
E mâreŋko fufua i fuawec, erâ i sawa mâcne, mâreŋ i ekizia wâc bâfuawec, eme waharâ fuame mâreŋkonec ŋic jaŋe e sifu mi šâŋitambiŋ.
E jahacne me hofao fisihame gurufâc-ticne jaŋe âgo mi ecnembiŋ.
Á âgo ecnembiŋ jaŋe ine Anuture naru motecfâc eniŋte hata bâfua-jarewec, i šâŋe-ticne mana maŋ eeŋgopieŋ jaŋe hâcne iŋuc ejareekac.
Jaŋe soc biucte hatao mi fuambiŋ, erâ ŋic mumupaŋte wâc mâcne, jaŋe Anuturaonec fuambiŋ.
Eme Micdâŋ e sahac biuchec fuarâ ŋondeŋ-nâŋecko ŋeŋe juju ewec. Eme nâŋe Wofuŋ qâreŋ-ticne honepene Mamacte ŋokâ jâmbâŋ mocjaha ere Wofuŋ qâreŋ ewec hâcne. E aki anonoc kadahe â dâŋ fâri qizecne bawahawec.
Fuŋne-ticne ine Johanezi mutaniŋkerâ hahaŋne bahuc kecšiŋuc muwec: “No ere hâcne ŋazapo, šâhec warekac e bâbâni juwec, eki no mi fuahape juwarehuc juwec hâcne.”
Nâŋe sasawa ere rowaŋkonec miti kadahe rorâ ro ehuc jumbeŋ.
Mose e sâcmutâc dâŋ nârewec, â Jesu Kristo eki ine aki anonoc â dâŋ fâri qizecne tahac-nâpowec.
Anutu e ŋic moczi moc mi honewec, Ŋokâ jâmbâŋ mocjaha, Mamacte bufuŋko juekaczi ine biŋe-ticne bawaharâ mufua-nârewec.
Jerusalem haeonec Judaŋic jaŋe taha bapa â taha ufuŋte kiŋaŋŋic sorec-jopapie Johanerao rarâ, go mo ŋic mo, muhuc wiocnepie fuŋne-ticne jazawec.
E fuŋne-ticne mi hesoŋkehuc mutaniŋkerâ kecšiŋuc jazawec: “No Kristo aricne.”
Mume jaŋe harierâ wiocnembiŋ, “Eme go mo, go Elia me?” Eme muwec, “No e aricne.” Eme mumbiŋ, “Go porofete-nâŋec me?” Mupie muwec, “Aricne.”
Eme jaŋe mumbiŋ: “Wiac go mo? Sorec-nâpopie warembeneŋ, ra weniŋuc jazanaŋmu? Go gahacnere weniŋuc muekic?”
Eme jazarâ muwec: “Porofete Jesajazi mu qâreŋ ewec, i norao sanaŋkekac. No biŋe mumu ŋic, mâreŋ tuhuo juhuc kecšiŋuc muekopac: `Wofuŋte hata bâšâweniŋ!”
Ŋic Johanerao fisimbiŋ i jaŋe farisaio jaŋere guruonec.
Irec mocwâc indiŋkerâ mumbiŋ: “Go Kristo aricne, â Elia aricne, â porofete aricne, eme wemocte ŋic Miti Opâ rua-jareekic?”
Mupie Johanezi šiŋuc jazawec: “Noni ŋic opâ sawa rua-jareekopac, â ŋondeŋ-ŋeŋicko moc fuawec jukac, ŋoŋe e mi hone taraeŋgopieŋ,
eki hâcne râpefuŋ-naneo warehuc jukac, e sâko no iŋucne maczi mafahe decnepe mi sâckeocmu.”
Wiac i Betania haeo Jordaŋ ocniŋucnao fuawec. Ira hâcne Johanezi juhuc ŋic Miti Opâ rua-jarewec.
Hae fureme Jesuzi Johanerao rame taicko honerâ ŋic šiŋuc jazawec: “Honeniŋ, kecocni Anuture lama, eki mâreŋ sâc ŋic sâqocne-jeŋic fainao feme âsickekac.
Ere hâcne kecšiŋuc ŋazapo: `šâhec warekac, e bâbâni juwec, eki no mi fuahape juwarewec. Ž
No nahac mârâc e mi hone tarapo. Israe ŋic ŋoŋe biŋe-ticne ŋazape mananiŋte hâcne fisirâ Miti Opâ fuŋkepo.”
Johane e iŋuc murâ muwec: “No Mârozi hapâ hawario sambâŋkonec waharâ fai-ticnao herâ ŋeme honepo.
No nahac mârâc mi hone tarahape Miti Opâre munareweczi šiŋuc nazawec: `Mâro waharâ fai-ticnao herâ ŋeme honecmu eki ŋic Tiri Mâro rua-jareocmu. Ž
No i hâcne honepore fuŋne-ticne kecšiŋuc mupo: `Eki hâcne Anuture Ŋokâ. Ž ”
Hae fureme Johane erâ motecfâcne jaŋeraonec jajahec mâreŋ ijaha domambiŋ.
Domahapie Jesu e ijaha fotâcneme honerâ motec jasarâ muwec: “Honenic, Anuture lama kecocni.”
Mume jahe dâŋ i manarâ Jesure râpefuŋko rapic.
Rapire Jesuzi forisierâ honec-jofarâ muwec” “Ŋohe wemocte warekopirec?” Eme jahe mupic: “Rabi (nâŋâcne dâŋko: Qaqazu), go fic wena jukomec?”
Eme šiŋuc jasawec: “Ware honenic.” Mume jahe bâjâperâ fic honerâ šoaŋ gie bapa ira juweckoa jupic. I šoaŋ otewezo eha iŋuc epic.
Johanere dâŋ manarâ Jesu bâjâpepic moc šâŋene Anderea, Simoŋ Petoro ɋaticne.
Eme eki biac hahac-ticne Simoŋ bâfuarâ šiŋuc âzâcnewec: “Nâhe Mesia (Kristo hâcne(c) bâfuakoperec.”
Iŋuc murâ Jesurao jowame rapic. Eme Jesuzi honerâ muwec: “Go Simoŋ, Johanere ŋokâ, gore šâŋe Kefa mukopac” (nâŋâcne dâŋko: Haroŋaŋ).
Hae fureme Jesu e Galilaia mâreŋko raocte šawierâ Filipo bâfuarâ âzâcnewec, “Go bâjâpecnuc.”
Filipo e Besaida haeonec, Anderea â Petoro jahe hae irecteaŋ.
Eme Filipozi Natanae bâfuarâ šiŋuc âzâcnewec: “Mose e sâcmutâc dâŋqâhâcko findaŋdâŋ-ticne qâreŋkewec, â porofete jaŋe wâc qâreŋkembiŋ, ŋic e hâcne bâfuaŋgopeneŋ, Jesu, Josefere ŋokâ, Nazarete haeonec.”
Eme Natanaezi dâŋ šiŋuc bâtikiecnewec: “Nazarete haeonec wemo wiac bipinehec fuaocmu?” Mume Filipozi šiŋuc âzâcnewec: “Murâ ware honec.”
Eme Natanaezi Jesurao ra fisime honerâ muwec, “Honeniŋ, ŋic kecizi Israe ŋic fârine, maŋticnao sioc moc mi fokac.”
Iŋuc mume Natanaezi wiocnerâ muwec: “Go wena jupe honecnumeŋ?” Eme Jesuzi muwec, “Filipozi mi hefârecguhame nemuja fuŋko ŋetec honecgupac.”
Mume Natanaezi šiŋuc âzâcnewec: “Qaqazu, go jâmbomac Anuture ŋokâ, Israe ŋic nâŋere ŋicwofuŋ.”
Eme Jesuzi muwec: “Nemuja fuŋko ŋemec i mufua-garepe manasiŋnukomec, manakic, hone manac ekomec ši susucne sawa, fâri ombâŋne miŋecnea hone manac erahuc jucmu.”
Iŋuc murâ muwec, “No jâmbomac jâmbâŋ ŋazape: Ŋoŋe sambâŋ aŋkeme Anuture aŋelofâc jaŋe Ŋic Fâri Wâtuŋne erao fec wahac epie honec-jopaniŋmu.”
Gie bapa jajahec tarame Kana haeo Galilaia mâreŋko ŋic ŋokac jajahec muturec-jofaniŋte irec tiwâ bâzi qapie fisiwec.
Ehuc Jesu neŋgoc-ticne erâ e jahacne â motecfâc-ticne mâmâc hefârec-jopapie fisimbiŋ.
Eme tumaŋnerâ bâzihec waiŋ nâpie šickeme Jesu neŋgoc-ticnezi e âzâcnerâ muwec: “Waiŋ-jeŋic omaekac.”
Mume Jesuzi šiŋuc âzâcnewec: “Ŋokac, i nâhâcne wiac me? Dameŋ-nane miŋecnea maickeocmu.”
Eme neŋgoc-ticnezi kiŋaŋ qaqa šiŋuc jazawec: “Wiac mocte ŋazame enšepieŋ.”
Eme fic ira opâ pake 6 ŋewec. Judaŋic jaŋe me sahac-jeŋic gâbâ šure jumbieŋte fic sâc opâ pake iŋuc ŋerawec. Pake i piticne mâcne, kâcɋene sâko.
Eme Jesuzi kiŋaŋ qaqa šiŋuc jazawec: “Ŋoŋe opâ fiarâ pakeo qapie huoc.” Eme jaŋe iŋuc erâ opâ qapie hurâ pake micnao qafârewec.
Iŋuc epie šiŋuc jazawec: “Ŋoŋe tucne fiarâ nânâ soŋaŋtao baraniŋ.”
Eme jaŋe fiarâ barahapie opâzi waiŋ eme nânâ soŋaŋzi nâhonerâ kâuc bawec. Kiŋaŋ motec opâ fiarâ pakeo qapie huwec jaŋe sawazi waiŋte fuŋne mana tarambiŋ. Eme nânâ soŋaŋzi ŋic ŋokac bawec, e hefârerâ
šiŋuc âzâcnewec: “Qanaŋ waiŋ aŋacne gumec-jopapene nâkupie maŋjeŋic bibiriwazo eme šâhec waiŋ oomane gumec-jopaeŋgopeneŋ, hata-nâŋec iŋuc fokac. Go ine qac qâtikic ehuc aŋacne hefacketec ŋeku šâhec fuakac.”
Jesu e Kana haeo Galilaia mâreŋko ira hâcne mâsi bapa gie-ticne fuŋkehuc Wofuŋ qâreŋ-ticnere foŋ bararuŋkewec. Eme motecfâcne jaŋe honerâ e manasiŋkembiŋ.
Eme Jesu e Kana haeonec Kafanaum haeo rame neŋgoc ɋafâc-ticne â motecfâc-ticne mâmâc bâjâperâ rafârembiŋ. Eme ira boc mi jumbiŋ.
Judaŋic aakic hombaŋ-jeŋic bembeŋkewecte Jesuzi Jerusalem haeo rafewec.
Eme taha ufuŋ šuhucnao lama bulimakao â hapâ wiac badomahuc nareŋ gareŋ embiŋ, ehuc irec moneŋ teboo wose biric embiŋ.
Iŋuc epie Jesuzi honec-joparâ repa mizeme šika eme ŋic mecne lama bulimakao mecne jâpec-jopame wisepie moneŋ tie-jarerâ irec tebo herândiŋkewec.
Erâ hapâ badomambiŋ jaŋe šiŋuc jazawec: “Ŋoŋe Mamac-nanere ficko wiac kosa mi epie situâc fic ezejec.”
Jesu e iŋuc eme motecfâcne jaŋe miti papiao dâŋqâreŋ kecšiŋuc fokac irec manasumbiŋ: “Gore ficte erâ bunane šoc šarâ šâfitacnukac.”
Eme Judaŋic jaŋe wiocnerâ mumbiŋ: “Go iŋuc ekomeczi wemo mâsi moc bahuc fuŋnege bataniŋke-nârecmu?”
Eme micjeŋicko rorâ šiŋuc jazawec: “Ŋoŋe taha ufuŋ kecši heropiepie noni šoaŋ jahec â moc eha mocwâc bâzickepemu.”
Iŋuc muhuc jazame mumbiŋ, “Kâcɋenefâc-nâŋec jaŋe taha ufuŋ ši jara 46 baku bâzickembiŋ, eme goki šoaŋ jahec â moc sawa ira bâzickezo mukomec me?”
Jesu eki ine sahac-ticnere ufuŋko ɋetickehuc muwec.
Juku hâmockonec ɋârerâ fahareme motecfâcne jaŋe dâŋ i manasumbiŋ. Ehuc ufuŋte muwec, â miti papiao ere dâŋ gâcne mukicne, irec mâmâc manapie fârine eha mana šakiembiŋ.
Jesu e aakic hombaŋko Jerusalem haeo juhuc fuŋne qaqa mâsi bame ŋic bocjahazi honerâ šâŋe-ticne mana sakac embiŋ.
Jesu e jahac ine ŋic hone tarac-jopa-fârewecte jaŋerao mi fohorewec.
E ŋic mocte fuŋne manaocte gâcne mu indiŋ mi ejarewec, e jahaczia ŋic maŋjeŋic hone šâŋitac ejare-fârewec.
Farisaio ŋic jaŋere âgo moc juwec šâŋene Nikodemo. E Judaŋic jaŋere micne sâko wâc juwec.
Ŋic eki hâcne Jesu ŋafeo iqickerâ šiŋuc âzâcnewec: “Qaqazu, nâŋe fuŋnege manaeŋgopeneŋ, go qaqazu fârinezi Anuturaonec wahameŋ, go mâsi baekic i ŋic moczi Anutu tâmiric juhuc bapane mi ekac.”
Mume Jesuzi šiŋuc âzâcnewec: “No jâmbomac jâmbâŋ gazape: Moc e harierâ fufua ɋâricne mi fuaocmuzi Anuture uucmaŋ sâcne mi bâfuaocmu.”
Eme Nikodemozi muwec, “Hâc, moc e kâcɋeŋkekicnezi fufua ɋâricne weniŋuc fuaocmu, wemocko neŋgoc bumaŋko mocwâc hume hâsine roocmu?”
Mume Jesuzi šiŋuc âzâcnewec: “No jâmbomac jâmbâŋ gazape: Moc e Opâ â Mârore kiwecko ɋâricne mi fuakicnezi Anuture uucmaŋko sâcne mi rašiocmu.
Ŋickiwecko fuakicnezi ŋic hawari jaha, Mârore kiwecko fuakicnezi Mârore hawari jaha.
Ŋoŋe fufua ɋâricne fuaniŋte mupe go manatec mi quŋkeoc.
Mâŋâŋ e kosa qaekac, eme go fânâŋ-ticne i manaekic, â fuŋne wenirec fuŋkerâ wareekac, â wena rataraekac, ine mi manaekic. Eme moc e Mârore kiwecko fuakicne, e fuŋne-ticne iŋucnea fokac.”
Mume Nikodemozi dâŋ šiŋuc bâtikiecnewec: “I weniŋuc erâ iŋuc ezo?”
Mume Jesuzi šiŋuc âzâcnewec: “Go Israe ŋic jaŋere qaqazuzi irec kâuc bakomec me?
No jâmbomac jâmbâŋ gazape: Nâŋe wiac hone manac eeŋgopeneŋ ijaha ŋaza mutâc eeŋgopeneŋ, eme ŋoŋe ine dâŋnâŋec qikiŋneeŋgopieŋ.
Wiac mâreŋko fufuane irec mac ŋazape sifu mi mana šakieeŋgopieŋ, eme wiac sambâŋko fufuane irec ŋazape wemo-ŋeŋiczi mana šakieniŋmu?
Ŋic moczi sambâŋko moc mi fewec, Ŋic Fâri Wâtuŋne, sambâŋkonec wahawec, e mocjahazi sambâŋko wâc juekac.
“Mose e mârâc jaha mâreŋ sawao homa bâfeŋnewec, iŋuc jaha Ŋic Fâri Wâtuŋne e bâfeŋnezo mukicne.
Eme e manasiŋkeniŋmu jaŋe juju sanaŋ bâfuaniŋmu.
Anutu e ŋic ŋoŋere mo iŋucne ecnewecte Ŋokâ jâmbâŋ-ticne mocjaha e râe qikiŋ ecnewec. Eme e manasiŋkeniŋmu jaŋe moc mi sipirickehuc ju ju sanaŋ bâfuaniŋmu.
Ŋokâ e ŋic jaŋere kiŋ bataraocte mâcne, ŋic bâpiaŋ-jopaocte Anutuzi soreme wahawec.
Moc e Ŋokâ manasiŋkekaczi okacnere biŋe mi ekac. Á moc e Ŋokâ mi manasiŋkekaczi ine biac okacnere biŋe ekac. Wemocte? E Anuture ŋokâ jâmbâŋ mocjaha ere šâŋe mana maŋ mi ekac irec.
Okacnere fuŋne šiŋuc fokac: Tatamaczi ŋic maic-jopame jaŋe tatamac bâsuerâ dapâcte wosâembiŋ, juju bapa-jeŋic sâqocnere iŋuc hâcne embiŋ.
Moc e sindaŋ eocmuzi tatamac râpeckeocmu, juju bapa-ticnere fuŋne jaŋgeŋkezacte wemocko tatamacko fua taniŋ eocmu.
Moc e dâŋ fâri qizecne reŋkeocmuzi ine tatamac maickeocmu, eme eebapa-ticne Anuture micdâŋte sâcko ekicne irec fuŋne taniŋkeocmu.”
Eme juku Jesu e motecfâcne rocjopame Jerusalem hae beherâ Judaia qaŋeŋnaopec ra jumbiŋ. Ira jaŋehec juhuc ŋic opâ rua-jarewec.
Johane e mâreŋ moc šâŋene Ainoŋ, Salim haeopec juhuc iŋuc jaha Miti Opâ gie bawec, ira opâ bocjaha fowecte ŋic jaŋe fisipie rua-jarewec.
Johane e dameŋ ira kâpâcwâru ficko mi ŋekicne.
Eme Judaŋic moczi Johane motecfâc-ticne jaŋehec opâ ruruare mu qaqatarac embiŋ.
Eme motec jaŋe Johanerao rarâ šiŋuc âzâcnembiŋ: “Qaqazu, go Jordaŋ ocniŋucnao juhaŋtecne ŋic moc bâfuacgume fuŋne-ticne mujaŋgeŋkerâ nâzâmeŋ, eki dameŋ šiŋuczia ŋic opâ rua-jareme erao rafâreŋgopieŋ.”
Mupie Johanezi šiŋuc jazawec: “Ŋic moc e sambâŋ runezi wiac râcne tahac mi ehame e jahac wemocko kâŋgâc roocmu.
No kecšiŋuc muhuc ŋazapo i wemocko mickeniŋmu, `No Kristo aricne, no biŋe mumu-ticne sawa. Ž
Ŋokac biŋe mucnekicne eki hâcne ŋokac rune. Eme ŋokac bahuc šeri kâcɋene šeri eme âgo-ticnezi manarâ bafickehuc bubiaŋ sâko bâfuaocmu wâc. Bubiaŋ i hâcne manapemurâ dameŋne maickekac ši.
Eki fua fehame noni pitiwazepac.
Faicnec wahaweczi qâhuc-nâpo-fârekac. Moc e mâreŋkonec fuakicnezi mâreŋte biŋe ekac â mâreŋkopec dâŋ muekac. Á sambâŋkonec wahaweczi ine qâhuc-nâpo-fârekac.
Eki wiac hone manac ewec irec dâŋ biŋe muekac. Mume ine ŋic jaŋe dâŋticne qikiŋneeŋgopieŋ.
Á dâŋticne mana maŋ ekac e Anutu mume sasanaŋ jukac dâŋ i dopeckekac.
Anutuzi ŋic sorewec eki Anuture dâŋ jaha muekac. Ŋic iŋucne e Anutuzi Mâro sâc tâmiric qikiŋnecneekac.
Mamac e Ŋokâ hone ririŋkehuc ere meo wiac sasawa râe-fârewec.
Moc e Ŋokâ manasiŋkeocmu e juju sanaŋ šiŋuczia fuacnekac, â moc e Ŋokâre dâŋ bâsuehuc juocmuzi juju sanaŋ mi bâfuaocmu. Iŋucnere faio Anuture kimbeŋ feweczi foocmu.”
Farisaio jaŋe Jesure šiŋuc manambiŋ: “Eki motec rocjoparâ opâ rua-jareekac, i Johanere gurufâc jowaruŋgopieŋ.”
Dâŋ i mâc mumbiŋ, Jesu e jahac ŋic opâ mi rua-jarewec, motec jaŋe mume rua-jarembiŋ.
Eme Wofuŋzi dâŋ iŋucne manarâ Judaia mâreŋ beherâ Galilaia mâreŋko risie rawec.
Rahuc Samaria mâreŋ fotâcnewec.
Fotâcnehuc Samariare hae moc šâŋene Sika ira fisiwec. Hae i Jakobozi ŋokâ-ticne Josefe mâreŋ qikiŋnecnewec irec mendâŋko ŋewec.
Eme ijaha Jakobore opâ nombâŋ fowec wâc. Eme Jesu e ira guŋpiticko fisirâ betaŋkerâ nombâŋmecko waha ŋemanawec.
Ŋehame Samaria ŋokac moczi opâ fiaocte fisiwec. Fisime Jesuzi šiŋuc âzâcnewec: “Go opâ moc gumecnuc.”
Motecfâcne jaŋe nânâ furine baniŋte haeo fehapie Jesu buc ŋehuc ŋokac opâre âzâcnewec.
Âzâcneme ŋokac e muwec, “Go Judaŋiczi weniŋuc erâ Samaria ŋokac norao opâre mukic?” Judaŋic â Samaria ŋic jaŋe bâtâcko jujumbieŋte ŋokac e iŋuc muwec.
Eme Jesuzi šiŋuc âzâcnewec: “Go Anutu jauŋ-ticnere fuŋne â opâre gazakopac nore fuŋne mâmâc kâuc bakic. Mana tararâ muzac numu-naretec opâ fifisine garezapo.”
Mume ŋokaczi šiŋuc âzâcnewec: “Bomboŋ, opâ nombâŋ i šoricne, erâ go opâ fifiage aricnere opâ fifisine wenirec fiacmu?
Mimiŋne-nâŋec Jakobo e opâ nombâŋ ši rowec. Erâ e jahacne â ŋokâfâcne â lama bulimakaofâc-ticne jaŋe opâ ši jaha nâhuc jumbiŋ. Goki Jakobore sâc i jâuruhuc opâ moc bâfuacmu?”
Iŋuc mume Jesuzi šiŋuc âzâcnewec: “Opâ ši gapecne tâmiric, irec i hati nârâ nâ ehuc juzo,
â nore opâ ine gapecnehec, moc e i nâocmu, e opâre mocwâc mi hâmohuc mâc jurašihuc juocmu. Noni opâ i ŋic moc râcnepe maŋticnao opâ šâŋe bâfuacneme juju sanaŋte šâkâŋko rahuc domaocmu.”
Mume ŋokaczi šiŋuc muwec: “Bomboŋ, go opâ i naretec nârâ opâre mocwâc mi hâmozepac, ehuc šira gâbâ ware fiahuc domaekopac i behezepac.”
Iŋuc mume Jesuzi šiŋuc âzâcnewec: “Ra ŋowege jowatec warenic.”
Eme ŋokaczi muwec, “No ŋowe-nane aricne.” Mume Jesuzi muwec, “Go ŋowege aricne, i sâcne mukomec”
go ŋic memoc ba behec ejaremeŋ, â šiŋuczia bakomec e gore ŋowe aricne, irec go dâŋ jâmbomac mukomec.”
Mume ŋokaczi šiŋuc âzâcnewec: “ŋicbomboŋ-nane, no miŋecne manakopac, go porofete.
Irec mutec manape: Kâcɋenefâc-nâŋec jaŋe tiki kecšira Anutu mai ecne jumbieŋ, â Judaŋic ŋoŋe ine Jerusalem haeoa Anutu mai ecnezo, iŋuc mueŋgopieŋ.”
Eme Jesuzi šiŋuc muwec: “Ŋokac, no gazape manac: Dameŋ moc bembeŋkekac, i maickeme ŋoŋe Mamac mai ecneniŋmu i tiki kecšira mâcne â Jerusalem haeo wâc mi eniŋmu.
Ŋoŋe kâuc bahuc mai ecneeŋgopieŋ, nâŋe ine mana tarahuc mai ecneeŋgopeneŋ. Bâbâpiaŋ i Judaŋic nâŋeraonec.
Dameŋ moc maickeocmu erâ ši biac maickekac hâcne, ira kikefuŋfâc-ticne fârine jaŋe maŋzi â dâŋ fâri qizecnere sâcko Mamac mai ecneniŋmu. Mamac e ŋic iŋucne jaŋere ecneekac.
Anutu e Mâro fuŋgâtâne, irec e mai ecneeŋgopieŋ ŋoŋe Mâro â dâŋ fâri qizec jahere ŋesiŋko mai ecnenšepieŋ.”
Mume ŋokaczi šiŋuc âzâcnewec: “No manakopac, Mesia fuaocte mukicne, šâŋene moc Kristo, eki fuarâ wiac sasawa mu bataniŋ enâreocmu.”
Eme Jesuzi âzâcnewec: “Dâŋ gazakopac, no hâcne ši.”
Iŋuc muhame motecfâcne fisimbiŋ. Fisirâ ŋokachec muc manac ewec irec wareckembiŋ. Erâ wemo wiacte dâŋ âzâcnekomec, me weniŋucte âzâcnekomec, iŋuc muhuc wiocneniŋte manapie quŋkeme behembiŋ.
Eme ŋokac e opâ râqâc-ticne beherâ haeo gasacke rarâ ŋic šiŋuc jazawec:
“Ŋoŋe warerâ ŋic moc honeniŋ, eki epo bapo irec dâŋ mutaniŋke-nare-fârekac. E Kristo wiac moc?”
Eme haeonec waharâ Jesurao fisi-fârembiŋ.
Eme motec jaŋe šiŋuc âzâcnembiŋ: “Qaqazu, nânâ nâc.”
Mupie jazawec, “Nânâ fuŋmoc fonarekac, i ŋoŋe mi manaŋgopieŋ.”
Iŋuc mume motec jaŋackoaŋ nazaŋ gazaŋ erâ mumbiŋ: “Moczi moc nânâ bafisirâ râcnembieŋ me?”
Mupie muwec, “Sorecnuwec ere mic reŋkehuc gie-ticne baku babatara izi nânâ-nane ekac.
Ŋaŋac šiŋuc mueŋgopieŋ: `Mosa 4 tarame nânâ fârine fuaocmu. Ž Á noni ine ŋazape mananiŋ: Ŋoŋe qâhâŋnerâ šâŋe fihuc gie honeniŋ, nânâ fârine fufua dameŋ šine hâcne maickekac.
Ro qânusuc gie baocmuzi furine roocmu, â fârinezi ju ju sanaŋte biŋe eocmu. Eme he sarac ewec â fârine rome fewec jahe mâmâc babafic erâ šeri enicmu.
Ehame dâŋ kecši sanaŋkeocmu: `Moczi he sarac eekac, â moczi fârine rome feekac. Ž
Noni ŋoŋe he sarac mi embiŋko fârine ropie feocte sorec-ŋopakopac. Gie i gâcnezi bapie fuawec eme ŋoŋe mâc rauckeŋgopieŋ.”
Eme Samaria ŋokac e haefâc-ticne šiŋuc jazawec: “Wiac epo bapo i mutaniŋke-nare-fârejec.” Eme dâŋ irec bocjahazi Jesu manasiŋkembiŋ.
Irec Jesurao fisirâ jaŋehec juocte hefârembiŋ. Eme Jesuzi mana-jarerâ šoaŋ gie bapa jajahec jaŋere haeo juwec.
Eme miti jazame bocjaha jâmbâŋzi mana šakiembiŋ.
Ehuc ŋokac šiŋuc âzâcnembiŋ: “Qanaŋ gore dâŋ binaŋte erâ manasiŋkembeneŋ, ši ine nâŋe nâŋâc micticnaonec dâŋ manarâ šiŋuc manapaŋkeŋgopeneŋ: Eki jâmbomac mâreŋ sâc ŋic nâŋâcne Bâbâpiaŋ.”
Eme Jesu e jaŋehec gie bapa jajahec jurâ Galilaia mâreŋko rawec.
Jesu e jahac qanaŋ šiŋuc mufuawec: “Porofete moc e jahacne hae mâreŋko jume sâcne mi sâseniŋmu.”
Eme Galilaia mâreŋko rafisime Galilaia ŋic jaŋe âgo ecnembiŋ. Ine jaŋe juwicnao mâmâc Jerusalem haeo rarâ aakic hombaŋko gie bame honembiŋte iŋuc ecnembiŋ.
Eme Kana haeo Galilaia mâreŋko mârâc mume opâzi waiŋ ewec ira hâcne mocwâc risiewec. Eme Kafanaum haeo kia moc juwec, e ŋokâ-ticne hucsâko bame fowec.
Eme Jesu e Judaia mâreŋkonec risierâ Galilaia mâreŋko mocwâc ware fisikac, iŋuc mupie manarâ kia e Kana haeo Jesurao rarâ ŋokâ-ticne hâmozo ehuc fowec irec jowame ranicte numucnewec.
Eme Jesuzi šiŋuc âzâcnewec: “Ŋoŋe mâsi â wiac šâŋe furu-ŋeŋic sawa honerâ dâŋnane mana šakieeŋgopieŋ.”
Eme ŋiczi muwec: “Wofuŋ, ŋokâ-nane hâmozacte biac fâzemec.”
Mume Jesuzi šiŋuc âzâcnewec: “Go mâc rac, ŋokâge ɋiɋic qakac.” Eme ŋic e Jesure dâŋ mana šakiehuc risie rawec.
Ehame motec jaŋe kiŋaŋ warerâ šiŋuc âzâcnembiŋ: “Ŋokâge ɋiɋic qajec jukac.”
Mupie ɋiɋic qawec dameŋ irec mu indiŋ ejareme mumbiŋ: “Jacne šoaŋ šâšâŋiŋ ŋehame ira hucticne âke niniŋkejec.”
Iŋuc mupie ŋiczi fuŋne kecšiŋuc manawec: Dameŋ ira hâcne Wofuŋzi sorecnuhuc mujec, “Ŋokâge ɋiɋic qakac.” Eme e jahacne â garikiŋfâc-ticne Jesu manasiŋke-fârembiŋ.
Jesu e Judaia mâreŋkonec Galilaia mâreŋko risierâ fuŋne qaqa mâsi i bame jajahec ewec.
Juku Judaŋic jaŋere hombaŋ sâko moc maickeme Jesu e Jerusalem haeo rafewec.
Eme Jerusalem haeo Lama Motâcko riqic moc ŋewec šâŋene Betesida Ere mecnao fic memoc ŋerawec.
Fic ira ŋic huchec â tiŋtuŋ â šeke puriŋ â soc kekereŋhec bocjaha fombiŋ, [ehuc opâ qiriŋ qaocte woŋeckembiŋ”
Wofuŋte aŋelo moczi dameŋ ocŋondeŋ sâc riqicko waharâ opâ qâuawec” qâuahame moczi bâbâni opâo huwec e huc ecnewec i niniŋkecneme ɋiɋic qawec.Ý
Eme moc fowec e puriŋ ecnehuc juhame jara 38 ewec.
Eme Jesuzi ŋic e honerâ dameŋ šora fohuc jukac, iŋuc manarâ wiocnerâ muwec: “Go ɋiɋic qacmurâ egarekac me?”
Eme puriŋzi muwec, “Bomboŋ, mo ŋic mo junarekaczi opâ qiriŋ qaha riqicko râecnuzac? Á no nahac huzo mupe ine moczi biac âkehocnurâ huekac.”
Mume Jesuzi šiŋuc âzâcnewec: “Go faharerâ fofoge rorâ rac.”
Mume izia sahac-ticne biaŋkeme faharerâ fofo-ticne ameckerâ rawec. Ʒoaŋ ira ine sabata hombaŋ ŋembiŋ.
Irec Judaŋic jaŋe ŋic ɋiɋic qawec e šiŋuc âzâcnembiŋ: “Miŋecgac hombaŋko fofoge hâpokomec i mi eene.”
Mupie šiŋuc jazawec: “Bâpiaŋnukaczi šiŋuc naza sorec ekac: `Fofoge rorâ rac. Ž ”
Mume wiocnerâ mumbiŋ, “Fofoge rorâ rac gazajec ŋic e šâŋene mo?”
Mupie ŋic biaŋkeweczi kâuc bawec. Jesu e ŋicguru ira domambiŋ jaŋere ŋondeŋko kamierâ rawec.
Izi šâhec Jesuzi ŋic e taha ufuŋko bâfuarâ uŋ šiŋuc âzâcnewec: “Go sahacge biaŋkejec, eme wiac ŋemâc bâmâcne jâmbâŋ fua-garezacte sâqocne mocwâc mi bazemec.”
Eme ŋic e Jesu hone tararâ ra Judaŋic šiŋuc jazawec: “Ŋic bâpiaŋnukac šâŋene Jesu.”
Jesu e sabata hombaŋko gie iŋucne bawecte Judaŋic jaŋe râsi ecnembiŋ.
Epie Jesuzi šiŋuc jazawec: “Mamac-nane e gie šušuhuc jaha baekac, eme noni iŋuc jaha wâc eekopac.”
Eme Jesu e sabata hombaŋ hesifuckewec â Anuture Mamac-nane muhuc Anuture sâcko šuhuckewec, Judaŋic jaŋe wiac jajahec irec erâ mana gâpârerâ qaniŋte mumbiŋ.
Eme Jesuzi dâŋ šiŋuc jazawec: “No jâmbomac jâmbâŋ ŋazape mananiŋ, Ŋokâzi maŋticnere sâcne gie mi baekac, Mamaczi bame sâc honehuc baekac. Eki baekac ijaha Ŋokâzi baekac.
Mamac e Ŋokâ honebâckeekacte gie baekac sâc jâutu-fâreekac, erâ gie ši honeŋgopieŋ sawa mâcne, fekicne sâko jâutume ŋoŋe honerâ wareckeniŋmu.
Mamac e hâmokicne wiwic-joparâ bâɋârec-jopaekac, iŋuc jaha Ŋokâzi e me e bâɋârezo murâ bâɋâreocmu.
Erâ Mamac e ŋic okacnere dâŋ mi mutara-jareekac, gie i Ŋokâre meo râewec.
Eme ŋic jaŋe Mamac sâseeŋgopieŋ iŋuc jaha Ŋokâ sâsenšepieŋ. Moc e Ŋokâ mi sâseocmuzi, Ŋokâ sorewec, Mamac hâcne, e iŋuc jaha mi sâseocmu.
No jâmbomac jâmbâŋ ŋazape mananiŋ: Moczi nore dâŋ mana maŋ ehuc, sorecnuwec e manasiŋkeocmu, ŋic e šiŋuczia juju sanaŋhec ekac. E okacnere biŋe mi ee hâmoc râpeckerâ jujuo rašiwec jukac hâcne.
No jâmbomac jâmbâŋ ŋazape mananiŋ: Dameŋ moc maickeocmu, erâ ši biac maickekac hâcne, ira hâmokicnezi Anutu Ŋokâ-ticne ere dâŋ manarâ ɋârerâ juniŋmu.
Mamac e jujure fuŋqizecne, eme Ŋokâ e iŋuc jaha jujure fuŋqizecne eocte qikiŋnecnewec
Erâ e Ŋic Fâri Wâtuŋne jukacte ŋic,okacnere dâŋ mutara-jareocte mucnewec.
Dâŋ irec manapie mi quŋkezejec. Dameŋ moc bakicne fokac i maickeme šâŋeruŋko foeŋgopieŋ jaŋe ere dâŋ wiwira manarâ wefunšoŋgopieŋ.
Ehuc juju biaŋne jumbiŋzi juju sanaŋte faharenšoŋgopieŋ, â juju sâqocne jumbiŋzi kiŋte okacne roniŋte faharenšoŋgopieŋ.
No nahacne maŋte gie i bapane mi fokac, Mamac-nanere micsâcko sawa okacnere dâŋ mutara-jareekopac. Iŋuc ehuc okacnere gie bape sâckoa eocmu. I no nahacne dâŋ mâcne, sorecnuwec ere dâŋ šaeckeekopac.
“No nahac fuŋne-nane mutaniŋkepe fârimâc eocmu.
Fuŋne-nane i moczi mutaniŋkeocmu, erâ no manakopac, fuŋne-nane mutaniŋkeme fârine eocmu.
Ŋoŋe Johane mu indiŋ ecnepie dâŋ fâri qizecne mutaniŋkewec.
Erâ ŋiczi fuŋne-nane mutaniŋkeniŋte ine mi muekopac, ŋoŋe fuŋne-nane manarâ jujure hata âteniŋte irec mâc ŋaŋacnere muekopac.
Johane e jâmbomac lambe sâko erâ tamae-ŋarewec. Ehame ŋoŋe mâc šâziriŋne nacbembeŋ hone aŋac ehuc jumbiŋ sawa.
“Á nore fuŋne mutaniŋkeekac, e Johane iŋucne mâcne, e sâc moc. Mamac gie munarewec, gie irec fârine bâfuape ine Mamaczi sorecnume wahapo irec fuŋne taniŋkeekac.
Mamac sorecnuwec eki hâcne fuŋne-nane mutaniŋkewec. Ŋoŋe ine e jahacne mickonec dâŋ mi manambiŋ â hawarine wâc mi honembiŋ.
Erâ ŋoŋe dâŋticne maŋŋeŋicko sâcne mi râepie fohuc juekac. Ŋic sorewec ere dâŋ qikiŋnehuc wemocko iŋuc eniŋmu.
Ŋoŋe miti papiao kecšiŋuc muhuc wose gufuc eeŋgopieŋ: Juju sanaŋ ira hâcne soŋkekicne. Erâ izi hâcne nore fuŋne mufuaekac.
Eme ŋoŋe norao juhuc juju sanaŋhec ee i sifu qikiŋneeŋgopieŋ.
“No ŋiczi sahac mumuteŋ wiac enareniŋte irec mi muekopac.
Ŋoŋere fuŋne ine jâmbomac manaekopac, maŋŋeŋic Anuturea mi domaekac.
No Mamac-nanere micte ŋoŋerao wahapo, eme ŋoŋe sifu âgo mi enareeŋgopieŋ. Juku ŋic moc e e jahacne maŋte fisime ine âgo ecneniŋmu.
Ŋoŋe ŋaŋaczia mumuteŋ eec ehuc Anutu qâqâhâc sâko ere mumuteŋte mi eŋareekaczi wemocko mamanasiŋhec eniŋmu?
Ŋoŋe nore šiŋuc mi munšepieŋ: Eki Mamactao dâŋnâŋec mugâpâre-nâreocmu. Iŋuc mâcne, ŋoŋe ŋic moctao roweckeeŋgopieŋ, Mose hâcne, eki mugâpâre-ŋareocmu.
Mose e dâŋ qâreŋkewec i nore qâreŋkewec. Eme ŋoŋe ere dâŋ mana šakierâ muzac nore mâmâc mana šakienšapiŋ.
Mosere dâŋqâreŋ qikiŋnehuc nore dâŋ wemocko mana šakieniŋmu?”
Jesu e dâŋ i mufârerâ Galilaia riqic, Tiberia riqic hâcne, fotâcnerâ ocniŋucnao rašiwec.
Rašime ŋic ŋokac bocjahazi huc šâichec ɋiɋicne bacjopame honembiŋte bâjâpembiŋ.
Eme Jesuzi motecfâcne rocjopame tikio ferâ ŋembiŋ.
Dameŋ ira Judaŋic aakic hombaŋ-jeŋic bembeŋkewec.
Eme Jesuzi šâŋe firâ ŋic guru sâko fisipie honec-joparâ Filipo wiocnerâ muwec, “Poroŋ wenirec furine barâ i sâko gumec-jopapene sâcjopaocmu?”
E wiac eocte manasume foha mâc esâickewec.
Eme Filipozi šiŋuc muwec: “20 kinazi poroŋ furine barâ gumec-jopapene mâc hesâsâc-jopaocmu.”
Mume motecfâcne jaŋeraonec moc, Anderea, Simoŋ Petorore ɋa, eki šiŋuc muwec:
“Ʒira motec moc jukac eki poroŋ memoc â opâ qowi jajahec bajukac, erâ ŋic guru sâko jâmbâŋte keci mac izi wemo ezo?”
Eme Jesuzi muwec, “Ŋoŋe ŋic ejarepie qâzuckerâ waha ŋeniŋ.” Eme mâreŋ ira kecɋaŋ fowec i toma âterâ ŋic 5 tauseŋ qâririŋ iŋuczi waha ŋerambiŋ.
Eme Jesuzi poroŋ rorâ daŋge murâ ŋic ŋerambiŋ jaŋe bâtâc bajarewec â qowi iŋuc jaha mupie sâc jarewec.
Nârâ gapec-jopame Jesuzi motecfâcne šiŋuc jazawec: “Tiwâne forâ sipirickezacte nuseniŋ.”
Eme jaŋe poroŋ memoc irec tiwâne nusepie sasac 12 hurâ fusewec.
Eme ŋic jaŋe fuŋne qaqa mâsi i hone manac erâ mumbiŋ, “Porofete sâko mâreŋko fuaocte mukicne, šine hâcne jâmbâŋ.”
Eme jaŋe Jesu orâŋkerâ mezi rorâ ŋicwofuŋ-jeŋic âkendâŋnezo ehapie hone tarac-joparâ behec-joparâ e jahackoaŋ tikio fewec.
Hae owâeme motecfâcne jaŋe riqicmecko humbiŋ.
Hurâ Kafanaum haeo risie raniŋte wokeo fembiŋ. Erâ hae dapâc eme Jesu juhame buc rambiŋ.
Ehuc mâŋâŋ sanaŋne domame siri kâcɋene qame rambiŋ.
Jaŋe kilometa 4 me 5 irec sâc rakuhapie Jesuzi riqic faio âte âte rarâ woke bâqiŋkeme honerâ fâfârembiŋ.
Iŋuc epie wira-jarerâ muwec: “Nâhâc fâkopac, mi hâwic-ŋopaoc.”
Eme wokeo ropie feocte ehapie izia woke mâreŋ razo mumbiŋko fisiwec.
Ŋic guru sâko jaŋe riqic ocniŋucnao fohapie hae furewec. Hae fureme šiŋuc mumbiŋ: “Jacne ŋafeo woke mocsâkoa ŋeme honembeneŋ, ira motecfâcne Jesu beherâ buc ferâ rambieŋ.”
Iŋuc manahuc ŋehapie Tiberia haeonec woke gâcne Wofuŋzi daŋge murâ poroŋ gumec-jopawecko ware fisimbiŋ.
Eme ŋic jaŋe Jesu e jahacne â motecfâcne basac-joparâ wokeo ferâ Kafanaum haeo risie rarâ ira basambiŋ.
Riqic šiŋucnao basaku bâfuarâ mumbiŋ, “Qaqazu, go wezimucne waremec?”
Wiocnepie šiŋuc jazawec: “No jâmbomac jâmbâŋ mupe mananiŋ, ŋoŋe fuŋne qaqa mâsi bape honeeŋgopieŋ irec mâcne, nânâ gumec-ŋopape nâ gapec embieŋ, irec basacnuŋgopieŋ.
Ŋoŋe gie banšepieŋ, erâ nânâ sisirowenere mâcne, juju sanaŋte nânâ irec giene banšepieŋ. Ŋic Fâri Wâtuŋne eki, Anutu Mamaczi kamac sarahuc âkendâŋnewecte, juju sanaŋte nânâ i sâcne ŋareocmu.”
Mume dâŋ šiŋuc bâtikiecnembiŋ: “Nâŋe weniŋuc erâ Anuture gie banaŋmu?”
Eme šiŋuc jazawec: “Ŋic sorewec e manasiŋkezo, izi Anuture gie biŋe-ŋeŋic ekac.”
Mume dâŋ šiŋuc âzâcnembiŋ: “Mo fuŋne qaqa mâsi mo batec honerâ manasiŋgunaŋmu? Mo gie mo bacmu?
Mimiŋnefâc-nâŋec jaŋe mâreŋ sawao mana nâjumbieŋ. Eme irec dâŋqâreŋ šiŋuc fokac: `Sambâŋkonec nânâ jareme nâjumbieŋ. Ž ”
Eme Jesuzi šiŋuc jazawec: “Jâmbomac jâmbâŋ mupe mananiŋ: Mose e sambâŋkonec nânâ mi bâfua-ŋarewec, Mamac-nanezi sambâŋkonec nânâ fârine ŋareekac hâcne.
Nânâ sambâŋkonec waharâ mâreŋŋic juju bâfua-ŋareekac izi Anuturaonec nânâ fârine ekac.”
Mume šiŋuc âzâcnembiŋ: “Wofuŋ, go nânâ mukic i dameŋ sâc nârezemec.”
Eme šiŋuc jazawec: “Jujure nânâ no hâcne. Moc e norao qohotaocmu e nânâre moc mi hâmoocmu, â moc e no manasiŋnuocmu e opâre moc mi hâmoocmu.
No ine ŋazape, ŋoŋe no honecnu-bipiehuc sifu mi manasiŋnueŋgopieŋ.
Mamaczi nareekac i jaŋe norao fisi-fâreniŋmu, â norao fisiocmu e mi bâsuepemu.
Sambâŋkonec wahapo i no nahacne micdâŋ dopeckepemurâ mâcne, sorecnuwec ere micdâŋ dopeckepemurâ wahapo.
Mamac-nanezi norao râec-jopaekac ŋic i jaŋe sipirickenšipiŋte hone qâzuc ejareku dameŋ sâkoo furu jaha wiwic-jopape faharenšoŋgopieŋ” sorecnuwec ere micdâŋ iŋuc hâcne fokac.
Ŋokâ hone dendeŋnehuc manasiŋkeniŋmu sâc juju sanaŋ rauckeniŋmu” Mamac-nanere micdâŋ iŋuc hâcne fokac. Eme noni dameŋ sâkoo bâɋârec-jopazokopac.”
Jesu e “sambâŋkonec nânâ no hâcne” iŋuc muwecte Judaŋic jaŋe mana sâqorecnehuc dâŋembiŋ.
Ehuc šiŋuc mumbiŋ: “Wiac Jesu e Josefere ŋokâ, neŋgoc mamac jahec-ticne i nâŋe honec-jofaeŋgopeneŋ. Eme wemocte šiŋuc mukac: `No sambâŋkonec wahapo'?”
Mupie Jesuzi šiŋuc jazarâ muwec: “Ŋoŋe boc mi manapie sâqorezejec.
Ŋic moc e jahacne maŋte norao fifisi i mi fokac, Mamac sorecnuwec eki fâreme fifisine ine fokac. Eme noni ŋic iŋucne e dameŋ sâkoo bâɋârezokopac.
