Gâcne nâŋe Paulozi mume wokeo ferâ Aso haeo rambeŋ. E jahacne ine tiŋko fâwec.
Eme Aso haeo fârâ bâfuac-nâporâ wokeo hefârâ qâsuec-nâpome mâmâc rambeŋ. Raku Mitilene haeo rašimbeŋ.
Irecnec raku hae fureme Ʒintacko Kio nucko fisirâ jâurumbeŋ. Izi raku Mituoc Samo nucko fisimbeŋ. Eme irecnec raku Sekiqanâcko Milete haeo fisimbeŋ.
Paulo e Mâro hombaŋko Jerusalem haeo ra fisiocte muwec. Irec Efeso haeo wokeonec waharâ Asia masunao juhame dameŋ qâtirizacte fofotâc raku Milete haeo fisiwec.
Ira fisirâ kiŋaŋ sorec-jopame Efeso haeo rarâ mitire micne bapa jowac-jopapie warembiŋ.
Fisipie Paulozi dâŋ šiŋuc jazawec: “No Asia mâreŋko fisirâ izia ŋoŋerao gie-nane fuŋkerâ wiac ehuc jupo, i fuŋnaonecteaŋ mana wareeŋgopieŋ.
No hone suŋgiŋnezi ki busâqochec Wofuŋte kiŋaŋ qahuc jupo, ehuc Judaŋic jaŋe keke suec suec enarehapie râsi faio jupo.
Erâ dâŋ ŋoŋe ŋaŋazane moc mi bâtiripe fowec, ŋoŋe biaŋkeniŋte mitidâŋ bocjaha hofao â ficne ficne ŋaza qazuc ehuc jupo.
Ehuc Judaŋic â Grikŋic Anutu maickerâ Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristo manasiŋkeniŋte maŋqaqa eŋarehuc jupo.
Eme ši Mârozi maŋnane niŋgiŋko fâreme Jerusalem haeo rakopac. Erâ ocna ra fisipe wiac weniŋucne moc fua-nareocmu i mi mana-hâmokopac.
Mâc kâpâcwâru â bušâic ocna woŋec-nane fokac, i hae sâc fisi fisi jupe Tiri Mârozi mufua-nareekac.
No ine juju-nanere manape furi sâko mi ekac, mâc hata mušâwe-narekicne i buafec jaha âte tarapemurâ enarekac, â Anutu aki anonoc-ticnere Biŋebiaŋ muiŋnepemurâ Wofuŋ Jesuzi munarewec, gie i baku bâjomirepemurâ maŋnane domakac.
Erâ ši moc mupe mananiŋ, no uucmaŋte biŋedâŋ ŋazahuc ŋondeŋ-ŋeŋicko ŋeŋe juju epe honecnueŋgopieŋ izi šâhec šâŋe mai-nane mocwâc mi honeniŋmu.
No Anutuzi mitire dâŋ šaeckewec i furu jaha ŋaza-fârepo, moc mi hetarape fowec”
irec miŋecgac hazec qâuŋ ŋazape mananiŋ, moc e sipirickeme kiŋticne norao mi foocmu.
“Ŋoŋe ŋaŋac soŋaŋ babac ehuc lama gurufâc-ŋeŋic iŋuc jaha sâcne soŋaŋ-jopanšepieŋ. Tiri Mârozi jaŋere micne bapa mucŋopawecte ŋoŋe Wofuŋte kikefuŋfâc, e jahacne soczi kitâc-jopawec, jaŋe hone maiŋ ejarehapie aimuŋ junšepieŋ.
No manakopac, no behec-ŋopape kâte qâto mimicne ŋoŋerao fisirâ lama mi akic-jopaniŋmu,
erâ wâc ŋaŋacne ŋondeŋko ŋic fuarâ miti bâsifuckerâ opâ ruaczi jaŋacne eniŋte hume gegetâc ejareniŋmu.
Irec ŋoŋe rucgereŋ-ŋeŋic junšepieŋ, erâ jara jahec â moc ŋafe furec ki busâqochec uŋsawaŋ buc buc ŋaŋaza i moc mi behepe wahawec, ŋoŋe irec manasuhuc junšepieŋ.
Eme ši Anuturao râec-ŋopahuc uruc jauŋ dâŋticnao guruc-ŋopakopac” e tâpiri runezi hofâ ɋâcgie sâcne eŋareocmu, erâ juku maŋfuru bacjopakicne sasawa jaŋehec sambâŋte huhure i tahac-ŋopame rauckenšepieŋ.
No moneŋ mafare mubâre mi eŋarepo,
no nahacne â ŋicfâc-nane nâŋere wiac piticne mejahec-nane šizi hotâckepe fua-narewec, i manaŋgopieŋ.
No wiac fuŋne fuŋne qaŋeŋke-ŋarepo, ehuc gie ɋicwânšâŋ bahuc gegec dodocne jaŋe bâmec bajarezo irec hatane wâc âtehuc ŋowatupo. Eme ŋoŋe ijaha âtehuc Wofuŋ Jesuzi dâŋ kecšiŋuc muwec i manasunšepieŋ: `Bâmec ro nâc eere bubiaŋzi mâcne, bâmec babajare irec bubiaŋzi fârine jâmbâŋ eekac. Ž ”
Paulo e dâŋ iŋuc mutararâ dieŋzi herâ jaŋehec numuwec.
Numume kio ŋâŋâtâc boc ehuc hâpo mumuduc ecnembiŋ.
E dâŋ kecšiŋuc jazawec: “Ŋoŋe šâŋe mai-nane mocwâc mi honeniŋmu”, irec boc mana hâhâtâwembiŋ. Eme wokeo râembiŋ.
Eme nâŋe jaŋe hetarac-joparâ fâretiŋ jaha raku Ko nucko fisimbeŋ. Hae fureme Rodo nucko raširâ raku Patara haeo fisimbeŋ.
Ira woke moc Foinike mâreŋko raocte šawiehame bâfuarâ ira ferâ rambeŋ.
Raku Kipiro nuc honerâ qanaopec ŋehame mâc jâurumbeŋ. Erâ Siria mâreŋkopec raku Tiro haeo fisimbeŋ. Ira wokezi mafa hesie-fârehame
nâŋe haeo ferâ mitiŋic bâfuac-joparâ jaŋehec šoaŋ 7 jumbeŋ. Eme Mârozi ejareme jaŋe Paulo Jerusalem haeo mi raocte mu hezuc ecnembiŋ.
Ira juhapene rara dameŋ maickeme ŋic ŋokac naru motec mâmâc sasawa moŋgeŋko jowac-nâpopie humbeŋ. Erâ moŋgeŋko dieŋzi herâ numumbeŋ.
Numurâ mâmâzoc erâ wokeo fehapene jaŋe haeo risiembiŋ.
Eme Tiro haeonec raku Tolemai haeo fisipene wokeo rara i tarawec. Eme ira mitiŋic iqic-joparâ ŋafe mocjaha jaŋehec fombeŋ.
Hae fureme raku Kaisarea haeo fisirâ Filipo bâfuambeŋ. Filipo e babafic 7 râec-jopakicne jaŋere guruonec. Ere ficko hâcne fembeŋ.
E otâfâcne 4 šeŋoŋ jumbiŋ jaŋe findaŋdâŋ mujumbieŋ.
Eme ira šuhuckerâ juhapene Judaia mâreŋkonec porofete moc šâŋene Agabo e nâŋerao fâ fisiwec.
Fisirâ Paulo umbika-ticne rorâ izi jahacne me kike qarâ muwec, “Tiri Mâro e kecšiŋuc mukac: `Umbika rune e Jerusalem haeo ra fisime Judaŋic jaŋe šiŋuc hâcne ecnerâ qâpuc jaŋere meo râeniŋmu. Ž ”
Dâŋ iŋuc mume nâŋe mecne â hae fâri mecne Paulo Jerusalem haeo mi feocte bâmâckehuc âzâcnembeŋ.
Âzâcnepene šiŋuc muwec: “Wemocte boc kiohuc bu heheric enareŋgopieŋ? No Jerusalem haeo kâpâcwâruo fepere sawa mâcne, Wofuŋ Jesure erâ hâmopere wâc šawiekopac.”
Dâŋ âzâcnepene mi maname beherâ šiŋuc mumbeŋ: `Wofuŋte dâŋ sanaŋkezejec.”
Ʒoaŋ gie bapa gâcne tarame Jerusalem haeo fenaŋte šawiembeŋ.
Eme Kaisarea haeonec mitiŋic gâcne jaŋe jowac-nâporâ ŋic moc šâŋene Ŋasoŋ, e mitiŋic raŋɋane Kipiro nucko fuawec, ere ficko hâcne râec-nâpombiŋ.
Eme raku Jerusalem haeo fisipene irecnec mitiŋic jaŋe 390 jauŋ enârembiŋ.
Eme hae fureme Paulozi Jakobore ficko jowac-nâpome fembeŋ. Ferâ juhapene mitire micne bapa gâcne fisi-fârembiŋ.
Fisipie Paulozi mejeŋicko barâ, Anutuzi neŋgoc ŋesiŋ ŋecnehame qâpuc jaŋerao miti gie bame fârine fuawec, irec dâŋ binaŋ ninic jaha ejarewec.
Paulozi dâŋ binaŋ ejare tarame Anutu muteŋkerâ Paulo šiŋuc âzâcnembiŋ: “Manakic, qomâ-nâŋec Paulo, Judaŋic tauseŋ guru wemo afecnezi Jesure kikefuŋ embiŋ juŋgopieŋ. Eme jaŋe mâmâc sasawa sâcmutâc dâŋ šoɋac erâ dopeckeeŋgopieŋ.
Ehame gore dâŋ šiŋuc wareme manaeŋgopieŋ: `Judaŋic qâpuc jaŋere ŋondeŋko juraŋgopieŋ jaŋe Mosere dâŋ qikiŋneniŋte jazaekac, ehuc ɋiefâc-jeŋic jaŋere sahacko ma mi bajareniŋte muac-jopaekac, â Judaŋic juju hata-nâŋec beheniŋte qafeŋ-jopaekac. Ž
Hae širec ŋic jaŋe gore iŋuc manaeŋgopieŋte weniŋuc ezo? Go Jerusalem haeo waremec irec biŋe mana-fâreniŋmu.
Irec nâŋe dâŋ moc gazapene ezemec. Nâŋerao ŋic 4 juŋgopieŋ, jaŋe Anuturao mumupaŋ-jeŋic râembiŋte qizec-jeŋic mi bâbâtâc mâc jueŋgopieŋ.
Eme nâŋe jaŋerao šuhucgupene jaŋere sâcko wiac ehuc tiwâ bâzi furine bajaretec rikerâ qizec-jeŋic bâtâcnenšepieŋ. Go iŋuc etecne honecgurâ gore šiŋuc mananiŋmu: Dâŋticne wareme manambeŋ i fârimâc, e sâcmutâc dâŋ reŋkehuc juekac wâc.
Á qâpuckonec opâ ruac jaŋe nemuɋâŋte taha bâzi, qowisoc, qowi bituakicne â sasec boe sau irec sawa bâec baniŋte mupaŋke-jarembeŋ.”
Eme Paulo e dâŋjeŋic manarâ ŋic 4 jaŋerao šuhuckeme hae fureme sahac ŋaqi wiac-jeŋic šure emasaŋ erâ taha ufuŋko fembiŋ. Ferâ Paulozi mumupaŋ dameŋ tatarare â bâzi ririkere dâŋ taha bapa jaŋe jazawec.
Ʒoaŋ gie bapa 7 wiac ehuc juniŋte mumbiŋ i tarazo eha Paulozi taha ufuŋko ferâ juhame Asia mâreŋkonec Judaŋic jaŋe e honerâ ŋic mâmâc sasawa maŋjeŋic bâiŋnembiŋ.
Ehuc Paulo rorâ kuku qajarehuc mumbiŋ, “Oe, Israe ŋicbureŋ, ware bafic-nâponiŋ¡ Ŋic šizi mâreŋ sâc jurahuc Judaŋic nâŋâc râsi enârehuc sâcmutâc dâŋnâŋec â ufuŋ-nâŋec ši mu qâsuac ehuc juekac. Erâ wâc ufuŋ-nâŋecko Grikŋic jowac-jopame wefuhuc furufic ši gâc hecneŋgopieŋ.”
Paulo e Efeso haeonec ŋic Trofimo ehec haeo rac warec eme honerâ mana sifuckehuc mumbiŋ, taha ufuŋko jowa wefujec.
Paulo e iŋuc ecnepie haeŋic mâmâc sasawa kike saoŋ qajareme ɋuruŋ herâ qâture-fârembiŋ. Ehuc ŋic gâcnezi Paulo rorâ ufuŋkonec fâre wahambiŋ. Fâre wahapie izia motâc hembiŋ.
Ŋic jaŋe Paulo rorâ qâhâmozo ehapie biŋe Roma momori jaŋere soŋaŋ sâkorao rame šiŋuc manawec: “Jerusalem ŋic jaŋe mâmâc sasawa râsi roroc eŋgopieŋ.”
Dâŋ iŋuc manarâ izia momori fekicne wahakicne rocjopame ɋuruŋ ɋuruŋ rambiŋ. Eme ŋic jaŋe Paulo qahuc juhapie soŋaŋ sâko â momorifâc-ticne fisipie honec-joparâ behembiŋ.
Eme momori soŋaŋ sâkozi fisirâ Paulo jowac rorâ mume kâpâcwâru jajaheczi bândeŋnembiŋ. Erâ Paulo šâŋe-ticnere â wemo wiac ewec irec iindiŋ gie bawec.
Eme ŋic jaŋe owage owa-nane epie qâsifuo dâŋ fuŋne sâcne mi mana-hâmohuc mume momori jaŋe Paulo ficjeŋicko barambiŋ.
Eme Paulo e ririo fezo eme ŋic jaŋe orâŋkerâ bâbâzickepie momori jaŋe Paulo hâporâ reŋke fembiŋ.
Ŋic guru sâko jaŋe bâjâpec-jopahuc owac owacke rahuc šiŋuc mumbiŋ: “Ŋic e arictac eoc!”
Eme Paulo ficmaŋko bafezo ehapie momori soŋaŋ sâko wiocnerâ muwec, “Manatec dâŋ moc gazape?” Mume soŋaŋzi muwec, “Go Grikdâŋ manaekic?
Mârâcko Aigita ŋic moczi šika bâfuaocte râsi 4 tauseŋ rocjopame mâreŋ tuhuo rambiŋ, go ŋic e me moc?”
Wiocneme Paulozi šiŋuc âzâcnewec: “No Judaŋic, erâ Kilikia mâreŋko Taso hae sâko ŋekac irec rune. Go mana-naretec ŋic dâŋ piticne jazape.”
Eme manacneme Paulo e riri botâŋko domahuc ŋic me bazuc ejareme dâŋemâc efârepie Judaŋic jaŋacne dâŋkoa kecšiŋuc jazawec:
“Âgofâc-nane â kâcɋenefâc-nane, no nahacne fuŋne ŋazape mananiŋ.”
Paulo e iŋuc muhuc Judaŋic jaŋacne dâŋko dâŋeme manarâ qiriŋ niniŋ jâmbâŋ efârembiŋ.
Eme šuhuckerâ jazawec: “No Judaŋic, Kilikia mâreŋko Taso haeo fuapo. Erâ hae šira mamana ficko juku sokapo. Qaqazu Gamalie ere maŋfuŋko juhape miti qazu-nareme kâcɋenefâc-nâŋec jaŋere dâŋ aimuŋ anonocke-fârepo. Ehuc ŋoŋe miŋecgac eeŋgopieŋ noni iŋuc jaha Anuture erâ hume kikiŋ faio juhuc sasanaŋ epo.
Ehuc miti ɋâricne ši omaeocte no râsi ecnehuc ŋic mecne ŋokac mecne mâmâc jaha niŋgiŋ-joparâ kâpâcwâru ficko râec-jopahuc jupo.
Taha bapa sâko â micne bapa guru jaŋe nore fuŋne manaeŋgopieŋ. Jaŋe hâcne âgofâc-nâŋec Damasko haeo jueŋgopieŋ jaŋere papia qâreŋkerâ narepie kecšiŋuc muhuc barapo: No ocna ŋic ŋokac iŋucne bâfuac-joparâ niŋgiŋ-joparâ Jerusalem haeo bacjopa warepe okacne jarenšepieŋ.
Iŋuc muhuc hata raku šoaŋ šâšâŋiŋko Damasko hae bâqiŋkehape sambâŋkonec šoc tatamac sâkozi uŋ herâ waha âkecnuwec.
Âkecnuhuc herândiŋnume mâreŋko fohuc dâŋ wiwira kecšiŋuc manapo: `Saulo, Saulo, go wemocte nu jâpec enarehuc jukomec? Ž
Eme noni mupo, `Wofuŋ go mo? Ž Mupe šiŋuc nazawec: `Nu jâpec enareekic Jesu Nazarete haeonec no hâcne. Ž
Ŋic nohec jumbiŋ jaŋe šoc tatamac sawa honembiŋ, dâŋ nazawec ine mi manambiŋ.
Eme no wiohuc mupo, `Wofuŋ, no wemo epemurâ munarekomec? Ž Mupe Wofuŋzi šiŋuc nazawec: `Go faharerâ Damasko haeo ratec wiac ecmurâ mugarekicne i gazaniŋmu. Ž
Eme šoc tatamaczi šâŋe-nane âke hâpowecte fipe dapâc eme ŋicfâc-nane jaŋe menaneo rorâ Damasko haeo bacnu rambiŋ.
“Hae ira ŋic moc juwec šâŋene Anania, e sâcmutâc dâŋ aimuŋ bâninipehuc jume Judaŋic hae ijaha jumbiŋ jaŋe šeŋgoma ere manapie biaŋkewec.
Ŋic izi hâcne norao fâ fisirâ šiŋuc nazawec: `Qomâ-nane Saulo, go šâŋe fitâcnec. Ž Mume izia fitâcnerâ e honepo.
Eme dâŋ šiŋuc nazawec: `Mimiŋnefâc-nâŋec jaŋere Anutu eki fuŋne-ticne gaza gowatuc eme tiŋne rune honehuc micticnaonec dâŋ manacmurâ rowosâecguwec.
Eme go wiac hone manac emeŋ irec biŋe mâreŋ sâc ŋic jaza razemec.
Eme ši weniŋuc mâc jutec šoraocmu? Go faharerâ Jesure šâŋe riwasecketec Miti Opâ rua-garepe sâqocnege tâmirezejec.'
“Eme no Jerusalem haeo risierâ taha ufuŋko ferâ numupe maŋnane ŋerisieme Jesu honepo.
Honepe šiŋuc nazawec: `Hae širec ŋic jaŋe gore mickonec dâŋnane manarâ qikiŋneniŋmu, irec go picpac Jerusalem-konec wiserâ rac. Ž
Mume no dâŋ šiŋuc bâtikiecnepo: `Wofuŋ, no ŋicfâcge kâpâcwâru bacjoparâ mitificne ficne bacjopa ferâ kâcbiŋzi jopahuc jupo,
erâ biŋe mumuge Stefano qaniŋte ŋaqi-jeŋic guruckepie soŋaŋke-jarehape qapie manape sâckewec, i hae širec ŋic mana-fâreŋgopieŋte gore biŋe sâcne jazapemu. Ž
Iŋuc mupe Wofuŋzi šiŋuc nazawec: `Go šawietec no mâreŋ wiwicko qâpuc jaŋerao sorecgupe razemec. Ž ”
Ŋic jaŋe hazec-jeŋic râehapie Paulozi dâŋ gâcne jazawec. Izi miŋecne dâŋ iŋuc mume ɋeŋɋeŋnea owa ruruckerâ mumbiŋ, “Ŋic iŋucnezi arictac eoc, jume mamakâcne ekac.”
Iŋuc owackehuc ŋaqi-jeŋic šoricne hetararâ rufe tiepie feme
soŋaŋ sâkozi mume momori jaŋe Paulo ficjeŋicko bafembiŋ. Erâ ŋic jaŋe wemo wiacte boc owackecnembieŋ irec fuŋne mufuame manazore kâcbiŋzi qaniŋte mujarewec.
Eme jaŋe kâcbiŋzi qaniŋte fâretiŋkerâ becsahaczi bândeŋnezo epie Paulozi micne-jeŋic šiŋuc muhuc wiocnewec: “Ŋoŋe Romaŋic fârine dâŋticne mi mutarahuc kâcbiŋzi qapie sâckeocmu me?”
Iŋuc mume micne-jeŋiczi soŋaŋ sâkorao rarâ âzâcnerâ muwec, “Weniŋuc ezo? Ŋic e Romaŋic fârine.”
Mume soŋaŋ sâkozi Paulorao rarâ wiocnerâ muwec, “Go muc, go jâmbomac Romaŋic fârine?” Eme Paulozi muwec, “I jâmbomac.”
Mume soŋaŋ sâkozi šiŋuc muwec: “No ŋic jabanezi moneŋ bocjaha rope kitâcnume Romaŋic jâmbâŋ epo.” Eme Paulozi muwec, “No ine fufua-nane Romaŋic fuapo.”
Eme izia Paulo wiac ecnezo mumbiŋ i behembiŋ. Momori soŋaŋ e ine, Paulo e Romaŋic, iŋuc manarâ, no wemocte ŋic iŋucne kâpâcwâru bapac muhuc fâfârewec.
Hae fureme momori soŋaŋ sâko e Judaŋic jaŋe Paulo wemo wiacte mana sâqorecnembiŋ irec fuŋne jâmbâŋ manaocte taha bapa micne â micne guru furu jaha ejareme tumaŋnembiŋ. Ehame Paulo jowa hurâ tutumaŋ-jeŋicko râewec.
Paulo e micne bapa hone dendeŋ-jopahuc dâŋ šiŋuc jazawec: “Ŋic âgofâc-nane, no sâcmutâc dâŋ qaqatarare maŋnanezi mumu hehec moc mi enareha Anuture maio juwefuhuc jupozi jukopac.”
Iŋuc mume taha bapa sâko Anania eki ŋic Paulore maŋfuŋko domambiŋ jaŋe šiŋuc jazawec: “Ŋoŋe masunao qaniŋ.”
Mume Paulozi šiŋuc âzâcnewec: “Maŋge tâŋzi qakicne go Anutuzi guocmu. Go sâcmutâc dâŋte sâcko norao mumutiŋ gie bazo mukiczi wemocte sâcmutâc dâŋ qâsuahuc nuniŋte jazakic?”
Iŋuc mume ŋic doma rambiŋ jaŋe šiŋuc âzâcnembiŋ: “Go Anuture taha bapa sâko wemocte musoriŋkekic?”
Mupie Paulozi šiŋuc muwec: “Âgo bureŋ, e taha bapa sâko jukac i mi manahuc dâŋepac. Mitio dâŋ kecšiŋuc qâreŋkekicne: `Go micne bapa mi musâqorec-jopazemec. Ž No dâŋ i manaekopac.”
Eme micne guru ŋic tucne sadukaio â tucne farisaio ŋic jumbiŋ, Paulozi i manahuc dâŋ baferâ šiŋuc jazawec: “Ŋicbureŋ, no farisaio ŋic â apa ŋosafâc-nane jaŋe farisaio ŋic jaha jumbiŋ. Hâmockonec fafahare fokac dâŋ i dopeckeekopacte dâŋko râecnuŋgopieŋ.”
Dâŋ iŋuc mume farisaio ŋic â sadukaio ŋic jaŋe qaqatarac epie micne bapa jaŋerao fâfâuc fuawec.
Sadukaio ŋic jaŋe hâmockonec fafahare â aŋelo â sawa qâqâtâc, wiac iŋucne micke-fâreeŋgopieŋ. Farisaio ŋic jaŋe ine irec fârine mueŋgopieŋ.
Eme irec tutumaŋ-jeŋicko ojowa sâko bambiŋ. Eku farisaio ŋic jaŋere guruonec miti qaqazu gâcne faharerâ dâŋ fârone kecšiŋuc mumbiŋ: “Nâŋe ŋic kecširec kiŋ manapene aricne ekac” aŋelo me sawa qâqâtâc moczi dâŋ âzâcnewecko weniŋuc moc munaŋmu?”
Eme fecko fefec mâretec epie momori soŋaŋ sâko e Paulo qâsuckenšipiŋte hâwickeme mume momori jaŋe fisirâ Paulo ŋicŋondeŋkonec fâre waharâ ficjeŋicko barambiŋ.
Eme ŋafe ira Wofuŋzi Paulo fuacnerâ šiŋuc âzâcnewec: “Go hâbige roc, šira Jerusalem haeo mutaniŋnukomec iŋuc jaha Roma haeo mutaniŋnuzemec.”
Hae fureme Judaŋic gâcne šâšâfic erâ nânâ sowa jujâmbâŋkeku Paulo qarâ nânâ opâ nâniŋte mumundeŋ embiŋ.
Ŋic šâšâfic erâ iŋuc mumbiŋ šare-jeŋic 40 jâuruwec.
Ŋic jaŋe hâcne taha bapa micne â soŋaŋ jaŋerao rarâ mufua-jarerâ šiŋuc jazambiŋ: “Nâŋe nânâ sowa jujâmbâŋkeku Paulo qarâ wiac nanaŋte mumundeŋ embeneŋ”
irec micne bapa ŋoŋe momori soŋaŋ sâkorao dâŋ šiŋuc râepie razejec: `Go Paulo nâŋere tutumaŋko soretec wareme dâŋticne mocwâc muhâmonšepeneŋ. Ž Eme dâŋŋeŋic manarâ iŋuc eme nâŋe Paulo hatao qanaŋmu.”
Eme Paulo baŋec-ticnezi šikadâŋ i manawec. Manarâ momori ficko rarâ wawa-ticne âzâcnewec.
Âzâcneme Paulozi momori jaŋere micne moc wiracnerâ šiŋuc âzâcnewec: “Go motec ši momori soŋaŋ sâkorao jowa ratec dâŋ moc âzâcneoc.”
Mume ŋic eki motec soŋaŋ sâkorao jowa rarâ šiŋuc âzâcnewec: “Kâpâcwâru ŋic Paulo eki wira-narerâ nazame motec ši dâŋ gazaocte jowape warekoperec.”
Iŋuc muhuc âzâcneme soŋaŋ sâkozi motec menao rorâ herâricnao bararâ wiocnerâ muwec, “Dâŋ weniŋuc nazacmu?”
Eme moteczi šiŋuc âzâcnewec: “Judaŋic jaŋe gorao dâŋ râepie wareocte muc manac embieŋ, jaŋe go Paulo tutumaŋ-jeŋicko jowa rarâ fuŋne-ticne bataniŋke-hâmocmurâ gazaniŋmu.
Gazapie dâŋjeŋic mi manazemec. Ŋic šare-jeŋic 40 jâurukac, iŋuczi Paulo qâhâmoniŋte muŋgopieŋ. Jaŋe nânâ sowa jujâmbâŋkeku Paulo qarâ wiac nâniŋte mumundeŋ embieŋ, erâ biac šawierâ gore dâŋte woŋec juŋgopieŋ.”
Motec e dâŋ iŋuc mume soŋaŋ sâkozi šiŋuc muhuc sorewec: “Go dâŋ mufuarâ nazakomec i ŋic moc mi jazazemec.”
Eme soŋaŋ sâkozi momori jaŋere micne jajahec hefârec-jofarâ šiŋuc jasawec: “Ŋohe mupire momori kikezi hata rara 200 â becâsicko rara 70 â damu bapa 200 izi šawierâ ŋafere 9 kiloë ehame Kaisarea haeo ranšepieŋ.
Erâ Paulore becâsic moc sate hecnenšepieŋ. Eme aimuŋ soŋaŋkehuc kia Feliki erao baranšepieŋ.”
Iŋuc murâ kiare papia moc šiŋuc muhuc qâreŋkewec:
“Klaudio Lisia noni kia biaŋ-nane Feliki gore papia ši qâreŋkekopac.
Momori jaŋe ŋic moc bafâŋgopieŋ e Judaŋic jaŋe qazo embiŋ. Eme noni e Romaŋic jâmbâŋ ere iŋuc manahuc momori jaŋehec rarâ mejeŋickonec batarambeŋ.
Eme dâŋko râembiŋ irec fuŋne manapemurâ micne bapa tutumaŋ-jeŋicko barapo.
Bararâ sâcmutâc dâŋjeŋicte qorickepie šiŋuc manapo: Wiac ewec izi ferâ šika kâpâcwâru bâbâfuane mi ekac.
Eme ŋic gâcne jaŋe somâ barâ Paulo qaniŋte mupie manarâ gorao sorepe fakac hâcne. Á qorickeeŋgopieŋ ŋic i jaŋe iŋuc jaha ejarepe gorao fârâ dâŋticne gazanšepieŋ.”
Eme momori jaŋe soŋaŋ-jeŋicte mic reŋkehuc Paulo ŋafeoa jowa raku Antipatri haeo fisimbiŋ.
Hae fureme momori gâcne jaŋe ficjeŋicko risiehapie becâsicko ŋeŋe jaŋe buc Paulo jowa raku Kaisarea haeo fisimbiŋ.
Fisirâ kia papia râcnehuc Paulo iŋuc jaha ere meo râembiŋ.
Eme kiazi papia woserâ Paulo mâreŋ qizec-ticnere wiocneme muwec, “No Kilikia mâreŋkonec.”
Eme kiazi šiŋuc âzâcnewec: “Dâŋko râecguŋgopieŋ ŋic i jaŋe ware fisipie gore dâŋ muzo.” Iŋuc murâ momori jazame Herodere ficko râerâ soŋaŋkembiŋ.
Ʒoaŋ gie bapa 5 tarame taha bapa sâko Anania e â soŋaŋ gâcne â dâŋŋic moc šâŋene Teatulo jaŋe Kaisarea haeo hurâ kiarao Paulore dâŋ muniŋte fuambiŋ.
Eme kiazi mume Paulo fisime Teatulozi e qorickehuc kia dâŋ šiŋuc âzâcnewec: “Kia biaŋ-nâŋec Feliki, go sâcne soŋaŋ-nâpotec wamaoa jueŋgopeneŋ, erâ ŋicguru ši nâŋere manabâc ehuc bafic-nâpotec
nâŋerao hae sâc wiac sasawa biaŋkeekacte gore manapene sâcke-hâmoekac.
Erâ dâŋ mupe šorazacte go uruerâ mana-nâretec dâŋ bembeŋne mac gazape.
Ŋic kecirec manapene boc sâqorekac, e sopa sâwec-ticnehec, Judaŋic mâreŋ sâc juraŋgopieŋ jaŋe maŋbâiŋ ejareekac, erâ Nazarete rune repicnefâc-ticne jaŋere qizec eki hâcne.
Eme taha ufuŋ-nâŋec gâc hecnezo ehame rombeŋ, [erâ nâŋe sâcmutâc dâŋnâŋecte sâcko wiac ecnenšapeŋ.
Ehame ine kapiteŋ sâko Lisia eki fisi šocnehec nâwoc rowec.
Ehuc dâŋko râembiŋ ŋic i jaŋe gorao fisi fuaniŋte mujarewec.Ý Eme nâŋe dâŋ gazaŋgopeneŋ i go gahac mu esâic ecnehuc fuŋne sâcne bataniŋkecmu.”
Dâŋ iŋuc mume Judaŋic jaŋe e bafickehuc dâŋticne dopeckembiŋ.
Eme kiazi Paulo mezi sâsâc ecneme dâŋ šiŋuc muwec: “Go mâreŋ šira jara bocjaha kia juekic i manasuhuc dâŋnane manabâc tâmiric mupemu.
No Jerusalem haeo Anutu mai ecnepemurâ ferâ juwarekupe šoaŋ gie bapa 12 sawa ekac, go dâŋ irec maŋjahec erâ ŋic esâic-jopatec gazaniŋmu.
No taha ufuŋko me mitific gâcnao me miti haeo ŋic jaŋehec mitire mu qaqatarac me ŋic maŋbâiŋ eejare i moc mi epe honecnumbiŋ.
Ŋic šizi qoricnuhuc dâŋ gazaŋgopieŋ, irec fârine wemocko gowatuniŋmu.
Erâ moc mufua-garepe manac: Hata ɋâri sureeŋgopieŋ i âteekopac mueŋgopieŋ, ine jâmbomac eekopac. Erâ jaŋere dâŋmiti bajuhuc sâcmutâc dâŋqâhâcko miti qâreŋkekicne fokac â porofete mu qâreŋ embiŋ i manape fârine ehame mimiŋnefâc-nâŋec jaŋere Anutu kiŋaŋ qacneekopac.
Erâ juku ŋic biaŋne â sâqocne hâmockonec fafahare maickeocmu, irec ŋic keci jaŋe â no mâmâc mamanac jueŋgopeneŋ.
Iŋuc ehuc Anuture maio â ŋicmaio bahacmâc jupemurâ rucnane bahuc jaha juekopac.
“Eme no jara bocjaha mâreŋ wiwicko juhuc mitire moneŋ qânusuckeku Jerusalem haeo ŋic âgofâc-nâŋec jaŋerao warepo.
Erâ bâzi ririkere bašawierâ taha ufuŋko ferâ juhape bâfuacnumbiŋ. Ira ŋicguruo juju me dâŋfânâŋ sâkohec juju ine arictac.
Asia mâreŋkonec Judaŋic gâcne jaŋe ine iŋuc embiŋ. Jaŋe hâcne nore bahac moc manaŋgopieŋko gorao fisirâ mutaniŋkenšapiŋ.
Me micne bapa tutumaŋko domahape nore bahac moc bâfuambiŋko ŋic domaŋgopieŋ šizi gazaniŋ.
Jaŋe no dâŋ mocjaha sawa ŋondeŋ-jeŋicko domahuc mupe manapie mi mecne sâckewec, ine hahaŋne bahuc kecšiŋuc jazapo: `Hâmockonec fafahare fokac, dâŋ i dopeckeekopacte gâcnezi dâŋko râecnupie mai-ŋeŋicko domakopac ši. Ž ”
Kia Feliki e Paulore dâŋ i mi mutarahuc mâc râeme fowec. E miti ɋâricnere biŋe mana-hâmowecte šiŋuc sawa jazawec: “Momori soŋaŋ Lisiazi Jerusalem haeonec wahame dâŋŋeŋic mutarapemu.”
Iŋuc murâ momori micne šiŋuc âzâcnewec: “Ŋoŋe Paulo soŋaŋkehuc râsi šâŋe mi ecnenšepieŋ, â âgofâcne fisirâ jauŋ bazo mupie mi qatara-jarenšepieŋ.”
Ʒoaŋ gie bapa tucne jurâ Feliki e Juda guruonec ŋonâŋ-ticne Drusila ehec mâmâc ŋehuc Paulo ecneme hefârâ Kristo Jesu manasiŋkembiŋ irec fuŋne jasawec.
Ehuc tiŋke biaŋ eere â sasecte sowa jujure â okac dameŋte mume Felikizi weaŋkerâ Paulo šiŋuc âzâcnewec: “Sâcne rac, juku nacnere dameŋ sawane moc fua-nareme mocwâc hefârecgupemu.”
Kia e Paulozi moneŋ narezejec muhuc dameŋ sâc hefârerâ ehec dâŋ muc manac ejujec.
Ehame jara jajahec tarame kia moc šâŋene Porkio Festo eki Feliki âkehockewec. Eme Feliki e Judaŋic bubiaŋ qajarehuc Paulo kâpâcwâru ficko ŋehame beherâ rawec.
Festozi kia erâ šoaŋ jahec â moc Jurâ Kaisarea haeonec Jerusalem haeo fewec.
Fe fisime taha bapa micne â Judaŋic fekicne erao fisirâ Paulore dâŋ âzâcnembiŋ.
Ehuc mana urue-jarerâ mume Paulo Jerusalem haeo fisiocte âzâcnembiŋ. Jaŋe hatao Paulo somâckerâ qaniŋte manasuhuc kia iŋuc âzâcnembiŋ.
Mupie Festozi šiŋuc jazawec: “Paulo e Kaisarea haeo kâpâcwâru ficko ŋekac” eme no ijaha biac mocwâc risie hupemu.
Paulo bahacdâŋ-ticne muzo murâ ŋoŋeraonec micne bapa nohec mâmâc hurâ munšepieŋ.”
Iŋuc murâ šoaŋ 8 me 10 Jerusalem haeo jurâ Kaisarea haeo rahuwec. Izi hae fureme dâŋficko ferâ mume Paulo bafembiŋ.
Ficko feme Jerusalem haeonec Judaŋic jaŋe orâŋkerâ samarierâ qorickehuc domambiŋ. Erâ qoqoricte fârine mi fuawec.
Mupie Paulozi dâŋjeŋic bawahahuc šiŋuc muwec: “No Judaŋic sâcmutâc dâŋjeŋic me taha ufuŋ me Roma ŋicwofuŋ moc mi musuaekopac.”
Eme Festozi Judaŋic bubiaŋ qajareocte Paulo indiŋkerâ muwec, “Go Jerusalem haeo jowacgu ferâ ira dâŋge mutarape me?”
Indiŋkeme Paulozi šiŋuc âzâcnewec: “Roma ŋicwofuŋte dâŋfic šine hâcne” nore dâŋ šira mutarazo” go gahac fuŋne-nane manakic, no Judaŋic wiac hehesic moc mi ejarepo.
No bahac me kiŋsâko moc bâfuarâ muzac, nuzo mutec sahac-nane mi sakarezapo. Jaŋe ine burecko qoricnuŋgopieŋte moczi moc bubiaŋ qajarehuc jaŋere meo sâcne mi râecnu-jâmbâŋkeocmu. Irec ši Roma ŋicwofuŋzi dâŋnane mutaraocte mukopac.”
Iŋuc mume Festo e ŋicfâc-ticne jaŋehec muc manac erâ Paulo šiŋuc âzâcnewec: “Ŋicwofuŋ sâkore mukomec, irec ŋicwofuŋ sâkorao razemec.”
Ʒoaŋ gie bapa tucne tarame ŋicwofuŋ Agripa â seŋticne Beanike jahe Kaisarea haeo hurâ Festo âgo bapic.
Eme jahe šoaŋ gâcne ehec ŋeŋe juju ehapire Festozi Paulore dâŋ binaŋ ecnehuc ŋicwofuŋ šiŋuc âzâcnewec: “Felikizi kâpâcwâru ŋic moc beherâ rame ŋehuc jukac.
Eme no fisirâ Jerusalem haeo fepe taha bapa micne â Judaŋic jaŋere soŋaŋ jaŋe norao tumaŋnehuc ŋic e qape hâmoocte munarembiŋ.
Munarepie no dâŋ ŋifecne šiŋuc jazapo: `Romaŋic nâŋe qoqoricte sawa ŋic moc šikare mi qikiŋneeŋgopeneŋ. Nâŋe ŋic dâŋko râekicne e mecne â dâŋrune mecne mâmâc hetumaŋ-jopapene ŋifec â ŋifec dâŋ sâckoa mueŋgopieŋ. Ž
Iŋuc jazape Judaŋic norao warepie izia hae fureme jaŋe â e dâŋficko bâturec-jopapo.
Eme jaŋe ere sâqocne qizecne moc mufuaniŋmu muhape
jaŋe miti-jeŋicte hehefaric dâŋ â ŋic hâmokicne moc šâŋene Jesu ere dâŋ bajumbiŋ” ŋic ere hâcne Paulozi šiŋuc muekac: `E faharewec jukac. Ž
Eme no dâŋ iŋucnere kâuc barâ Paulo Jerusalem haeo feme ira dâŋticne mutarapemurâ âzâcnepo.
Âzâcnepe Paulo e Roma ŋicwofuŋzi dâŋticne mutaraocte muwec. Eme Paulo e rara dameŋ maickeme mupe Roma ŋicwofuŋtao raocte kâpâcwâru ficko woŋec jukac.”
Festozi iŋuc muhuc âzâcneme Agripazi muwec: “No ŋic e hâcne dâŋ moc mume manapemurâ enarekac.” Eme Festozi muwec, “Sâcne, tomâcko manazemec.”
Hae fureme Agripa â Beanike jahe eri qaraweŋ-jekichec tutumaŋ ficko fepire momori soŋaŋ kâcɋene â hae irec ŋic fekicne mâmâc bâjâpec-jofarâ fembiŋ. Fefârepie Festozi mume Paulo bafembiŋ.
Bafepie Festozi dâŋ šiŋuc jazawec: “Ŋicwofuŋ Agripa â ŋicfâc-nane gâcne dâŋ ŋazape mananiŋ. Ŋic domakac ši ere erâ Judaŋic wemo afecnezi Jerusalem haeo fotarie-narehuc wira owac erâ mumbiŋ, `E mi jujâmbâŋkezejec. Ž
No ine bahac-ticnere manape šika kiocte irec sâc mi ewec. Eme Roma ŋicwofuŋte muwecte erao sorepe raocmu.
Erâ dâŋ fârine basahuc ŋicbomboŋ sâkore papia qâreŋkepemurâ fâcke turuŋ ekopac. Eme irec hâcne ŋic kecši e ŋoŋerao â ŋicwofuŋ Agripa gorao râepe domakac. Eme ŋoŋe fuŋne-ticne bataniŋkepie dâŋticne qâreŋkepe razejec.
No kâpâcwâru ŋic moc kiŋticnere dâŋ mi qâreŋkehuc Roma haeo mâc sorepe raocte manape quŋkekac.”
Eme Agripazi Paulo šiŋuc âzâcnewec: “Gahac fuŋnege mutec mananaŋ.” Eme Paulozi meticne sicnerâ dâŋ šiŋuc jazawec:
“Judaŋic dâŋzi dâŋ enarehuc jueŋgopieŋ irec ŋifecne ŋicwofuŋ Agripa miŋecgac gore maio mupemurâ bunane biaŋkekac.
Go hâcne Judaŋic mitire hehefaric-nâŋecte â wiac eenâŋecte fuŋne manaekic. Irec go mana uruehaŋtec dâŋnane mupe.
“No motec ɋie-naneoa Jerusalem haeo ŋic âgofâc-nane jaŋere ŋondeŋko juku sokapo.
Irec Judaŋic mârâc honecnumbiŋzi juju-nanere fuŋne manaeŋgopieŋ. No farisaio ŋic mitire neŋgocne embiŋ Jaŋere guruo hâcne jupo. Eme fuŋne-nane hone manac embiŋzi muzo murâ munšapiŋ.
No kâpâcwâru ficko foekopac i wiac mocte mâcne, Anutuzi mimiŋnefâc-nâŋec biŋedâŋ jazawec,
eme dâŋ i fârinehec eocte Israe ŋicguru 12 jaŋe ŋafe šoaŋ qâqâtiri Anutu tiwâ bâzi rikecnehuc mai ecneeŋgopieŋ, ŋicwofuŋ-nane, biŋedâŋ irec hâcne Judaŋic jaŋe dâŋgie nareeŋgopieŋ.
Anutu e hâmokicne bâɋârec-jopaekac, i ŋoŋe wemocte manapie mi eene tinac eekac?
Erâ no nahacnere mupe, no Jesu Nazarete haeonec ere šâŋe biŋe imackepe sifuckeocte gie-nane ewec.
Jerusalem haeo iŋuc hâcne epo, ehuc taha bapa micne jaŋerao mupe pasi narepie opâ ruac wemo afecne kâpâcwâru ficne ficne râec-jopahuc jupo. Erâ šika kirâ hâmoniŋte mujarepie dâŋjeŋic dopecke jupac wâc.
Judaŋic jaŋere mitificne ficne opâ ruac jopahuc jaŋe Jesure šâŋe musoriŋkeniŋte wiac qacne gâpâcne ejare jupac. Erâ no momori wânšâŋ erâ hae šoricko ra jopa jâpec ejare jupac wâc.
“Ekupe taha bapa micne jaŋe papia narehuc munarepie Damasko haeo rapemurâ rapo.
Rakuhape qâqâtâc bembeŋkeha sambâŋkonec šoc tatamac bâricnehuc waha no â ŋicfâc-nane âke tamaec-nâpowec. Opoŋ, ŋicwofuŋ-nane, šoaŋ tatamacne i weweaŋne, â honepo tatamac izi hâhâwicne jâmbâŋ.
Eme nâŋe mâreŋko rândiŋke qarâ fohuc dâŋ wiwira moc Judadâŋko šiŋuc manambeŋ: `Saulo, Saulo, go wemocte nu jâpec enarehuc juekic? Go šârâ hewâcnetec âkecgume šâic manacmu. Ž
Eme no šiŋuc mupo: `Wofuŋ go mo? Ž Mupe šiŋuc nazawec: `Nu jâpec enarehuc jukomec Jesu no hâcne.
Go fahare domac, no ši kiŋaŋ qaqa-nane bacgupemurâ fua-garekopac, irec go ši wiac honekomec â juku gowatupe honecmu irec biŋe mumu-nane erâ juzemec.
No ŋicguru ši â ŋic qâpuc jaŋere meonec bataracguhuc jupemu.
Erâ jaŋerao sorecgupe šâŋe-jeŋic bâtâcnetec dapâc honerâ râpeckerâ tatamac maickenšepieŋ, erâ wâc Sataŋte gie beherâ Anuture enšepieŋ. Eme sâqocne-jeŋic tâmirehame no manasiŋnuhuc ɋaɋackembiŋ jaŋere guruo raširâ sambâŋ kâdoc-jeŋic rauckenšepieŋ.'
“Ŋicwofuŋ-nane Agripa, no sambâŋkonec dâŋ mana rereŋ ehuc
ine qanaŋ Damasko haeonec ŋic â Jerusalem haeonec ŋic erâ wâc Juda mâreŋ rune sasawa â ŋic qâpuc mâmâc maŋjeŋic bârisierâ Anuturao qohotahuc maŋ bâbârisiere fârine bâfuaniŋte irec miti jazahuc jupo.
Eme iŋuc epore Judaŋic jaŋe taha ufuŋko rocnurâ qâhâmocnuzo embiŋ.
Eme Anutu e ŋezicnu warehame miti mupozi muekopac, ehuc ŋic fekicne â wahakicne mâmâc jazaekopac. Erâ dâŋ furune mâcne, porofete â Mose findaŋdâŋ muhuc qâreŋkembiŋ ijaha muekopac.
Kristo e šâic manaku hâmoocte mucnekicne erâ hâmokicne jaŋeraonec micne barâ faharerâ Judaŋic â ŋic qâpuc šâziriŋ dâŋ bâfua-jareocte mucnekicne, dâŋ i hâcne dopeckeekopac.”
Paulo e fuŋne-ticne mutiŋnehuc dâŋ iŋuc jazame Festozi dâŋ hahaŋne bahuc muwec, “Paulo go maŋge sifuckekac i¡ Papia bocjaha wose qâreŋ ekutec maŋge sifuckewec hâcne.”
Mume Paulozi dâŋ šiŋuc bâtikiecnewec: “Ŋicbomboŋ-nane Festo, no maŋsifuc dâŋ mâcne, no dâŋ tiŋne â fârine mukopac.
Dâŋ mukopac irec fuŋne ŋicwofuŋzi sâcne manakac, erao hâcne afeckehuc mukopac. Wiac mukopac i soŋsoŋko mi fuawec, irec ŋicwofuŋzi wemocko kâuc baocmu.
Ŋicwofuŋ Agripa, go porofete jaŋere dâŋ mana šakieekic me? No manakopac, go mana šakieekic.”
Mume Agripazi Paulo šiŋuc âzâcnewec: “Enarekutec mi šoraha Kristoŋic ezipohec ine.”
Eme Paulozi muwec, “Go â ŋic gâcne miŋecgac dâŋ ši mupe manaŋgopieŋ, ŋoŋe Wofuŋzi bafic-ŋopame mi šoraha no iŋucne ejâmbâŋkeniŋte mukopac, kâpâcwâru ŋic jukopac irec mâcne, mitire mukopac.”
Iŋuc mume ŋicwofuŋ â kia â Beanike â ŋic gâcne faharerâ râwiŋnembiŋ.
Râwiŋnehuc nazaŋ gazaŋ erâ šiŋuc mumbiŋ: “Ŋic e šika me kâpâcwâru mi hotâckewec.”
Á Agripazi Festo šiŋuc âzâcnewec: “Ŋic e Roma ŋicwofuŋzi dâŋticne mutaraocte mi mume muzac, go sâcne firuetec ra juzac.”
Italia mâreŋko ranaŋte dameŋ maickeme kiazi mume Roma momori jaŋere soŋaŋ moc šâŋene Julio, eki Paulo â kâpâcwâru ŋic gâcne rocjopame wokeo fembiŋ.
Woke i Adramiteŋ haeonec, erâ Asia masunao hae biri ŋerawec ira raši-fâreocte mucnekicne. Woke ira hâcne ferâ Makedonia ŋic moc šâŋene Aristako, Tesalonike haeonec, ehec mâmâc rambeŋ.
Hae fureme woke Sidoŋ haeo rašime Juliozi Paulo âgo ecnehuc manacneme haeo raferâ âgofâcne iqic-jopame hata nâsiŋ wiac râcnembiŋ:
Eme mâŋâŋ rambeŋkonec warewecte ine Kipiro nuc â Asia mâreŋ ŋondeŋ-jekicko rambeŋ.
Ehuc Kilikia â Pamfilia mâreŋ hecne hecne raku Mira haeo Likia mâreŋko fisimbeŋ.
Ira Alesandria haeonec woke moc ŋewec. Izi Italia mâreŋko razo ewecte momori soŋaŋzi rocnâpome ira fembeŋ.
Ferâ uneŋ uneŋ ŋe qatarac raku Kinido hae ŋeweckopec fisimbeŋ. Eme mâŋâŋzi bârisiec-nâpome hae i râpeckerâ Kreta nuckopec rambeŋ.
Raku nuc irec masune moc šâŋene Salimone i qatararâ Lasaia hae ramicnao hâwec motec moc fowec, šâŋene Woke Haebiaŋ, ira neneŋ gie baku rašimbeŋ.
Hâwecko dameŋ šora rahuc jumbeŋ erâ wâc hoemaŋ biac maickewec, irec Paulozi uŋdâŋ jazarâ muwec,
“Ŋicbureŋ, ši mocwâc ranaŋmu i manape fâsâcne rarane mi ekac, woke herickeme mafa sawa mâcne, ŋic mâmâc hâwecko hunšipeŋte manabâc erâ mukopac.”
Iŋuc mume momori soŋaŋ eki Paulore dâŋ mana takirehuc kapiteŋ â woke rune jahere dâŋ manawec.
Eme hâwec motec honepie wokezi ira hoemaŋko sâcne ŋeŋene mi ewec. Irec Kreta nuc irec hâwec motec moc fowec šâŋene Foiniki, ira raširâ ŋehapie hoemaŋ taraocte mumbiŋ. Hâwec motec irec masunezi mula â jowarec mâmâc sâoc-jofawec.
Eme râpefuŋ-nâŋeckonec mâŋâŋ burec burec mac qame wokeŋic raniŋte murâ aŋga fârepie wefume Kreta nuc heririŋkerâ rambeŋ.
Raha rahapene nuckonec mâŋâŋ hâhâwicne šâŋene kagu,
izi qahuc woke qâtuŋkeme bâipieku behepie qâso bâsoriewec.
Eku nuc piticne moc šâŋene Kauda, irec ŋifecnao rahapene woke gombazi hâwecko huzo eme
gie sâko baku fârepene woke faio fewec. Erâ woke fâuckezacte repazi rowaŋauckehuc bândeŋnembeŋ. Eme haroŋaŋ moc šâŋene Siriti, ira fenšipeŋte rac fârepie wahame mâŋâŋzi qâsoriec-nâpome rambeŋ.
Eme mâŋâŋ tâpirinehec qahuc fowecte hae fureme mafa gâcne hâwecko behepie huwec.
Eme hae mocwâc fureme wokere wâcwiac gâcne iŋuc jaha ropie huwec.
Ŋafe šoaŋ gâcnao mâŋâŋ hâhâwicnehec qahuc domahame šoaŋ me bâpiŋ moc mi fuame honerâ maŋ mamanasu-nâŋec šickeme ši ine mi junaŋmu mumbeŋ.
Eme ŋic jaŋe nânâ qikiŋne-fârerâ juhapie Paulozi ra ŋondeŋ-jeŋicko domahuc šiŋuc jazawec: “Ŋicbureŋ, ŋoŋe dâŋnane manapie muzac, ine Kreta nucko junšapeŋ. Eme wiac hâhâwicne â mafa sisipiric ine mi fua-nârezac.
Ʒi ine sifu hâhâwic qamaseniŋ, ŋiczi mi sipirickenaŋmu, wokezi ine jâmbomac sipirickeocmu.
Jacne ŋafeo runane Anutu eki kiŋaŋ qaqa-ticne norao aŋelo moc soreme fua-narerâ
šiŋuc nazajec: `Paulo go mi hâwicguoc, go Roma ŋicwofuŋtao fisi-jâmbâŋkecmu, erâ manakic, Anutuzi go ŋezicguhuc ŋic gohec wokeo juŋgopieŋ jaŋe mâmâc gore erâ ŋezic-jopa-fâreocmu. Ž
Irec, âgofâc-nane, ŋoŋe buŋeŋic biaŋkezejec. No Anuture maŋ jahec mi ekopac, dâŋ nazajec i sanaŋkeocmu.
Wokezi ine nuc mocko ferâ henšaŋneocmu.”
Eme Adria hâwecko qac qâsoric ehuc juhapene ŋafe šoaŋ 14 eme wokeŋic jaŋe manapie mâreŋ bâqiŋkeŋgopeneŋ tinac ewec.
Iŋuc manahuc sâc behepie hume 30 meta ewec. Erâ ipec rarâ sâc mocwâc râepie hume 22 meta sawa ewec.
Eme haroŋaŋko fenšipeŋ muhuc hâwic-jopame woke šâhecnao aŋga 4 behepie hume hae fureocte hejâpehuc ŋembiŋ.
Ŋeku wokeŋic jaŋe woke beherâ wiseniŋte manasuhuc woke gomba râepie hume burec ehuc kecšiŋuc mumbiŋ: “Nâŋe woke masunao aŋga moc behepene huocmu.”
Iŋuc epie Paulozi momori soŋaŋ â ŋicfâc-ticne šiŋuc jazawec: “Wokeŋic jaŋe wisepie ŋoŋe hâwecko hufâreniŋmu.”
Jazame momori jaŋe woke gombare niŋgiŋ hetâcnepie gomba hâwecko hume behembiŋ.
Eme hae fureocte woŋec juhuc Paulozi ŋic mâmâc sasawa šiŋuc jazawec: “Ŋoŋe maŋ sahac-ŋeŋic soka fâkic eme nânâ mi nâhuc mâc juhapie miŋecgac šoaŋ 14 ekac.
Irec ši nânâ nâniŋte ŋazape mi qataraniŋ. Nânâ nâqiŋnerâ sâcne tiŋko ferâ juniŋmu. Qizec susuc-ŋeŋic moc mi waharâ sifuckeocmu.”
Iŋuc murâ hone-fârehapie poroŋ moc rorâ Anutu daŋge âzâcnehuc bazurâ nâwec.
Nâme honerâ maŋjeŋic firieme iŋuc jaha nâfârembiŋ.
Ŋic wokeo jumbeŋ šare-nâŋec 276.
Nânâ nâ gapec erâ wokemaŋkonec padi hâwecko behepie hume woke afeckerâ wefuwec.
Hae fure-fâreme mâreŋ šâŋitaniŋte hone-bipiembiŋ. Ehuc hâwec kenšuŋne moc haroŋaŋ tâmiric honerâ wokezi ira raširâ moŋgeŋko feocte
ŋic jaŋe aŋga niŋgiŋne hetâcnepie hâwecko hume rac fârepie feme guriŋ goroŋkerâ moŋgeŋkopec ma bahuc rambiŋ.
Guriŋ bâipiehapie woke mâreŋ masunao fewec. Ehuc woke masune kindeŋnerâ sanaŋkehame hâwec siri sâkozi woke šâhecne qanšaŋnewec.
Woke šaŋkeme kâpâcwâru ŋic jaŋe fifia bahuc wisenšipiŋte momori jaŋe qâhâmoc-jopazo mumbiŋ.
Soŋaŋ-jeŋiczi ine Paulore erâ qatara-jarewec. Erâ mume fifia bapa jaŋe qanaŋ hâwecko rucnerâ fifia bahuc tiŋko fembiŋ,
â gâcne jaŋe palaŋ faio â wokere dâkâ faio ferâ rambiŋ. Iŋuczi iŋuc ehuc furu jaha tiŋko fefârembiŋ.
Tiŋko fefârerâ nuc šâŋene Melite mupie manambeŋ.
Eme nuc irec rune jaŋe âgo jauŋ bocjaha enârembiŋ. Ehuc hoe mâmâteŋte šocsâko ruqe-nârepie šame ruambeŋ.
Eme Paulozi nâŋ gagate wiac qânusuckerâ šocko râeme hume irec maŋnaonec homa moc andaŋ mandaŋte wefurâ Paulo menao kiŋ qaŋatie domawec.
Ehame mâreŋ rune jaŋe menao homa domame honerâ nazaŋ gazaŋ erâ mumbiŋ, “Ŋic e šika qaqa jâmbâŋ, hâwecko mi hurâ hâmojecte šira tiŋko wefume okacne fisicnekac.”
Eme Paulozi homa qatatiŋkeme šocko hume homazi mi kiwec tinac fâsâcne domawec.
Domahame jaŋe sisiwiŋ fuacneocmu me onšoŋ jaha hâmorâ rândiŋkeocmu muhuc woŋec ŋembiŋ. Ŋekuhapie iŋuc me iŋuc mi ecneme honerâ mumbiŋ, “Ŋic e nemu. “
Jumbeŋ irec bembeŋnao ŋicbomboŋ-jeŋic šâŋene Popilio ere hae mâreŋ fowec. Eme ŋic eki hâcne hezu hewâneŋ enâreme ere ficko šoaŋ jahec â moc ŋeŋe juju embeŋ.
Juhapene Popilio mamac-ticne huc fuacneme woke socnehec qawec. Eme Paulozi manarâ ficticnao ferâ mene qizecnao râerâ numuhuc bâpiaŋkewec.
Iŋuc eme biŋene manarâ nuc irec ŋic gâcne huc šâic-jeŋichec fisipie iŋuc jaha ɋiɋicne bacjopawec.
Eme irec okacne ŋic jaŋe bubiaŋ mana-nârehuc uruc jauŋ fekicne enârembiŋ. Erâ rara dameŋ maickeme hata nâsiŋ wiac wokeo râe-nârembiŋ wâc.
Nuc ira hâcne juhapene mosa jahec â moc tarame woke furunao fembeŋ. Woke i Alesandria haeonec, qoruc-ticnao nemu hahac ɋa jahere hawari bakicne. Nâŋe jumbeŋko ijaha woke i ŋehuc juhame hoemaŋ tarame ira hâcne ferâ rambeŋ.
Raku Siraku haeo fisirâ raširâ šoaŋ jahec â moc jumbeŋ.
Irecnec mâŋâŋ hecnehuc bac bâŋoric raku Regioŋ haeo fisimbeŋ. Eme hae fureme râpefuŋ-nâŋecko mula qahuc ficne suec-nâpome ŋafe šoaŋ jajahec sawa raku Puteoli haeo fisimbeŋ.
Fisipene hae irec miti mamanazi hefârec-nâpopie šoaŋ 7 jaŋehec ŋeŋe juju embeŋ. Eme irecnec mocwâc raku Roma haeo fisimbeŋ.
Eme hae irec miti mamanazi biŋe-nâŋec biac manambiŋte gâcnezi wareku Apio haeo bâfuac-nâpombiŋ â gâcnezi Tetrabeŋ haeo bâfuac-nâpombiŋ. Eme Paulozi honec-joparâ Anutu daŋge âzâcnerâ bubiaŋ manawec.
Roma haeo fisipene kiazi mume Paulo kâpâcwâru ficko mi râembiŋ, momori moczi soŋaŋkeha fic omane mocko ŋec juc ewec.
Juhame šoaŋ jahec â moc eme Judaŋic jaŋere micne hefârec-jopame fisipie dâŋ šiŋuc jazawec: “Âgo bureŋ, no Judaŋic âgofâc-nâŋec mi kisuec-jopapo â mimiŋnefâc-nâŋec jaŋere dâŋ mi qâsuapo. Eme jaŋe sifu Romaŋic jaŋerao qikiŋnupie Jerusalem haeo kâpâcwâru bacnumbiŋ.
Eme Romaŋic jaŋe fuŋne-nane mu rituc ehuc nuniŋte kiŋnane basarâ firuecnuniŋte mumbiŋ.
Ehame Judaŋic jaŋe sanaŋne qatarapie Roma ŋicwofuŋzi dâŋnane mutaraocte mupo, Judaŋic âgofâc-nâŋec jaŋere dâŋ šira bawarerâ mupemurâ ine mi warepo.
Eme no irec hâcne honec-ŋoparâ ŋoŋehec muc manac enaŋte hefârec-ŋopape fisimbieŋ. No ine Israe ŋic woworic-nâŋec ewec ere erâ kâpâcwâru ŋic epo jukopac ši.”
Iŋuc muhuc jazame mumbiŋ, “Ocna Judaŋic mâreŋfuŋ-nâŋecko jueŋgopieŋ jaŋe gore dâŋ mi qâreŋke-nârembiŋ me ŋicjeŋic moc mi sorepie ware gore bahacdâŋ mume manambeŋ.
Irec dâŋ bajuekic i go gahac mutec mananaŋte muŋgopeneŋ. Á opâ ruakicne jaŋere šiŋuc manaeŋgopeneŋ: Mâreŋ sâc ŋiczi mu supaic ejareeŋgopieŋ.”
Iŋuc murâ šâfo babac embiŋ. Eme i maickeme Judaŋic bocjahazi Paulore ficko tumaŋnembiŋ. Eme Anuture uucmaŋte dâŋ binaŋ uupicte fuŋkerâ jazahuc juhame hae ŋafewec, ehuc Mosere sâcmutâc dâŋqâhâcko â porofete jaŋerao biŋedâŋ qâreŋkekicne fokac i Jesurao fâri fideteŋ ewec, irec fuŋne muhuc maŋuruc qajarewec.
Ejareme ŋic gâcne jaŋe dâŋticne âgo bambiŋ â gâcnezi ine qaisockembiŋ.
Ehuc mu qaqatarac epie Paulozi dâŋ mocjaha šiŋuc jazawec: “Tiri Mârozi porofete Jesaja ecneme mimiŋnefâc-ŋeŋic sowine dâŋ kecšiŋuc jazawec:
`Go rarâ ŋicguru keci šiŋuc jazac: Hazeczi mamana i mananiŋmu, maŋzi mamana tara ine mi eniŋmu. Ʒâŋezi fifi finiŋmu, wiac hohone tara ine mi eniŋmu.
Ŋicguru ši jaŋe maŋjeŋic sanaŋkekicne, â hazec-jeŋic bâzickekicne, â šâŋe-jeŋic hâmonšambiŋ. Irec šâŋe-jeŋiczi wiac mi hone taraeŋgopieŋ, â hazec-jeŋiczi wiac mi mana taraeŋgopieŋ, â maŋjeŋiczi wiac mi manasu-hâmoeŋgopieŋ, ehuc maŋjeŋic mi bârisiepie no wemocko bâpiaŋ-jopazapo.'
Irec no ŋazape mananiŋ, Anutuzi bâbâpiaŋ hata bâfuawec i qâpuc jaŋere biŋe ekac, jaŋe sâcne mana aŋac eniŋmu.” [
Iŋuc muhuc jazame Judaŋic jaŋe jaŋackoaŋ mu wioc bocjaha eec ehuc rambiŋ.]
Eme Paulozi jara 2 Roma haeo fic omanao juhame ŋic jaŋe iqickehuc jumbiŋ.
Iqickepie Anuture uucmaŋte dâŋ binaŋ ejarehuc Wofuŋ Jesu Kristo ere fuŋne hâwicmâc jaha muhezuc tâmiricko jaza qazuc ehuc juwec.
Paulo no Jesu Kristozi kiŋaŋ qaqa-ticne bacnurâ aposolo-ticne mucnuhuc Anuture Biŋebiaŋ râepe qareŋko raocte rowosâecnuwec.
Miti i hâcne fuaocte Anutuzi mârâc jaha porofete ejareme irec findaŋdâŋ tiri papiao qâreŋkembiŋ.
Qâreŋkepie Ŋokâ-ticnerao iticnewec. E sahachec fufua i Dawidi ɋâricfâc-ticne jaŋeraonec fuawec,
erâ e maŋɋaɋac bâbâfua Mârohec jujuzi Anuture Ŋokâ jukac, irec fuŋne hâmokonec faharewecko fua taniŋke-jâmbâŋkewec.
Jesu Kristo e Wofuŋ-nâŋeczi aki anonoc enarehuc aposolo gie tahacnuwec. Ehuc mâreŋ sâc ŋic miti jazepe mana rereŋ epie Jesure šâŋe biŋe raocte munarewec.
Eme ŋoŋe jaŋere âgofâc jaha, Jesu Kristore ŋicfâc eniŋte hefârec-ŋopakicne, irec gie i ŋoŋerao iŋuc jaha bapere munarewec.
Roma haeonec Anuture jorofâc, tiriŋic mucŋopakicne, ŋoŋere hâcne papia ši qâreŋkekopac. Mamac-nâŋec Anutu â Wofuŋ Jesu Kristo eraonec aki anonoc â wama ŋoŋerao fotâcnerâ fozejec.
Miti babaju-ŋeŋicte mâreŋ sâc manapie biaŋkekacte qanaŋ ŋoŋere erâ daŋge mupe Jesu Kristorao qarâ Anutu-nanerao fotâcnekac.
No Ŋokâ-ticnere Biŋebiaŋ muhuc maŋnanezi Anutu kiŋaŋ qacnepe fuŋne-nane manakacte ere maio dâŋ ši mupe mananiŋ:
No numucneekopac sâc ŋoŋere mâmâc hati manasuekopac, ehuc Anutu maname sâckeme hata bâfua-nareme ŋoŋerao fâpemurâ âzâcneekopac.
No ŋoŋe honec-ŋopapere enareekac. Ehuc fârâ maŋte bâmec moc baŋarepe qiŋ herâ juniŋte muekopac.
Me kecšiŋuc mupe: No ŋoŋerao fâpe mamanasiŋte fârine nowac gowatuŋ ehuc keketeŋ enšepeneŋ.
Erâ âgofâc-nane, fuŋne-nane kâuc banšipiŋte šiŋuc ŋazape: No ŋicguru gâcne jaŋerao eeckopac iŋuc jaha ŋoŋerao fârâ miti giere fârine piticne bâfuapemurâ hati muekopac. Erâ fâzo mupe sâc wiac gâcnezi niŋgiŋnume juekopac.
Noni ŋic kosa. Grikŋic â kâte sanaŋ, mamanahec â mutucne mâmâc mitizi tofa bazu-jarepemurâ munarekicne.
Irec Romaŋic ŋoŋe iŋuc jaha Biŋebiaŋ ŋazapemurâ maŋnanezi afeckeekopac.
No Biŋebiaŋte manape mimi gaŋgaŋnehec mi eekac, i Anuture tâpirihec, irec mana sakac eniŋmu sâc bâpiaŋ-jopaocmu, Judaŋic hâcne, erâ Grikŋic mâmâc.
Biŋebiaŋko hâcne Anuture tiŋne fua taniŋkeekac, i hâcne eki mamanasiŋhec jaŋe tahac-jopaekac, ehame mamanasiŋko utuckeniŋmu. Dâŋqâreŋ šiŋuc hâcne fokac: “Biaŋkekicnezi mamanasiŋte erâ juju hotâckeocmu.”
Ŋiczi ine Anutu qamaserâ sindaŋ ehuc kike hata-ticne hesifuckeeŋgopieŋte kimbeŋ ticnezi sambâŋkonec fua taniŋkeekac.
Anuture fuŋne gâcne ŋiczi mamanane i manaeŋgopieŋ, Anutu jahac bataniŋke-jarewec.
Anutu e ŋiczi mi hohonene, â mâreŋ bâfuahuc ine wiac fuŋne fuŋne râewec izi tâpiri sanaŋ-ticne â qâreŋ-ticne bataniŋkeme sâcne hone mana tarac eeŋgopieŋ. Irec ŋic gâcne jaŋe wemocko kâuc bahuc sahac ŋeŋezic dâŋ muniŋmu.
Jaŋe ine Anutu jukac i mana-bipiehuc mi jukac-tinac eha araŋ mi bacnembiŋ â mucne bacne mi ecnembiŋ, aricne. Jaŋe mumusifuc fuŋne fuŋne bâfuahuc maŋmutuc epie dapâczi foŋjopawec.
Ehuc nâŋe mamanahec juŋgopeneŋ muhuc sâke bâbâc eku maŋmutuc embiŋ.
Iŋuc ejareme jaŋe Anutu juju hati e araŋ mi bacnehuc ŋic â wipe â qowi â homa, wiac sisirowene hâcne irec ɋâŋ qâqâtâc barâ araŋ bacnembiŋ.
Iŋuc epie Anutuzi hone suŋgiŋ ejareme maŋzi sasec kosa hurerâ mamakâc ehuc maŋ sahac-jeŋic bâsâqorembiŋ.
Jaŋe Anutu jâmbomac rune râpeckerâ burec maickembiŋ. Ehuc ru bâbâfua-Jeŋic qikiŋnerâ wiac bâfuakicne araŋ bacnehuc kiŋaŋ qacnembiŋ. Wiac bâfua-fârewec e mumuteŋheczi mumuteŋhec jurašihuc jume sâckeocmu. Jâmbomac.
Ŋic jaŋe e hâcne râpeckembiŋte suŋgiŋ-jopame sasec sâqocne jâmbâŋ bâfuambiŋ. Ehuc ŋokac jaŋe Anutuzi hata muwec i qâsorierâ mi jujuo rambiŋ.
Á ŋic jaŋe iŋuc jaha ŋowe ŋonâŋ juju qikiŋnerâ maŋjeŋicko sasecte šocsâko šame jaŋe jaŋackoaŋ mamakâc fuŋmoc bâfuambiŋ. Erâ bâbâsifuc-jeŋicte okacne maŋ sahac sisipiric rombiŋ.
Jaŋe Anuture fuŋne mana-bipiehuc enšaŋauc ecnepie suŋgiŋ-jopame maŋjeŋic bâzickeme wiac mi eene i hâcne embiŋ.
Ehuc wiac hehesicne fuŋne fuŋne hurepie fewec, sindaŋ, andac, râŋgeŋne, erâ maŋjeŋicko iiŋguuŋ â šika â rârâsi â eeatuc, erâ gibioc izi fusucmakicne.
Jaŋe gupe bapa, micko âkec ŋic, Anutu kisâ eecne, šaubacne, pepecne, sahac mumuteŋ, sâqocnere hata bâbâfua, neŋgoc mamac dâŋ qaqatara,
maŋ mamanasu tâmiric juju, doc bapa, uruc jauŋ tâmiric juju.
Wiac iŋucne ehuc sipirickezo, Anuture micdâŋ iŋuc fokac i mana-bipiehuc sifu eeŋgopieŋ, erâ i sawa mâcne, gâcnezi epie hume keteŋ ejareeŋgopieŋ wâc.
Irec ŋic go wemocko fuŋnege murârâŋnecmu? Ŋic gâcnezi bahac bâfuapie mana sâqore-jarehuc gahacne fuŋne bataniŋkeekic hâcne. Mana sâqore-jareekomec, go ijaha hâcne eekomec i¡
Eme Anutuzi ŋic iŋuc eeŋgopieŋ jaŋe okacne bazu-jareme sâcke-hâmoekac iŋuc manaŋgopeneŋ.
Ŋic go gâcne jaŋere dâŋbahac muhuc ijaha eekic, ehuc “no Anutuzi akicnuocmu” iŋuc mu wiac moc ezic ine¡
Me Wofuŋzi buuruc â wama ruaine sâc fekicne egarehuc akicguhuc jume go wemocte manatâc qatakic ehuc juekic? Go maŋge bârisiecmurâ Anutuzi buuruc egareekac i mi mana taraekic me?
Go maŋsanaŋ erâ maŋge mi bârisiehuc šocfiki bafeku seroŋ batec šoc šaza dameŋko Anuture mumutara dâŋ fârine fua taniŋkeme šâhâmocguocmu.
Anutuzi ŋic eebapa-nâŋecte sâc furine nârezokac hâcne.
Ŋic eehâmo gie paŋšâic bahuc eri tatamac â juju saric bâfuaniŋte samarieniŋmu jaŋe juju sanaŋ jarezokac.
Ŋic râŋgeŋne dâŋ fâri qizecne bâsuehuc wiac hehesicne bajuniŋmu jaŋerao ine wiac šâšâicne â mimicne bâfuaocmu.
Sâqocne bapa sasawa, Judaŋic hâcne â Grikŋic mâmâc, jaŋe šâic serereŋ â hâhâwic sâko fua-jareocmu.
Tiŋne Juniŋmu sasawa, Judaŋic hâcne â Grikŋic mâmâc, jaŋe eri tatamac â wama fua-jareocmu.
Anutu e ra rowec ware rowec mi focnekac.
Ŋic sâcmutâc dâŋ tâmiric juhuc sâqocne baeŋgopieŋ jaŋe sasawa sâcmutâc dâŋ tâmiric jaha sipirickeniŋmu. Á sâcmutâc dâŋhec juhuc sâqocne baeŋgopieŋ jaŋe sasawa Anutuzi sâcmutâc dâŋte sâcko dâŋjeŋic mutara-jareocmu.
Sâcmutâc dâŋ mâc hazeczi mananiŋmu jaŋe Anutuzi honec-jopame tiŋne mi eŋgopieŋ, manarâ reŋkeeŋgopieŋ jaŋe ine tiŋne mujareocmu.
Ŋic qâpuc sâcmutâc dâŋ mi mufua-jarekicne jaŋe maŋjeŋicte sâcmutâc dâŋ reŋkehuc ine sâcmutâc dâŋ tâmiriczi sâcmutâc dâŋhec tinac eeŋgopieŋ.
Iŋuc epie sâcmutâc dâŋ i maŋjeŋicko qâreŋkekicne, irec fuŋne jaŋgeŋkeekac. Sâcmutâc dâŋ maŋjeŋicko qâreŋkekicnere maŋjeŋiczi tutuc qajareekac, erâ wâc maŋ mamanasu-jeŋiczi foc forisic ehuc ŋifec mu qatarac eekac â ŋifec mu bâmiriŋ eekac.
I dameŋ sâkore iŋuc eekac. Ira Anutuzi Jesu Kristo ecneme maŋnâŋecko wiac soŋsoŋ fokac irec fuŋne bataniŋkeocmu. No Biŋebiaŋ muekopac irec sâcko bataniŋkeocmu hâcne.
Go šâŋege Judaŋic muhuc sâcmutâc dâŋzi roŋgâŋ egareme herâ foekic. Erâ no Anuture fuŋne manakopac muhuc sahac fefe juekic.
Go Anuture micdâŋ manaekic, erâ sâcmutâc dâŋ qazu-garekicnere keci ezo, keci mi ezo i mana wosâeekic.
Ehuc gahacnere šiŋuc muekic: “No tiŋtuŋ sâcne jowa qataŋ ejarepemu, â dapâcko juŋgopieŋ jaŋe sâcne batamae-jarepemu,
â ŋic maŋpuriŋhec jaŋe sâcne jaza bâtiŋ ejarepemu, â ɋiemaŋ jaŋe wiac sâcne qazu-jarepemu. No sâcmutâc dâŋhecte mamana â dâŋfâri irec wamboŋne rauckerâ jukopac i.”
Go iŋuc muekiczi ŋic gâcne miti qazu-jarehuc gahacne maŋ mi qazucneekic. Go ŋic fiuc mi ronšepieŋ jazahuc gahac fiuc roekic.
Ŋowe ŋonâŋ ŋohe bebehec mi ezepirec jazahuc gahac ŋonâŋge beheekic. Go nemuɋâŋ sureekiczi nemu ufuŋte wiac fiuc roekic.
Go sâcmutâc dâŋte manasuhuc maŋfefe eekiczi sâcmutâc dâŋ qâsuahuc Anutu gâc hecneekic.
Irec hâcne kecšiŋuc qâreŋkekicne: “Qâpuc jaŋe ŋoŋere kiŋte erâ Anuture šâŋe musoriŋkeeŋgopieŋ.”
Go sahacgao Anuture ma bakicne i sâcmutâc dâŋ reŋketec fârinehec eocmu. Me sâcmutâc dâŋ qataratec sahacgao ma izi fârimâc eocmu.
Erâ dâŋ irec ŋifecne qac qârisic fokac wâc. Ŋic moc ma tâmiriczi sâcmutâc dâŋ reŋkeocmuo mahec tinac eocmu.
Ehuc ma tâmiric fuarâ juekaczi sâcmutâc dâŋte gie baocmu eki ine fuŋnege rituocmu, miti papia â mahec juhuc sâcmutâc dâŋ qâsuaekic gore fuŋne hâcne rituocmu.
Moc e mâc sahaczi Judaŋic hawari eocmu â sahacko sawa mahec juocmu, iŋucnezi Judaŋic fârine mi eocmu.
Maŋzi Judaŋic izi fârine. Á sahacko sâcmutâc dâŋte ma rojuju i mâcne, maŋko Mârore ma rojuju izi fârine. Ŋic iŋucnere ŋiczi mâcne, Anutuzi maname biaŋkeocmu.
Hâc, eme Judaŋic jaŋe qâpuc jaŋehec sâc mocjaha eŋgopieŋ, â sahacko ma i wiac racne me?
Iŋuc aricne. Judaŋic jaŋe wiac bocjaha tahac-jopakicne. Jaŋe hâcne Anutuzi biŋedâŋ fuŋne fuŋne jazame irec rune embiŋ.
Eme weniŋuc? Judaŋic gâcne jaŋe dâŋte woŋec juku pârâckembiŋte šiŋuc muzo me? “Dodocke-jeŋiczi Anutu mume sasanaŋ-ticne bawahaocmu.”
I aric kereŋne¡ Anutu e buc mume sasanaŋ â ŋic ine mumu dodocne, iŋuc muzo. Miti qâreŋ moc šiŋuc hâcne fokac: “Go mumutiŋgezi dâŋfâri eocmu, â mumutaragezi ɋaɋacne eocmu.”
Eme hehesic-nâŋeczi Anutu tiŋne-ticnere fuŋne bajaŋgeŋkekacte weniŋuc muzo? šiŋuc muzo me? “Fuŋne iŋuc fokacte Anutuzi irec okacne nâreme mi sâckeocmu.” (Dâŋ i ŋic mamanare sâcko mukopac.(c)
I aric kereŋne¡ Anutu e hehesic-nâŋecte okacne nâreme sâckeocmu. Mâc muzac wemocko mâreŋŋic šeŋgoma dâŋnâŋec sâcne mutarazac.
Eme ŋifec ine burecdâŋ-nanezi Anuture dâŋfâri dopeckeme šâŋe biŋe-ticne irec erâ fekacko wemocte sifu no wâc sâqocne bapa munarehuc okacne nareekac?
Erâ wemocte šiŋuc mi mueŋgopeneŋ: “Sâqocne bapene ŋerisierâ fârine biaŋne fuaoc me.” Nâŋe iŋuc mueŋgopeneŋ munârehuc micko âkec enâreeŋgopieŋ hâcne. Dâŋ iŋucne muhuc hata i âteeŋgopieŋ jaŋe okacne fua-jareme sâckeocmu.
Eme weniŋuc? Judaŋiczi ŋic gâcne jowarurâ sâc moc juŋgopeneŋ me? I aricne jâmbâŋ. Biac mumbeneŋ, Judaŋic â Grikŋic nânâc mâmâc sâqocnere kiŋaŋ qaeŋgopeneŋ.
Dâŋqâreŋ moc šiŋuc hâcne fokac: “Ŋic moczi tiŋne moc mi jukac, aric ɋaɋacne;
moczi mamanahec moc mi jukac, moczi Anutu wira basac mi ecneekac.
Jaŋe qâsoriekicne sasawa, šeŋgoma repirembiŋ; moczi moc wiac biaŋne mi eekac, arictac jâmbâŋ.
Marac-jeŋic i hâmoc qâŋɋâŋ bâbâfua, nameŋ-jeŋic forisieme eatuc dâŋ wefuekac, qotâ marasiŋ kisoŋnerâ jueŋgopieŋ.
Bipic-jeŋic sâwec â aaric dâŋte gegerockeekac.
Ʒikare kike afec jueŋgopieŋ.
Ima samaki bahuc tuhu bâfuaeŋgopieŋ.
Wamare hata ine kâuc baeŋgopieŋ.
Á šâŋe mai-jeŋicko Anuture hâhâwic mi fokac.”
Nâŋâc šiŋuc manaeŋgopeneŋ: Sâcmutâc dâŋ i dâŋ rune nâŋe nazakicne. I ŋic sasawa fuŋne-nâŋec rituhuc micnâŋec ɋâtâocte ekicne. Eme ŋic mâmâc sasawa kiŋnâŋec Anuturao fua-fârekac.
Sâcmutâc dâŋte erâ kiŋ nânâwoc ro i Anuturao moc mi fokac. Sâcmutâc dâŋzi sindaŋ-nâŋec bataniŋkeekac hâcne.
Eme irec sâcmutâc dâŋ fohame Anutuzi tiŋne-ticne fua taniŋkeocte hatane moc bâfuawec fokac, hata i sâcmutâc dâŋqâhâcko â porofete jaŋerao wâc biŋedâŋ-ticne mu qâreŋ ekicne.
Jesu Kristo manasiŋkehuc kiŋfâsâc erâ juju, hata i hâcne mamanasiŋhec sasawa jaŋere biŋe ekac. Fuŋne-nâŋec bârâwiŋ mi fokac,
Nâŋâc mâmâc sasawa sâqorembeŋte Anuture eri tatamacko fifisinere sâc mi eŋgopeneŋ.
Ehame Kristo Jesu e kiwiric-nâŋec rowecte Anutuzi aki anonoc-ticnere erâ kiŋfâsâc bacnâpoekac.
Eki mume Jesu e socticnezi sâqocne-nâŋecte erâ taha bawec, eme e manasiŋkeniŋmuzi taha i biŋeckeniŋmu. Sâqocne ewarehuc jukicne irec kiŋ i Anutuzi buuruc-ticnere râeme fowarehuc juwecte Jesu hâmocko râewecko tiŋnere fuŋne bataniŋkewec.
E tiŋnere rune juekac, â Jesu manasiŋkeniŋmu jaŋe kiŋfâsâc bacjopaekac, irec fuŋne dameŋ šiŋuczia taniŋkeocte iŋuc hâcne ewec.
Eme mumuteŋ-nâŋec moc fokac me? Aricne, mumuteŋ-nâŋec hetâtiekicne. Wemozi hetâtiewec? Eehâmo giere hatazi me? Aricne, mamanasiŋte hatazi.
Irec dâŋ šiŋuc manapene fozejec: Ŋic nâŋâc sâcmutâc dâŋ rereŋkere mâcne, mamanasiŋte erâ kiŋfâsâc fuaeŋgopeneŋ.
Me Anutu e Judaŋic nâŋere Anutu sawa, qâpuc jaŋere aricne? Iŋuc mâcne, e qâpuc jaŋere Anutu jaha wâc.
E Anutu-nâŋec mocjaha jukaczi hâcne Judaŋic â qâpuc mâmâc mamanasiŋ-nâŋecte erâ kiŋfâsâc bacnâpoekac.
Eme iŋuc muhuc mamanasiŋte erâ sâcmutâc dâŋ hetâtieŋgopeneŋ me? Aric kereŋne, sâcmutâc dâŋ hešakieŋgopeneŋ.
Eme sahackopec mimiŋne-nâŋec Abraham e wemo bâfuawec munaŋmu?
E jahacne eehâmo giere erâ kiŋticne hefâsâewecko ropaŋ sâcne focnezac. Erâ Anuture maio ine arictâc.
Miti papiao dâŋ šiŋuc fokac i: “Abraham e Anutu manasiŋkeme irec erâ maname kiŋticne tarawec.”
Moc e gie bame furime râcnepene izi katucmâc rârâcne mi ekac, tofa babazucne ekac.
Á moc e ine eehâmo gie mi bapa, sâqocne bapa kiŋjeŋic beheekac e manasiŋkeocmu, eme Anutuzi ere hâcne mamanasiŋ-ticnere erâ maname kiŋfâsâc eocmu.
Dawidi e iŋuc jaha Anutuzi ŋic moc eehamo gie mi baha, akickehuc kiŋ behecneocmu ere mu šeri ehuc kecšiŋuc qâreŋkewec:
“Bahac-jeŋic behekicne, â sâqocne-jeŋic bâtâmirekicne, jaŋere manape šerine ekac;
ŋic moc Wofuŋzi manacneme kiŋhec mi eekac, ere manape šerine ekac.”
Mušeri dâŋ kecši i mahec nâŋere biŋe sawa ekac me ma tâmiric jaŋere mâmâc ekac? Abrahamte šiŋuc manaeŋgopeneŋ: E Anutuzi mamanasiŋ-ticnere erâ kiŋ behecnewec.
Mo dameŋko behecnewec, mahec juhame me ma tâmitric juhame behecnewec? Mahec mâcne, ma tâmiric juhame behecnewec.
E ma tâmiric juhuc Anutu manasiŋkeme kiŋticne behecnewec irec maqâreŋ šâhec râecnewec. Eme Abraham e iŋuc ehuc ine ma tâmiric jaŋe Anutu manasiŋkehuc kiŋfâsâc eeŋgopieŋ jaŋere micne ewec.
Erâ mahec nâŋere micne bapa wâc ewec, erâ mahecte sawa mâcne, e ma tâmiric juhuc mamanasiŋte kike hata âtewec, hata ijaha mimiŋ qâjâpec âtehuc Abraham micne bapa-nâŋec mucnepene sâckeocmu.
Anutuzi Abraham â ɋâricfâc-ticne mâreŋ sâko mâreŋ biŋe qajarewec, i sâcmutâc dâŋ rereŋte erâ mâcne, mamanasiŋ-ticnere erâ kiŋticne behehuc iŋuc ecnewec.
Eme biŋe qajarekicne hâcne i sâcmutâc dâŋ rune jaŋere ezac muzac, ine mamanasiŋzi wiac jawane ezac â mitio biŋedâŋ feŋec-nâpokicne i fârimâc ezac.
Sâcmutâc dâŋzi kiŋte okacne fai-nâŋecko râeekac. Sâcmutâc dâŋ tâmiricko ine qaqatara mi fuaekac.
Irec hâcne wiac biŋe qanarekicne i mamanasiŋte erâ fuaocmu. Wemocte? I aki anonoczi feŋeŋ râecneme Abrahamte ɋâricfâc sasawa nâŋâcnao sanaŋkeocte. Sâcmutâc dâŋko roweckembiŋ jaŋe sawa mâcne, Abrahamzi mamanasiŋ hata âtewec ijaha âteeŋgopeneŋ nâŋâcnao mâmâc. Eki hâcne Anuture maio apa wirec-nâŋec ekac.
Dâŋqâreŋ šiŋuc hâcne fokac: “Noni go ŋic gurune gurune jaŋere mamac ecmurâ mugarepo.” Abraham e ine Anutu manasiŋkehuc šiŋuc manapaŋkewec: “E hâmoc qâŋɋâŋ bâɋârezo murâ bâɋâreocmu â wiac mi fokac i mume fuaocmu.”
E ŋicguru bocjaha jaŋere mamac ezokac, dâŋ i mana hameŋke-bipiehuc sifu irec mamanac juwec, šiŋuc âzâcnekicnere: “Ɋâricfâcge iŋuc fuanšoŋgopieŋ.”
Erâ wâc e jara-ticne 100 bazukicnezi e jahacne sahac bâmuzuckekicne â Sarare sahac kereŋkekicne i hone-bipiehuc mamanasiŋ-ticne sifu mi ŋeŋgoroŋkewec.
Anutuzi biŋedâŋ âzâcnewec i maname fârimâc mi ewec, ehuc mamanasiŋte sanaŋkerâ Anuture maname fekicne sâko ehame šiŋuc muhuc mana utuckewec:
Anutu e wiac mocte biŋe qaocmu i fârine sâcne bâfuaocmu.
Irec Abraham e mamanasiŋ focnewecte Anutuzi ere maname kiŋfâsâc ewec.
Anutuzi maname kiŋfâsâc ewec, dâŋ i Abrahamte sawa mi qâreŋkekicne, nâŋâcnere wâc mâmâc.
Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu hâmockonec bâɋârewec Anutu hâcne e manasiŋkepene nâŋâcnere iŋuc jaha maname kiŋfâsâc enaŋmu.
Jesu hâcne kiŋbahac-nâŋecte erâ hâmocko râekicne, erâ wâc kiŋfâsâc enaŋte hâmockonec bâɋârekicne.
Nâŋâc mamanasiŋte erâ kiŋfâsâc embeŋte Jesu Kristorao qohotahuc Anuture wamao juŋgopeneŋ.
Jesu ekizia motâc ronârewecte akio juŋgopeneŋ wâc. Erâ juku Anuture huriri qâreŋ fua tâcneme hone šiziwenaŋmu irec mamanac juhuc mu šeri eeŋgopeneŋ.
Erâ i sawa mâcne, hume serereŋ jujure wâc mu šeri eeŋgopeneŋ, ehuc šiŋuc manaeŋgopeneŋ: Hume serereŋ jujuzi maŋuruc bâfuaekac,
maŋuruczi sasanaŋ bâfuaekac, sasanaŋzi sambâŋte woworic bâfuaekac.
Sambâŋte woworic juocmuzi ine mi qurutuaocmu. Tiri Mâro nârekicne eki Anuture maŋjauŋ maŋnâŋecko qoŋgiŋkewecte mi qurutuanaŋmu.
Kristo e ŋic nâŋâc hâŋ qa otec qa ehuc juhapene dameŋ-ticne maickeme sâqocne bapa nâŋâcne okacne hâmowec.
Ŋic tiŋne mocte erâ hâhâmo i ŋic nâŋâcnao mi mecne fokac, mâc ŋic biaŋne mocte erâ hâhâmo ine fufuane mecne.
Anutu eki ine, sâqocne bâfuahuc bunao bahuc juhapene maŋjauŋ-ticne bâfuahuc mume Kristozi okac-nâŋec hâmowec.
Eme ši socticnere erâ kiŋfâsâc embeŋte okac dameŋko roroŋ sasapec sâcne enâre-jâmbâŋkeocmu.
Nâŋâc Anutu râsi ecnehuc juhapene ŋokâ-ticnere hâmocte erâ miriŋ bacnâpowec. Eme ši miriŋ bacnâpowecko juju-ticnere erâ sâcne juju saricko râec-nâpo-jâmbâŋkeocmu.
Erâ i sawa mâcne, Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristozi aki bâfuahuc Anutuhec bâturec-nâpowecte Anutu hâcne mu šeri ecneeŋgopeneŋ.
Irec šiŋuc mananaŋ: Ŋic mocjahare erâ sâqocne mâreŋko fuawec, â sâqocnere erâ hâmoc fuawec, ehuc ŋic sasawa jaŋerao fotâcnewec. Iŋuc fuame ŋic sasawa sâqore-fârembiŋ.
Sâcmutâc dâŋ mi fuahame sâqocnezi qanaŋ fuarâ fowec.Erâ sâcmutâc dâŋ arictacte mâc forâ fowefuwec.
Ehame hâmoczi Adamtao fuŋkerâ ŋic juwefumbiŋ jaŋe ŋicbomboŋ ejare warehuc juhame Mose fuawec, ine dâŋ qâhuckehuc Adamte sâc mi bâfuambiŋ jaŋerao wâc sifu fotâcnewec. Adam e hâcne hâmocte micne bapa ehuctecne, šâhecko jujure micne bapa fuaocte mukicne ere sâsâcne ewec.
Aki anonoczi ine dâŋ qaqare sâc mi ekac. Ŋic mocjaha dâŋ qaqa-ticnere bocjahazi hâmo sipiric embiŋ. Ehame Anuture uruc jauŋ i ine ŋic mocjaha Jesu Kristo ere aki anonocte erâ, Adamte dâŋ qaqa sirickehuc, ŋic bocjaha tahac-nâpokicne
Ŋifec aki anonoc â ŋifec ŋic mocjaha dâŋ qaqa-ticnere fârine jahe sâcjekic bârâwiŋ. Ŋic mocjahare bahaczi hârâcte mumutara bâfuawec, aki anonoczi ine bahac bocjaha qofackehuc kiŋfâsâc bâfuawec.
Ŋic mocjaha dâŋ qaqa-ticnere erâ hâmoczi ŋicbomboŋ ewec, ehame ine aki anonoc fofo dunduŋ â kiŋfâsâc katucmâc fufua i ro maŋ eeŋgopeneŋzi ine ŋic mocjaha Jesu Kristo ere erâ juju sanaŋko ŋicbomboŋ ejâmbâŋkerâ junaŋmu.
Irec šiŋuc: Ŋic mocjahazi dâŋ qaqa bâfuame ŋic mâmâc sasawa hârâcte biŋe embeŋ, iŋuc jaha ŋic mocjaha tiŋne jume kiŋfâsâc ehuc juju biŋecke-fârembeŋ.
Ŋic mocjahare qaqatarare bocjahazi sâqorembeŋ, iŋuc jaha ŋic mocjahare dâŋrereŋte bocjahazi biaŋkenaŋmu.
Sâcmutâc dâŋ e ine sâqocnezi ɋârâŋkeocte ŋondeŋnao rašiwec. Eme sâqocnezi fua fehame aki anonoczi sirickehuc meckecnewec.
Fârine šiŋuc fuaocte: Sâqocnezi hâmocte uucmaŋko ŋicbomboŋ ewec jukac, iŋuc jaha aki anonoczi ŋicbomboŋ erâ kiŋfâsâc bacnâpohuc juju sanaŋko râec-nâpozejec. I Jesu Kristo Wofuŋ-nâŋec ere erâ iŋuc fuazejec.
Eme weniŋuc muzo? Sâqocnere gie bahuc jaha jupene aki anonoczi fua ɋârâŋkehuc sirickezejec, iŋuc muzo me?
Iŋuc misac¡ Sâqocne hâmocnembeŋzi wemocko irec maŋnao šuhuckerâ junaŋmu?
Me kecšiŋuc mi manaŋgopieŋ? Miti Opâ ruahuc Jesu Kristorao šuhuckembeŋzi hâmoc-ticnao ŋeutuckembeŋ.
Ine hâcne, nâŋâc Miti Opâ ruahuc Kristohec mâmâc hâmo duduc ekicne, eme Mamac eri tatamac-ticnezi Kristo bâɋâreme hâmockonec faharewec jukac, iŋuc jaha nâŋâc ɋârerâ juju ɋâri moc junšepeneŋ.
Nâŋâc hâmoc-ticnere hawari ehuc erao šuhuckembeŋte fafahare-ticnao sâc i jaha ehuc šuhuckenaŋmu.
Ʒiŋuc manaŋgopeneŋ: Maŋraŋɋa-nâŋec Jesuhec mâmâc maripoŋko qakicne, i maŋsahac-nâŋecko sâqocnere tâpiri ŋeŋgoroŋkeocte â sâqocnere kiŋaŋ mocwâc mi qanaŋte.
Moc e hâmome sâqocnere niŋgiŋ ŋetaracneocmu.
Kristohec hâmombeŋko ine ehuc wâc junaŋmu, iŋuc manapaŋkenaŋmu.
Kristore manaŋgopeneŋ, e hâmockonec fahareweczi mocwâc mi hâmoocmu, hâmoczi ŋicbomboŋ mocwâc mi ecneocmu.
Hâmowec i sâqocnere arec mocjaha hâmome tarawec eme ši jukac i Anuture erâ jukac.
Eme ŋoŋe iŋuc jaha ŋaŋacnere manapie sâqocne hâmocnembiŋ ehuc Jesu Kristo ehec Anutu jucneŋgopieŋ ezejec.
Sâqocnezi sahac-ŋeŋic sisirowenao ŋicbomboŋ eŋarezo mume mi manacnenšepieŋ, â sahac-ŋeŋiczi sasecte suruc-ŋopame i wâc mi manacnenšepieŋ.
Erâ wâc me sahac-ŋeŋic i hehesicte mi qikiŋnepie sâqocnere kiŋaŋ qazejec. Aricne, ŋoŋe hâmockonec bâɋârec-ŋopakicnezi Anuture gieo rašinšepieŋ, ehuc mesahac-ŋeŋic Anuture qikiŋnepie tiŋnere kiŋaŋ qazejec.
Ŋoŋe sâcmutâc dâŋko mâcne, Anuture aki anonocko jueŋgopieŋte sâqocnezi ŋicbomboŋ mi eŋareocmu.
Eme ši wenac ezo? Anuture aki anonocko rašihapene sâcmutâc dâŋte aka râriewecte sâqocne bazo me? Iŋuc aricne¡
Me ŋoŋe šiŋuc mi manaŋgopieŋ me? Ŋicbomboŋ moc maŋ sahac-ŋeŋic qikiŋnecnehuc micne reŋkeniŋmuzi ere kiŋaŋ qaqafâc erâ gie-ticne baniŋmu. Sâqocnezi ŋicbomboŋ-ŋeŋic eme ere kiŋaŋ qahuc juku hâmo sipiric eniŋmu me micrereŋzi ŋicbomboŋ-ŋeŋic eme ere kiŋaŋ qahuc tiŋkeniŋmu.
Ŋoŋe sâqocnere kiŋaŋ qaqa juwarembiŋ i tarawec, eme ši mitire hata qazu-ŋarekicne irec sâcko maŋzi manahuc reŋkeeŋgopieŋ irec Anutu muteŋkezo.
Ŋoŋe sâqocnaonec batarac-ŋopakicnezi tiŋnere kiŋaŋ qaqa embiŋ juŋgopieŋ.
Maŋraŋɋa-ŋeŋic gegec dodocnere ŋicko wiac fokac ira sâc hehuc dâŋ ŋazakopac. Ŋoŋe mârâc jaha me sahac-ŋeŋic qikiŋnepie sasec â sindaŋ irec kiŋaŋ qaqa ehame kosa jujumbieŋ, eme dameŋ šiŋuczia me sahac-ŋeŋic qikiŋnepie tiŋnere kiŋaŋ qaqa ehame maŋfuru erâ junšepieŋ.
Sâqocnere kiŋaŋ qaqa jumbiŋko tiŋnere niŋgiŋ mi foŋarewec.
Eme dameŋ ira wemo fârine bâfuambiŋ? Fârine hotâckembiŋ irec šiŋuczia manapie miminehec eekac” eme irec faicnao hâmoc bâbâfuane fokac.
Dameŋ šiŋuczia ine sâqocnere niŋgiŋ ŋeŋgoroŋkeme Anuture kiŋaŋ qaqa embiŋ juŋgopieŋ, ehuc fârine maŋfuru rombiŋ â šâhec juju sanaŋ bâfuaniŋmu.
Sâqocnere furine hâmoc rozo, â Anutu aki anonoc-ticnere fârine ine Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristo erao šuhuckehuc juju sanaŋ rozo.
Âgo bureŋ, sâcmutâc dâŋ mamana ŋoŋere mukopac ŋoŋe kecšiŋuc mi manaŋgopieŋ me? Sâcmutâc dâŋ rereŋke i hâmocko taraekac.
Irec hâcne ŋokac moc e ŋowene ɋâricne juhame bebehene mi fokac. sâcmutâc dâŋko iŋuc mukicne. Ŋowe-ticne hâmome ine sâcmutâc dâŋko ŋowe ŋonâŋ jahere mukicne i tarakac.
Ŋokac moc e ŋowe-ticne ɋâricne juhame beherâ ŋic moctao qohotame šuhuc bâtâcte kiŋ hurekac muzo. Ŋowe-ticne hâmome ine sâcmutâczi niŋgiŋ-jofawec niŋgiŋ i tâcneocmu: ehame ŋic moc baocmuo šuhuc bâtâcte kiŋ mi hureocmu.
Âgo bureŋ, ŋoŋere fuŋne ijaha fokac. Kristo e sahac-ticne hâmocte qikiŋnewec, erao šuhuckehuc sâcmutâc dâŋ hâmocnembiŋ. Ʒi ine ru mocte embiŋ. Hâmockonec faharewec jukac ere hâcne embiŋ. Irec nâŋâc Anutu fârine bâfuacnenšepeneŋ¡
Juju raŋɋa jujumbeneŋ dameŋ ira sâqocnere sasec i sâcmutâc dâŋzi šocticne ficneme me sahac-nâŋecko gie-ticne bajujec. Iŋuc enâreme hâmo sipiricte fârine bâfuambeŋ.
Ʒi ine sâcmutâc dâŋ hâmocnepene niŋgiŋ-ticne tarawecko dâŋqâreŋte hata raŋɋane mi âtehuc Mârore hata ɋâricne âteŋgopeneŋ.
Eme ši weniŋuc muzo? Sâcmutâc dâŋ i sâqocne me? I aricne i¡ Mâc sâcmutâc dâŋ tâmiric muzac, no sâqocnere fuŋne mi mana tarazapo. Sâcmutâc dâŋzi šiŋuc mufua-nâreekac: “Go andac mi ezemec.” Dâŋ i mi fome muzac andacte kâuc bazapo.
Sâqocne e ine sâcmutâc dâŋzi ŋesiŋ ecnehame maŋnane suruckeme andac fuŋne fuŋne fuawec. Sâcmutâc dâŋqâhâc mi fome muzac sâqocnezi mâc mâteŋkerâ fozac.
No mârâc jaha sâcmutâc dâŋqâhâc tâmiricko sâcne juhâmopo. Izi šâhec sâcmutâc dâŋzi bâfuacnume sâqocnezi maŋnaneo ɋâreme hâmopo.
Sâcmutâc dâŋzi enareme juhâmopemurâ mukicne izi hâcne ŋerisierâ šikanehec ewec.
Ine hâcne sâqocnezi hobeteŋko ŋesiŋnehuc sâcmutâc dâŋte erâ eatucnuhuc qâhâmocnuwec.
Erâ ine šiŋuc: Sâcmutâc dâŋqâhâc e bahacmâc, â bâfâuckehuc moc moc mutâcnekicne i wâc bahacmâc â tiŋne â biaŋne.
Hâc, eme dâŋ biaŋnezi hâmoc bâfua-narewec? Iŋuc mâcne, sâqocnezi nuwec. Sâqocne fuŋne-ticne taniŋke-jâmbâŋkeocte dâŋ biaŋnezi âki heha hâmocne nuwec. Sâqocnere manapene gâgâpâcne jâmbâŋ eocte sâcmutâc dâŋzi âki heha nuwec.
Nâŋâc šiŋuc manaŋgopeneŋ: Sâcmutâc dâŋ e Mârore tofa, no ine mâreŋte tofa, sâqocnere hozine.
No eebapa-nanere manape ririsi eekac. No wiac moc ezo enare-bipieme mi eekopac, â wiac sureekopac ine eekopac.
Erâ wiac sureekopac i ehuc ine sâcmutâc dâŋzi biaŋne irec fuŋne bataniŋkeekopac.
Eme hehesic eekopac i no nahacne maŋte mâcne, sâqocnezi maŋnaneo fohuc surucnume eekopac.
No fuŋne šiŋuc manakopac: Maŋnaneo, sahac biuc-nanere maŋko hâcne, biaŋnezi fic hae mi ewec jukac, wiac biaŋnere mumu I muekopac, â fârine bâbâfua ine arictac.
No wiac biaŋne ezepac muhuc mi eekopac, â wiac sâqocne mi ezepac muhuc ine eekopac.
Sâqocne mi ezo muhuc sifu eekopac ine šiŋucte, i no nahac mâcne, sâqocnezi maŋnaneo fic hae ewecte jâiŋko eekopac.
Norao sâcmutâc kecšiŋuc fuaekac: Wiac biaŋne ezo muhape sâqocnezi maicnuekac.
No maŋwâmbuŋ-nanezi Anutu sâcmutâc dâŋticnere mana aŋac eekopac.
Ehame me sahac-naneo sâcmutâc moc fokac izi maŋ mamanasu-nanere dâŋhec rârâsi eekopirec, ehuc niŋgiŋnume sâqocnere sâcmutâc dâŋ me sahac-naneo fic hae ewec ere kâpâcwâru ŋic eekopac
Ŋic huacbucne no mozi sahac-nane hâmocte biŋe ekicne hetara-nareocmu?
Anutu e Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristore erâ muteŋkekopac. Eme šiŋuc hâcne: No nahac maŋ mamanasu-nanezi Anuture sâcmutâc dâŋ kiŋaŋ qacneekopac, sahac-nanezi ine sâqocnere sâcmutâc dâŋ kiŋaŋ qacneekopac.
Eme Jesu Kristohec jueŋgopieŋ ŋic i jaŋerao sâqocnere okacne mumutara-jare moc mi fufuane.
Kristo Jesure erâ juju bâfua-nâreekac Mâro hâcne, ere sâcmutâc dâŋzi sâqocne â hâmoc irec sâcmutâc dâŋ bârârie-nârewec.
Sâcmutâc dâŋ e maŋraŋɋa-nâŋeczi tâpirine bawahame nâŋâcnao gie bâipiewec. Irec Anutu e šiŋuc ehuc maŋraŋɋa sâqocne-ticnere tâpiri qame wahawec: Ŋokâ-ticne soreme sâqocne bapa nâŋâcne sahac hawari rorâ sâqocnere due bawec.
Ine maŋraŋɋare hata mâcne, Mârore hata âteeŋgopeneŋ nâŋâcnao sâcmutâc dâŋrereŋ biaŋ fua-fâreocte iŋuc ekicne.
Juju raŋɋare hata âteeŋgopieŋ jaŋe maŋ mamanasu-jeŋic juju raŋɋare wiacte foekac, â Mârore hata âteeŋgopieŋ jaŋe maŋ mamanasu-jeŋic Mârore wiacte foekac.
Maŋraŋɋare wiacte manasuhuc sisipiric bâfuazo, â Mârore wiacte manasuhuc juju â wama bâfuazo.
Maŋraŋɋare wiacte mamanasu izi Anutu kisâ ecneekac. Ehuc sâcmutâc dâŋticne mi dapecneekac, i wemo-ticnezi sâcne ezac¡
Maŋraŋɋahec jueŋgopieŋ jaŋere Anutuzi takickeekac.
Anuture Mârozi maŋŋeŋicko fic hae ewecko ine maŋraŋɋaopec mâcne, Mâroraopec utuckerâ jueŋgopieŋ. Moc e Kristore Mâro tâmiric juocmuzi ere ŋicbiŋe mi juocmu.
Kristozi maŋŋeŋicko jukacko sahac-ŋeŋiczi sâqocnere erâ hâmoc ruckekac, â maŋ qâqâtâc-ŋeŋiczi ine kiŋfâsâc bacŋopakicnere juju ruckekac.
Eme Jesu hâmockonec bâɋârewec Anutu hâcne, ere Mârozi maŋŋeŋicko ŋeŋe juju ekacko, Kristo Jesu hâmockonec bâɋâreweczi maŋŋeŋicko Mâro-ticne jukac ere erâ sahac-ŋeŋic hâmocne i iŋuc jaha bâɋâreocmu.
Âgo bureŋ, irec hâcne maŋraŋɋazi wemo nâre tahac eekacte nâŋâc tofa bazucnehuc ere wiacko qohotanaŋmu?
Ŋoŋe maŋraŋɋare wiacko qohotaniŋmuo sipirickeniŋmu. Á Mârore tâpirio sahacte dâŋ qaniŋmuo ine juju sâcne jurašihuc juniŋmu.
Anuture Mârozi de âsic ejareha jueŋgopieŋ jaŋe hâcne Anuture naru motecfâc.
Anutu e Mâro ŋarewec i kiŋaŋ qaqafâcne juhuc harierâ hâhâwic bacneniŋte mâcne, naru motecfâcne erâ juniŋte ŋarewec. Irec hâcne “Mamac biaŋ-nâŋec” muhuc wasickeeŋgopeneŋ.
Nâŋâc Anuture naru motecfâc jueŋgopeneŋ, dâŋ i Mârozi maŋnâŋecko musokame manaeŋgopeneŋ.
Naru motecfâcne juŋgopeneŋzi Anuture huhure wâc rauckenaŋmu, Kristohec mâmâc wirec rauckenaŋmu. Ʒira mâreŋko ehec šârâ hâriŋ faio junaŋmuo ehec eri tatamac biaŋko mâmâc jaha junaŋmu.
Sambâŋko Anutuzi eri aŋac bâfua-nâreocmu, i mâreŋko šâic busâqoc fokac ira sâc hepe mamakâc eocmu.
Anuture naru motecfâc eri aŋac-nâŋec fua tâcneocte, wiac bâfuac-jopakicne jaŋe irec woŋec juhuc maŋ hâhâŋ ejareekac.
Wiac omane jaŋe wâc bie gufec hâmo qanšaraŋte maŋnao râec-jopakicne, erâ jaŋacne maŋte mâcne, ŋiczi sahacko râec ejarewec. Erâ jaŋe iŋuc hati fohuc juniŋte mi mujarekicne.
Wiac omane jaŋe wâc hâmo qanšaraŋte niŋgiŋ hetararâ firiehuc Anuture naru motecfâc nâŋâcne eri aŋacko šuhuckeniŋmu hâcne.
Nâŋâc manaŋgopeneŋ, dameŋ i hâcne maickeocte wiac omane jaŋe harac huacbuc ehuc gozi kicjopame šâic manaeŋgopieŋ.
Erâ wiac omane jaŋe sawa iŋuc mi eeŋgopieŋ, sambâŋkonec qaqasune Mâro hâcne nârekicne nâŋâc iŋuc jaha, naru motecfâc-ticne juŋgopeneŋ irec fuŋne Anutuzi, sahac-nâŋec bâfiriehuc, bataniŋkeocte woŋec juhuc maŋzi harac huacbuc eeŋgopeneŋ.
Nâŋâc bâpiaŋ-nâpokicne irec fârine tapamaŋko fokâc. Fârine tâtâc fuame muzac harac huacbuc mi enšapeŋ. Wiac i basahuc ine harac huacbuc ezo.
Fârine tâtâc mi fuame honeeŋgopeneŋte maŋzi worickehuc woŋec jueŋgopeneŋ hâcne.
Mâro e wâc gegec dodoc-nâŋecte erâ bafic-nâpoekac. Nâŋâc iŋuc me iŋuc numupene sâckeocmu, i mi mana-hâmoeŋgopeneŋte Mârozi âkehoc-nâporâ saŋuc ŋiczi mi mamanane i qaekac.
Ehame Anutu e maŋ hohonezi Mârore dâŋ manaekac. Mâro e mitiŋic jaŋere okacne Anutu dâŋsâc-ticnao numuekac.
Nâŋâc manaŋgopeneŋ, Anutu maŋzi jauŋkeniŋmu jaŋe wiac izi me izi fua-jarehuc bâbâpiaŋ-jeŋic dopecke-fâreocmu, ine eki hefârec-jopaocte maname fowecte hefârec-jopawec jaŋe hâcne.
Ŋic qanaŋ honec-jopame sâckewec jaŋe ŋokâ-ticnere hawari eniŋte mucjopawec. Eme ɋafâc-ticne bocjaha ehapene e jahac ine mârâc hahac-nâŋec erâ juocmu.
Anutu e ŋic qanaŋ hone wosâec-jopawec sâc hefârec-jopawec. Hefârec-jopawec sâc kiŋfâsâc bacjopawec. Kiŋfâsâc bacjopawec sâc eric-jopawec.
Dâŋ irec fuŋne weniŋuc fokac? Anutuzi âgo enârehame mozi râsi enâreocmu?
E ŋokâ-ticne mi sakarehuc nâŋâcnere erâ qaisockeweczi ere erâ wiac sasawa mi sesi qeqeric jaha tahac-nâpoocmu me?
Anutu bâwosâecfâc-ticne jaŋe mozi dâŋko râec-jopaocmu? Anutu e jahac kiŋfâsâc bacjopakac.
Me mozi tuŋjopaocmu? Kristo Jesu e jahac hâmowec, erâ hâmowec sawa mâcne, e hâmockonec wâc faharerâ Anuture mefâreo feweczi nâŋâcne riŋ rohuc juekac.
Kristore uruc jauŋkonec wemozi moc batarac-nâpoocmu? Ʒâic busâqoczi me hume serereŋzi me fific guguriŋzi me roroczi me qarâ suriŋnezi me šârâ šâpâzi me šika kâpâcwâruzi?
Dâŋqâreŋ kecšiŋuc fokac irec sâcko wiac enâreeŋgopieŋ: “Gore erâ šoaŋne šoaŋne qa imac enâreeŋgopieŋ, lama qa hezuc eejarene jaŋere sâcko râec-nâpoŋgopieŋ.”
Erâ wiac iŋucnezi mi bâdoc-nâpoocmu, aricne, Jesure uruc jauŋko âtesiŋnehuc sasanaŋ fekicne bâfuarâ domaeŋgopeneŋ.
Irec no šiŋuc manapaŋkekopac: Hâmoczi me jujuzi, aŋelozi me ŋicbomboŋzi, wiac šiŋucne fofonezi me šâhec fufuanezi, me wiac tâpirineheczi,
wiac faicne wawahanezi me juwicnec wewefunezi, wiac izi me izi Anuture uruc jauŋkonec moc mi batarac-nâpo-jâmbâŋkeocmu. Uruc jauŋ i Wofuŋnâŋec Kristo Jesu ere erâ ɋoroc-nâpoekac.
No Kristore ŋiczi burec mi ehuc dâŋ jâmbomac mupe mananiŋ. Tiri Mârozi maŋnane batamaehame mana-jâmbâŋkehuc ŋazape:
No busâqoc fârine manahuc maŋnane wemo afecne fârorockeekac.
Judaŋic âgofâc-nane, soctofafâc-nane hâcne, jaŋere erâ no nahac Kristore sacmaŋkonec wawahare sâcne afeckezapo.
Jaŋe hâcne Israe ŋic, eme Anutuzi fuŋfuŋfâc-ticne bacjopawec, ehuc tâpiri tatamac-ticne jowatuwec. Erâ jaŋehec šâšâfic erâ sâcmutâc dâŋ mufua-jarewec â mai ecnehuc juniŋte hatane jowatuwec. Erâ wâc biŋedâŋ jazawec.
Á mimiŋnefâc-jeŋic jaŋe mitire fuŋqizecne jumbiŋ. Eme Kristozi ŋicsahac rohuc fuawec i jaŋere guruo fuawec. Wiac sasawa irec Wofuŋ jukac, Anutu hâcne, e mumuteŋheczi mumuteŋhec jurašihuc juzejec sanaŋ. Jâmbomac.
Wiac iŋuc fuawec irec Anuture dâŋ dodocne ewec mi muzo. Israeraonec fuambiŋ jaŋe Israe ŋic fârine ninic mi efârembiŋ.
Á Abrahamte tofafâc jaŋe ɋâricfâc-ticne fârine wâc mi efârembiŋ. Eme irec hâcne dâŋ šiŋuc âzâcnekicne: “Isakare ɋâricfâc jaŋe sawa gore biŋe eniŋmu.”
Dâŋ irec fuŋne šiŋuc fokac: Sahaczi Abrahamtao fuambiŋ sâc Anuture ŋicfâc mi efârembiŋ, biŋedâŋko fuakicne jaŋe sawa Abrahamte ɋâricfâc fârine embiŋ.
Biŋedâŋ kecšiŋuc mukicne: “Jara moc tarame Sarazi motec rorâ bajuhame mocwâc warepemu.”
Erâ i sawa mâcne, Rebekarao sâc ijaha fuawec. E mimiŋne-nâŋec Isaka ehec juhuc motec jajahec kiwec-jofawec.
Eme motec jahe mi fuahuc wiac biaŋne me sâqocne mi ehapire Anutuzi jahere šiŋuc âzâcnewec: “Hahaczi ɋare kiŋaŋ qazejec.”
Ine Anutu mumupaŋ-ticne sanaŋkeocte manasuhuc motec juju-jekicte mâcne, e jahacne maŋte ro bârâwiŋ ejactehuc dâŋ i muwec.
Irec dâŋ moc šiŋuc hâcne fokac: “No Jakobore enarewec â Esaure takicnuwec.”
Eme irec weniŋuc muzo? Anutu erao guriŋ bapa hehesicne moc fokac me? I aric kereŋne.
E Mose dâŋ šiŋuc âzâcnewec: “No ŋic moc akickezo murâ akickepemu â ŋic moc buuruc ecnezo murâ ecnepemu.”
Irec ŋicmaŋte me ŋic eebapare mi muzo, Anutu buuruc-ticnere sawa muzo.
Anutuzi Farao dâŋ âzâcnewec, irec miti papiao šiŋuc qâreŋkekicne: “No gorao tâpiri-nane bataniŋkepe šâŋe biŋe-nane mâreŋ sâc raocte muhuc âkendâŋgupo hâcne.”
Eme irec Anuture šiŋuc manazo: E ŋic moc akickezo murâ akickeocmu â moc e maŋne bâzickezo murâ bâzickeocmu.
Eme ŋifecne šiŋuc mecne nazacmu: “Anutu e ŋic nâŋâcne wemocte maname sâqoreekac? E wiac moc ezo mume ŋiczi aka hehecne i mi fokac.”
Ŋic go wemogere Anuture dâŋ mucmu? Kušizi wemocko kuzi bapa šiŋuc âzâcneocmu: “Go wemocte sâc iŋucne bacnumeŋ?”
Me kuši bapa e afe izia kuši gâcne ŋic jaŋere biŋe â gâcne bec qâto jaŋere biŋe bame sâqoreocmu me?
Eme Anutu e kuši kimbeŋ-ticnere biŋe, šâhecko qanšaŋ-joparâ behec-jopaocte maname fokac, kuši i jaŋerao šika bâfuahuc tâpiri-ticne bataniŋkeocte sifu bumâteŋ-ticnere erâ jâbu ejare warehuc juekac.
Erâ ŋifecne kuši buuruc-ticnere biŋe, juku eri tatamac-ticnao biric-jopaocte maname fokac, kuši i jaŋerao eri aŋac mâriri hejareocte bacjopa juekac.
Eme Judaŋic sawa mâcne, qâpuc mâmâc kuši buuruc-ticnere biŋe enaŋte hefârec-nâpoekac.
Eme irec porofete Hoseare papiao dâŋticne šiŋuc fokac: “Ŋicguru mi rucjopapo jaŋe `nore ŋicfâcƷ mucjopapemu, â biŋemâc juwec e šâŋene `joroc-naneƷ mucnepemu.”
“Eme `ŋoŋe nore ŋicfâc aricneƷ ŋazakicne, mâreŋ ira wâc šâŋe-jeŋic `Anutu jujunere naru motecfâcƷ fuaocmu.”
Erâ Jesajazi hahaŋne bahuc Israe ŋic jaŋere šiŋuc muwec wâc: “Israe ɋâricfâcne jaŋe hâwecmecko moŋgeŋ fokac irec sâc bâfuazo murâ bâfuaniŋmu, eme sifu uuc šanšaŋne sawazi biaŋkeniŋmu.”
Wofuŋ e mâreŋko dâŋticnere fârine ɋeŋnea bâfuame fideteŋ efâreocmu.
Jesajazi findaŋdâŋ moc šiŋuc hâcne muwec: “Sambaŋ momori jaŋere Wofuŋ e ŋicukic moc mi getâc-jopa-nâreme muzac, ine Sodom jaŋere sâc bâfuanšapeŋ, â Gomora jaŋe iŋucne enšapeŋ.”
Eme ši weniŋuc muzo? Kecšiŋuc: ŋic qâpuc tiŋke biaŋ eniŋte mi fotariembiŋzi tiŋke biaŋ embiŋ, mamanasiŋte tiŋke biaŋ embiŋ hâcne.
Á Israe ŋic sâcmutâc dâŋ reŋkehuc tiŋke biaŋ eniŋte fotariembiŋzi sâcmutâc dâŋ bâmâmâckembiŋ.
Wemocte? šiŋucte: Jaŋe mamanasiŋte mâcne, mâc juju bapa-jeŋicte tiŋke biaŋ eniŋte mumbiŋ. Ehuc hatao qânâ fowec ira kike-jeŋic hezumbiŋ.
Kecšiŋuc hâcne qâreŋkekicne fokac: “Manakic, no Zioŋ haeo qânâ moc râekopac ira kike-jeŋic hepirickeniŋmu, â buse ŋeŋene moc hekopac ira heariweniŋmu. Eme moczi e manasiŋkeocmu ine mi qurutuaocmu.”
Qomâfâc-nane, Judaŋic âgofâc-nane biaŋkeniŋte maŋnanezi boc enareme Anutu irec numucneekopac.
Jaŋe Anutu kiŋaŋ qacneniŋte šoɋac ehuc jueŋgopieŋ i honeekopaczi mukopac. Erâ i hatane kâuc bahuc eeŋgopieŋ.
Jaŋe Anuturaonec kiŋfâsâc eere hata fokac i kâuc baeŋgopieŋte jaŋac tiŋke biaŋ eniŋte giene baeŋgopieŋ. Irec Anutu tiŋne rune mi dapecnembiŋ.
Ŋiczi mamanasiŋhec erâ kiŋfâsâc bâfuanaŋte Kristozi sâcmutâc dâŋte hata hebâzicke-nârewec.
Mose e dâŋ šiŋuc qâreŋkewec: “Ŋic moc e sâcmutâc dâŋte tiŋke biaŋ hata âteocmuzi juju bâfuaocmu.”
Á mamanasiŋte tiŋke biaŋ eere dâŋ ine kecšiŋuc fokac: “Go maŋgezi šiŋuc mi muzemec: Mozi sambâŋko ferâ Kristo bawahaocmu,
me mozi hârâcko hurâ Kristo hâmokicne jaŋeraonec jowa wefuocmu?”
Iŋuc mâcne, tiri papiao kecšiŋuc mukicne: “Miti i šoricko mi fokac, i mumugao â mamanagao râekicne.” I mamanasiŋte dâŋ ŋaza qazuc eeŋgopeneŋ irec mukicne.
Jesu e Wofuŋ-nane i mumugao foocmu â Anutuzi Jesu hâmockonec bâɋâre-narewec i mamanagao foocmu eme biaŋkerâ jucmu.
Maŋzi Jesu manasiŋkehuc kiŋfâsâc ezo, â miczi e mutaniŋkehuc biaŋkezo.
Eme irec hâcne miti papiao kecšiŋuc qâreŋkekicne: “E manasiŋkeocmuzi mi qurutuaocmu.”
Judaŋic â Grikŋic bârâwiŋ mi eŋgopeneŋ, e mocjahazi Wofuŋ junâre-fâreekac, erâ wiac fuŋne fuŋne hezu henâreekac.
Irec hâcne šiŋuc mukicne: “Wofuŋte šâŋe riwaseckeocmuzi biaŋkerâ juocmu.”
Ririwasecke i e mi manasiŋkeeŋgopieŋzi wemocko eniŋmu? Anutu mamanasiŋke i dâŋticne mi manaeŋgopieŋzi wemocko eniŋmu? Anutu dâŋticne mamana i biŋe mumu tâmiric wemocko eniŋmu?
Á biŋe mumu i moczi jaza sorec mi ejarehame wemocko fuaniŋmu? Dâŋqâreŋ šiŋuc hâcne fokac: “Biŋebiaŋ mumuŋic jaŋere kike fânâŋzi maŋ baafec bâfuaekac.”
Biŋebiaŋ ine ŋic gâcnezi mana rereŋ mi embiŋ. Jesajazi wâc šiŋuc muwec: “Wofuŋ, biŋedâŋ muhaŋnekicne i mozi mana šakiewec?”
Irec šiŋuc manazo: Mamanasiŋ i miti mu manacte fârine, â miti mu manac i Kristore micte fuaekac.
Hâc, eme šiŋuc muhuc wiokopac: Jaŋe miti mi manambiŋ me? Iŋuc mâcne, “Micfânâŋ-jeŋiczi mâreŋ sâcke-fârewec â dâŋjeŋiczi mâreŋ qaŋeŋnao fisiwec.”
Eme mocwâc wiohuc mukopac: Israe ŋic jaŋe mi mecne mana-hâmombiŋ? Iŋuc mâcne, qanaŋ Mosezi šiŋuc qâreŋkewec i mupe: “No ŋic omane rocjopape siric-ŋopapie iiŋguuŋ ejarenšepieŋ; ŋicguru mutucne hefârec-jopape buŋeŋic gâpârezejec.”
Eme šâhec Jesajazi dâŋ bâutuckehuc kecšiŋuc muwec: “Mi basacnuhuc jumbiŋzi bâfuacnumbiŋ, nore mi muhuc jumbiŋ jaŋe maic-jopapo.”
Erâ Israe ŋic jaŋere ine šiŋuc mu qâreŋ ewec: “No ŋicguru mana qâomane â mickobacne dameŋ šora meoric qajarehuc jupo.”
Eme wiokopac: Anutuzi ŋicfâc-ticne behec-jopawec me? Aricne, iŋuc mi ewec. Noni Israe ŋic jaha wâc, Abrahamte ɋâric, Benjamiŋte guruonec
Anutuzi qanaŋ manac-jopawec ŋic i mi behec­ jopawec. Me ŋoŋe Eliare binaŋ miti papiao i wose manac mi eeŋgopieŋ me?
E Israe ŋic jaŋere dâŋ muhuc Anutu šiŋuc âzâcnewec: “Wofuŋ, jaŋe porofetefâcge jopa-fârehuc alatage henšaŋnembiŋ, eme ši buc juhape no wâc nuniŋte muŋgopieŋ.”
Iŋuc mume Anutuzi dâŋ weniŋuc bâtikiecnewec? “No ŋic 7000 sakarec-jopape Baali nemu mi dapecnembiŋ.”
Eme dameŋ ši iŋuc jaha Anutuzi aki anonoc-ticnere erâ ŋic tiwâne rowosâec-jopawec juŋgopieŋ.
I aki anonoc-ticnere iŋuc ejarewecko juju bapa-jeŋicte mi ejarewec. Iŋuc mi eme muzac, ine aki anonoc fârine mi ezac.
Eme weniŋuc? Israe ŋic jaŋe wiac fârine bâfuazo mumbiŋ i mi bâfuambiŋ” rowosâec-jopakicne jaŋe sawa bâfuambiŋ, gâcne sâko ine maŋsanaŋ embiŋ.
Irec šiŋuc hâcne qâreŋkekicne fokac: “Anutu e maŋjeŋic bâsifuckewec, šâŋe-jeŋic bâhâpowec â hazec-jeŋic qâzic qawec. Iŋuc ejareha jumbiŋzi jueŋgopieŋ.”
Á Dawidizi mu qâreŋ ewec: “Jaŋe nânâ nahapie râsi fisipie fâfâc-jopazejec, Mâreŋko jopaha okacne fisi-jarezejec.
Go šâŋe-jeŋic bâhâpotec tiŋtuŋ qanšepieŋ, â râpe-jeŋic bahasicketec miŋgeŋ miŋgeŋ junšepieŋ sanaŋ.”
Eme wiokopac: Israe ŋic jaŋe fâfâc-jopawec i waha qâhâmoc-jopaocte iŋuc fuawec me? Iŋuc aricne, jaŋe bâbâpiaŋ râpeckepie qâpuc jaŋere biŋe ewec, ine qâpuc jaŋe manapie Israe ŋic jaŋe honec-joparâ iiŋguuŋ ejareniŋte iŋuc fuawec.
Eme miti qiqikiŋ-jeŋiczi mâreŋ sâc ŋic jaŋerao miti mâriri bâfuawecko, â dodocke-jeŋiczi ŋic qâpuc jaŋerao miti šâkâŋ bâfuawecko, opoŋ, juku furu jaha maŋjeŋic bârisiepie fârine mo iŋucne fuazokac!
Qâpuckonec opâ ruac ŋoŋe dâŋ ši ŋazape mananiŋ: No qâpuc ŋoŋere aposolo juekopaczi gie-nane baericko bašihuc baekopac,
i soctofafâc-nane âkeriŋ-jopape gâcnezi bâjâpecnuhuc biaŋkeniŋte.
Anutuzi Israe ŋic behec-jopame mâreŋ sâc miti fuawec, izi juku rocjopame mi hâmockonec ɋâɋârezi fuazokac me?
Nânâ hata qaqasune jambuŋkepene nânâ mâmâc sâcke-fâreekac, â jâc gâtânezi furu fome tieŋne iŋuc jaha furu foocmu.
Eme Anutuzi tieŋne gâcne hetâcne behec ehuc irec dodoma tacko oliwa kâteo fuakicne irec tieŋne go râe šuhuc egarewec. Eme oliwa gâtânere ŋiŋic wokemaŋzi gume hesiwiŋ egarehame,
go tieŋne raŋɋane mi mana pitiwac-jopahuc maŋfefe mi ezemec. Iŋuc ezicte šiŋuc manac: Go gâtâ gume hesiwiŋ mi ecnekomec, gâtâzi go egareekac.
Mupe go ŋifecne šiŋuc mecne mucmu: “Anutuzi no hâcne râe šuhuc enareocte tieŋne raŋɋane hetâcne behec ejarewec.”
I mukic mac. Jaŋe miti qiqikiŋ-jeŋicte hetâcne behec ejarekicne â go ine mamanasiŋgere dodomatac-jeŋicko domakomec. Irec go sahacge mi bafehuc rumerâ juzemec.
Anutu e oliwa e jahacne tieŋne mi akickewecko go iŋuc jaha mi akicguocmu.
Irec go buuruc-ticnere mecne â fâro-ticnere mecne mi nikecguzejec. Fâro-ticnere fârine i miti râpeckembiŋ jaŋerao fuawec, â buuruc-ticnere fârine i gorao fuawec. Eme go erao qohotahuc jutec fârine i sâcne fogareocmu. Iŋuc mi etec ine go wâc hetâcne behec egareocmu.
Erâ wâc tieŋne raŋɋane jaŋe maŋsanaŋ-jeŋic beheniŋmuo Anutuzi mocwâc râe šuhuc ejarezo murâ sâcne ejareocmu.
Eme kâteonec oliwa rocgurâ hae oliwa jâcnao râe šuhuc egareweczi hae oliwa e jahacne tieŋfâc mocwâc šuhuc-jopazo murâ mi quŋkeocmu, i onšoŋ jaha šuhuc-jopaocmu.
Âgofâc-nane, ŋoŋe, kâuc bahuc ŋaŋacne mamanao roweckerâ mana sifuckenšipiŋte dâŋ soŋne ši mufua-ŋarepe. Israe ŋic tucne jaŋe maŋsanaŋ erâ juhapie qâpuc sâko jaŋe mitire maŋko rašiniŋmu.
Rašihapie šâhec Israe ŋicguru qâqâhâc biaŋke-fâreniŋmu. Ʒiŋuc hâcne qâreŋkekicne fokac: “Zioŋ haeonec Bâbâpiaŋ moc fuarâ Jakoborao jawa âsu gârec ofaŋneme raocmu.
Iŋuc eme no sâqocne-jeŋic šurerâ jaŋehec mocwâc šâšâfic epemu.”
Israe ŋic jaŋe qâpuc ŋoŋere erâ Biŋebiaŋte râsi juŋgopieŋ â rowosâec-jopakicnere ine mimiŋnefâc-jeŋic jaŋere erâ Anuture jorocfâc juŋgopieŋ.
Anutu e âgo šâšâfic dâŋsaric-ticne â hehefâre dâŋticne mi dockeocmu.
Qâpuc ŋoŋe mârâc jaha maŋsanaŋ erâ jumbiŋ, eme šâhec Israe ŋic jaŋe maŋsanaŋ ehapie Anutuzi buuruc-ticnao râec-ŋopawec.
Iŋuc jaha jaŋe maŋsanaŋ juhapie Anutuzi buuruc-ticnao ŋec-ŋopawec, i jaŋe wâc buuruc ejareocte iŋuc ewec.
Anutu e ŋic sasawa bâturec-jopahuc qaqatarao basanaŋ-jopawec, i mâmâc sasawa buuruc-ticnao ŋec-jopaocte iŋuc ewec.
Opoŋ, Anutu e mitire mâriri â maŋɋârâŋ â mamana saric-ticne irec šâkâŋne mo iŋucne fokac¡ Mumutara-ticnere fuŋne i ŋiczi mi mamanane gie bapa-ticnere hata i ŋiczi mi hohonene.
“Wofuŋte maŋko dâŋ fokac i mo ŋiczi manawec, me dâŋ muhame mozi bafickerâ muwec?”
“Me mo ŋiczi e qanaŋ wiac moc qikiŋnecnewecko tofane bazucneocmu?”
Wiac sasawa eraonec wareekac â erao siŋkerâ foekac â erao rafâreekac. Mumuteŋzi mumuteŋ i erao šuhuckeme šuhuc forašihuc juzejec sanaŋ. Jâmbomac.
Âgofâc-nane, no Anutu buuruc-ticnere erâ dâŋ hazec qâuŋ ŋazape mananiŋ. Ŋoŋe sahac-ŋeŋic Anutu qikiŋnecnepie taha bâzi ɋaɋacne â tirine eme honeme biaŋkezejec. Iŋuc ehuc Anutu kiŋaŋ fârine qacnenšepieŋ.
Erâ juju bapa-ŋeŋiczi miti tâmiric jaŋere sâc mi ezejec. Ŋoŋe maŋ mamanasu-ŋeŋic bâtikiepie hawarine moc eme Anutu micdâŋ-ticnere sâcko gie biaŋne â hohone šiziwene â tirine irec wosâenšepieŋ.
Aki anonoc tahacnukicnere mâmâc sasawa ŋazape mananiŋ: Moc e jahacnere maname fefene boc mi ezejec, Anutuzi miti râcnewec sâc i sawa ezejec, sâc jâuruhuc ine mi ezejec.
Ʒiŋuc mananiŋ: Fâri ombâŋ-nâŋec mocjaha e kiŋaŋ qaqafâc-ticne bocjahazi gie fuŋne fuŋne baeŋgopieŋ.
Eme ŋifec Kristorao iŋuc jaha bocjahazi qâfâsâepene fâri ombâŋ mocjaha ekac, erâ me kikefâcne juhuc dodopec eeŋgopeneŋ.
Mitire tâpire fuŋne fuŋne i aki anonoc nâre tahac ekicne sâc fonâre rakac. Eme irec sâcko gie banšepeneŋ. Irec moc e Anuture micdâŋ mumufuare tâpiri focnekacko mamanasiŋ-ticnere sâcko muzejec.
Moc e kiŋaŋ qaqa giere tâpiri focnekaczi gie i bazejec, â moc e qaqazu gie baocmu e irec tâpiri focnekac sâc bazejec.
Uŋsawaŋ dâŋ muekac e irec tâpiri focnekacko muzejec, bâmec gie baekac e maŋticne bawahahuc bazejec, moc e micne juocte mucnekicko šoɋachec juzejec, â moc e jauŋ gie baocmuzi buafec jaha bazajec.
Jauŋ babac i sahaczi sawa mi enšepieŋ. Wiac sâqocnere mamakâc-ŋopazejec â wiac biaŋnao qohotanšepieŋ.
Ŋoŋe ââgo fârine junšepieŋ, erâ sâsâsec eniŋte sisiric efârenšepieŋ.
