Nâŋe Anuture gieŋic jueŋgopeneŋ irec fuŋne bataniŋkehuc wiac šiŋuc eraeŋgopeneŋ: Ʒâicmaŋko maŋuruc jueŋgopeneŋ, šârâ hâriŋ faio jueŋgopeneŋ, fific guguriŋ faio jueŋgopeneŋ, hâhâwic maŋko jueŋgopeneŋ,
šika faio jueŋgopeneŋ, kâpâcwâru ficko ŋeeŋgopeneŋ, râsi ŋondeŋko jueŋgopeneŋ, giere šâic manaeŋgopeneŋ, guŋɋâri jueŋgopeneŋ, nânâ tâmiricko jueŋgopeneŋ,
bahac fâsâc jueŋgopeneŋ, mamana tarahec jueŋgopeneŋ, bumâteŋ jueŋgopeneŋ, âgo jauŋ ejareeŋgopeneŋ, Tiri Mârohec jueŋgopeneŋ, maŋjauŋ fârihec jueŋgopeneŋ,
dâŋ fâri qizecne mueŋgopeneŋ, Anuture tâpirio jueŋgopeneŋ, mitire sându marohec jueŋgopeneŋ,
mumumbiaŋ â mimi qaqa ŋoŋondeŋko jueŋgopeneŋ, mu bâsâoc â mufec muriŋ ŋoŋondeŋko jueŋgopeneŋ, burecŋic munârehapie siocmâc jueŋgopeneŋ,
fuŋne-nâŋec basahapie biŋe rarahec jueŋgopeneŋ, hâmozo eeŋgopeneŋzi sifu ɋâricne jueŋgopeneŋ, nâpo sipiric ekicnezi sifu mi omaeeŋgopeneŋ,
busâqoc enârekicnezi sifu bubiaŋko jueŋgopeneŋ. hapetaczi sifu ŋic bocjaha bâmec bajareeŋgopeneŋ, wiac babasanezi sifu mâriri sâkohec jueŋgopeneŋ.
O Korinti ŋicbureŋ, maŋnâŋec ŋoŋerea kâcɋene domame micnâŋec afeckekac hâcne.
Maŋzi sanaŋnea šâfic-ŋopaŋgopeneŋ, ŋoŋere maŋjauŋ ine afecne mac fokac.
Eme no naru motecfâc-nane ŋoŋe ŋazape: Ŋoŋe okacne bazuhuc iŋuc jaha maŋŋeŋic nâŋere râepie kâcɋenea domazejec.
Ŋic qâpuc jaŋe jâcjeŋic reŋkepie ŋoŋe mi bafic-jopanšepieŋ. Tiŋne â hehesic jahe wemocko ââgo enicmu? Me tatamac â dapâc jahe wemocko šâšâfic enicmu?
Me Kristo â râsi qizec-ticne jahe wemocko maŋ mocjaha enicmu? Me opâ ruac â qâpuc jaŋe wemocko qâfâsâeniŋmu?
Me Anuture ufuŋ â nemuɋâŋ jahe wemocko šušuhuc enicmu? Manaŋgopieŋ, Anutu jujunere ufuŋ i nâŋâc. Anutuzi šiŋuc hâcne muwec: “No ŋondeŋ-jeŋicko ŋeŋe juju epemu, ehuc Anutu-jeŋic ehape jaŋe ŋicfâc-nane junšepieŋ.
Irec qâpuc behec-joparâ bâtâcko junšepieŋ, Wofuŋzi iŋuc mukac. Erâ wiac mamakâcne ba bâuac mi enšepieŋ, eme noni hezu hewâneŋ eŋarepemu.
Erâ mamac eŋarehape naru motecfâc-nane erâ junšepieŋ. Wofuŋ bapa-fâre e dâŋ iŋuc mukac.”
Âgo bureŋ, wiac iŋucnere biŋe qanârekicnere wiac mamakâcnezi maŋ sahac-nâŋec hegâpâreekac i šure ɋaɋackenšepeneŋ. Erâ Anutu araŋ bacnehuc maŋɋaɋac jaha junšepeneŋ.
Ŋoŋe maŋŋeŋic mi sakare-nârenšepieŋ. Nâŋe ŋoŋerao wiac hehesic mi embeŋ, me wiac-ŋeŋic ima mi qambeŋ, me wiac-ŋeŋic moc kâŋgâc mi rombeŋ.
No dâŋ i musâqorec-ŋopahuc mi mukopac. No miŋecne mac ŋazapac, maŋnâŋeczi šâfic-ŋopaŋgopeneŋ, i ŋoŋehec mâmâc hâmonaŋte me junaŋte.
Maŋnanezi ŋoŋerao siŋkeha wemo afecne muafec-ŋopakopac, no bunane boc bâmiriŋkekicne, šâic busâqocko šeri kâcɋene fua-narekac.
Makedonia mâreŋko ware fisirâ wemocko âke uruerâ junšapeŋ. Ʒira sahacte biŋe šika â maŋte biŋe hâhâwic, wiac izi fuarâ sisi hâhâŋ enâreha jumbeŋ.
Bebekâne bâmiriŋ-jopaekac Anutu eki hâcne ine nâŋere bâbâmiriŋte Tito ecneme risiewec.
Erâ risiewec irec sawa mâcne, ŋoŋe bubiaŋ dâŋ âzâcnembiŋ, i bafisime manarâ bunâŋec uruewec. Erâ no woricnuhuc jueŋgopieŋ â ki busâqochec jueŋgopieŋ â nore erâ gie-ŋeŋic dopeckehuc šoɋac eeŋgopieŋ, i nâzâme bubiaŋ fekicne manapo.
No mârâc papia moc qâreŋke-ŋarehuc maŋšâic bâfua-ŋarepo, irec bunane mi sâqorekac. Qâreŋkepo ira jâmbomac bunane sâqorewec. Ʒi ine manakopac, i dameŋ bembeŋne sawa maŋšâic bâfua-ŋarewec.
Eme ši bubiaŋ manakopac, ine bušâic manambiŋ irec mâcne, bušâiczi ŋoŋerao maŋ bâbârisie bâfuawec, irec bunane biaŋkekac. Anutu mamana-ticnere sâcko bušâic ɋaɋacne manambiŋte dâŋnâŋeczi mi bâsâqorec-ŋopawec.
Bušâic ɋaɋacne izi maŋ bâbârisie bâfuame ŋiczi biaŋkezo, eme bušâic iŋucne bâfuaocmuzi šâhec irec mi maname sâqoreocmu. Á bušâic gâpâcne, ŋic mamanare sâcko fuaekac, izi ine maŋmutuc bâfuame sipirickezo.
Honeniŋ me, bušâic ɋaɋacnezi ŋoŋerao fârine wemo afecne bâfuawec: Fâro, fuŋne babataniŋ, sâqocne bâbâsue, hâhâwic, mu hejâpec, šoɋac, bâbâtiŋ, wiac iŋuc hâcne bâfuawec. Eme sâqocnere hehesoŋ â ŋeŋezic ŋoŋerao mi fokac, irec fuŋne taniŋkewec.
Mârâc papia qâreŋke-ŋarepo, i ŋic sâqocne bawec ere erâ mâcne, me sâqocne bajarewec jaŋere erâ wâc mâcne, dâŋ ŋazapene Anuture maio micrereŋ-ŋeŋicte fuŋne taniŋkeocte irec qâreŋke-ŋarepo. Eme ŋoŋe iŋuc hâcne ehuc bunâŋec bâmiriŋkembiŋ.
Erâ bunâŋec bâmiriŋkembiŋ sawa mâcne, ŋoŋe Tito bubiaŋ qacnepie risieme nâŋe wemo afecne mana biaŋ embeŋ.
No mârâc jaha muafec-ŋopahuc Tito âzâcnepo, dâŋ i burec mi ewec. Ŋoŋe dâŋ ŋazape fârinehec efârewec, iŋuc jaha Tito ŋoŋere mumumbiaŋ dâŋ âzâcnepo i wâc fârinehec jaha ewec.
Tito ŋoŋerao fâme araŋ bacnehuc micne reŋkembiŋ, e irec manasuhuc maŋne ŋoŋere boc ecneekac.
No ŋoŋere erâ maŋbahac tâmiric sâcne jupemu, irec bunane biaŋkekac.
Âgo bureŋ, Makedonia mâreŋkonec kikefuŋ jaŋerao Anuture jauŋ fuawec irec ŋazanaŋ.
Jaŋe šârâ hâriŋ sâkoo juhuc bahac qahameŋ erâ tac qararacne jueŋgopieŋ, ehame sifu mitire šeri fekicne fojareekacte bubiaŋ wiac ɋâfoŋne bâmockembiŋ.
No jaŋere mana-jâmbâŋkekopac, jaŋe jaŋacne maŋte afeckerâ tâpiri-jeŋicte sâc, erâ wâc sâc i jâuruhuc râembiŋ.
Nâŋe mi ejarehapene jaŋe jaŋac hota-nârehuc mitiŋic jaŋere bubiaŋ wiac bâfuarâ bafic-nâponiŋte mumbiŋ.
Erâ wiac afecne eniŋmu muhapene šiŋuc embiŋ: Qanaŋ maŋjeŋic Wofuŋ qikiŋnecnerâ nâŋe mâmâc Anuture erâ qikiŋne-nârembiŋ.
Jaŋe iŋuc embiŋte Titozi ŋoŋerao bubiaŋ gie barâ tofane râewec i bataraocte mucneŋgopeneŋ.
Eme mamanasiŋ â miti mumu â miti fuŋne mamana tara â giere šoɋac â maŋjauŋ eenare, wiac iŋucnere fârine bocjaha bâfuambiŋte bubiaŋ gie mukicne irec iŋuc jaha afeckenšepieŋ.
No hotâ-ŋarehuc mi mukopac, miti mamana gâcne jaŋerao aafec fuawec, eme ŋoŋere maŋjauŋ sâc weniŋucne fokac irec fuŋne taniŋkeocte mukopac.
Ŋoŋe Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristo uruc jauŋ-ticnere manaeŋgopieŋ, e mâriri sâkoheczi ŋoŋere erâ hapetac ewec, i ŋoŋe hapetac-ticnere erâ mâririhec eniŋte iŋuc hâcne ewec.
Eme ši dâŋ mâc ŋazakopac i reŋkepie fârinehec ezejec. Ŋoŋe hâcne jara raŋɋanao biac moneŋ bâtureniŋte afeckerâ fuŋkembiŋ.
Eme i šuhuckerâ etarapie aafec-ŋeŋicte fârine, wiac foŋarekac sâc fuazejec.
Wiac buafecte rârâe irec mamana biaŋ fuaocmu, rârâe ine moc e focnekac irec sâc râezejec, mi focnekac irec sâc mâcne.
Bubiaŋte wiac rârâere mukicne i jaŋe sahac mâteŋ juhapie ŋoŋe šocne šâicne mananiŋte mâcne,
ŋoŋere mafa mâririzi dameŋ šiŋuczia jaŋere roroc jâpeme wiac sâckoa fuaocte mukicne, eme juku dameŋ mocko jaŋere mâririzi ŋoŋere roroc jâpeme iŋuc jaha sâckoa fua-ŋarezejec.
Dâŋqâreŋ šiŋuc hâcne fokac: “Bocjaha nusembiŋzi mâririhec mi embiŋ, â afecne nusembiŋzi roroc mi embiŋ.”
Anutu e Tito esockeme, maŋnâŋezi ŋoŋere erâ bâruŋkekac sâc ijaha erao fuakacte muteŋkenaŋ.
Nâŋe mucnepene manawec sawa mâcne, e jahac maŋticnere afecke-jâmbâŋkerâ fâzo ekac.
Opâ ruac âgo-nâŋec moc, kikefuŋ sasawa jaŋe Biŋebiaŋte gie bapa-ticnere mana biaŋ eeŋgopieŋ, e mâmâc sorepene fâkopirec.
Kikefuŋ jaŋe ŋic e hâcne bubiaŋ moneŋ rorore bafic-nâpoocte bâwosâembiŋ. Gie i Wofuŋ sâsehuc buafec-nâŋecte baŋgopeneŋ.
Mumusifuc fuazacte moneŋ sâko i šâŋe šereŋko sosoŋaŋ ehuc ro qâzuc eeŋgopeneŋ.
Nâŋe wiac epene Wofuŋzia maname biaŋkeocte mâcne, ŋiczi mâmâc manapie sâckeocte mueŋgopeneŋ.
Nâŋe jahehec âgo-nâŋec moc mâmâc sorec-jopapene fâŋgopieŋ, ŋic e dameŋ gâcnao esâicke honepene šoɋac-ticnere fuŋne taniŋkewec, ši ine ŋoŋere bubiaŋ manahuc šoɋac fekicne bâfuakac.
Ŋoŋe Titore manaeŋgopieŋ, e âgo babafic-nane, mâmâc gie bapa ŋicjahec-ŋeŋic jukoperec, â âgo jahec-nâŋec jahere wâc manaŋgopieŋ, jahe kikefuŋ jaŋe sorec-jofaŋgopieŋ, erâ jahe Kristore šuŋe gâpiŋ hâcne.
Nâŋe ŋoŋe muafec-ŋopaeŋgopeneŋ irec dâŋ i fârinehec eocte ŋic iŋucnezi fâpie âgo jauŋ ejarepie kikefuŋ gâcne jaŋe mananšepieŋ.
Mitiŋic ehâmo-jarehuc moneŋ jareniŋte i sâcne manaŋgopieŋ, irec wemocte boc qâreŋke-ŋarepemu.
Akaia opâ ruac ŋoŋe jara raŋɋanao biac afeckerâ moneŋ bâbâfua fuŋkembiŋ, irec binaŋ Makedonia ŋic bajarepe ŋic gâcne sâko jaŋe šoɋac-ŋeŋicte biŋe manarâ bujeŋic âeckewec.
No muafec-ŋopapo i racne ezacte âgofâc-nane sorec-jopape fâpie mupo iŋuc hâcne erâ šawienšepieŋ.
No nahac šâhec Makedonia ŋic jaŋehec fâpe moneŋ rârâere bititiepie dâŋnane wawahane eme no â ŋoŋe mâmâc mimienšipeŋ.
Irec hâcne ŋic ejarepe bânierâ fâŋgopieŋ. Fâ fisipie bubiaŋ moneŋ râeniŋte nazambiŋ i qanaŋ râe bâmoc epie ŋezejec. Eme micneneŋte moneŋ mâcne, mitire bubiaŋte moneŋ ezejec.
Erâ ine šiŋuc mukopac: Moc e wiac afecne he sarac eocmu, e wiac afecnea nâ roroc eocmu, â moc e wiac ŋemâcne he sarac eocmu e wiac ŋemâcnea nâ roroc eocmu.
Irec šiŋuc efârezo: Moc e buafec-ticnere sâcko wiac-ticne qikiŋnezejec, jâiŋko me micneneŋte misac. Wiac buafec qikiŋneocmu, ŋic iŋucnere Anutuzi maname biaŋkeocmu.
Anutu e tâpiri runezi buafec-ticnere jambuŋ-ŋopame mâriri fua-ŋareme ŋaŋacne nâ bac eipiehuc bâmec gie fuŋne fuŋne baniŋte wiac mi basaniŋmu.
Dâŋqâreŋ šiŋuc hâcne fokac: “E kada bahuc ŋic hapetac bâmec bajareekac, â buafec-ticne i tofamâc fohuc juocmu.”
Ŋic ukicne bâfua-jareme he sarac eeŋgopieŋ â fârine bâfua-jareme nâ bac eeŋgopieŋ, Anutu e hâcne ŋoŋe wâc he sarac eniŋte ukicne bâfua-ŋarerâ jambuŋkeme buafec-ŋeŋicte fârine fua sawec eocmu.
Eme mâriri sâkohec erâ ŋic bâmec fuŋne fuŋne bajarepie jaŋe nâŋâcnere erâ Anutu daŋge mumuteŋ ecneniŋmu.
Ŋoŋe mitiŋic bubiaŋ wiac ejarepie izi roroc-jeŋic jâpeocmu sawa mâcne, izi daŋge mumuteŋ irec mâriri wâc bâfuame Anuturao qacneocmu.
Ŋoŋe Kristore Biŋebiaŋ mana rereŋ eeŋgopieŋ irec fuŋne bubiaŋ wiac-ŋeŋiczi bataniŋkeme Jerusalem haeonec mitiŋic â opâ ruac gâcne sasawa jaŋehec ââgo šušuhuc-ŋeŋic fuame Anutu mumbiaŋkeniŋmu.
Erâ ŋoŋerao Anutu miti-ticnere fârine fua sawec ekacte maŋzi šâfic-ŋopahuc ŋoŋere erâ Anutu numucneniŋmu.
Anutu buafec-ticne i wemocko sâcne mutaniŋkezo, irec mâc wareckehuc daŋge âzâcnenaŋ.
Ʒi Paulo noni Kristo bumâteŋ-ticnere â uruc-ticnere erâ ŋazape mananiŋ. Gâcnezi nore mueŋgopieŋ, “Ʒira ware juhuc miriŋdâŋ enâreekac, â ocna ra juhuc momori dâŋ enâreekac.”
Âgofâc, ŋoŋerao fâ juhuc momori dâŋ ŋazapemurâ irec mi qafeŋnunšepieŋ. Gâcnezi “sahacte wiacko utuckerâ juekac”, nore iŋuc mueŋgopieŋ, ŋic i jaŋe momori dâŋ jazapemurâ maŋnane afeckekac.
Wiac nâŋe sahachec juju i jâmbomac jueŋgopeneŋ, â momori juju ine sahacte hata fokac iŋucko mi jueŋgopeneŋ.
Sându maro bajuhuc juju gie baeŋgopeneŋ, i mâreŋkonec mâcne, i Anuture tâpiri sanaŋhec. Eme izi râsire sac bazueŋgopeneŋ, â qac momori-ticne qapene wahaekac,
â hârâc huec Anuture dâŋ sirickeekac i qa imac eeŋgopeneŋ, erâ Kristore micrereŋ sawa fuaocte mamana fuŋne fuŋne kâpâcwâru baeŋgopeneŋ.
Ŋoŋe micrereŋte afecke-fârehapie nâŋe ŋic gâcne jaŋe qaqatara-jeŋicte bâtiŋ-jopazore woŋec juŋgopeneŋ.
Wiac moc ši tâtâc fokac i honeniŋ: Ŋoŋe wemocte sahackopec wiac omanere manapie fârine eekac? Ŋoŋeraonec ŋic moczi e jahacnere maname Kristore ŋic fârine eekacko šiŋuc manazejec: E buc Kristore ŋic mi juekac, nâŋe wâc Kristore ŋicfâc jaha jueŋgopeneŋ.
Erâ Wofuŋzi giere tâpiri râe-narewec, ŋoŋe âkesiŋ-ŋopapere, sipiric-ŋopapere mâcne, no irec erâ ropaŋdâŋ piticne murašihuc mupe boc mi sâqore-nareocmu.
Á papia qâreŋke-ŋareekopac irec manapie mu hâhâwic dâŋ mi ezejec.
Ʒiŋuc hâcne munareeŋgopieŋ: “Papiao dâŋ bipinehec â tâpirinehec qâreŋkeekac, sahaczi maic-nâpoekac ine weweaŋne, â dâŋ mumu-ticne ine wawahane.”
Ŋic iŋucne jaŋe šiŋuc mananšepieŋ: Nâŋe šoricko juhuc dâŋ qâreŋkeeŋgopeneŋ, dâŋ irec fârine ŋondeŋ-ŋeŋicko juhuc bâfuaeŋgopeneŋ.
Ŋic sahac fefe jueŋgopieŋ jaŋerao nâŋe iŋucnezi wemocko šuhuckerâ sâc babac enaŋmu. Ŋic i jaŋe hâcne gâcne nâŋere eebapa irec mi manasuhuc jaŋacnere sawa muhuc sahac fefe dâŋ kosa woseeŋgopieŋ.
Nâŋe ine Anutuzi giere sâc banârewec iŋuc bafâku ŋoŋerao fisimbeŋ, irec mac manasuhuc mumuafec dâŋ mueŋgopeneŋ, â sâc tâmiricko kosa mumu ine mi eeŋgopeneŋ.
Nâŋe gie-nâŋecte sâc i mi musokaeŋgopeneŋ, gie rukec-nâŋec i jâmbomac ŋoŋerao fokac, nâŋe hâcne bâbâni ŋoŋerao fisirâ Kristore Biŋebiaŋ qanaŋ ŋazambeŋ.
Nâŋe ŋic gâcne jaŋere gieo kâŋgâc raši domahuc sahac fefe dâŋ kosa mumu i mi eeŋgopeneŋ. Mamanasiŋzi ŋoŋerao fua sawec eme gie rukec-nâŋec bâsokanaŋte ine jâmbomac maŋnâŋec domaha jueŋgopeneŋ.
Eme ŋic râpe-ŋeŋicko juŋgopieŋ jaŋerao Biŋebiaŋ muranaŋmu. Á ŋic mocte gie fârine rauckehuc pepec dâŋ mumu i mi eeŋgopeneŋ.
Moc e mumuteŋ dâŋ muzo murâ Wofuŋte erâ muzejec.
Moc e jahacne sahac mumbiaŋkeme e miti fârihec ekac mi mucnezo, Wofuŋzi mumbiaŋkeme miti fârihec ekac muzo.
Ŋoŋe manahapie mutucdâŋ piticne ŋazape. Sifu mac mananšepieŋ.
No ŋoŋere erâ qizec qaekopac, erâ qizec qaqa dâŋnane i Anuturaonec. Noni ŋoŋe Kristore biŋefâc erâ pectâc juniŋte ŋic mocjaha ehec bâturec-ŋopapo.
Ʒi ine homazi Ewa sioc ecnehuc bâdockewec iŋuc jaha ŋoŋe ŋic gâcnezi eatuc-ŋopapie maŋŋeŋic fâuckeme Kristo râŋgeŋ rocnenšipiŋte manabâc ekopac.
Ŋoŋerao ŋic moczi fisirâ Jesure fuŋne nâŋe ŋazaeŋgopeneŋ ijaha mâcne, hawarine moc ŋazaocmu, â Mâro nâŋeraonec rombiŋ i mâcne, furune moc ŋareocmu, â Biŋebiaŋ nâŋeraonec manambiŋ i mâcne, maracne moc ŋazaocmu, i ŋoŋe mi qatarahuc mâc manapie sâckeekac.
No nahacnere manape norao wiac i me i basahuc aposolo fekicne sâko jaŋere jujuwicnao jukopac mi eekac.
No miti muminširiŋkerâ mumu i mi mecne fonarekac, â mitire fuŋne mamana ine manaekopac, erâ irec fuŋne baratie-fârehuc mâmâc-ŋeŋic bataniŋke-ŋarepo.
Me nahac wahamicne juhuc ŋoŋe ikisiŋ-ŋopahuc Anuture Biŋebiaŋ katucmâc ŋazapo i sâqorewec me?
Ŋoŋerao miti gie bapemurâ kikefuŋ gâcne jaŋe jâmbomac moneŋ mafa jowac ropo.
Ŋoŋerao ine wiac basac bahameŋ juhuc mubâre mi eŋarepo. No batac qatac juhape Makedonia mâreŋkonec âgofâc-nane fisirâ wiac nare gumec embiŋ. Á ŋoŋerao ine mâc juhape nore šâic mi manambiŋ â jufehuc wâc mi mananiŋte mukopac
Kristore dâŋfâri maŋnaneo foha mukopac: šeridâŋ inane Akaia mâreŋko moc mi bawaha-narezo.
Muŋgopieŋ,ŋoŋere mi enarehame iŋuc eekopac? Iŋuc aricne,i Anutuzi manakac.
Wiac eekopac i ehuc jupemu, erâ i mâc mâcne, ŋic gâcne jaŋe Paulore sâcko juŋgopeneŋ muhuc maŋjeŋic bafenšipiŋte siŋ qatara-jareekopac
Ŋic iŋucnezi aposolo burecne â miti gie bapa siochec juhuc Kristore aposolofâc nâŋere sahac hawari sawa eeŋgopieŋ.
Erâ i wiac furune mi eeŋgopieŋ, Sataŋ e jahacne wâc aŋelo tatamachec jaŋere hawari tinac eekac,
eme irec gie bapa ŋicfâc-ticne jaŋe iŋuc jaha tiŋnere kiŋaŋ qaqa jaŋere hawari rojueŋgopieŋ.
Mupac i mocwâc mupe, nore manapie ŋic mutucne mi ezejec. Erâ sifu muzo murâ muniŋ, ehuc mana-narehapie sahac-nane piticne muteŋkepe
No ši dâŋ mupemu i Wofuŋte micsâcko mi mupemu, mâc mumuteŋ dâŋ fuŋkekicnere sifu mutuc erâ mupemu.
Ŋic gâcnezi sahackopec wiacte mumumbiaŋ dâŋ mueŋgopieŋte no iŋuc jaha epemu.
Oi, fuŋne mamana ŋoŋe, gâcnezi mutucdâŋ ŋazapie manapie sâckeekac hâcne.
Á kiŋaŋ qaqafâc-jeŋic bacŋopapie iŋuc jaha manapie sâckeekac, â ŋowac ro nâc eŋareniŋmu me eatuc-ŋopaniŋmu me ŋicbomboŋ eŋareniŋmu me imac-ŋopaniŋmu, i ŋoŋe manapie sâcke-fâreocmu hâcne.
Nâŋe gegec dodocnezi iŋuc sâko wemocko eŋarenšapeŋ, i mana sâqorehuc mukopac. Moc e wiac irec me irec penaroŋ eocmu, i no ezo murâ sâcne epemu. Dâŋ i mutucne, i mana-bipiehuc mukopac.
Jaŋacnere Judaŋic mueŋgopieŋ, no wâc ijaha. Jaŋacnere Israe ŋic mueŋgopieŋ, no wâc ijaha. Jaŋacnere Abrahamte ɋâric mueŋgopieŋ, no wâc ijaha.
Jaŋacnere Kristore gieŋic mueŋgopieŋ, no ši sifu maŋmutuc dâŋ mupe, no Kristore gieŋic sâc moc. No giere šâic manaekopac i sâc moc, â kâpâcwâru ficko feekopac i sâc moc, â šika kiekopac i sâc moc, â sipirickezo eekopac i sâc moc.
Judaŋic jaŋe dameŋ memoc repazi 39 numbiŋ,
dameŋ jahec â moc kâcbiŋzi nukicne, moc i qânâzi hehâmocnumbiŋ, dameŋ jahec â moc woke hericke fâuc eme hâwecko hurâ hu epo, ŋafe šoaŋ moc woke sâqoreme hâwecko qac qâsoriehuc jupo.
Erâ sopâc kâte hârâc tiki fotâcne qâqâwiric bazu bâfeŋ ehuc jupo, opâ rumio šârâ šâpâ faio fehuc jupo, râsi ŋondeŋko šârâ šâpâ faio fepo, Judaŋic ŋondeŋko šârâ šâpâ faio fepo, qâpuc ŋondeŋko šârâ šâpâ faio fepo, ŋic jujuo šârâ šâpâ faio fepo, tuhuo šârâ šâpâ faio fepo, hâwecko šârâ šâpâ faio fepo, mitiŋic burecne jaŋere ŋondeŋko šârâ šâpâ faio fepo.
Iŋuczi iŋuc ehuc hume serereŋ â huacbuc qâbucne juwarepo, ehuc ŋafeo guŋɋâri juju,nânâ opâre hâhâmo, hoe mâmâteŋte ɋarac ɋarac qaqa, ŋaqi bilaŋke babasa, iŋuc ehuc juekopac.
Erâ i sawa mâcne, šoaŋne šoaŋne kiŋaŋ fisihuc fâro âkefec enarepie hae sâc kikefuŋ jaŋere mana mezac ehuc juekopac.
Wemocko hae moczi qau bititicne juhapie âke uruerâ sâcne jupemu? Wemocko hae moczi qâsoriehapie sâcne ŋemâteŋkepemu?
Eme no irec wemo-nane musokapemu? Gegec dodoc-nane mocjaha musokape sâckeocmu.
Wofuŋ Jesu ere Anutu â Mamac, e mumuteŋ hatizi dâŋ jâmbomac mukopac i manakac.
Damasko haeo juhape ŋicwofuŋ Areta ere kiazi kâpâcwâru bacnuocte hae upeo somâ râewec.
Eme irec âgofâc-nane jaŋe kâdocko ŋihecnurâ sacrâpeo âke suecnupie hurâ wisepo.
Mumuteŋ dâŋ mupene mi sâckeekac, erâ sifu mupe. Ehuc Wofuŋzi maŋko fuac â maŋbâwiŋ enarewec, irec dâŋ binaŋ epe.
No Kristore ŋic moc manakopac e wiac moc honerâ jukuhame jara 14 ekac. Ŋic e hâcne Wofuŋzi maŋbâwiŋ ecneme sambâŋ namba 3 ira fewec. I sahachec me sahac tâmiric ewec, i no mi manakopac,Anutuzia manakac.
Eme ŋic e Wofuŋzi maŋbâwiŋ ecneme paradisio hâcne ferâ dâŋ miczi mi mumune â mâreŋŋiczi mi mumufuane i manawec.
No ŋic e manakopac, â sahachec juhuc me sahac hetarahuc ewec, i no mi manakopac, Anutuzia manakac.
Ŋic ere erâ mumuteŋ dâŋ mupemu, nahacnere mi mupemu, ine muzo murâ gegec dodoc-nane sawa musokapemu.
Mumuteŋ dâŋ mupe muzac, i jâmbomac dâŋ muzapore ŋic mutucne mi ezapo. Erâ nore manapie fefene boc ezacte ine mi epemu, wiac mupe bape ŋaŋac hone manac eeŋgopieŋ izia fozejec.
Wofuŋzi wiac šâŋe hazec furu nowatuwec, irec maŋnane fezacte sahac biuc-naneo šârâ moc duckewec, i Sataŋte kiŋaŋŋic moc e maŋnanezi boc fezacte mehuhuŋzi hecnuhuc juocte mukicne.
Eme behecnuocte Wofuŋ wâsickekuhape jahec â moc ewec.
Eme dâŋ šiŋuc nazawec: “Jauŋ-nanezi sâcguekac â tâpiri-nanezi dodoc rorokacko fua ɋârâŋkeekac.” Irec Kristore tâpirizi norao mâckeocte dodoc rorokac-nanere manape feha mumbiaŋkezepac.
Eme Kristore erâ dodoc rorokac epemu me šika kipemu, me hume serereŋ jupemu, me fific guguriŋ â imaŋ gomaŋ faio jupemu, i sifu bubiaŋ manaekopac. No dodoc rorokacko sanaŋkeekopac hâcne.
Ʒi mutucdâŋ mupac, i ŋoŋe enarepie mupac. Ŋaŋac mumbiaŋnupie sâckezac. No jawa omane juekopac i manakopac, erâ aposolo fekicne jaŋere wahamicne juju ine mi juekopac.
No ŋoŋerao gie maŋuruc jaha bape mâsi â wiac šâŋe furu â wiac tâpirihec fuahuc izi aposolo fuŋne-nane bataniŋkewec.
Eme ŋoŋe wemo basahuc kikefuŋ gâcne jaŋere sâc mi embiŋ? Mâc wiac ŋowac ro nâc ee i mocjaha mi eŋarepo. Hehesic-nane i mi mana sâqore-narenšepieŋ.
No jajahec iqic-ŋopapo, eme ši mocwâc fâpere šawiehuc jukopac. Fârâ mârâc epo ijaha ehuc sahacte dopere mi bâšâic-ŋopapemu. No moneŋ mafa-ŋeŋicte mâcne, ŋaŋacnere harac eekopac. Naru moteczi neŋgoc mamac wiac hure-jareniŋte mi mukicne, neŋgoc mamaczi naru motec hure-jareniŋmu ine sâckeocmu.
No ine maŋ qâqâtâc-ŋeŋic biaŋkeocte moneŋ mafa sawa mâcne, juju-nane wâc qaisockezo afeckekopac. Nore maŋzi ŋoŋere kâcɋene domaha ŋoŋerezi nore piticne domaoc me?
Ŋic gâcnezi nore šiŋuc mueŋgopieŋ: Wiac tâtâc nânâwoc ro i mi ewec. Á soŋsoŋko ŋic eatuc-jopahuc wiac jojowac ro i ewec mecne.
Irec ŋoŋe muniŋ, no ŋicfâc-nane ŋoŋerao sorec-jopahuc ejarepe wiac moc ŋowac rombiŋ me?
Erâ Tito fâocte mucnepo ehuc opâ ruac moc sorepe jojowac erâ fâpic. Eme Titozi fârâ wiac moc ŋowac rowec me? Nâhe Mâro wirec â hata wirec mi jukoperec me?
Dâŋ mueŋgopeneŋ i esecne mana warepie sahac ŋeŋezic dâŋ eekac me? Erâ iŋuc mâcne, nâŋe Kristohec juhuc Anuture maio dâŋ mueŋgopeneŋ, erâ âgofâc, irec me irec mâcne, ŋoŋe âkesiŋ-ŋopanaŋte dâŋ mueŋgopeneŋ.
No ŋoŋerao fârâ honec-ŋopape mi sâckezacte, â ŋoŋe nore iŋuc jaha manapie mi sâckezacte manabâc ekopac. Ŋoŋerao kisâ, iiŋguuŋ, kimbeŋ, hehefaric, micko âkec, gupe, penaroŋ, hesi qâsifuc, wiac i fohame fâ bâfuazipore maŋbahacnukac.
Ŋoŋeraonec gâcnezi maŋwânâŋ, boe sau, nânâ qowi âmbâŋ nânâ, i ehuc maŋjeŋic mi bârisieeŋgopieŋ, eme iŋuc juhapie ŋoŋerao fâpe Anutu-nanezi bawahacnume ŋic iŋucne jaŋere ki busâqoc ezipore mana mezac ekopac.
Ʒi ŋoŋerao mocwâc fâpe jahec â moc eocmu. Fâ fisipe ŋic jajahec me jahec â moczi mocte bahacte fuŋne mupie dâŋticne munaŋmu.
Ŋic bahachec â gâcne ŋoŋe mâmâc arecne 2 fâpo ira uŋ ŋazapo ijaha wiwicko juhuc mukopac, ši šâhec mocwâc fârâ mi akic-ŋopapemu.
Nore maŋko dâŋ râeme muekopac Kristo hâcne, ere tâpiri fuame honezo mueŋgopieŋte honenšepieŋ. Kristo e ŋoŋerao gie-ticne rorokacne mâcne, tâpirihec baekac.
Mârâc jâmbomac rokaweme maripoŋko qambiŋ, ši ine Anuture tâpirihec faharewec jukac. Nâŋe iŋuc jaha ere erâ rokaweeŋgopeneŋ irec ere erâ wâc Anuture tâpirio ŋesiŋnehuc jujure fuŋne ŋoŋerao bajaŋgeŋkenaŋmu.
Ŋoŋe mamanasiŋhec jueŋgopieŋ me mâcne, irec maŋŋeŋic esâicke honehuc fuŋne bataniŋkenšepieŋ. Me Jesu Kristozi maŋŋeŋicko juekac irec fârine basaeŋgopieŋ? Iŋuc eeŋgopieŋko sahaczi mitiŋic muŋarezo.
Nâŋe ine sahaczi mitiŋic mi jueŋgopeneŋ, iŋuc hone tarac-nâponiŋte worickekopac.
Anutuzi soŋaŋ-ŋopame bahac mi bâfuaniŋte numucnehuc jueŋgopeneŋ. Nâŋe honec-nâpopie mitiŋic fârine enaŋmu me mâcne, irec mi mueŋgopeneŋ, ŋoŋe mitidâŋ reŋkepie fârinehec eocte mocjaha mueŋgopeneŋ.
Nâŋe iŋucnezi wemocko dâŋfâri râsi ecnenaŋmu, âgo ecnenaŋmu sawa fokac.
Nâŋe tâpiri basahuc juhapene ŋoŋe tâpirihec juniŋmu i bunâŋec biaŋkeocmu. Erâ maŋŋeŋiczi soka sanaŋ eocte Wofuŋ numucneeŋgopeneŋ.
No ŋoŋerao fârâ šâire-ŋarezipore qanaŋ šoricko juhuc uŋdâŋ qâreŋke-ŋarekopac. Wofuŋzi tâpiri narewec, izi imac-ŋopapemurâ mâcne, hume keteŋ eŋarepemurâ narewec.
Erâ dâŋ mutarahuc kecšiŋuc mupe: Ŋoŋe bubiaŋko junšepieŋ, erâ uŋsawaŋ dâŋ manarâ maŋŋeŋic ba emasaŋ enšepieŋ. Ŋoŋe maŋ mocjaha efârerâ wamao junšepieŋ. Eme Anutu e maŋjauŋ â wama runezi ŋoŋehec juocmu.
Ŋoŋe mitio meo babac efârenšepieŋ. širec mitiŋiczi manasuc-ŋopa-fâreŋgopieŋ.
Wofuŋ Jesu Kristore aki anonoc â Anuture maŋjauŋ â Tiri Mârore miriŋ i ŋoŋerao fohuc juzejec.
Paulo no aposolo, ŋiczi mi sorecnumbiŋ â ŋic moczi gie wâc mi munarewec, Jesu Kristo â Anutu Mamac e hâmockonec bâɋâreweczi gie i munarewec.
No â âgo gâcne nohec juŋgopieŋ nâŋe kikefuŋ Galatia mâreŋko juraŋgopieŋ ŋoŋe papia ši râe-ŋareŋgopeneŋ.
Anutu Mamac â Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristo eraonec aki anonoc â wama ŋoŋerao fotâcnerâ fozejec.
Jesu e Mamac-nâŋec Anutu ere micte juju sâqocne ši jueŋgopeneŋkonec bâhoc-nâpoocte sindaŋ-nâŋecte erâ sahac-ticne qaisockewec.
Irec erao mumuteŋzi mumuteŋ fohuc juzejec. Jâmbomac.
Ŋoŋe Kristore aki anonocko râec-ŋopahuc hefârec-ŋopawec ehec jupie mi šoraha e râpeckehuc miti fuŋmoc irec hazec rârâe eŋgopieŋ, no irec wareckekopac.
Erâ Biŋebiaŋ fuŋmoc wena fokac? I aricne i. Mâc ŋic tucnezi maŋ bâsifuc eŋarehuc Kristore Biŋebiaŋ âke sipueŋgopieŋ, i sawa fokac.
Irec nâŋe wâc, me sambâŋkonec aŋelo moczi, Biŋebiaŋ ŋazakicne i âke sipuhuc moc ŋazanaŋmuo, iŋucnezi hârâcte biŋe ezejec.
Dâŋ mârâc mumbeŋ ijaha ši wâc mukopac: Moczi Biŋebiaŋ qazu-ŋarekicne i âke sipuhuc moc ŋazaocmu e hârâcte biŋe ezejec.
Eme weniŋuc, dâŋ ši mukopac i ŋiczi honecnupie biaŋkeocte me Anutuzi honecnume biaŋkeocte mukopac? No ŋic dape-jarehuc gie bazapo muzac, wemocko Kristore kiŋaŋ qaqa juzapo.
Âgofâc-nane, no dâŋ ŋazape mananiŋ: Biŋebiaŋ ŋazapo i ŋickonec mâcne,
erâ wâc ŋiczi mi naza qazuc embiŋ, i Jesu Kristo e jahac mufua-narewec.
No mârâc jaha Judaŋic jaŋere guruo juhuc wiac epo, i ŋoŋe manaeŋgopieŋ. No Anuture kikefuŋfâc jopa jâpec ejarehuc mâretec sipiric-jopapo.
Ehuc kâcɋenefâc-nâŋec jaŋere dâŋ mi wahazejec muhuc samac qamandiŋkerâ motec âgofâc-nane siric-jopapo.
Eme Anutu e qanaŋ neŋgoc bumaŋko hone wosâecnurâ uruc jauŋ-ticnere erâ hefârec-nuweczi maname sâckeme
Ŋokâ-ticnere biŋedâŋ qâpuc jaŋerao musawepere ere fuŋne bataniŋke-narewec. Iŋuc enareme sahac biuchec jaŋe mu wioc mi ejarepo,
erâ wâc Jerusalem haeo mi ferâ aposolo fuŋkerâ juwarembiŋ jaŋe mi iqic-jopapo. Aricne, no Arabia mâreŋko ra juku Damasko haeo risiepo.
Juhape jara 3 tarame Kefa honepemurâ Jerusalem haeo ferâ šoaŋ gie bapa 15 ehec jupo.
Aposolo gâcne mi honec-jopapo, Wofuŋ ɋaticne Jakobo e sawa honepo wâc.
Dâŋ qâreŋkekopac i Anuture maio jâmbomac muhuc qâreŋkekopac.
Iŋuc erâ Siria â Kilikia mâreŋko ra jupo.
Á Judaia mâreŋko Kristore kikefuŋ jaŋe ine mi honecnumbiŋ.
Jaŋe nore biŋedâŋ šiŋuc sawa manambiŋ: “Nâpo jâpec enârehuc miti ima qaocte muweczi ŋic miti i hâcne jazahuc juekac.”
Iŋuc muhuc nore erâ Anutu muteŋkembiŋ.
Ehame jara 14 tarame Jerusalem haeo mocwâc fepemurâ Banaba â Tito rocjofape mâmâc fembeŋ.
Erâ i mâc mi epo, Wofuŋzi dâŋ mufua-narehuc bufahac qanareme fepo. Ferâ qâpuc jaŋerao Biŋebiaŋ musaweekopac i mutaniŋke-jarepo. Micne šâŋe biŋehec jaŋe bucko wâc ejarekicne, jaŋe hâcne manapie mi sâckeme gie maŋgâŋ bawefuhuc jupo iŋuc ezacte.
Jupe juju-nane Tito e Grikŋizi opâ ruakicne juwec, eme e wâc sahacnao mahec eocte mi mucnembiŋ.
Eme nâŋere giemaŋko mitiŋic burecnezi raširâ, nâŋe Kristo Jesure erâ rambaŋ juhapene rucko honetâc-nâporâ Mosere kiŋaŋ qaqa bacnâpozo mueŋgopieŋ,
ŋic izi hâcne bawahac-nâpozo mupie nâŋe Biŋebiaŋzi ŋoŋerao bâbâsifucnehec ezacte moc mi docke-jarembeŋ.
Eme ŋic micne jaŋe mârâc jaha iŋuc me iŋuc jumbiŋ, no irec manape hawarine moc mi eekac, Anutuzi iŋuc jaha sahackopec honec-nâpome bârâwiŋ mi eekac. Ŋic micne jaŋe hâcne dâŋ furune mi šuhucke-narembiŋ.
Aricne, šiŋuc ine manambiŋ: Anutuzi Petoro ŋic mahec jaŋerao Biŋebiaŋ muiŋneocte mucnewec, iŋuc jaha no ŋic ma tâmiric jaŋerao muiŋnepere munarewec.
Ehuc Petoro aposolo gie-ticne baha bafickeme fârinehec ewec, iŋuc jaha no baficnume bape fârinehec jaha wâc ewec.
Eme Wofuŋ e gie tahacke-narewec, i Jakobo, Kefa â Johane jaŋe Jesure kikefuŋ guru jaŋere jâcne jumbiŋzi mana tararâ no â Banaba âgo bacnâfohuc menâhecko bambiŋ, erâ nâhe qâpuc jaŋerao gie bahapere jaŋe jaŋac ŋic mahec jaŋerao baniŋte mumbiŋ.
Erâ hapetacfâc-jeŋic ehâmo-jarenaŋte irec sawa nazambiŋ. Eme no irec dâŋ hâcne šoɋac erâ muekopac.
Eme Kefazi Antiokia haeo warerâ wiac babahacnehec eme honerâ maiqanšaŋ jaha âzâcnepo.
E qanaŋ qâpuczi opâ ruac jaŋehec nânâ wirec nâwec. Ehame Jakobore ŋicfâc fisipie honec-joparâ mahec jaŋere hâwickeme qâpuckonec opâ ruac bâtâc bajarerâ hone takirec-jopawec.
Erâ âkeac ehuc ra rowec ware rowec eme Judaŋic gâcne bafickepie Banaba jaŋerao šuhuckerâ sâc ijaha ewec.
Eme Biŋebiaŋte hata fâretiŋ mi âtepie honec-joparâ ŋic gâcne jaŋere maio Kefa šiŋuc âzâcnepo: “Go Judaŋiczi Judaŋic nâŋâcne eebapao mâcne, qâpuc jaŋere eebapao eekic, izi wemocte qâpuc jaŋe Judaŋic nâŋâcne eebapao eniŋte muekic?”
Nâŋâc qâpuc kosa jujune jaŋe iŋucne mi fuambeŋ, Judaŋic fuambeŋ.
Erâ ine šiŋuc manaŋgopeneŋ: Ŋiczi sâcmutâc dâŋ reŋkehuc kiŋfâsâc eene mi fokac. Eme Kristo e sâcmutâc dâŋ rereŋkere mâcne, mamanasiŋ-nâŋecte erâ kiŋfâsâc bâcnâpoocte, nâŋâc wâc Jesu Kristo manasiŋkeeŋgopeneŋ. Sâcmutâc dâŋte gie bahuc moczi moc kiŋfâsâc eene mi fokac.
Eme Kristorao qohotahuc kiŋfâsâc ezo mueŋgopeneŋzi sifu sâqocne baeŋgopeneŋko weniŋuc muzo? I Kristozi sâqocnere qafeŋ-nâpoekac me? Aricne, iŋuc mi fokac.
Á wiac duckepo i mocwâc heɋârepemu, ine jâmbomac qaqatara ŋic epemu.
Á sâcmutâc dâŋzi nume hâmocnepo i Anutu jucnepemurâ epo.
No Kristohec maripoŋko nukicne. Eme ši juekopac i no nahacne mâcne, Kristozi maŋnaneo juekac. Sahachec juju i juekopac, erâ Anutu Ŋokâ-ticne manasiŋkehuc e sawa jucneekopac. Eki hâcne maŋjauŋ enarehuc juju-ticne nore due bawec.
No Anutu aki anonoc-ticne mi qâsuakopac. Sâcmutâc dâŋ reŋkehuc kiŋfâsâc eene fozacko Kristo e maŋgâŋko hâmowec ezac.
O Galata ŋic mutucne¡ Ŋoŋe mozi maŋ bâsifuc eŋarewec? Jesu Kristo maripoŋko qakicne ere hawari ŋaza ŋowatuc epe šâŋe fâri-ŋeŋiczi honembiŋ i¡
Wiac mocjahare wio-ŋarepe nazaniŋ: Mâro rombiŋ i weniŋuc ehuc rombiŋ? Sâcmutâc dâŋ reŋkehuc rombiŋ, me miti manarâ mamanasiŋhec ehuc rombiŋ?
Maŋmutuc wemocte eŋgopieŋ? Mârore hata fuŋkerâ âtembiŋzi juju raŋɋare hatao rašiŋgopieŋ me?
Wiac fekicne sâko i maŋgâŋ fua-ŋarewec me? ­ jâmbomac fârimâc ewecko.
Mâro ŋarehuc wiac tâpirihec ŋoŋerao eekac, eki sâcmutâc dâŋ rereŋte me mamanasiŋ-ŋeŋicte eŋareekac me?
Abraham e iŋuc hâcne ecnekicne. E Anutu manasiŋkeme kiŋfâsâc mucnewec.
Irec šiŋuc mananiŋ: Mamanasiŋhec jaŋe Abrahamte ɋâricfâc fârine.
Ŋic qâpuc jaŋe Anutu manasiŋkepie kiŋfâsâc bacjopaocmu, irec hâcne mârâc jaha manasuhuc Abrahamte Biŋebiaŋ dâŋ šiŋuc mume miti papiao qâreŋkembiŋ: “Qâpuc guru jaŋe gore jambuŋko raši-fâreniŋmu.”
Irec hâcne, Abrahamzi mamanasiŋ hata âtewec ijaha âteniŋmuzi ere jambuŋko rašiniŋmu.
Á sâcmutâc dâŋte giezi fosiŋ-jeŋic eha juniŋmu jaŋe ine sâwechec eniŋmu. šiŋuc hâcne qâreŋkekicne fokac: “Sâcmutâc birio dâŋ forakac i moc mi qâsuazo. Moc e qâsuaocmuzi sâwec hotâckeocmu.”
Sâcmutâc dâŋte maŋnao juhuc Anuturao kiŋfâsâc eene mi fokac, i dâŋ šizi mujaŋgeŋkekac: “Mamanasiŋte erâ biaŋkekicnezi juju hotâckeocmu.”
Sâcmutâc dâŋko ine mamanasiŋte moc mi mukicne. Ine šiŋuc mukicne: “Giene bafâreocmuzi juju hotâckeocmu.”
Dâŋqâreŋ moc šiŋuc fokac: “Ŋic jâcko ɋetic-jopakicne jaŋe sâwecte biŋe.” Eme Kristo e nâŋâcnere iŋuc hâcne erâ sâwec hotâckewec, ehuc sâcmutâc dâŋte sâwec i bâsue-nârewec.
Eme irec Jesu Kristore erâ Abrahamte jambuŋzi ŋicne ŋicne jaŋerao sâcne raocmu. Eme Mâro biŋe qanârekicne ine mamanasiŋhec erâ ronaŋmu.
Âgofâc, no wiac omanao sâc hehuc mupe: Ŋic moczi hâmohuc merâfâc-ticne biŋe qajareocmu, i moczi qâsuarâ fainao dâŋ moc mi šuhuckeocmu.
Eme miti merâfâc i Abraham â ɋâric-ticne biŋe qajactekicne hâcne. Ɋâricfâc-ticne bocjaha jaŋere mi mukicne, mocjahare mukicne Kristo hâcne.
No kecšiŋucte mukopac: Anutuzi mârâc jaha miti merâfâc irec biŋedâŋ muwec, ehame šâhecko jara 430 tarame sâcmutâc dâŋ mufuawec, eme sâcmutâc dâŋ šâhec mufuakicne izi wemocko biŋedâŋ mârâc mukicne qame wahaocmu.
Miti merâfâc i sâcmutâc dâŋte erâ rorone eme muzac ine biŋedâŋte erâ rorone i arictac ezac. Anutuzi ine miti merâfâc i katucmâc-ticnere erâ Abraham biŋe qacnewec.
Hâc, eme sâcmutâc dâŋ wemocte mukicne? I qaqatarare mufuakicne, erâ fofo sanaŋ foocte mâcne, Abrahamte ɋâric biŋedâŋ rune fuame rârieocte mukicne. Sâcmutâc dâŋ i aŋelo miczi mukicne â ŋicwirec ere meo râekicne.
Ŋicwirec moczi ŋic mocjahare mâcne, bocjaha jaŋere qâqâhâc domaocmu. Anutu eki ine mocjaha.
Eme sâcmutâc dâŋzi Anuture biŋedâŋ âkehockeocmu me? Iŋuc aricne. Sâcmutâc dâŋzi ŋicmaŋ mi heɋâreocmu. I eene eme muzac, ine jâmbomac sâcmutâc dâŋte erâ kiŋfâsâc ee i fuazac.
Ŋic mâmâc sasawa sâqocnere niŋgiŋko jueŋgopeneŋ, fuŋne-nâŋec iŋuc hâcne miti papiao mufuakicne. Eme irec hâcne Jesu Kristo manasiŋkehuc mitihec erâ biŋedâŋte fârine ronaŋmu, i sawa fokac.
Judaŋic nâŋâc mârâc jaha mamanasiŋ tâmiric juhapene sâcmutâc dâŋzi kâpâcwâru bacnâpome niŋgiŋko fokuhapene mamanasiŋte biŋedâŋzi fua tâcnewec.
Eme irec sâcmutâc dâŋzi bâbâtiŋ-nâŋec erâ Kristorao râec-nâpowec, i mamanasiŋhec erâ kiŋfâsâc enaŋte iŋuc ekicne.
Nâŋâc mamanasiŋte hata fuame i âtepene bâbâtiŋte niŋgiŋ tâcnewec.
Eme ŋoŋe Kristo Jesu manasiŋkeŋgopieŋte šeŋgoma Anuture naru motecfâc embiŋ juŋgopieŋ.
Miti Opâ rua-ŋarehuc Kristorao šuhuc-ŋopakicne ŋoŋe mâmâc sasawa Kristozi ŋaqi-ŋeŋic ehame hepie huwec.
Eme irec Judaŋic â Grikŋic, fekicne â wahakicne, ŋic â ŋokac, bârâwiŋ juju i tarame ŋoŋe mâmâc sasawa Kristo Jesurao sâc mocjaha embiŋ.
Ŋoŋe Kristore biŋe embiŋzi Abrahamte ɋâricfâc fârine juŋgopieŋ, erâ biŋedâŋte sâcko merâfâc-ticne bajuniŋmu.
Moc šiŋuc mupe mananiŋ: Motec ɋiene moc e mamac hâmocnere merâfâc raucke-bipiehuc sifu kiŋaŋ motec hawari juocmu.
Ehame wawa rau â âgo tofazi merâfâc qâzuckerâ bacne juhapie dameŋ mamaczi bawec i maickeocmu.
Nâŋâcne sâc ijaha fokac. Mârâc jaha maŋzi ɋiene juhuc mâreŋte wiac omanere kiŋaŋ qajumbeneŋ.
Eme šâhecko dameŋ bakicne i qosackeme Anutuzi Ŋokâ-ticne soreme ŋokackonec fuawec â sâcmutâc dâŋte kiŋaŋ qawec.
Ine nâŋâc sâcmutâc dâŋte niŋgiŋkonec goroŋ-nâpome Anuture naru motecfâc enaŋte iŋuc ewec.
Eme ŋoŋe naru motecfâc-ticne eŋgopieŋte Anutuzi Ŋokâ-ticnere Mâro maŋnâŋecko soreme hurâ šiŋuc wirâ wâwâsic eekac: “O Mamac biaŋ.”
Irec go kiŋaŋ qaqa-ticne mâcne, motec-ticne juekic. Erâ motec-ticne juhuc Anutu katucmâc-ticnere erâ merâfâc rune wâc juekic.
Ŋoŋe mârâc jaha Anuture kâuc bahuc nemu, Wofuŋ fârine mi jujune, jaŋe kiŋaŋ qajare jumbieŋ.
Eme šâhec Anutuzi hone šâŋitac eŋareme ŋoŋe e wâc hone tarambiŋ. Ehame wiac tâpiri tâmiric â fârimâc i wemocte mocwâc maickehuc kiŋaŋne qaŋgopieŋ?
Ehuc hombaŋ fuŋne fuŋnere manapie fârine eme ŋeeŋgopieŋ.
Gie-nanezi ŋoŋerao fârimâc ezacte mana mezac boc eekopac.
Âgofâc-nane, no numu-ŋarehuc mupe: No ŋoŋere sâc epore ŋoŋe nore sâc enšepieŋ. Ŋoŋe ši juwarehuc wiac hehesicne moc mi enarembiŋ.
Ŋoŋe manaŋgopieŋ, no mârâcko huc šâic enarehame Biŋebiaŋ ŋazapo.
Eme sahac dodoc mâretec enareme ŋoŋe nore sifu tatakicne mi eŋarewec â mi mamakâc-ŋopawec. Aricne, ŋoŋe honecnupie Anuture aŋelo tinac epo, opoŋ, Kristo Jesu tinac epe hefârecnumbiŋ.
Joi, dameŋ ira mu šeri embiŋ i weniŋucte omaekac? Ŋoŋe šâŋe hândâŋ-ŋeŋic unuckerâ no nanarene fome muzac enšapiŋ, i jâmbomac manahuc mukopac.
Eme dameŋ šiŋuczia dâŋ fârine ŋazape honecnupie râsi-ŋeŋic ekopac me?
Ŋic gâcnezi ŋoŋere harac baeŋgopieŋ i âke râwiŋ-nâpopie ŋoŋe jaŋere harac eniŋte manasuhuc eeŋgopieŋ. Ine hâcne sioc ehuc ŋoŋere harac baeŋgopieŋ.
Wiac biaŋnere erâ harac ee i biaŋne. Ine ŋoŋerao fârâ juhape sawa mâcne, dameŋ sâc epie biaŋkeocmu.
Naru motecfâc-nane, no ŋoŋere erâ gozi kicnuha šâic manapo, ijaha harierâ manakopac, erâ Kristore hawari ŋoŋerao fua tâcneocte šâic i mana rahuc jupemu.
No ŋoŋere mana guruc boc ekopacte ŋoŋerao biac fârâ dâŋ mu hetikic ehuc ŋazazore enarekac.
Wio-ŋarepe nazaniŋ, sâcmutâc dâŋte kiŋaŋ qazo mueŋgopieŋzi irec papia wose manac mi eeŋgopieŋ me?
Ira hâcne šiŋuc qâreŋkekicne: Abrahamte ŋokâ jajahec fuapic, moc i kiŋaŋ naruzi rowec â moc i ŋonâŋzi rowec.
Eme kiŋaŋ naruzi rowec e omanao fuawec, â ŋonâŋzi rowec e Anuture biŋedâŋte sâcko fuawec.
Eme dâŋ irec ŋifecne šiŋuc fokac: Ŋokac jahe mitire šâšâfic jajahec irec sâsâcne epic. Ʒâšâfic moc Sinai tikio ekicne, ere kikefuŋzi ine kiŋaŋ qaqa embiŋ, eme irec sâsâcne Hagazi ewec.
Haga i Sinai tiki, Arabia mâreŋko ŋekac, irec šâŋe moc. Á Jerusalem hae i Sinai tikihec sâcjekic mocjaha ekopirec, ere kikefuŋ jaŋe kiŋaŋ qaqa jaha wâc eŋgopieŋ hâcne.
Á Jerusalem hae faic ŋekac izi Sara ere sâc, hae izi hâcne neŋgoc jâmbâŋ-nâŋec ekac.
Dâŋqâreŋ šiŋuc hâcne fokac: “Ŋokac hufiŋne, motec mi roro go bubiaŋ manazemec, gozi mi kicguekac go šeri ehuc kiwaezemec. Ŋokac ŋichec e ɋâric afecne fuacnehapie me sawanezi naru motec bocjaha rocjopaocmu.”
Âgofâc-nane, ŋoŋe Isakare sâc erâ biŋedâŋte fuambiŋ.
Eme mârâc jaha motec omanao fuakicnezi Mârore dâŋte fuakicne e râsi ecnewec, sâc ijaha miŋecgac fokac.
Eme miti papiao dâŋ weniŋuc fokac? “Kiŋaŋ naru e ŋokâ-ticnehec jâpec-jofatec ranic, kiŋaŋ narure ŋokâzi ŋonâŋte ŋokâhec merâfâc mi rauckezejec.”
Âgofâc-nane, nâŋâc kiŋaŋ narure ɋârifâc aricne, nâŋâc ŋonâŋte ɋâricfâc.
Niŋgiŋ tâmiric junaŋte Kristozi goroŋ-nâpowec. Irec gâcnezi niŋgiŋko râec-ŋoparâ kiŋaŋ qaqa eniŋte muŋarepie qikiŋnenšepieŋ.
No Paulozi ŋazape mananiŋ, ŋoŋe sahac-ŋeŋicko ma bapie Kristozi ŋoŋerao wiac omane tinac eocmu.
Mocwâc harierâ ŋaza-jâmbâŋkepe, moc e sahac-ticnao ma baocmuzi sâcmutâc dâŋ gâcne sâko mâmâc hâpo-fâreme sâckeocmu.
Sâcmutâc dâŋ reŋkehuc kiŋfâsâc ezo mueŋgopieŋ ŋoŋe Kristohec šâšâfic embiŋ i tâcnekac â aki anonoczi ŋoŋerao fârimâc ekac.
Nâŋe ine Mârorao ŋesiŋnehuc mamanasiŋte erâ kiŋfâsâc ee bâfuanaŋte irec mamanac jueŋgopeneŋ.
Kristo Jesurao fisirâ mahec juju â ma tâmiric juju irec mâmâc jaha fârimâc muzo, mamanasiŋte qâreŋ maŋko fuame irec mocjaha fârine muzo.
Ŋoŋe mitire hata sâcne fuŋkerâ âtembiŋ. Âtehapie mozi aka heŋareme dâŋ fâri qizecne râpeckeŋgopieŋ?
Hefârec-ŋopawec eki irec esoc qafeŋ mi eŋarekac.
Qowi hâhâtâcne pitic siŋgaŋ gaucnezi nânâ sicko hurâ mâmâc sâcke-fâreocmu.
Erâ ŋoŋe nore dâŋ mi qikiŋneniŋmu, i Wofuŋte erâ manabâc tâmiric mukopac. Á ŋic izi me izi maŋ bâsifuc eŋareocmu, e kiŋ irec okacne fisicneocmu.
Âgofâc, no ine mahec eniŋte ŋic jazazapo muzac, wemocko fific guguriŋ moc enarenšapiŋ? Iŋuc jazazapoo maripoŋte mamana gâpâre i mâmâc omaezac.
Maŋqaqa eŋareeŋgopieŋ ŋic iŋucnezi sahac-jeŋic hetâc qâtâcnenšapiŋ me!
Âgofâc-nane, ŋoŋe niŋgiŋ tâmiric juniŋte hefârec-ŋopakicne, erâ niŋgiŋ tâmiric jujuzi âki eha sahacte dâŋ reŋkeniŋte mâcne, maŋjauŋko kiŋaŋ qaqac eniŋte irec hefârec-ŋopakicne.
Irec hâcne sâcmutâc dâŋte qâqâhâc šiŋuc mukicne: “Gahacnere egareekac, sâc ijaha âgogere egarezejec.”
Ŋoŋe ine miczi nânâc ehuc kikic qaqac boc erâ oomaec enšipiŋte uŋ ŋazakopac.
Erâ ine šiŋuc mukopac: Ŋoŋe Mârore tâpirio siŋkerâ junšepieŋ, iŋuc ehuc maŋraŋɋare sasec gie mi baniŋmu.
Maŋraŋɋare aŋaczi hâcne Mâro kisueekac â Mârozi maŋraŋɋa kisueekac, eme jahe hâcne rârâsi epire ŋoŋe wiac ezo mueŋgopieŋ i sâcne mi afeckerâ eeŋgopieŋ.
Mârozi jowa baafec eŋareme ine sâcmutâc dâŋzi ŋicbomboŋ mi eŋareocmu.
Maŋraŋɋare gie i soŋsoŋko mi foekac, i šiŋuc fuaekac: Boe sau, mamakâc, nâ areŋ,
nemu araŋ babajare, hafec qaŋgec, rârâsi, sosopec, iiŋguuŋ, kimbeŋ, hehefaric, fâfâuc, rârâwiŋ,
mu kâroŋ, opâ momori me bec qowi âmbâŋ nânâ, erâ wiac gâcne. Wiac iŋucnere mârâc jaha ŋazapo erâ ši mocwâc ŋazape: Sâqocne i baniŋmuzi Anuture uucmaŋko mi rašiniŋmu.
Mârore fârine ine kecšiŋuc fuaekac: Maŋjauŋ, bubiaŋ, wama, bumâteŋ, buafec, buuruc, ââgo sanaŋ,
ruaine, maŋzi sowa juju. Mârore fârine hâcne irec aka mi fokac.
Kristo Jesure biŋe jueŋgopieŋ jaŋe juju raŋɋa-jeŋic sasec â sâqocnere andachec i maripoŋko qapie omaewec.
Mârore tâpirire jueŋgopeneŋko Mârore hata jaha âtenšepeneŋ.
Sahaczi fecko fec ehuc hehesuac mi enšepeneŋ, erâ wâc iiŋguuŋ mi eec enšepeneŋ.
Âgofâc-nane, ŋic moczi dockerâ bahac bâfuame ŋoŋe Mâroheczi bumâteŋ erâ iŋucne mu bâtiŋ ecnenšepieŋ. Ehuc go gahac eesâicko pârâckezicte rucge bazemec.
Wiac kihuhuŋ-ŋopaekac i nowac gowacroŋ ehuc babaficko banšepieŋ. Iŋuc ehuc Kristore sâcmutâc dâŋ sâcne reŋkeniŋmu.
Ŋic moc e wiac fârine moc mi ehuc e jahacnere maname fefene eocmu, iŋucnezi maŋticne fagac ecnekac muzo.
Irec moc e jahacne juju bapa hone šâŋitac ezejec. Eme šeridâŋ i e jahacnere erâ fuaocmu, ŋic mocte erâ mâcne.
Giere ŋemâc kâdoc qakicne i ru sâc areckezo.
Miti ŋaza qazuc eeŋgopieŋ ŋic i jaŋe wiac fuŋne fuŋne boki bahuc jare gumec enšepieŋ.
Anutu mu qâtimbuc ecnepie mâc foocmu, iŋuc moc mupie. I aricne jâmbâŋ, ŋic moc gie baocmu e irec fârine juku ijaha roocmu.
Moc e maŋraŋɋare gie baocmu, e juku maŋraŋɋa-ticnere fârine sisipiric bâfuaocmu, â moc e Mârore gie baocmu, e juku Mârore fârine juju sanaŋ bâfuaocmu.
Wiac biaŋne i rorokac tâmiric enšepeneŋ, eme mi betaŋkenaŋmuo juku dameŋ-ticnao mâriri bâfuanaŋmu.
Irec dameŋ-nâŋec fohame ŋic sasawa ehâmo-jarenšepeneŋ. Ehuc mitio âgofâc-nâŋec wiac bafehuc ejarenšepeneŋ.
Ŋoŋe qâreŋ sâko ši honeniŋ, no nahacne mezi qâreŋke-ŋarekopac.
Ŋic gâcne jaŋe sahaczi miti hawari biaŋ erâ ŋoŋe sahacko mahec eniŋte fotarie-ŋareeŋgopieŋ jaŋe Kristo maripoŋ-ticnere erâ fific guguriŋ faio fenšipiŋte iŋuc hâcne eeŋgopieŋ.
Sahacko mahec embiŋ ŋic i jaŋe jaŋac wâc sâcmutâc dâŋ mi reŋkeeŋgopieŋ. Jaŋe mâc ŋoŋe mahec erâ jaŋerao šuhuckepie sahac-jeŋic muteŋkeniŋte manasueŋgopieŋ.
No ine wiac irec mi Irec mâcne, Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristo maripoŋ-ticnere biŋedâŋ irec mocjaha mumuteŋ bajuekopac. Ere erâ mâreŋkonec wiaczi maripoŋko hâmo-narewec, â no iŋuc jaha maripoŋko mâreŋkonec wiac hâmocnepo.
Sahacko mahec juju me ma tâmiric juju izi fârine aricne, juju ɋâricne izi mocjaha fârine ekac.
Gaŋ rukec ira hâcne domaeŋgopieŋ sâc ŋoŋerao wama â buuruc fotâcnerâ fozejec, erâ Anuture Israe ŋic jaŋerao mâmâc.
Ʒi moczi moc neneŋ gie mocwâc mi narezejec. No Wofuŋ Jesure râfu qâreŋ sahac-naneo fome bajuekopac.
Âgofâc-nane, Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristore aki anonoczi maŋŋeŋicko fozejec. Jâmbomac.
Paulo no Anuture micte Jesu Kristore aposolo epozi Efeso haeonec mitiŋic, Kristo Jesu manasiŋkeeŋgopieŋ hâcne, ŋoŋere papia ši râekopac
Mamac-nâŋec Anutu â Wofuŋ Jesu Kristo eraonec aki anonoc â wama ŋoŋerao fotâcnera fozejec.
Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristo ere Anutu â Mamac, eki sambâŋkonec miti jambuŋ-ticne fuŋne fuŋne Kristore erâ nâre tahac ewecte mumbiaŋkenšepeneŋ.
Eki mârâc jaha jâmbâŋ mâreŋte hobeteŋne mi fuahame mai-ticnao maŋfuru â bahacmâc junaŋte Kristore erâ mana wosâc enârewec.
E qanaŋ maname fowecte hâcne Jesu Kristore erâ maŋjauŋ enârehuc naru motecfâc-ticne erâ junaŋte buafec-ticnere mupaŋke-nârewec.
E joroc Ŋokâ-ticnere erâ aki anonoc biaŋ-ticne tahac-nâpowecte muteŋ bâteŋ ecnenšepeneŋ.
Jesu e socticnezi kitâc-nâpowecte sâqocne bâbâtâmire fua-nârewec, i aki anonoc-ticnere šâkâŋ fokac irec sâc hâcne.
Eme šâkâŋ-ticnao maŋɋârâŋ â mamana fâri bâmâckehuc qoŋgiŋke-nârewec.
Ehuc maŋbuc-ticnere dâŋ, qanaŋ maname biaŋkeme šiŋuc âkendâŋnewec i mujaŋgeŋke-nârewec:
“No guriŋne bahape dameŋ maŋkepo i qosackeme Kristozi wiac sasawa, sambâŋko mecne mâreŋko mecne, qâturehuc irec fuŋqizecne ezejec.”
Ere erâ, wiac sasawa maŋticnere mupaŋkerâ baekaczi mârâc jaha hone wosâec-nâporâ miti merâfâc rauckenaŋte munârewec.
Eme irec Kristore mamanac jumbeŋ jueŋgopeneŋzi Anutu šâŋe rara-ticnere mumuteŋfâc erâ junšepeneŋ.
Eme ŋoŋe iŋuc jaha dâŋ fâri qizecne, bâbâpiaŋ-ŋeŋicte Biŋebiaŋ hâcne, ro maŋ ehuc Kristo manasiŋkepie Tiri Mâro qanaŋ biŋe qanarekicne i ŋareme maqâreŋhec embiŋ.
Sambâŋko huhure biŋe-nâŋec fokac, irec šâšâficne Mâro nârekicne. Eme Anutu šâŋe rara-ticnere mumuteŋ sâko fuaocte biŋefâc-ticne nâŋâcnao Mârozi bâbâpiaŋ gie fuŋkewec i batarazokac.
Eme ŋoŋe Wofuŋ Jesu manasiŋkeeŋgopieŋ â mitiŋic âgofâc-nâŋec maŋjauŋ ejareeŋgopieŋ, irec biŋedâŋ manapore
ŋoŋere dameŋ sâc manasuhuc Wofuŋ daŋge mumuteŋ ecneekopac.
Ehuc ŋoŋere šiŋuc numuekopac: Wofuŋ Jesu Kristo ere Anutu, eri tatamac Mamac hâcne, eki Mâro ŋareme izi maŋɋârâŋhec bacŋoparâ Wofuŋte fuŋne mufua-ŋareme mana taranšepieŋ.
Erâ maŋšâŋe-ŋeŋic bâtâcneme ine Wofuŋzi rocŋopahuc sambâŋ šeŋaŋ biŋe qaŋarewec, irec manapie fârine ezejec, â fuŋfuŋfâc-ticne ŋoŋe huhure šâŋe rara biaŋ kadahe ŋarewec, irec wâc manapie fârine ezejec,
â mamanasiŋhec nâŋâcnao tâpiri soka makakicne i teqâ saki-ticnezi gie baekac sâc bâfuawec, irec iŋuc jaha manapie fârine ezejec.
Tâpiri irec fuŋne Kristo hâmockonec bâɋârerâ sambâŋko mefâre-ticnao râehuc bataniŋkewec.
Ehuc kia gawamaî â ŋicwofuŋ â fekicne fuŋne fuŋne jaŋere femicne sâko râewecte mâreŋko â sambâŋko šâŋe biŋe fokac izi gâkowakac, dameŋ šiŋucziare sawa mâcne, iŋuc fohuc juocmu sanaŋ.
Erâ wiac sasawa maŋfuŋnao heteckehuc kike-ticnere rurumaŋko guruc-jopahuc qizec-jeŋic eocte âkendâŋnerâ kikefuŋ gurufâcne jaŋerao râewec.
Eme jaŋe me kikefâc-ticne ehapie ŋihe umbiŋ ejarehuc fofotâc juhuc wiac sasawa sâcke raekac.
Ŋoŋe mârâc jaha sindaŋ hârindaŋ ehuc hâmocne jujumbieŋ.
Ine mâreŋte juju hata maŋnao juhuc saware tâpiri irec ŋicbomboŋ erao qohota jumbieŋ. Ere mârozi hâcne dameŋ šiŋuczia wâc qaqatara ŋic jaŋerao gie baekac.
Nâŋâc mârâc jaha jaŋere sâc jaha jufârehuc maŋraŋɋa-nâŋecte aŋac bâjâpembeŋ. Ehuc sahac-nâŋecte â maŋ mamanasu-nâŋecte dâŋ reŋkehuc gâcne jaŋe iŋucne kimbeŋte biŋefâc embeŋ.
Anutu eki buuruc-ticne bocjaha fokacte maŋjauŋ kâcɋene enârehuc
qaqatara-nâŋecte erâ hâmokicne nâŋâc Kristohec mâmâc bâɋârec-nâpowec. Manaŋgopieŋ, katucmâc-ticnere erâ bâpiaŋ-ŋopawec ŋoŋe.
E Kristo Jesuhec bâɋârec-nâporâ ehec mâmâc sambâŋte jujuo ŋec-nâpowec hâcne.
i nacnere mocko šiŋuc fuaocte ewec: Aki anonoc-ticnere rowaŋ sâko i Kristo Jesuo maŋuruc qanârehuc qaratie-nâreocmu.
Manaŋgopieŋ, e aki anonoc eŋarehuc mamanasiŋ-ŋeŋicte erâ bâpiaŋ-ŋopawec, i ŋaŋacnere mâcne, Anutu buafec-ticnere iŋuc eŋarewec.
Mo gie mo bambiŋte iŋuc eŋarezac, i aricne. Irec sahac mumuteŋ moc mi fuazejec.
Nâŋâc Anuture metofafâc, eki Kristo Jesuo bâfuac-nâpowec hâcne, erâ hata biaŋne Anutuzi hâcne mušâwe-nârewec i âtehuc junaŋte munârewec.
Ŋoŋe mârâc jaha qâpuc jujumbieŋ, irec manasuhuc junšepieŋ. Eme dameŋ ira ma tâmiric juhapie Judaŋic jaŋe sahac-jeŋicko maheczi šâgu muŋare jumbieŋ.
Dameŋ ira Kristo tâmiric jumbiŋ, erâ Israe ŋic jaŋe hae fâri juhapie ŋoŋe mafa jumbiŋ, â jaŋe fuŋfuŋfâc-ticne bacjopame biŋedâŋ-ticne bajuhapie ŋoŋe šoŋifecfâc-ticne erâ metariŋ jumbiŋ, erâ maŋzi wiac fârine moc mi worickehuc Anutu tâmiric hâcne jumbiŋ.
Dameŋ šiŋuczia ine ŋoŋe kâteo jumbiŋzi Kristo Jesurao šuhuckehuc Kristo socticnere erâ haeo fisimbiŋ jueŋgopieŋ.
E jahac wama-nâŋec juekac. E ŋic jâcne jajahec ŋondeŋ-jekicko rârâsizi aka sanaŋ fowec i qâropiehuc, mocjaha bacjofawec.
Ine sâcmutâc dâŋqâhâcko bâtâc â mumuac bocjaha mukicne i e jahacne sahac qaisockehuc bârâriewec. Ehuc ŋic jâcne jajahec jahere dodoma tacko ŋic ɋâricne mocjaha ine e jahac fuarâ domahuc wama bâfuawec.
E maripoŋlo hâmowecko ŋic jâcne jajahec fâri ombâŋ mocjahao qâturec-nâpohuc Anutuhec miriŋ bacnâpowec, ehuc rârâsi qame wahawec.
Erâ fisirâ kâteo jukicne ŋoŋe â haeo jukicne nâŋe mâmâc wamare biŋedâŋ nâzâme manambeŋ.
Erâ wâc hata bâšâwe-nârewecte nâŋâc Mâro mocjaha rauckerâ Mamactao fisieŋgopeneŋ.
Eme irec dameŋ šiŋuczia mafa â jaba mocwâc mi jueŋgopieŋ, ŋoŋe mitiŋic gâcne jaŋehec hae fâri â Anuture kikefuŋfâc embiŋ juŋgopieŋ.
Ŋoŋe aposolo â porofete jaŋe wâtuŋ ŋokacne ehuc decŋopapie doma raŋgopieŋ, â Jesu Kristozi wâtuŋ ŋicne ekac.
Erao ŋicne ŋicne šuhucke itic epene Wofuŋte furu ufuŋ fua feekac.
Mârozi ŋoŋe iŋuc jaha erao râe šuhuc eŋareme Anuture fic eŋgopieŋ hâcne.
Eme Paulo no irec hâcne qâpuc ŋoŋere erâ Kristo Jesure kâpâcwâru ŋic epo jukopac.
Ŋoŋe nore manambiŋ, Anutuzi uruc jauŋ-ticnere erâ ŋoŋerao miti gie bapemurâ munarewec.
Munarehuc dâŋ soŋne mufua-narewec, dâŋ i hâcne biac bembeŋne qâreŋkepac,
ŋoŋe i wosehuc, no Kristore dâŋ soŋne maŋzi hone raruŋkekopac iŋuc sâcne mananiŋmu.
Dâŋ soŋne i mârâc jaha ŋic juwarembiŋ jaŋerao mi mufuakicne, tiri aposolo â porofete nâŋerao šâhec Mârozi mufuawec.
Dâŋ soŋne kecšiŋuc: Biŋebiaŋte fârine qâpuc ŋoŋe Judaŋic nâŋehec sâc mocjaha â guru mocjaha erâ Kristo Jesurao biŋedâŋ deŋkewec i mâmâc rauckerâ bajuniŋte mukicne.
Eme Biŋebiaŋ irec kiŋaŋ qaqa jupemurâ Anutuzi uruc jauŋ-ticnere erâ tâpiri sâko-ticnere fuŋne norao bataniŋkewec. Dâŋ soŋnere fârine Jesuzi bâfuawec
Kristorao mâriri sâko fofone fokac irec dâŋ soŋne qâpuc mutaniŋke-jarepemurâ irec gie biaŋ mitiŋic wawahane jâmbâŋ no hâcne munarekicne.
Dâŋ soŋne muraruŋkepere mukicne, i Anutu bapafâre e maŋbuc-ticnere dameŋne dameŋne baju warehuc juwec.
Ʒi ine Anutuzi kikefuŋ gurufâc-ticne nâŋâcnao maŋɋârâŋ-ticnere fârine qaratiekume qâreŋne fuŋne fuŋne fuame sambâŋko ira fekicne â tâpirihec jaŋe wâc hone šâŋitac eeŋgopieŋ.
Anutu e mârâc jaha dameŋ tâmiricko maŋnezi dâŋ mupaŋkewec irec fârine hâcne Wofuŋ-nâŋec Kristo Jesu sorehuc bâfuawec.
Eme eki hâcne hata bâšâwe-nâreme e manasiŋkehuc hâhâwic tâmiric Anutu maickeeŋgopeneŋ.
Irec šiŋuc ŋazape mananiŋ: No ŋoŋere erâ fific guguriŋ faio jupe irec maŋŋeŋic mi wahazejec, aricne, ŋoŋe irec manapie eri qoqonaŋ-ŋeŋic ezejec.
Irec hâcne sambâŋko â mâreŋko ŋic guru sâc jueŋgopeneŋ
nâŋâcne Mamac fârine e dieŋzi hecnehuc ŋoŋere erâ numucnehuc šiŋuc muekopac:
Anutu e hahaŋnehec sâkozi Mâro ecneme tâpiri bâfua-ŋareme maŋŋeŋiczi soka sanaŋ ezejec.
Eme Kristo manasiŋkepie maŋŋeŋicko ŋeŋe juju ezejec. Eme ere maŋjauŋko gâtâ barâ qiŋ herâ domanšepieŋ.
Ehuc mitiŋic gâcne sasawa jaŋehec mâmâc mitire fuŋne botâŋne, hâŋne otecne. i afeckerâ mana taranšepieŋ,
erâ wâc Kristore maŋjauŋ, ŋic mamana jâuru-fâreekac, i sifu mana-hâmonšepieŋ. Ehame Anuturao maŋ mâriri fufusuc fokac izi bâfusec-ŋopazejec.
Tâpiri-ticnere fuŋne nâŋâcnao bataniŋkeekac Anutu hâcne, e wiac bapa-ticnezi nunumu-nâŋec â mamanasu-nâŋec siricke-fâreekacte
kikefuŋko â Kristo Jesurao mumuteŋ-ticne mimiŋzi ɋâric šuhuckeme šuhuc fofehuc juzejec sanaŋ. Jâmbomac.
No Wofuŋte kâpâcwâru ŋiczi faŋ qaŋarehuc ŋazape: Wiac fekicnere hefârec-ŋopakicne irec sâcko junšepieŋ.
Ehuc maŋhuhuŋ â buuruc â bumâteŋ juhuc maŋjauŋko dedec ââsic enšepieŋ.
Erâ Mâro e wamare muczi qâzuc-ŋoparâ dâtâc-ŋopawec, i qâtâcnenšipiŋte ruc babac ehuc junšepieŋ.
Fâri ombâŋzi mocjaha â Mârozi mocjaha erâ wâc sambâŋ šeŋaŋ mocjahare biŋe qaŋarehuc hefârec-ŋopakicne.
Ine hâcne, Wofuŋzi mocjaha, mamanasiŋzi mocjaha, Miti Opâzi mocjaha.
Erâ Anutu e Mamac wirec-nâŋec mocjaha, eki mâmâc sasawa qâhuc-nâpokac erâ maŋnâŋec sâc tâpiri sicne-nâreekac â mâŋnâŋec sâc ŋeŋe juju eekac.
Kristo e ŋicne ŋicne mitire kâdoc nârewec sâc bajueŋgopeneŋ.
Irec hâcne dâŋqâreŋ moc šiŋuc fokac: “E faic jâmbâŋ fehuc kâpâcwâru ŋic bacjopa rawec, e ŋic wiac tahac-jopawec.”
“Faic fewec”, i mâc mi mukicne, mâreŋko juwic jâmbâŋ wahaweckonec risie fewec.
E wahaweczia risierâ sambâŋne sambâŋne fotâcnerâ fewec, i sambâŋ â mâreŋ fusucmarâ jufâreocte fewec hâcne.
Erâ ekizia wâc ŋic gâcne aposolo râec-nâpowec, gâcne porofete, gâcne miti kiŋaŋ ŋic, gâcne lama guru jaŋere soŋaŋ â qaqazu,
i mitiŋic ŋokac bašawiec-jopapene kikefuŋte kiŋaŋ qaqa gie bapie Kristore me kike fâri ombâŋ soka sanaŋ eocte ŋic iŋuc râec-nâpowec.
Iŋuczi iŋuc gie bakupene mamanasiŋ-nâŋec â Anutu ŋokâ-ticnere fuŋne mamana-nâŋec i niniweme maŋ mocjaha enšepeneŋ. Ehuc mitio sosoka-nâŋecte sâc mukicne i Kristore rowaŋkonec tâpiri fârehuc fua sokac eku ŋic kâcɋene erâ bâfuanšepeneŋ.
Nâŋâc ɋiene hati mi ee sanaŋkerâ juhapene eeatuc ŋic jaŋe sioc enârepie gibioc dâŋ â mumusifuc-jeŋicte mâŋâŋzi ba bâsoriŋ â qac qârândiŋ moc mi enârezejec.
Aricne, nâŋâc dâŋfâri paŋšâic bajupene maŋjauŋ-nâŋeczi fua sawec ehame qizec-nâŋec Kristo erao šuhucke sanaŋkenšepeneŋ.
Erao šuhuckepene ruazi ŋeturec-nâporâ bândeŋ-nâpome ɋâɋâdoc erâ me sahac-ticne eeŋgopeneŋ. Ehuc tofafâc-ticne erâ tâpiri fonâreekac sâc gie bahuc maŋjauŋko soka sawec enaŋmu.
No Wofuŋte maio ŋaza-jâmbâŋkepe: Ŋoŋe qâpuc, maŋ mamanasu-jeŋic wiac jawanere foekac, jaŋere sâc mi junšepieŋ.
Jaŋe maŋjeŋic dapâc ekicnere mutuc â maŋsanaŋ erâ Anuture juju râpeckembiŋ.
Eme maŋjeŋic šickeme nânâ qowire nâ areŋ ehuc sasec mamakâc fuŋne fuŋne takicmâc ebac eeŋgopieŋ.
Ŋoŋe ine juju iŋucne juniŋte Kristore fuŋne mi qazu-ŋarekicne.
Ŋoŋe fuŋne-ticne qazu-ŋarekicko Jesurao dâŋfâri kecšiŋuc fokac i hâcne manambiŋ:
Qâpuc juju râpeckerâ maŋraŋɋa-ŋeŋic burec ehuc sasecko sipirickeekac, i heunuckenšepieŋ.
Erâ mâro manacnepie mamanasu-ŋeŋic heɋârehame
maŋɋâri hepie huzejec. I hâcne Anuture hawari iŋucne tiŋne â furu jâmbâŋ bâfuakicne.
Irec ŋoŋe burec beherâ dâŋ jâmbomac sasawa nazaŋ gazaŋ enšepieŋ, nâŋâc qoqomâ efâreŋgopeneŋte.
Kimbeŋko mi sâqorenšepieŋ. Kimbeŋ aaric mi bajuhapie šoaŋ ŋeutuckezejec.
Erâ Sataŋ mi mana uruecnenšepieŋ.
Fiuc rorozi fiuc qikiŋnerâ meticnezi gie šoɋac bahuc nânâ mafa bâfuarâ waha qaqane boki bajarezejec.
Dâŋ simbiŋne micŋeŋickonec mi wahazejec, dâŋ biaŋne sawa, ine dodopec eere hatane fuame mupie ŋic âgo bacjopazejec.
Anuture Tiri Mâro mi qaisockenšepieŋ, e hâcne roroc-nâpo dameŋko maqâreŋ-ŋeŋic eocte tahac-ŋopakicne.
Râsidâŋ, kimbeŋ aaric, mu ojowa, susurec, erâ wiac gâgâpâcne gâcne i ŋondeŋ-ŋeŋicko mi fuazejec.
Ŋoŋe ââgo erâ eehâmoc ehuc kiŋ bebehec enšepieŋ, Anutu e iŋuc jaha Kristore erâ kiŋŋeŋic behewec.
Ŋoŋe joroc naru motecfâcne juŋgopieŋzi Anutu sâckehuc junšepieŋ.
Erâ maŋjauŋhec junšepieŋ. Kristo e iŋuc jaha maŋjauŋ enârehuc nâŋâcnere erâ sahac-ticne qaisockerâ Anutu taha bâzi biaŋ ecnewec.
Boe sau, sasec mamakâc, buchâro, irec saŋuc wâc mitiŋic ŋoŋere ŋondeŋko mi fuazejec.
Dâŋ miminehec, mutucdâŋ, dâŋ simbiŋne, i epie sâqoreocmu. Daŋge mumuteŋ ine epie sâckeocmu.
Ŋoŋe šiŋuc mana sanaŋkenšepieŋ: Boe sau ŋic â sasec mamakâchec â buchâro, nemu qaŋgec ŋic hâcne, jaŋe Kristo â Anutu uucmaŋ-ticnao ŋeŋe basaniŋmu.
Eatuc-ŋopahuc siocdâŋ ŋazapie manapie fârine mi ezejec. Sâqocne iŋucnere hâcne Anuturaonec okacne qaqatara ŋic jaŋerao fuaocmu.
Irec ŋoŋe mi bafic-jopanšepieŋ.
Ŋoŋe mârâc jaha dapâchec jujumbieŋ, ši ine Wofuŋtao fisirâ tatamachec embiŋ juŋgopieŋ. Irec tatamacte ɋâricfâc erâ irec hawari junšepieŋ.
Tatamacte fârine fuaekac i maŋbiaŋhec juju â tiŋne ju ju â jâmbomac dâŋ mumu.
Wiac ezo murâ ine Wofuŋzi maname biaŋkeocmu me mâcne, i qanaŋ mana wosâerâ enšepieŋ.
Gâcnezi dapâcte wiac jawane epie mi qâsuec-jopanšepieŋ, aricne. Ŋoŋe irec tapa qararuŋkehuc qatara-jarenšepieŋ.
Wiac soŋsoŋko eeŋgopieŋ i mu bâuac epene miminehec jaha eocmu.
Wiac iŋucne tapane qararuŋkepene tatamaczi âeckeme fuaocmu. Eme tâtâc fuakac wiac izi wâc tatamac bâfuaocmu.
Irec hâcne šiŋuc mukicne: “Guŋ foekiczi faharec, â hâmockonec ɋârec, eme Kristozi batamaecguocmu.”
Ŋoŋe juju bapa-ŋeŋicte ruc bahuc junšepieŋ. Erâ mutuc matacne mâcne, maŋ mamanasuhec junšepieŋ.
Dameŋ šira sâqocnezi haŋ bawec fokacte dameŋ gâcne mi behehuc gie šoɋachec banšepieŋ.
Maŋ tâmiric tinac mi junšepieŋ, Wofuŋzi gie muŋareekac i hone šâŋitac enšepieŋ.
Waiŋ opâ wiacte âmbâŋ mi enšepieŋ, izi maŋ sisipiric gie. Mârore ine âmbâŋ enšepieŋ.
Mârozi esoc-ŋopaocmu sâc gae mânec hehuc maŋ nareŋ gareŋ enšepieŋ. Á maŋŋeŋicko Wofuŋ gaezi â musizi mu šeri ecnenšepieŋ.
Erâ Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristore erâ dameŋ sâc Anutu Mamac wiac fuŋne fuŋnere daŋge mumuteŋ ecnenšepieŋ.
Ŋoŋe Kristo araŋ bacnehuc micrereŋ eec efârenšepieŋ.
Ŋonâŋ ŋoŋe Wofuŋte rereŋfâc juŋgopieŋ iŋuc jaha ŋowefâc-ŋeŋic jaŋere junšepieŋ.
Ŋowezi ŋonâŋte qizec ekac hâcne, iŋuc jaha Kristozi kikefuŋte qizec ekac, ehuc me sahac-ticnere bâbâpiaŋ wâc ekac.
Eme kikefuŋzi Kristore mic reŋkeekac, iŋuc jaha ŋonâŋ jaŋe ŋowefâc-jeŋic jaŋere mic dameŋ sâc reŋkenšepieŋ.
Ŋowe ŋoŋe ŋonâŋfâc-ŋeŋic maŋjauŋ ejarenšepieŋ. Kristo e iŋuc jaha kikefuŋ-ticne maŋjauŋ ecnehuc ere due bawec.
Erâ kikiruhucne â sâfânehec â wâc wiac gâcnehec juzacte mitidâŋzi opâ umbiŋkeha šurehuc jambuŋkerâ
ericke bâpiaŋ ecnerâ e jahacne biŋe furu â bahacmâc juocte mucnewec.
Eme ŋowe jaŋe jaŋacne sahac jauŋ bacneeŋgopieŋ, sâc ijaha ŋonâŋfâc-jeŋic bajarenšepieŋ. Moc e ŋonâŋ-ticne maŋjauŋ ecnehuc e jahacne sahac mâmâc ecneocmu.
Ŋic moczi moc sahac-ticne râsi mi eecne, gume jauŋ ecnehuc jaha juekac, Kristozi kikefuŋ ecnehuc juekac iŋuc”
nâŋâc me sahac-ticnere tofafâc juŋgopeneŋ hâcne.
“Irec hâcne ŋic moczi neŋgoc mamac jahec-ticne behec-jofarâ ŋonâŋ-ticnerao qohotame jahe maŋ sahac mocjaha erâ junicmu.”
I dâŋ soŋne, qame hukicne. Ine Kristo â Kikefuŋ jahere muhuc mukopac.
Ŋoŋe ine ŋic sasawa sahac-ŋeŋic jauŋ baeŋgopieŋ sâc ijaha ŋonâŋfâc-ŋeŋic jauŋ bacjopanšepieŋ. Á ŋokac ine ŋowefâc-ŋeŋic araŋ bajarenšepieŋ.
Naru motec ŋoŋe Wofuŋte erâ neŋgoc mamacfâc-ŋeŋic jaŋere dâŋ reŋkenšepieŋ. Izi hata biaŋne.
“Go neŋgoc mamac jahecge sâsec-jofazemec”, i sâcmutâc dâŋ fekicne, erâ biŋedâŋ-ticne šiŋuc šuhuckerâ mukicne:
“Iŋuc erâ mâreŋko dameŋ šora juhâc qâhâmocmu.”
Mamac ŋoŋe naru motecfâc-ŋeŋic aaric bâfuanšipiŋte wiac kosa mi ejarenšepieŋ. Ŋoŋe mitio jaza bâtiŋ â uŋ sawaŋ ejarehuc soŋaŋ-jopahapie sokanšepieŋ.
Kiŋaŋ qaqa ŋoŋe mâreŋ ŋicbomboŋfâc-ŋeŋic araŋ bajarehuc, maŋŋeŋiczi qâzuc foha, Kristo ecneŋgopieŋ tinac, mana mezac ehuc micjeŋic reŋkenšepieŋ.
Ŋoŋe ŋicbomboŋfâc-ŋeŋic maizi qambaraŋ ejarepie honec-ŋopapie biaŋkeocte mâcne, nâŋe Kristore kiŋaŋ qaqa, iŋuc muhuc Anutuzi hata muwec i maŋafec jaha âtenšepieŋ.
Ŋic jaŋere manasuhuc aricne, Wofuŋte manasuhuc gie-ŋeŋic tatakic tâmiric banšepieŋ.
Ŋoŋe manaeŋgopieŋ, moc e kiŋaŋ qaqa me ŋicbomboŋ juhuc wiac biaŋne ehuc juocmu, e Wofuŋzi okacne sâc ijaha bazucneocmu.
Erâ ŋicbomboŋ ŋoŋe kiŋaŋ qaqafâc-ŋeŋic iŋuc jaha ehâmo-jarenšepieŋ, ehuc mu imac mi ejarenšepieŋ. Erâ šiŋuc mananšepieŋ: Kiŋaŋ qaqa â ŋicbomboŋ ine sambâŋko Wofuŋ wirec-ŋeŋic jukac, e ra rowec ware rowec mi focnekac.
Mutarahuc mupe: Wofuŋtao roweckepie tâpiri sâko-ticnezi ŋoŋerao fotâcneme qaboc-ŋeŋichec junšepieŋ.
Erâ Anuturaonec sându maro šika wiac ro barâ juhapie Sataŋzi rucko râsi fisi-ŋareme hâbi-ŋeŋic rorâ jâpenšepieŋ.
Ŋoŋe manaŋgopieŋ, nâŋâc râsi sahac biuchec jaŋehec šika qaqa mi eeŋgopeneŋ, aricne, ŋicbomboŋ sâko â momori sanaŋ, dameŋ ši dapâc fokac irec guriŋ bapa, demoŋ sâqocne sambâŋ rurumaŋko jueŋgopieŋ, jaŋe râsi enâreeŋgopieŋ.
Irec Anuturaonec sându maro šika wiac ro bajuhuc šika dameŋko qiŋ herâ domahapie râsi jaŋe bâipiec-ŋoparâ wisenšepieŋ.
Ŋoŋe kecšiŋuc domanšepieŋ: Dâŋ fâri qizecnezi umbika-ŋeŋic eme jomanšepieŋ, kiŋfâsâczi maruku-ŋeŋic eme rufanšepieŋ,
wamare Biŋebiaŋ bašawiehuc badomanšepieŋ, izi kikehuhu hepie hume âte sanaŋkeŋgopieŋ ezejec.
Erâ neŋgocne sâko ine mamanasiŋzi maro-ŋeŋic eme dameŋ sâc he bâfeŋnerâ domahapie sâqocne runere šoc tepe moteczi kisowarierâ hâpozejec.
Erâ wâc aeŋdu šâŋene bâbâpiaŋ hepie huzejec, â Mâroraonec šika, Anuture dâŋ hâcne, i bajunšepieŋ.
Ŋoŋe šâfo sâc Mârore tâpirio Wofuŋ šušuhuc jaha numucnehuc wâsickenšepieŋ, erâ qâoma mi ehuc rucjaric-ŋeŋic banšepieŋ, erâ hae sâc mitiŋic guru jaŋere nunumu gie banšepieŋ wâc.
Erâ nore mâmâc numuhuc jupie Wofuŋzi micnane baafeckeme Biŋebiaŋ soŋsoŋ fowec i asa feferaŋko mutaniŋkezepac.
No irec biŋe mumu kâpâcwâruo foekopaczi hâhâwic tâmiric mutaniŋkepe sâckezejec.
Juju-nanere fuŋne â gie baekopac i kâuc banšipiŋte Tikikozi fârâ dâŋ binaŋ eŋare-fâreocmu, e âgo biaŋ-nâŋec â Wofuŋte kiŋaŋ qaqa micrereŋhec.
Eki nâŋere dâŋ binaŋ eŋarehuc bubiaŋ qaŋareocte sorepe fakac hâcne.
Anutu Mamac â Wofuŋ Jesu Kristo eki âgofâc-nane ŋoŋe wama bâfua-ŋarehuc mamanasiŋ-ŋeŋic basanaŋkeme maŋjauŋhec junšepieŋ.
Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristo erao qohota sanaŋkeeŋgopieŋ ŋoŋerao aki anonoczi fozejec.
Paulo â Timoteo, Jesu Kristore kiŋaŋ qaqa, nâhe Filipi haeonec Kristo Jesure mitiŋic ŋokac â soŋaŋ babafic ŋoŋere papia ši râekoperec.
Mamac-nâŋec Anutu â Wofuŋ Jesu Kristo eraonec aki anonoc â wama ŋoŋerao fotâcnerâ fozejec.
No ŋoŋere manasuhuc Sâc Anutu-nane daŋge âzâcneekopac.
Ŋoŋe Biŋebiaŋ manahuc izia nâŋehec qâturerâ giene bawarehuc jumbiŋ,
eme irec numuekopac sâc mâmâc-ŋeŋicte bubiaŋ manahuc Wofuŋ daŋge numumu ecneekopac.
Erâ šiŋuc manapaŋkekopac, gie biaŋ ŋoŋerao fuŋkeweczi baku bataraha Jesu Kristo fifisi dameŋ-ticne maickezokac.
No ŋoŋe sasawa iŋuc mana-ŋarekopac i fuŋne šiŋucte sâckekac: No šira kâpâcwâru ficko Biŋebiaŋte erâ dâŋgie bahuc feŋeŋ râecnepe ŋoŋe sasawa baficnuhuc ŋesiŋ ŋenareeŋgopieŋ” eme no irec hâcne maŋnanezi šâfic-ŋopaekopac.
Jesu Kristozi maŋjauŋ enâreekac ira hesiŋnehuc no ŋoŋere erâ maŋhâhâŋ boc enareekac, i Anutuzi manaha jâmbomac mukopac.
Erâ maŋjauŋ-ŋeŋiczi maŋ mamanasu â mamana wosâc-ŋeŋic bâsoka raocte numuhuc juekopac.
Eme ŋoŋe wiac fâri wâmbuŋne hone šâŋitac erâ Kristo fifisi-ticnere manasuhuc maŋtaniŋ â bahacmâc junšepieŋ,
ehuc Jesu Kristozi hume keteŋ eŋareme mitire fârine mâririhec bâfuapie Anuture šeri mumuteŋ ezejec.
Âgofâc-nane, kâuc banšipiŋte ŋazape, no šira wiac fua-narewec izi Biŋebiaŋ hatacke hâmoocte fuawec.
No Kristore erâ kâpâcwâru ŋic epo, dâŋ izi šira kia â momori â ŋic gâcne jaŋere hazecko hufârewec.
Eme kâpâcwâruo ŋehape širecnec âgofâc-nâŋec gâcne sâko jaŋe Wofuŋte manasuhuc afeckerâ Anuture dâŋ hâhâwic tâmiric mueŋgopieŋ.
Tucne Kristore miti i iiŋguuŋko â hehefaricko mueŋgopieŋ, â tucnezi ine buurucko mueŋgopieŋ.
I jaŋe mueŋgopieŋ ine no šira fohuc Biŋebiaŋ ŋezickeekopac irec maŋjauŋ enarehuc mueŋgopieŋ,
â gâcnezi ine sioc ehuc iiriacko Kristore šâŋe muromackeeŋgopieŋ, i kâpâcwâru-nanere faio bušâic bâfua-nareniŋte eeŋgopieŋ.
Erâ iŋuc me iŋuc, miti qâtiŋ ehuc muniŋmu me jâmbomacko muniŋmu irec wemocte boc muzo, mâc Kristore dâŋzi haŋ baocmu izi fârine, eme i fuakacte bunane biaŋkekac.
Erâ šiŋuc muhuc bubiaŋ hati jupemu: Ŋoŋe nore erâ nunumu gie bapie Jesu Kristore Mârozi baficnume wiac kecšizi bubiaŋ bâfua-nareocmu.
Erâ mimi mi bâfuapemu, i manapaŋkepe šickeha maŋzi worickehuc jupemu. Ewarepo iŋuc erapemu, jujure me hâhâmore sahac-nane maŋafec jaha Kristo qikiŋnecnepe izi mumuteŋ-ticne ezejec.
Kristozi juju-nane ekac â hâmoczi wiac fekicne bâfua-nareocmu.
Me mâreŋko šuhuckerâ jupemu, ine giere fârine mocwâc bâfuapemu. Irec wenimoire afeckepe muhuc maŋguru ekopac.
No mocte â mocte mâmâc enarekac. Mâreŋ beherâ Kristo bâfuarâ ehec juju irec aŋacnukac, izi hâcne wiac fekicne.
Á ŋoŋe bekâ enšipiŋte ine ŋoŋere erâ mâreŋko mocwâc šuhuckerâ jupe sâckeocmu.
Eme irec hâcne šiŋuc manapaŋkekopac: No mi hâhâmo ŋoŋehec jupemu, erâ bafic-ŋopape mamanasiŋ-ŋeŋic ɋârâŋkeme bubiaŋhec junšepieŋ.
Á ŋoŋerao mocwâc fârâ jupe nore erâ Jesu Kristo muteŋkeeŋgopieŋzi hati erâ muteŋkenšepieŋ.
Mocjaha, ŋoŋe kikefuŋte maio Kristore furu Biŋebiaŋ irec sâcko junšepieŋ. Erâ maŋ mocjaha ehuc šâšâfic erâ keketeŋ domahuc Biŋebiaŋte juju gie bapie fârâ honec-ŋopazepac, me taicko juhuc biŋe-ŋeŋic manazepac.
Keketeŋ epie kisâfâc-ŋeŋic hâhâwic heŋarepie hâbi-ŋeŋic mi goroŋkezejec. Iŋuc epie Anutuzi jaŋe behec-jopaocmu â ŋoŋe rocŋopaocmu irec fuŋne bataniŋkeocmu.
Anutuzi Kristo wiac ecneniŋte mana-ŋarewec i manasiŋkeniŋte sawa mâcne, ere erâ šâic fâro faio juniŋte mâmâc mana-ŋarewec.
Eme no mârâcko juju gie bape honecnumbiŋ â šiŋuczia bape biŋene manaeŋgopieŋ, juju gie ijaha ŋoŋe baeŋgopieŋ.
Ŋoŋerao Kristore erâ sawaŋ qaqac me maŋjauŋko muketeŋ, me Mârohec šâšâfic, me miriŋ â buuruc, wiac i sasawa fokacko
bubiaŋ-nane ferâ foocte mamanasu-ŋeŋic qâturenšepieŋ, erâ maŋzi šâšâfic ehuc mocjaha efârerâ wiac irecteaŋ henširiŋnehuc junšepieŋ.
Ŋoŋe hehefaricko â sahac mumuteŋko wiac mi enšepieŋ, moc e jahacne maŋ bawahahuc âgofâcne jaŋere maname fezejec.
Erâ moc e jahacne wiac embiaŋkeocte sawa mâcne, âgofâcne jaŋere fua biaŋ eocte mâmâc manasuzejec.
Kristo Jesure maŋ mamanasu fowec, iŋuc jaha ŋoŋerezi fozejec.
E Anutu juju juweczi ine, Anuture sâcko juekopac weniŋuc behepemu, iŋuc muhuc mi sakarewec.
Aricne, e juju-ticne hetararâ kiŋaŋ qaqa hawari rohuc ŋic iŋucne fuawec, â eebapa-ticne honepie ŋic nâŋâcne sâc ewec.
E wahakicne erâ juhuc micrereŋte hata âte raku hâmoc maickewec, maripoŋko hâmoc hâcne.
Iŋuc ewecte Anutuzi bafehuc fekicne sâko âkendâŋnewec. Âkendâŋnerâ šâŋe biŋe-ticne fuŋmoc izi haŋ bahuc ŋic šâŋe biŋe getâcke-fâreocte mucnewec.
Eme sambâŋko â mâreŋko â mâreŋ jujuwicnao jueŋgopieŋ jaŋe šeŋgoma Jesure šâŋe muhuc dieŋzi hecnenšepieŋ
â micne mic sâc Jesu Kristo e Wofuŋ jukac iŋuc musereckenšepieŋ. Eme mumuteŋ izi Anutu Mamacte biŋe ezejec.
Jorocfâc-nane, ŋoŋe dameŋ sâc micrereŋ eeŋgopieŋ, ŋoŋehec juhape sawa mâcne, taicko juhape wâc ejâmbâŋkeeŋgopieŋ, irec bâbâpiaŋ-ŋeŋicte fârine bâfuaniŋte mezac-ŋopaha fotac qatarienšepieŋ.
Anutu e jahac hâcne, honec-ŋopame biaŋkeocte aafecke mecne fârine bâbâfua mecne irec tâpiri ŋareekac.
Ŋoŋe wiac sasawa kâroŋ â maŋguru tâmiric enšepieŋ.
Erâ bahacmâc â maŋtaniŋ junšepieŋ, ehuc ŋicguru bac bâŋoricne â qaqaharicne jaŋere dapâc ŋondeŋko Anuture naru motecfâc maŋɋaɋac erâ juhuc bâpiŋ iŋucne tamaenšepieŋ.
Tamaehuc jujure dâŋ paŋnea bajunšepieŋ. Iŋuc epie juku Kristo fifisi dameŋ-ticnao, šâic mi mana-bipiepo â gie mi bâipiepo, irec fuŋne taniŋkeme šeri bubiaŋ manazepac.
No mamanasiŋ-ŋeŋic Anutu taha bacnehuc sahac-nane due bapemuo sifu irec šeri ehuc ŋoŋehec bubiaŋ manapemu.
Á ŋoŋe iŋuc jaha šeri ehuc nohec bubiaŋ mananšepieŋ.
Wofuŋ Jesuzi maname sâckeme Timoteo biac ŋoŋerao sorepe fâocte mukopac. Eme ŋoŋere dâŋ biŋe moc risie wareme manarâ bunane mâteŋkezejec.
Ŋic e iŋucne moc mi junareŋgopieŋ, eki jâmbomac ŋoŋere manoniehuc maŋticnezi dopec-ŋopaocmu.
Ŋic gâcne jaŋe jaŋacnere sawa manasuhuc Jesu Kristo gie-ticnere mi mueŋgopieŋ.
Timoteo ine juju-ticnere fuŋne manaeŋgopieŋ, ŋokâzi mamac-ticne bafickeekac iŋuc jaha no Biŋebiaŋte giere baficnuekac.
Eme no nahacnao wiac iŋuc me iŋuc fuaocmu i mana-hâmorâ e hâcne biac sorepe fâocmu.
Erâ Wofuŋzi mana-nareme no nahac wâc mi šoraha ŋoŋerao fâpemu, iŋuc manakopac.
No wiac basahuc juhape ŋoŋe Epafodito sorepie ware dope hutuŋ enarewec, ehuc qomâ-nane â babafic-nane â momori âgo-nane juekac, e sifu bârisie-ŋarezo mukopac.
E huc bame biŋene manambiŋ, eme ere manabâc enšipiŋte ŋoŋere maŋhâhâŋ ecnekac.
E huc ŋemâcne bame hâmozo ewec. Anutuzi ine ehâmocnewec, erâ e sawa mâcne, norao busâqoczi busâqoc fuazacte no mâmâc ehâmo-narewec.
Ŋoŋe honerâ buŋeŋic biaŋkeocte â no iŋuc jaha manabâc tâmiric jupemurâ e mi sakarehuc šiŋuczia râepe fakac.
Irec fâme bubiaŋ manacnehuc Wofuŋte erâ âgo ecnenšepieŋ. Ŋoŋe ŋic iŋucne hâcne sâsec-jopanšepieŋ.
E Kristore giere erâ hâmozo ewec. Ŋoŋere okacne kiŋaŋ qanareocte sahac-ticne qaisockewec.
Âgofâc-nane, moc mupe. Wofuŋte erâ bubiaŋhec junšepieŋ. Dâŋ hâsine ijaha qâreŋke-ŋarezore manape mi quŋkekac, â ŋoŋe ine hume keteŋ eŋarezejec.
Ŋoŋe qâto jaŋere rucsoŋaŋ junšepieŋ, miti gie bapa bâbâsifucne, sahac hehetâc ŋic jaŋere rucsoŋaŋ hâcne junšepieŋ.
Anutu maŋzi kiŋaŋ qacneeŋgopeneŋ â Kristo Jesurao qohotaeŋgopeneŋ â mamanasiŋ-nâŋec sahacko mi râeeŋgopeneŋ, nâŋâc hâcne ma fârine bajueŋgopeneŋ.
No nahac sahacko siŋkezo murâ sâcne ezapo. Ŋic gâcne jaŋe sahacko siŋkeeŋgopieŋ no ijaha ezo murâ siric-jopazapo.
No fuarâ fohape šoaŋ 8 eme sahac-naneo ma bambiŋ, no Israe ŋicguruonec, Benjamiŋte ɋâric, no Judaŋiczi Judaŋic jaŋeraonec fuakicne hâcne, sâcmutâc dâŋte neŋgocne farisaio ŋic jupo,
šoɋac-nanere erâ kikefuŋ jaŋere râsi epo, sâcmutâc dâŋ sâcko tiŋne juju â bahacmâc jupo.
Eme no mârâc wiac bajuhuc manape fârine ewec, i šâhec ine Kristore erâ manape racne ewec.
No Wofuŋ-nane Kristo Jesu ere fuŋne hone šâŋitâc erâ manape furi sâko eme wiac mârâc epo bapo irec jâmbomac manape racne eekac. No Kristo rauckepemurâ ere erâ wiac sasawa ho jawa muhuc qikiŋne-fârepo.
No erao qohotahuc, sâcmutâc reŋkehuc kiŋfâsâc bâbâfua i mâcne. Kristo manasiŋkehuc kiŋfâsâc juju irec enareekac. Mamanasiŋhec jupe Anutuzi kiŋnanere maname tatara, irec mukopac.
Erâ no Kristo maŋzi hemiriŋkepe fafahare-ticnere tâpiri norao fuame šâic manawecko šuhuckerâ ehec manazepac. Eku hâmoc-ticnere hawari wâc bâfuazepac.
Iŋuc eerâ raku hâmockonec fafahare bâfuapere enareekac.
No nahacnere šiŋuc mi mukopac: Biac mao fisirâ eri bâfuapo. Mâc Kristo Jesuzi no rocnuwecte eri bâfuapemurâ hata gagasa i gasackeekopac
Âgofâc-nane, eri biac bâfuarâ ropo, i no nahacnere manape iŋuc mi ekac Kecšiŋuc ine eekopac: Wiac hetarapo i râpeckeekopac, â wiac mai-naneo râekicne irec menane sicneekopac,
ehuc Anutuzi Jesu Kristore erâ sambâŋte hefârecnuhuc mao eri râe-narewec, i bâfuapemurâ šâŋezi hone dendeŋnehuc gasackeekopac.
Soka tarakicne nâŋâc mâmâc sasawa wiac irecteaŋ hâcne henširiŋnehuc junšepeneŋ. Eme wiac mocte manapie hatane moc ekacko Anutuzi maŋŋeŋic batamaeme mana taraniŋmu.
Mâc hata âte warembeŋ ijaha âte ranšepeneŋ.
Âgofâc-nane bânie-ŋarepe honecnuhuc ijaha bâjâpecnunšepieŋ. Á ŋic gâcne sâc ijaha juhuc bânie-ŋareeŋgopieŋ jaŋerao wâc šâŋe fihuc junšepieŋ.
Ŋic tucne jaŋere ŋaza warehuc jupo, ši ine ki busâqochec mocwâc ŋazape: Jaŋe Kristo maripoŋ-ticne râsi ecneeŋgopieŋ.
Ŋic i jaŋe hâcne sisipiric bâfuaniŋmu. Hobu-jeŋiczi wofuŋ ejareekac, â wiac mimineheczi bubiaŋ qajareekac, â mâreŋkonec wiac maŋ mamanasu-jeŋic rofâreekac.
Nâŋâc ine sambâŋ hae irec fârine, eme irecnec hâcne bâbâpiaŋ-nâŋec Wofuŋ Jesu Kristo, e waharâ rocnâpoocte woŋec jueŋgopeneŋ.
E ŋic â wiac sasawa bawahac-joparâ jahacne rurumaŋko guruc-jopaocte tâpiri focnekac, tâpiri izi sahac-nâŋec waha qaqane bâtikieme e jahacne sahac iŋucne tatamac huririnehec eocmu.
Âgo biaŋfâc-nane, maŋnane ŋoŋere boc ecneekac, ŋoŋe hâcne eri bubiaŋfâc-nane, ŋoŋe Wofuŋtao qohota sanaŋkenšepieŋ, jorocfâc-mae.
Euodia â Sintike ŋokac jahec jahe Wofuŋte erâ maŋ mocjaha erâ juzepirec.
Á babafic fâri-nane go ine ŋokac jahec hâcne hone maiŋ ejactezemec. Jahe mecne â Kelemento â âgo gâcne jaŋe Biŋebiaŋte giere dopecnumbiŋ. Ʒâŋe-jeŋic juju sanaŋte papia qizecko fofârekac.
Ŋoŋe Wofuŋte erâ šeri bubiaŋ manahuc junšepieŋ, no harierâ mupe, šeri bubiaŋ mananšepieŋ.
Wofuŋzi bâqiŋ-nâpokacte ŋic sasawa wamane ejarenšepieŋ.
Wiac irec me irec mana mezac mi ee maŋŋeŋicte dâŋ fuŋne fuŋne i Anutu daŋge nunumu ecnehuc mutaniŋkecnenšepieŋ.
Eme Anuture wama e ŋic mamana sirickeekaczi maŋ mamanasu-ŋeŋic qâzuckeme Kristore fosanaŋkeocmu.
Erâ âgofâc, dâŋ moc mupe: Wiac fârine â wiac araŋ bapanehec, wiac tiŋne â wiac ɋaɋacne, wiac hohone šiziwene â wiac mamana šiziwene, wiac eesaricne â wiac bubiaŋ bâbâfuane, wiac i sasaware henširiŋnehuc junšepieŋ.
No wiac mu qazuc â ŋaza ŋowatuc epe hone manac embiŋ, ijaha ehuc jupie Anutu wama runezi ŋoŋehec juocmu.
Ŋoŋe ŋondeŋne moc mâc juwareku ši nore mocwâc manasurâ buafec-ŋeŋicte ehâmo-narembiŋ, irec manape Wofuŋtao qacneme bubiaŋ kâcɋene manakopac. Ŋoŋe nore mamanasu i manasumbiŋ, mâc wiac enareniŋte hata basarâ quŋkembiŋ.
No kâroŋ qaŋarehuc mi mukopac, no wiac i me i basarâ mâc juhuc manape mi sâqoreekac.
No qafec qawahac juju me fofo dunduŋ fonareha juju, iŋuc me iŋuc juzo murâ sâcne jupemu. Nâ gapehec juju â natac qatac juju, mâriri faio juju â roroc faio juju, irec fuŋne mâmâc manaekopac.
Tâpiri nareme sanaŋkeekopac, ere erâ jupe bape sâcke-fâreekac.
Ŋoŋe ine busâqocko juhape ehâmo-narembiŋte manape biaŋkekac.
Filipi haeonec ŋic ŋokac ŋoŋe manaŋgopieŋ, no Biŋebiaŋte gie fufuŋke dameŋko Makedonia mâreŋ behepoo kikefuŋ gâcnezi mâc juhapie ŋoŋe buc nohec nareŋ gareŋ embeŋ.
Erâ Tesalonike haeo juhape sahacte wiaczi dopecnuhuc jumbiŋ wâc.
No moneŋ mafare mi mukopac, mâc miti-ŋeŋicte fârine fuaocte mukopac, eme fârine izi ŋoŋeraopec hamârekao hâcne.
Ʒi wiac bâfuacnu-fârewec, bocjaha fonarekac. Epafoditozi ŋoŋeraonec wiac bafisi-nareme mâririhec epo jukopac. Ŋoŋe no wiac enarembiŋ, irec manape Wofuŋ taha bâzi biaŋ âsu mumundoŋnehec ecnembiŋ ekac.
Anutu-nane e mâriri bâbâfuazi Kristo Jesure erâ wiac hezu heŋareme hâmoc huriaŋ tâmiric juniŋmu.
Anutu Mamac-nâŋec erao ine mumuteŋzi mumuteŋ forašihuc juzejec sanaŋ. Jâmbomac.
No Kristo Jesure erâ manasuc-ŋopakopac, i mitiŋic ŋokac jaza-fârenšepieŋ. Á âgofâc-nane nohec juŋgopieŋ jaŋe wâc manasuc-ŋopaŋgopieŋ.
Mitiŋic sasawa â Sisare ŋicfâc jaŋe wâc boc manasuc-ŋopaŋgopieŋ.
Wofuŋ Jesu Kristo ere aki anonoczi maŋ qâqâtâc-ŋeŋicko fofârezejec. Jâmbomac.
Paulo no Anuture micte Jesu Kristore aposolo epo, erâ âgo-nâŋec Timoteo,
nâhe Kolosai haeonec mitiŋic â âgofâc-nâhec Kristorao qohotaŋgopieŋ ŋoŋe papia ši râe-ŋarekoperec. Anutu Mamac-nâŋec eraonec aki anonoc â wama ŋoŋerao fotâcnerâ fozejec.
Nâŋe Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristo ere Mamac Anutu hâcne ŋoŋere erâ dameŋ sâc daŋge nunumu ecneeŋgopeneŋ.
Ŋoŋe Kristo Jesu manasiŋkeeŋgopieŋ â mitiŋic hae gâcnaonec maŋjauŋ ejareeŋgopieŋ irec mecne,
â sambâŋ miti šeŋaŋ ŋoŋere biŋe râekicne irec mâmâc Anutu muteŋkeeŋgopeneŋ. Ŋoŋe miti šeŋaŋte kâuc mi baeŋgopieŋ. Dâŋ fâri qizecne Biŋebiaŋ hâcne ŋoŋerao fuawec irec biŋe mârâc manambiŋ.
Biŋebiaŋ i mâreŋ sâc fua bâbâriŋ rahuc fârinehec eekac. Eme Anutu akidâŋ-ticne ŋoŋerao fâme jâmbomacko mana maŋ embiŋ, dameŋ ira ŋoŋerao iŋuc jaha fârinehec ewec.
Joroc âgo babafic-nâŋec Epafara, Kristore kiŋaŋ qaqa micrereŋhec, eki qazu-ŋareme manambiŋ hâcne.
Erâ ekizia wâc, Mârozi ŋoŋerao maŋjauŋ bâfuawec, irec dâŋ binaŋ enârewec.
Eme nâŋe dâŋ binaŋ-ŋeŋic manarâ izia fuŋkerâ Anutuzi maŋ mamana-ŋeŋic bâsokame micdâŋ-ticnere â Mârore maŋɋârâŋ dâŋ mana taraniŋte numucne warehuc jueŋgopeneŋ.
Wofuŋzi iŋuc hâcne eŋareme ju ju-ŋeŋiczi fuŋne-ticne mutaniŋkeme honec-ŋopame biaŋkezejec. Á mitio gie fuŋne fuŋne fokac, i bahuc irec fârine bâfuanšepieŋ, ehuc Anuture fuŋne mana ɋârâŋke rahuc junšepieŋ.
Erâ Anuture tâpiri mu wawarec-ticnehec izi âkesiŋ-ŋopame hâbi sâko hepie hume juhapie fai-ŋeŋicko wiac ŋemâcne feme sâc docke pârâc tâmiric bumâteŋ jaha de domahuc bubiaŋ mananšepieŋ.
Erâ Mamac-nâŋec e faic tatamacko merâfâc-ticne râe-nârewec, i mitiŋic nâŋâc ru sâc enaŋte bâmoc-nâpoekacte buafec jaha daŋge âzâcnenšepeneŋ.
Anutu e dâpac runere tâpirionec batarac-nâporâ joroc Ŋokâ-ticnere uucmaŋko râec-nâpowec.
Ŋokâ-ticne eki hâcne sâqocne-nâŋec tâmireote kiwiric-nâŋec rowec.
Anutu soŋne ere hawari tâtâc fufua Ŋokâ-ticne hâcne. E wiac sasawa mi fuahame micne barâ juweczi juwec.
Ere jujuo wiac sasawa sambâŋko â mâreŋko fua-fârewec, wiac hohonene â mi hohonene, ŋic me aŋelo ɋuŋɋasaŋhec me tâpirihec, fekicne sâko me araŋ bapa-jarene, i mâmâc sasawa ere tâpirio â ere biŋe fuakicne.
E wiac sasawa irec juwicnao juwec erâ wiac sasawa irec micne sâko, erâ wiac sasawa ere dope sisiŋko fowarehuc juekac.
Erâ e me sahac-ticne, kikefuŋ-ticne hâcne, nâŋâcne qizec juekac. Erâ fufuŋke ŋic, hâmockonec micne barâ faharewec, ehuc wiac sasawa irec jâcne ewec.
Anutu e juju â tâpiri-ticnere rowaŋ Ŋokârao guru fufusuc foocte maname sâckewec.
Erâ wiac sasawa sambâŋko â mâreŋko Anutu jahacnehec miriŋ bacnâpoocte mucneme eki hâcne maripoŋko socticnezi wama bâfuahuc iŋuc ewec.
Ŋoŋe mârâc jaha Anutu râpeckerâ nâme nikecne erâ sâqocne fuŋne fuŋne bahuc maŋšârâhec jujumbieŋ.
Eme Kristo sahac biuchec fuarâ hâmoc-ticnezi miriŋ bacŋoparâ Anuture maio furu â maŋɋaɋac â bahac fâsâc juniŋte râec-ŋopawec.
Eme irec ŋoŋe mamanasiŋko qiŋ herâ domahuc, Biŋebiaŋzi woworic bâfua-ŋarewec i sifucke-ŋarezacte biric borocne mi enšepieŋ. Biŋebiaŋ i ŋoŋe qazu-ŋarekicne, erâ ŋoŋe sawa mâcne, ŋicne ŋicne mâreŋ sâc jaza rakicne. Paulo no hâcne irec kiŋaŋŋic juekopac.
No ŋoŋere erâ šâic serereŋ faio juekopac irec ši manape biaŋkeekac. Kristozi me sahac-ticne, kikefuŋ-ticne hâcne, ere erâ šâic serereŋ manawec, šâic irec tofanao šuhuckehuc mamanane fokacte nore sahacko fehuc micne qazejec.
No Anutu dâŋbiri-ticnere sâcko kikefuŋte kiŋaŋ qaqa erâ ŋoŋerao micdâŋ-ticnere qaqazu gie batarapemurâ munarekicne.
Dâŋ i dameŋne dameŋne soŋne fome mimiŋzi ɋâric mi mamana mâc juwefuhuc jumbiŋ, eme dameŋ šiŋuczia ine mitiŋicfâc-ticne mufua-nârekicne.
Erâ qâpuc jaŋerao dâŋ soŋnere mâriri biaŋ sâko fuakac i mitiŋicfâc-ticne mutaniŋke-nârekac. Kristo maŋŋeŋicko juekac e hâcne dâŋ soŋnere fârine â sambâŋ šeŋaŋ irec hozine.
Ere fuŋne mutaniŋkehuc ŋicne ŋicne uŋ sawaŋ ejarerâ maŋɋârâŋ dâŋ sasawa jaza qazuc eeŋgopeneŋ, i Kristoo ŋic fârine epie erao guruc-jopanaŋte iŋuc eeŋgopeneŋ.
Ere tâpirizi eferenšoŋnume gie i hâcne fotariehuc baekopac.
No ŋazape mananiŋ, ŋoŋe mecne â Laodikea haeonec â ŋic gâcne šâŋe mai-nane mi honembiŋ, ŋoŋere šâic afecne mi manaekopac.
Ŋoŋe maŋŋeŋiczi âte tâcnerâ roroc efâreme Anutu dâŋsoŋ-ticnere fuŋne, Kristo hâcne, mana maŋ ehuc mana utuckerâ mana taranšepieŋ.
Erao hâcne maŋɋârâŋ â mamana tara irec šâkâŋne soŋkekicne fokac.
Moczi moc mu hemiriŋ eŋarehuc maŋ bâsifuc eŋarenšipiŋte dâŋ mukopac.
No sahac-nanezi wiwicko juekopac, maŋnanezi ine ŋoŋehec juhuc ŋoŋe Kristo manasiŋkehuc šišimic erâ sosoŋaŋko domapie honec-ŋoparâ bunane biaŋkekac.
Ŋoŋe Kristo Jesu Wofuŋ eŋareocte rombiŋ erao qohotahuc junšepieŋ,
ehuc eraoa gâtâ barâ fua-hâmonšepieŋ, â mamanasiŋte hata ŋaza ŋowatuc ekicne ijaha âte sanaŋkerâ daŋge mumuteŋ ecnehuc jupie ferâ fe ehuc fozejec.
Moczi moc ŋickonec mamana dâŋ, eeatuc dâŋ racne hâcne, qazu-ŋarehuc maŋŋeŋic bawisenšipiŋte rucŋeŋic banšepieŋ. Dâŋ iŋucne i mimiŋne jaŋere maŋko fuac dâŋ â mâreŋte wiac tâpirihec ira roweckehuc mueŋgopieŋ, Kristorao siŋkehuc mâcne.
Manaŋgopieŋ, Anuture sâc i Kristo maŋ sahac-ticnao qaja fuserâ qâniniwerâ fokac.
Irec ŋoŋe erao wiac moc mi basaniŋmu, eki hâcne micne â fekicne sasawa jaŋere qizecne.
Eraonec maŋeŋic wâc rombiŋ, mezi sahacko ma bapa i mâcne, juju-ŋeŋic raŋɋane heunuckehuc Kristore maqâreŋhec embiŋ hâcne.
Ihec eniŋte Miti Opâ rua-ŋarehuc ere hâmocko šuhuc-ŋopakicne, erâ Anutu e tâpiri-ticnezi Kristo hâmockonec bâɋârewec, tâpiri ijaha manasiŋkepie ŋoŋerao fotâcneme fafahare-ticnao wâc šuhuc-ŋopakicne.
Ŋoŋe mârâc jaha ma tâmiric juhuc sâqocne kosa barâ hâmocne juhapie Anutu e kiŋŋeŋic behehuc Kristohec bâɋârec-ŋopawec.
Erâ dâŋ qaqatara-nâŋec qâreŋkekicne i âke sifuckehuc irec kiŋ papia i bâsuckerâ maripoŋko ɋetickeme arictâc ewec.
Iŋuc ehuc fekicne â tâpirihec hâbi-jeŋic bâŋgoroŋkerâ saoreŋ qahuc fuŋne-jeŋic bataniŋkewec.
Ŋic moczi nânâ qowi soware me sabata hombaŋ me mosa hombaŋ i me i ŋeŋere me mi ŋeŋere mu supaic mi eŋarezejec.
Wiac iŋucnere nâkumucne muzo, fârine šâhec fuaocte irec nâkumucnezi qanaŋ bâniewec. Á fârine ine Kristorao fuawec fokac.
Ŋic gâcnezi maŋhuhuŋ hawari erâ juhuc aŋelo araŋ bajareeŋgopieŋ, â maŋnâŋec ŋerisieme wiac honeeŋgopeneŋ muhuc irec manapie fârine eme sahac-jeŋic maŋgâŋ mušoraeŋgopieŋ, ŋic iŋucne jaŋe boreŋ fâri-ŋeŋic mi ŋowac ronšepieŋ.
Jaŋe hâcne Kristorao sâcne mi siŋkeeŋgopieŋ. Eki qizec-nâŋec â nâŋâc me sahac-ticne. Eme qizeckonec ruazi fâuckerâ wahahuc me kike fâri ombâŋ-ticne basanaŋ-nâpohuc bândeŋ-nâpoekac. Ehuc gume hesiwiŋ enâreme soka sanaŋte tâpiri Anuturaonec fua-nâreekac.
Ŋoŋe Kristore hâmocko šuhuckehuc mâreŋte wiac tâpirihec râpeckembiŋko wemocte mâreŋte hae fâri juhuc tinac sâcmutâc dâŋticne reŋkeeŋgo-pieŋ?
Dâŋ kecšiŋuc: “Keci mi bâuac, keci mi nâc, keci mi roc.”
Wiac nâ bac erâ bebehene hâcne, irec kibâtâc dâŋ i ŋiczi maŋjeŋicte manasurâ mu qaqazuc eeŋgopieŋ.
Ŋic iŋucnezi maŋɋârâŋ hawari erâ “bâtâcko â sowa juhuc sahac bâpitiwazo” iŋuc mupie dâŋ izi fârine tinac eekac. Erâ wiac iŋucnezi fârine aricne, izi sasec aka sâcne mi hecneocmu.
Ŋoŋe Kristo fafahare-ticnao šuhuckembiŋko ine faic Anuture maŋfuŋko Kristo jukacko wiac fokac, irec henširiŋnehuc junšepieŋ.
Mâreŋko wiac fokac irec mâcne, faic wiac fokac irec maŋ mamanasu-ŋeŋic râepie fozejec.
Ŋoŋe hâmombiŋ hâcne, eme juju-ŋeŋic Kristohec Anuturao soŋkekicne fokac.
Juku Kristo e juju runâŋeczi fua taniŋkeme ŋoŋe iŋuc jaha ehec mâmâc tatamac huririnao fua taniŋkeniŋmu.
Wiac kecšiŋucte ine sowa juhuc sahac-ŋeŋic bâhâmonšepieŋ: Boe sau, maŋwânâŋ, bu gâgâpâcne, sasec sâqocne, buchâro, i eocmu e sahac-ticnezi wofuŋ ecnekac muzo.
Wiac i sasaware Anuturaonec okacne fisiocmu.
Ŋoŋe mârâcko iŋuc jaha wiac i bajupie maŋ fâri-ŋeŋic ejujec.
Ʒi ine wiac iŋucne sasawa hetaranšepieŋ. Ehuc aaric, kimbeŋ, râŋgeŋ bârâŋgeŋ, dâŋ gâgâpâcne â simbiŋne i qikiŋnenšepieŋ.
Burec eec i wâc mi enšepieŋ. Maŋraŋɋa-ŋeŋic mâsi qâqâreŋ-ticnehec heunucke behec erâ
maŋɋâri-ŋeŋic hepie hume rojuŋgopieŋ. Maŋ i hâcne bâbâfuazi bâpiaŋkeme mamanahec erâ e jahacne hawari iŋucne fuahuc jukac.
Irec bârâwiŋ juju i tarawec, Grikŋic â Judaŋic, mahec â ma tâmiric, hâwecŋic â kâte sanaŋ, kiŋaŋ qaqa â ŋicbomboŋ, mâmâc sasawa Kristozi qâhâc-nâporâ micne junâre-fâreekac.
Eme Anuture biŋefâc, e jahac maŋjauŋ eŋarehuc rowosâec-ŋopawec, ŋoŋe buuruc â buafec â maŋhuhuŋ â miriŋ â bumâteŋ izi ŋaqi-ŋeŋic eme hepie hume rojunšepieŋ.
Ŋoŋe aakic enšepieŋ, â ŋondeŋ-ŋeŋicko dâŋ fuame kiŋ bebehec enšepieŋ. Wofuŋzi kiŋ behe-ŋarewec iŋuc jaha eec enšepieŋ.
Eme wiac sasawa irec fainao maŋjauŋ bajupie izi wiac bâture-fârehuc ematauckezejec.
Erâ Kristore wamazi maŋŋeŋicko guriŋne bazejec. Ŋoŋe wamahec erâ me sahac mocjahao juniŋte rocŋopakicne hâcne. Erâ wâc daŋge mumuteŋ ehuc junšepieŋ.
Kristore dâŋzi ŋondeŋ-ŋeŋicko sawe mâririackezejec. Eme maŋɋârâŋ dâŋ fuŋne fuŋne qaqazuc ehuc faŋ qaqac enšepieŋ. Erâ miti gae mânec i Mârozi baafec-ŋopaha maŋŋeŋiczi Anutu muteŋkehuc hecnenšepieŋ.
Eme maŋzi me mezi wiac ezo murâ i Wofuŋ Jesu manasiŋkehuc enšepieŋ, ehuc ere erâ Anutu Mamac daŋge âzâcnenšepieŋ.
Ŋokac ŋoŋe ŋowefâc-ŋeŋic jaŋere rereŋfâc junšepieŋ, Wofuŋte biŋe ekicnezi iŋuc epie sâckeocmu.
Ŋic ŋoŋe ŋonâŋfâc-ŋeŋic maŋjauŋ ejarenšepieŋ, šâšâicne ine mi ejarenšepieŋ.
Naru motec ŋoŋe neŋgoc mamacfâc-ŋeŋic dâŋ mupie sâc reŋkenšepieŋ, iŋuc epie Wofuŋzi maname biaŋkeocmu.
Mamac ŋoŋe naru motecfâc-ŋeŋic hâwic sahac enšipiŋte aaricko wiac mi ejarenšepieŋ.
Kiŋaŋ qaqa ŋoŋe mâreŋ ŋicbomboŋfâc-ŋeŋic jaŋere mic reŋke-fârenšepieŋ, maizi qambaraŋ ejarepie ŋiczi sawa honec-ŋopapie sâckeocte mâcne, maŋsiocmâc Wofuŋ araŋ bacnehuc epie sâckeomu.
Gie-ŋeŋic sasawa i ŋic jaŋere erâ mâcne, Wofuŋte erâ aafec faio banšepieŋ.
Kecšiŋuc manahuc: Gie furi sambâŋko merâfâc fokac i Wofuŋtaonec roniŋmu. Irec Wofuŋ Kristo ere kiŋaŋ qaqafâc juŋgopieŋ hâcne.
Moc e gie-ticne bâsâqoreocmu, e irec okacne jaha roocmu. Wofuŋtao ra rowec ware rowec mi fokac.
Ŋicbomboŋ ŋoŋe kiŋaŋ qaqafâc-ŋeŋic wiac sâkoa etiŋnehuc ejarenšepieŋ, ehuc ŋaŋacne femicne Wofuŋ sambâŋko jukac i manasunšepieŋ.
Paŋšâic jaha numuhuc junšepieŋ. Erâ rucgereŋ juhuc daŋge nunumu enšepieŋ.
Erâ nâŋere wâc numupie Anutuzi mitire hata bâšâwe-nâreme Kristore dâŋ soŋne mufuanšepeneŋ. Dâŋ irec hâcne niŋgiŋko fokopac.
Nunumuzi dopecnupie dâŋ afeckehuc mujaŋgeŋkepe sâckezejec.
Qâpuc jaŋehec bâbâfuac erâ wiac mana tara-hâmohuc enšepieŋ. Ehuc gie bapa dameŋ mi sipirickenšepieŋ.
Dâŋŋeŋic hâwec ruacnepie aŋacne ezejec. Eme ŋic dâŋ iŋuc me iŋuc bâtikie-jareniŋte mi bititienšepieŋ.
No nahacne dâŋ binaŋ i Tikikozi eŋareocmu. E joroc âgo babafic-nâŋec â Wofuŋte kiŋaŋ qaqa micrereŋhec.
E hâcne juju-nâŋecte dâŋ binaŋ eŋarehuc mu âkeriŋ eŋareocte ŋoŋerao sorepe fakac.
Erâ Onesimo, miti mamana âgo biaŋ-nâŋec, ŋoŋere haeonec, e mâmâc ecnepe fârâ širec dâŋ binaŋ eŋare-fâreocmu.
Kâpâcwâru ŋic âgo-nane Aristako â Banaba nafe-ticne Mareko â Jesu, šâŋe-ticne moc Justo, jaŋe manasu-ŋareŋgopieŋ. Mareko ere sâcmutâc eŋarepo, fâ fisiocmuo âgo ecnenšepieŋ.
Ŋic i jaŋe sawa Judaŋic jaŋeraonec fuakicnezi Anutu uucmaŋ-ticnere giere baficnueŋgopieŋ, ehuc bubiaŋ qanareeŋgopieŋ.
Erâ ŋoŋere haeonec ŋic moc Epafara, Kristore kiŋaŋ qaqa, ere mamanac ŋoŋerao fokac, erâ ŋoŋe sanaŋkerâ Anuture micsâcko juhuc wiac mana tararâ etiŋneniŋte dameŋ sâc nunumuzi dopec-ŋopaekac.
No fuŋne-ticne manakopac, e ŋoŋere mecne erâ Laodikea haconec â Hierapoli haeonec mitiŋic jaŋere mecne mâmâc šâic gie wemo afecne baekac.
Luka dokta biaŋ-nâŋec â Dema jahe mu šeri eŋarekopirec.
Erâ no Laodikea haeonec mitiŋic â Nimfasi â wiacfâcne mu šeri ejarekopac i mufua-jarenšepieŋ.
Papia ši ŋic ŋokac wose-jarepie mana-fârepie Laodikea haeonec kikefuŋ jaŋerao râepie rame wosenšepieŋ. Á jaŋere moc qâreŋkepo iŋuc jaha ŋarepie wosenšepieŋ.
