Arikipo e šiŋuc âzâcnenšepieŋ: “Miti gie Wofuŋzi neŋgoc ŋeha mugarekicne i aijakic jaha bâhâmozemec.”
Paulo no nahacne šâŋe qâreŋ ši râekopac. Kâpâcwâru ŋic nore manasunšepieŋ. Aki anonoczi ŋoŋerao fozejec.
Paulo, Siliwano â Timoteo nâŋe Tesalonike haeonec kikefuŋ, Anutu Mamac â Wofuŋ Jesu Kristo ere ŋicfâc, ŋoŋere papia ši râeŋgopeneŋ. Aki anonoc â wama ŋoŋerao fotâcnerâ fozejec.
Nâŋe dameŋ sâc ŋoŋere erâ Anutu daŋge âzâcneeŋgopeneŋ, erâ nunumu gie bahuc sâc ŋoŋere manasu-fâreeŋgopeneŋ.
Ŋoŋe mamanasiŋ-ŋeŋicte fârine bâfuaeŋgopieŋ â maŋjauŋte bâmec gie baeŋgopieŋ â Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristo paŋšâic jaha worickeeŋgopieŋ, irec Mamac-nâŋec Anutu ere maio hati manasurâ mufuahuc âzâcneeŋgopeneŋ.
Âgofâc, nâŋe manaŋgopeneŋ, Anutuzi maŋjauŋ eŋarehuc rowosâec-ŋopawec.
Iŋuc eŋarewecte Biŋebiaŋ bafârâ ŋazapene dâŋ sawa mi ewec, i tâpirihec â Tiri Mârohec â buâkecnehec ewec. Ŋoŋerao jumbeŋko ŋoŋere erâ wiac ebac embeŋ i manaŋgopieŋ.
Eme nâŋe bâjâpec-nâpombiŋ, bâjâpec-nâpohuc Wofuŋ e jahacne mâmâc bâjâpembiŋ. Ehuc miti i fific guguriŋ faio Tiri Mârozi bufahac qaŋarehame ro maŋ embiŋ.
Ŋoŋe iŋuc ehuc Makedonia â Akaia mâreŋkonec miti mamana jaŋe micne bajarehuc fuŋne qazu-jarembiŋ.
Ŋoŋeraonec hâcne Wofuŋte dâŋzi haŋ barahuc Makedonia â Akaia mâreŋko fuawec, erâ i sawa mâcne, ŋoŋe Anutu manasiŋkembiŋ irec dâŋ biŋe i hae sâc mana-fârepie nâŋe jajazane moc mi fuawec.
Jaŋe jaŋac ŋoŋerao gie bapene fârine fuawec irec dâŋ nâzâeŋgopieŋ. Erâ ŋoŋe nemuɋâŋ râpeckerâ Anutu jujune â fârine maickerâ ŋicfâc-ticne embiŋ,
erâ Ŋokâ-ticne Jesu hâmockonec bâɋârekicne, e juku sambâŋkonec waharâ okac dameŋko ŋezic-nâpozokac, ere šawiehuc jueŋgopieŋ, irec dâŋ binaŋ-ŋeŋic hae sâc eeŋgopieŋ.
Âgofâc-nane, ŋoŋerao fisirâ gie bapene fârimâc mi ewec i ŋaŋac manaŋgopieŋ.
Qanaŋ Filipi haeo qa imac enârembiŋ i manaŋgopieŋ wâc. Enârepie sifu mi dockembeŋ. Aricne, Anuturao roweckepene bubiaŋ qanâreme afeckerâ ŋoŋerao fârâ Anuture Biŋebiaŋ i juju gie sâko bahuc mufua-ŋarembeŋ.
Babaafec dâŋ mueŋgopeneŋ i mamana sifuc faio mâcne, me maŋsifuc faio mâcne, me kege wage eŋarehuc mâcne”
Anutuzi honec-nâpome sâckeme Biŋebiaŋ muromackenaŋte betoŋ-nâpowec irec sâc mueŋgopeneŋ. Ŋiczi mana-nârepie biaŋkeocte aricne, Anutu e maŋ hohonezi mana-nâreme biaŋkeocte mocjaha mueŋgopeneŋ.
Ŋoŋe nâŋere manaeŋgopieŋ, nâŋe bâbâmiriŋ dâŋ moc mi ŋazambeŋ mitio ake hehuc moneŋ mafare andac i wâc mi embeŋ, i Anutuzi manaha mukopac.
Kristore aposolo nâŋe mana-nârepie feme sâckeocmu i manahuc sifu ŋoŋe me hae gâcnaonec ŋicbomboŋ eŋarenaŋte mi mumbeŋ.
Aricne, neŋgoc moczi kogocfâcne hemiriŋ-jopaekac, iŋuc jaha nâŋe ŋoŋerao juhuc eŋarembeŋ.
Aŋac-nâŋec ŋoŋerao fowecte Anuture Biŋebiaŋ ŋaŋazare sawa mâcne, ŋoŋere erâ juju-nâŋec qiqikiŋ irec mâmâc afeckembeŋ, maŋnâŋec ŋoŋerao âeckewec irec.
Âgofâc, micneneŋ eŋarepene takic-ŋopazacte ŋafe furec sahacte gie mâmâc šocne fârone bahuc domambeŋ, i ehuc Anuture Biŋebiaŋ ŋazambeŋ, ŋoŋe irec manasueŋgopieŋ.
Nâŋe maŋtaniŋ â tiŋne â bahacmâc juhuc miti mamana ŋoŋe wiac eŋarembeŋ, i ŋoŋe mecne â Anutu mecne fuŋne-nâŋec manaŋgopieŋ.
Erâ moc šiŋuc wâc manaŋgopieŋ: Mamac moczi naru motecfâcne ejareekac, sâc ijaha nâŋe ŋoŋe eŋarehuc buc buc mu sawaŋ dâŋ ŋazambeŋ â esoc qafeŋ eŋarembeŋ â šiŋuc mušakiehuc ŋazambeŋ:
“Uucmaŋ-ticne â eri tatamac-ticne rauckeniŋte hefârec-ŋopaekac Anutu hâcne, ere ŋicfâc fârine erâ irec sâcko junšepieŋ.”
Nâŋe Anuture dâŋ ŋazapene manapie ŋicdâŋ mi ewec. Eme iŋuc sâcne manambiŋ, i Anuture dâŋ jâmbâŋ, eki miti mamana ŋoŋerao gie baekac. Eme nâŋe irec hâcne Anutu daŋge mumuteŋ kuduc jaha ecnehuc jueŋgopeneŋ.
Âgofâc-nane, ŋoŋe Anuture kikefuŋ Judaia mâreŋko Kristo Jesurao qohotambiŋ jaŋehec sâc mocjaha embiŋ. Jaŋe Judaŋiczi jopa qâšâic ejarembiŋ iŋuc jaha âgofâc-ŋeŋic gâcnezi ŋoŋe ŋopa qâšâic eŋarembiŋ.
Judaŋic jaŋe Wofuŋ Jesu â porofete iŋuc jaha qâhâmoc-jopambiŋ, erâ wâc nâŋe nâpo jâpec enârembiŋ. Jaŋe Anutu âgo mi ecneeŋgopieŋ â ŋicne ŋicne kisuec-jopaeŋgopieŋ.
Ehuc qâpuc miti jazapene manarâ biaŋkenšipiŋte aka henareeŋgopieŋ. Jaŋe iŋuczi iŋuc ehuc sâqocne faio fefec hefekupie kiŋjeŋicte sâc micne qame Anuture kimbeŋ fisi-jarewec.
Âgofâc, nâŋe behec-ŋopambeŋ, erâ maŋzi mâcne, sahaczi dameŋ ŋondeŋ ši ŋoŋe tâmiric juhuc huacbuc eŋgopeneŋte mocwâc honec-ŋopanaŋte boc enâreekac.
Eme irec fârâ iqic-ŋopanaŋte mumbeŋ, Paulo no nahac dameŋ moc â moc fâzo mupe Sataŋzi aka henarewec.
Ŋoŋere aŋac-nâpoekac i šiŋucte: Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu ere fifisi dameŋko weni jaŋe gie fâri-nâŋec â šeri-nâŋec â eri-nâŋec eniŋmu? Ŋoŋe wâc enâreniŋmu hâcne.
Ŋoŋe mumuteŋ-nâŋec â bubiaŋ-nâŋec.
Ŋoŋere maŋhâhâŋ boc enarekume nâŋe gâcnezi sifu Ateŋ haeo buc juhuc
Timoteo sorepene behec-nâporâ ŋoŋerao fâwec. E âgo-nâŋec â Anuture gieŋic juhuc Kristore Biŋebiaŋ muekaczi fârâ mitio hume keteŋ eŋarehuc faŋ qaŋareocte mucnembeŋ.
Ŋoŋe šârâ hâriŋ faio juhuc dockenšipiŋte iŋuc embeŋ. Ŋoŋe manaŋgopieŋ, miti mâteŋne juhuc mananaŋte mi munârekicne.
Nâŋe ŋoŋerao juhuc qanaŋ dâŋ šiŋuc ŋazambeŋ: “Ʒika biac fai-nâŋecko feocmu.” Eme dâŋ i sanaŋkewec, i manaŋgopieŋ.
Eme eesâic runezi bârokawec-ŋopame gie-nanere fârine omaezacte maŋ kukumbuc boc enareme jupe bape sâqoreme ŋic e miti babaju-ŋeŋicte fuŋne manaocte sorepe fâwec.
Eme ši Timoteo e risie warerâ mamanasiŋ â maŋjauŋ-ŋeŋicte biŋe biaŋ nâzâwec” Erâ nâŋere boc manasueŋgopieŋ, â nâŋe ŋoŋe honec-ŋopazo muhapene ŋoŋe iŋuc jaha nâŋe honec-nâpozo mueŋgopieŋ, dâŋ i nâzâ-fârewec.
Âgofâc, nâŋe šârâ hâriŋ â bušâiczi maŋnâŋec hehâriŋkeme juhapene miti babaju-ŋeŋicte dâŋzi bunâŋec bâuruewec.
Ŋoŋe Wofuŋ heme hariŋ ecnehuc sanaŋkeeŋgopieŋ i manahuc maŋnâŋec fie ruruckekac.
Ŋoŋere erâ Anuture maio bubiaŋ sâko manaeŋgopeneŋte Anutu daŋge mo iŋucne ecnepene sâckeocmu?
Mâc mana-nâreha ŋoŋerao fârâ hohonec erâ miti gâcne forakac i moc šuhucke-ŋarenaŋte ŋafe furec mu wâwâsic ecneeŋgopeneŋ.
Mamac-nâŋec Anutu â Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu e jahac hata bâfua-nâreme ŋoŋerao fânšepeneŋ.
Ŋoŋerao ine Wofuŋzi maŋjauŋ-ŋeŋic bâŋɋârâŋkeme ŋedâmâreme ŋaŋackoaŋ â gâcne jaŋehec eec enšepieŋ” nâŋe iŋuc jaha ŋoŋe eŋareeŋgopeneŋ.
Erâ Anutuzi maŋŋeŋic keteŋkeme ŋoŋe Mamac-nâŋecte maio bahacmâc â maŋfuru juhapie Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu tiŋnefâc-ticne sasawa jaŋehec fisizejec.
Âgofâc-nane, Wofuŋ Jesure erâ uŋ sawaŋ eŋarehuc moc šiŋuc ŋazapene mananiŋ: Mitio juju bapa-ŋeŋiczi Anutu âgo ecneocte fuŋne ŋaza qazuc embeŋ, ijaha junšepieŋ. Mitio juju i sâcne jueŋgopieŋ, mâc juŋɋârâŋkeniŋte ŋazaŋgopeneŋ.
Wofuŋ Jesure micte dâŋ ŋaza qâmoc embeŋ, irec kâuc mi baŋgopieŋ.
Anutu e šiŋuc hâcne muekac: Boe sau qikiŋnehuc maŋɋaɋac junšepieŋ.
Ŋoŋerao moczi e jahacne ŋonâŋ maŋɋaɋacko â pectâcko rauckezejec,
sasecte šocbâruŋko misac, i ŋic qâpuc Anuture kâuc baeŋgopieŋzi eeŋgopieŋ.
Moczi moc aka huckehuc wiac iŋucnao âgo-ticne mi eatuckezejec. Wofuŋ e wiac irec okacne bazu-fâreocmu” nâŋe dâŋ i mârâc jaha mujomirerâ ŋazambeŋ.
Maŋwânâŋhec junaŋte aricne, maŋɋaɋac junaŋte Anutuzi hefârec-nâpowec.
Irec moc e dâŋ i bâsueocmu, e ŋic moc mâcne, Anuctu e jahacne bâsueocmu, Tiri Mâro maŋŋeŋicko râeekac e hâcne bâsueocmu.
Ŋoŋe miti mamanazi maŋzi jauŋ babac eniŋte wemocte boc qâreŋke-ŋarenaŋmu, Anutu e jahac maŋzi jauŋ babac eniŋte fuŋne ŋaza ŋowatuc ewec.
Erâ ŋoŋe Makedonia mâreŋ hae sâc opâ ruac juraŋgopieŋ jaŋe maŋjauŋ ejarehuc jueŋgopieŋ. Erâ sifu mocwâc ɋârâŋkeocte ŋazaŋgopeneŋ.
Erâ dâŋ moc šiŋuc ŋaza qâmoc embeŋ: Rac warec juhuc dâŋ ojowa mi ee, hae-ŋeŋicko ŋezurâ ŋehuc mezi gie muŋarekicne aijakic jaha baniŋte ɋicwânšâŋ enšepieŋ.
Ehuc qâpuc jaŋere maio roroc tâmiric pectâc junšepieŋ.
Âgofâc, ŋoŋe hâmokicne jaŋere kâuc bârâ, miti tâmiriczi maŋjeŋic šickeme ki mamakuc eeŋgopieŋ iŋuc enšipiŋte ŋazapene mananiŋ:
Nâŋâc Jesu hâmorâ faharewec dâŋ i maŋkerâ šiŋuc mananšepeneŋ: Anutu e Jesu ecneme hâmokicne jaŋe e jahacnehec amec-jopa fisiocmu.
Á moc i Wofuŋ e jahacne micdâŋ ŋazanaŋ: Mâreŋko ɋâricne juhapene fisiocmu nâŋâc hâmokicne mi siric-jopanaŋmu.
Wofuŋ e sambâŋkonec wahaocte ine dâŋ wiwira â aŋelo qizecte micšonšoŋ â Anuture qeŋfânâŋ fuahame wahaocmu. Wahame Kristo manasiŋkehuc hâmombiŋ jaŋe bâbâni fahareniŋmu.
Faharepie ɋâricne junaŋmu, tiwâne hâcne, izi jaŋerao šuhuckepene karoraczi bafec-nâpome sawao Wofuŋhec bâbâfuac enaŋmu. Erâ Wofuŋhec juhuc junaŋmu sanaŋ.
Ŋoŋe dâŋ i hâcne muc manac ehuc maŋ bâbâmâteŋ enšepieŋ.
Âgofâc-nane, dameŋte â šâfore dâŋ wemocte moc qâreŋke-ŋare mu?
Ŋaŋac šiŋuc sâcne manaŋgopieŋ: Râsi jaŋe ŋafeo ututuŋ fisieŋgopieŋ, iŋuc jaha dameŋ-ticne ɋeŋfâfâc jaha maickeocmu.
Eme ŋic jaŋe aki wama sâko fokac muhuc mana fâsâerâ juhapie wiac hâhâwicnezi acmâc jaha fisi-jareocmu. Ŋokac kiwechec moc e gozi onšoŋ jaha kime fâfâreocmu, iŋuc jaha ŋic iŋucne jaŋe wiac onšoŋ jaha fua-jareme wemocko moc wiseniŋmu.
Âgofâc, ŋoŋe ine dapâcko mi juŋgopieŋ, irec wemocko Wofuŋte dameŋzi râsi iŋucne erâ ututuŋ maic-ŋopame bipic tatara eniŋmu.
Ŋoŋe tatamacte â šoaŋte kikefuŋ ekicne, nâŋâc ŋafere me dapâcte biŋe aricne.
Irec ŋic gâcnezi guŋ fopie qâtec-joparâ guŋ mi fonšepeneŋ, rucgereŋ-nâŋec bahuc maŋte sowa junšepeneŋ.
Guŋ fofo jaŋe ŋafeo foeŋgopieŋ gae wowo jaŋe ŋafeo wohuc bâbâsifuc bâfuaeŋgopieŋ.
Ʒoaŋte biŋe ekicne nâŋâc ine maŋte sowa junšepeneŋ, ehuc mamanasiŋ â maŋjauŋ izi maruku enârezejec, â bâbâpiaŋte woworiczi dunâŋec ezejec.
I šiŋucte: Anutu e kimbeŋ-ticnere fârine hotâckenaŋte mâcne, Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristore erâ bâbâpiaŋ rauckenaŋte muekac.
E hâcne okac-nâŋec hâmowec, i hâmohuc me ɋâricne juhuc ehec mâmâc junaŋte iŋuc ewec
Ŋoŋe irec hâcne faŋ qaqac â hehe šakiec eeŋgopieŋ iŋuc jaha ehuc junšepieŋ.
Âgo bureŋ, wiac mocte esoc-ŋopaŋgopeneŋ: Ŋoŋerao šâic gie baeŋgopieŋ â Wofuŋte erâ micne baŋareeŋgopieŋ â mu bâtiŋ eŋareŋgopieŋ i jaŋe sâsec-jopanšepieŋ.
Ehuc gie-jeŋicte erâ maŋjauŋ ejarehuc mana-jarepie fejâmbâŋkezejec. Erâ wâc wama qaqac ehuc junšepieŋ.
Âgofâc, hazec qâuŋ dâŋ moc ŋazape mananiŋ. Ŋic kosa jujune jaŋe uŋ sawaŋ ejarenšepieŋ, ŋic manabâcne jaŋe mu âkeriŋ ejarenšepieŋ, betaŋkekicne jaŋe dopec-jopanšepieŋ, erâ mâmâc hezu hemiriŋ ejarenšepieŋ.
Sâqocnere okac babazuc enšipiŋte sosoŋaŋ enšepieŋ. Ŋaŋackoaŋ â ŋic gâcne sasawa jaŋehec eehâmoc erâ erahuc junšepieŋ.
Bubiaŋ faio jurâ jurahuc junšepieŋ.
Nunumu moc mi hetaranšepieŋ.
Wiac irec me irec daŋge mumuteŋ enšepieŋ, i Kristo Jesure erâ eniŋte Anutuzi muŋarekac.
Mârore šoc mi hehâponšepieŋ.
Anuture micdâŋ mufua-ŋarepie mana qâoma mi enšepieŋ.
Dâŋ sasawa mana wosâerâ bâtâc banšepieŋ, â biaŋne eme bajunšepieŋ.
Sâqocne fuŋne fuŋne ine qikiŋnenšepieŋ.
Anutu wama rune e jahac šure bâpiaŋ eŋareme maŋfuru ejâmbâŋkenšepieŋ, eme mâro â maŋ qâqâtâc â sahac-ŋeŋic furu fohame Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristo ere fifisi dameŋko bahacmâc domanšepieŋ.
Hefârec-ŋopakac e mume sasanaŋ, irec gie-ticne baku batarocmu.
Âgofâc, ŋoŋe nâŋere erâ numunšepieŋ.
Opâ ruac ŋoŋe mitio meo babac efârenšepieŋ.
No Wofuŋte maio ŋaza sanaŋkepe: ŋoŋe papia kecši opâ ruac mâmâc sasawa wose-jarepie mananšepieŋ.
Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristo ere aki anonoczi ŋoŋerao fotâcnerâ fozejec.
Paulo, Siliwano â Timoteo nâŋe Tesalonike haeonec kikefuŋ guru, Mamac-nâŋec Anutu â Wofuŋ Jesu Kristo ere ŋicfâc, ŋoŋere papia ši râeŋgopeneŋ.
Anutu Mamac â Wofuŋ Jesu Kristo eraonec aki anonoc â wama ŋoŋerao fotâcnerâ fozejec.
Âgofâc, maŋnâŋeczi jâiŋ-nâpome ŋoŋere erâ Anutu dameŋ sâc daŋge âzâcneeŋgopeneŋ. Mamanasiŋ-ŋeŋic boc fua ɋârâŋ eekac, â maŋjauŋ-ŋeŋic fua sawec eme qame qoŋgiŋ eeŋgopieŋ. Eme irec Anutu daŋge âzâcnepene i jâmbomac sâckeekac.
Erâ ŋoŋe fific guguriŋ eŋarepie šâic busâqochec juhuc mamanasiŋ-ŋeŋic mi ŋeŋgoroŋkeha sifu sanaŋkerâ jueŋgopieŋ, irec dâŋ binaŋ hae sâc Anuture kikefuŋfâc ejareeŋgopeneŋ.
Ŋoŋe wiac fua-ŋareekac, irec šiŋuc muzo: Anutuzi okac dameŋko wiac sâckoa enâreocmu, irec sâsâcne ši qanaŋ fuakac. Anutuzi ŋoŋere maname sâckeme uucmaŋ-ticnao rarašire sâc bâfuaniŋte šârâ hâriŋ faio jueŋgopieŋ.
Eme juku Anutu mana wosâc-ticne tiŋne fokac irec sâc enâreocmu: Ŋoŋe šâic fâro eŋareeŋgopieŋ jaŋe šâic fâro jaha bâfua-jareocmu,
â šâic fâro manaeŋgopieŋ ŋoŋe ine nâŋehec mâmâc bâgunuc-nâpoocmu. I juku Wofuŋ Jesu e aŋelo guru hâhâwicne jaŋehec sambâŋkonec waha fua tâcneocmu ira iŋuc enâreocmu.
E šocbâruŋko waharâ ŋic Anuture kâuc baeŋgopieŋ â Wofuŋ Jesu Biŋebiaŋ-ticne mana rereŋ mi eeŋgopieŋ jaŋe okacne jareocmu.
Ŋic i jaŋe Anutuzi furine sisipiric sanaŋ jarehuc šâŋe mai-ticnaonec â tâpiri-ticnere huriri biaŋkonec bârâriec-jopaocmu.
Eme dameŋ ira fuŋfuŋfâc-ticne jaŋerao eri tatamac-ticne fuaocmu, â miti-ticne ro maŋ embiŋ jaŋe hone warec ecneniŋmu. Ŋoŋe ine mumutaniŋ dâŋnâŋec mana šakiembiŋ hâcne.
Irec hâcne ŋoŋere erâ dameŋ sâc numuhuc šiŋuc mueŋgopeneŋ: Anutu-nâŋec e hefârec-ŋopaweczi irec sâcko juniŋte bašawiec-ŋopazejec, erâ tâpiri-ticnezi dopec-ŋopahame wiac biaŋnere mu manasuc ehuc mamanasiŋte gie fâri bâfua-fârenšepieŋ.
Iŋuc epie Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu ere šâŋe qâreŋzi ŋoŋerao fua jaŋgeŋkezejec, â ŋoŋe iŋuc jaha erao taniŋke biaŋ enšepieŋ. I Anutu-nâŋec â Wofuŋ Jesu Kristo eki aki anonoc-ticnere iŋuc eŋarezejec.
Âgofâc, Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristo fifisi-ticnere â ehec bâbâfuac ee irec dâŋne moc ŋazapene mananiŋ.
Ŋic gâcne jaŋe Wofuŋte dameŋ maickekac muhuc Mârorao muhotaniŋmu, me nâŋe micko itic enâreniŋmu me papia-nâŋecte mu ɋetic eniŋmu, eme ŋoŋe mi mutuc erâ fâfârepie maŋŋeŋic hockezejec.
Eatuc dâŋ iŋuc me iŋuc ŋazapie mi mananšepieŋ. Wofuŋ dameŋ-ticne maickezo eha qanaŋ miti ima qaqa sâko fuaocmu, erâ sindaŋŋic sisipiricte biŋe eki hâcne fua tâcneocmu.
Eme šâŋene Anutu me miti wiac mueŋgopieŋ i sasawa râsi ecnehuc qâhuckerâ ro waha âte ecne-fâreocmu. Erâ Anuture ufuŋko ferâ ŋehuc e jahacnere muocmu, “No Anutu.”
No ŋoŋerao juhuc irec hâcne ŋazapo, i moc manasuŋgopieŋ me?
Dameŋ šiŋuczia aka fokac, i manaŋgopieŋ, i hâcne rârieme dameŋ-ticnao fua tâcneocmu.
Ʒi ine sindaŋzi soŋsoŋko biac gie-ticne baekac. Á aka hecneekac e rârieme sindaŋŋic fua tâcneocmu.
Eme Wofuŋ Jesu e micrombâŋ-ticnezi qarâ fifisi-ticnere šâziriŋnezi imackeocmu.
Ŋic e Sataŋzi neŋgoc ŋesiŋ ŋecnehame tâpiri wiac fuŋne fuŋnehec fuarâ burecko mâsi â qaŋgec wiac šâŋe furu baocmu.
Erâ ŋic gâcne, dâŋ fâri qizecne manarâ bibiaŋke i qaisockerâ sisipiricte biŋe eeŋgopieŋ, jaŋe sâqocnere maŋ bâsifuc ejareocmu.
Ŋic jaŋe iŋuc eeŋgopieŋte Anutuzi eeatuc neŋgoc qizecne sâko mume fuame burecko qohotaniŋmu hâcne.
I mâc mâcne, dâŋ fâri qizecne qikiŋnerâ wiac hehesicnere aŋac-jopaekac, ŋic i jaŋe okacne fisi-jareocte iŋuc hâcne eocmu.
Âgofâc-nâŋec, Wofuŋte jorocfâc, ŋoŋe Mârozi baɋaɋac-ŋopame dâŋ fâri qizecnao qohotahuc biaŋkeniŋte Anutuzi mârâc jaha rowosâec-ŋopawec, irec daŋge hati âzâcnenaŋte maŋnâŋeczi jâiŋ-nâpoekac.
Irec hâcne Biŋebiaŋ ŋazapene manarâ Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristo eri tatamac-ticne rauckeniŋte hefârec-ŋopawec.
Eme irec âgofâc ŋoŋe sanaŋkerâ dâŋ miczi â papiazi ŋaza qazuc embeŋ i paŋšâic bajunšepieŋ.
Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristo â Anutu Mamac-nâŋec eki maŋjauŋ enârehuc katucmâc-ticnere erâ bubiaŋ fofo sanaŋ bâfua-nârewec â šeŋaŋ fâri woŋec-nâŋec râewec,
eki hâcne maŋŋeŋic bâinaŋkerâ dopec-ŋopame dâŋfâri â gie fâri i ŋoŋerao mi wahazejec.
Âgofâc, dâŋ moc fokac mananiŋ: Nâŋere erâ numupie Wofuŋte dâŋzi fofotâc haŋ barame qâreŋ biaŋ-ticne ŋoŋerao fuawec iŋuc jaha fua razejec.
Erâ ŋic maŋbâiŋ bâbâfuane â sindaŋne jaŋere erâ Anutuzi ŋezic-nâpoocte nunumuzi wâc bafic-nâponšepieŋ. Miti i ŋiczi furu ninic ro maŋ mi eeŋgopieŋ.
Wofuŋzi ine mume sasanaŋ, irec hume keteŋ eŋarehuc sâqocne runere roroŋ sasapec eŋareocmu.
Ŋoŋe dâŋ ŋazapene reŋkerâ reŋke rahuc juniŋmu, irec Wofuŋte erâ ŋoŋere maŋjahec mi eŋgopeneŋ
Wofuŋzi maŋŋeŋic jowame Anuture maŋ jauŋko â Kristore bumâteŋko iticnezejec.
Âgofâc, Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristo ere micte ŋazapene mananiŋ, dâŋ qazu-ŋarembeŋ i opâ ruac gâcnezi mi reŋkehuc kosa jueŋgopieŋ, ŋic i jaŋehec mi junšepieŋ.
Nâŋe hata fuŋkerâ âte-ŋarembeŋ ijaha bâjâpec-nâponiŋte kâuc mi baŋgopieŋ. Nâŋe ŋoŋerao ojoŋ mi jumbeŋ.
Erâ ŋoŋeraonec nânâ furimâc mi nâmbeŋ, aricne, nânâ mafare micneneŋ eŋarenšipeŋte ŋafe furec mezi gie šocnehec bahuc šâic manambeŋ.
Erâ iŋuc enaŋte mi munârekicne, nâŋe qaŋeŋ-ŋopahuc fuŋne ŋowatupene nâŋere mimiŋ qâjâpec juniŋte iŋuc eŋarembeŋ.
Ŋoŋerao juhuc šiŋuc hâcne boc ŋazambeŋ: Ojoŋ juocmuzi nânâ mi nâzejec.
Eme ši ŋoŋeraonec dâŋ šiŋuc wareme manambeŋ: Ŋic gâcnezi gie-jeŋic hetârarâ qâoma erâ jueŋgopieŋ.
Ŋic iŋucne jaŋe Wofuŋ Jesu Kristore micte uŋdâŋ šiŋuc jazapene mana-jâmbâŋkenšepieŋ: Ŋezu ŋewâneŋ erâ gie-jeŋic bapie fârine fuame jaŋacneonec nânšepieŋ.
Âgofâc, ŋoŋe ine eehâmo gie tatakic tâmiric banšepieŋ.
Ʒi papiao dâŋ qâreŋke-ŋareŋgopeneŋ, i ŋic moczi qikiŋneme fuŋne-ticne mujaŋgeŋkerâ behepie buc juhuc mimiezejec.
Râsi ecneniŋte mi mukopac, âgo-nâŋec muhuc mu bâtiŋ ecnehuc tutuc qacnenšepieŋ.
Wofuŋ e wama runezi ine wama bâfua-ŋareme ŋoŋerao dameŋ sâc sâcke-fârerâ fozejec. Wofuŋ e ŋoŋehec jufârezejec.
Ʒi Paulo no nahacne mezi šâŋe qâreŋ-nane râekopac. Papia qâreŋkeekopac sâc ma izi fuaekac. Iŋuc hâcne qâreŋkeekopac.
Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristo ere aki anonoczi ŋoŋerao fotâcnerâ fozejec.
Paulo no Anutu bâbâpiaŋ-nâŋecte micte â Kristo Jesu mamanac-nâŋecte micte Kristo Jesure aposolo juekopaczi
mitio motec jâmbâŋ-nane Timoteo go papia ši qâreŋke-garekopac. Anutu Mamac â Wofuŋ-nâŋec Kristo Jesu eraonec aki anonoc â uruc jauŋ â wama gorao fotâcnerâ fozejec.
No Makedonia mâreŋko razo ehuc gazapo iŋuc ezemec, ehuc Efeso haeo šuhuckerâ juhuc, ŋic tucnezi miti musifuckeeŋgopieŋ jaŋe qatara-jaretec behenšepieŋ.
Jaŋe nemu binaŋ bahuc ŋic gaŋne gaŋne juwefumbiŋ irec fuŋne qapie rašic wefuc eme mu qaqataranehec fuaekac. Iŋuc epie Anutu manasiŋkehuc kiŋaŋ qaqacne i wahame sâqoreekac.
Miti mumure fârine ine šiŋuc fuame sâckeocmu: Maŋtaniŋ â maŋšuruc â maŋ mamanasiŋhec juhuc maŋjauŋ bâfuazo.
Ŋic tucnezi ine miti hata i qâsorierâ dâŋ jawane fârimâc bâfuambiŋ bajuŋgopieŋ.
Erâ jaŋacnere šiŋuc mueŋgopieŋ: Nâŋe Mosere sâcmutâc dâŋ irec qaqazu, iŋuc murâ dâŋ kosa muhuc irec sasanaŋ bâfuaeŋgopieŋ.
Nâŋâc sâcmutâc dâŋte šiŋuc manaeŋgopeneŋ: I dâŋ biaŋne, erâ fuŋneticne mana-hâmohuc bajuzo.
Fuŋne-ticne ine šiŋuc fokac: Sâcmutâc dâŋ i ŋic bahacmâc jaŋere biŋe mi ekac, ŋic sindaŋne, râŋgeŋne, araŋ bapa tâmiric, sâqocne bapa, maŋwânâŋhec, šaubacne, neŋgoc mamac sisipiric, šika qaqa,
boe sau ŋic, ŋiczia ŋicko sasec gie bapa, ŋic ŋokac fiuc rocjoparâ gâcne qikiŋne-jarehuc moneŋ bâbâfua, burecŋic, Wofuŋte šâŋe muhuc burecko mumupaŋ ee, erâ wiac gâcne moc dâŋ fari biaŋ râsi ecneekac, wiac iŋucne eeŋgopieŋ jaŋere hâcne sâcmutâc dâŋ mukicne.
Anutu juju aŋac rune ere Biŋebiaŋ eri tatamacnehec tahacnukicne izi hâcne iŋuc mufuakac.
Tâpiri narehuc basanaŋnuwec Wofuŋ-nâŋec Kristo Jesu e daŋge âzâcneekopac. Eki mana-nareme sâckeme betoŋnuhuc miti gie munarewec hâcne.
Juwicnao e musoriŋkehuc ŋicfâcne râsi ejarerâ jopa qâšâic ejarehape sifu iŋuc enarewec. No Wofuŋte fuŋne kâuc bahuc mamanasiŋ-nane tâmiricte iŋuc epore akicnuwec.
Eme Wofuŋ-nâŋecte aki anonoczi norao qaja fuseme Kristo Jesuraonec mamanasiŋ â maŋjauŋhec epo.
Jesu Kristo e sâqocne bapa bâpiaŋ-nâpoocte mâreŋko wahawec, dâŋ i fârine jâmbâŋ â mâmâc sâko ro maŋ eenere sâc. Sâqocne bapa jaŋere micne no hâcne.
Eme Jesu Kristo e akicnurâ, uruc jauŋ-ticne ŋemâcne fokac, irec fuŋne norao furu jaha bataniŋkewec i mâc mâcne, ŋic šâhec mâsi i hâcne norao honerâ e manasiŋkerâ juju sanaŋko fisiniŋte iŋuc enarewec.
Juju sanaŋte Wofuŋ Sâko, mi hâhâmone â mi hohonene, Anutu sâko mocjaha hâcne, ere šâŋe biŋe â eri tatamac forašihuc juzejec sanaŋ. Jâmbomac.
Motec-nane Timoteo, qanaŋ gore findaŋdâŋ fuawec irec sâcko dâŋ mutâcne-garekicne i hâcne râe-garekopac. Go i bajuhuc momori gie biaŋ sanaŋkerâ bazemec.
Erâ mamanasiŋge fošakierâ fohame maŋge soŋaŋketec ɋaɋacnea fozejec. Ŋic tucnezi maŋɋaɋac juju râpeckembiŋte mamanasiŋ-jeŋic ŋeŋgoroŋkeme qâsoriembiŋ.
Jaŋeraonec moc Himenaio â moc Alesande, eme jahe Sataŋzi bâšâic-jofakume mumusoriŋ-jekic behenicte erao râec-jofapo.
No bâbâni dâŋ moc gaza qâmoc epe: Nunumu wâwâsic â daŋge mumuteŋ izi ŋaŋacne â ŋic gâcne sasawa dopec-jopahuc
ŋicwofuŋ â kia gawamaî mâmâc dopec-jopanšepieŋ. Eme soŋaŋ-nâpohapie wamao mâteŋne â mitine juhâmopene ŋiczi mana-nârepie fezejec.
Izi biaŋkeocmu, â bâbâpiaŋ-nâŋec Anutu e irec maname sâckeocmu.
Eki ŋic mâmâc sasawa biaŋkerâ dâŋ fâri qizecne mana maŋ eniŋte muekac hâcne.
Anutu mocjaha hâcne junârekac, erâ Anutu â ŋic ŋondeŋ-nâŋecko ŋicwirec-nâŋec mocjaha Jesu Kristo e ŋic ekicnezi junâre-fârekac.
Eki hâcne juju-ticne qikiŋnehuc mâmâc sâko kiwiric-nâŋec rowec, irec biŋezi dameŋ-ticnao haŋ baocte.
No irec biŋe mumu â aposolo jupemurâ râecnukicne, erâ ŋic qâpuc dâŋ fâri qizecne â mamanasiŋte fuŋne jaza mutâc epemurâ qaqazu gie munarekicne. Dâŋ i burec mâcne, jâmbomac mukopac.
Ŋic jaŋere mukopac, jaŋe hae sâc aaric â maŋjahec tâmiric juhuc mejeŋic ɋaɋacne foha Anuturao sicnerâ numunšepieŋ.
Á ŋokac jaŋere mukopac, jaŋe ŋaqi aickerâ rojuhuc rume rume jupie izi eri-jeŋic ezejec, â qizec susuc-jeŋicko mâsi qâreŋ ee, me eri wiac furi sâko qoqonaŋ, me ŋaqi hohonebâcne ro juju ine mi enšepieŋ.
Ŋokac mitio juzo muŋgopieŋzi eehâmo gie bapie sâckeocmu.
Ŋokac jaŋe wahamicne juhuc niniŋkerâ hazec râehuc mamana gie banšepieŋ.
Ŋokaczi qaqazu gie baocte me ŋic qâhuc-jopaocte mi manacnekopac, e mâc rumerâ juzejec.
Adam e bâbâni bâfuakicne â Ewa ine šâhec.
Adam e eesaic rune mi manacnewec, ŋokaczi ine manacnerâ qaqatara bâfuawec.
Ŋokaczi motec roro-ticnere biaŋkeocmu, ine mamanasiŋhec â maŋjauŋhec erâ maŋɋaɋac juniŋmu ŋokac i jaŋe iŋuc hâcne eniŋmu.
Moc e mitire micne bapa juocte muocmu, e gie furi sâkore ecnekac muzo, dâŋ i jâmbomac.
Eme mitire micne bapazi bahacmâc juhuc ŋokac mocjahahec juzejec, erâ maŋsowa juzejec, eesifuc tâmiric metâne juzejec, jauŋhec juzejec, qaqazu gie basarickehuc bapane,
waiŋ opâ âmbâŋ mi nâzejec, šikafac aricne, urucne â wamane juzejec, moneŋ mafare mubâre mi ezejec,
e jahacne wiacfâc sâcne soŋaŋ-jopazejec erâ pectâc juhuc naru motecfâcne mu bâtiŋ ejareme micrereŋhec junšepieŋ.
Moc e wiacfâc-ticne sâcne mi soŋaŋ-jopaocmu, e wemocko Anuture kikefuŋ mamac ejareocmu.
Erâ opâ ruac ɋâricne moczi mitire micne bapa mi juzejec, iŋucnezi penaroŋ eme Sataŋzi doc bazacte.
Ŋic ŋokac kikefuŋko mi rašimbiŋ jaŋe wâc manacnepie sâckeekac ŋic iŋucnezi mitire micne juzejec, jaŋe musoriŋkepie Sataŋzi maŋne bâsifuckeme ere bitiŋko kizacte.
Babafic jaŋe iŋuc jaha ŋic metâne junšepieŋ, nameŋ sosohoc mi junšepieŋ, waiŋ opâ nâ âmbâŋ mi enšepieŋ, moneŋ mafare mubâre mi enšepieŋ.
Miti boreŋ soŋsoŋ fowarehuc juwec i maŋɋaɋacko duckepie fozejec.
Jaŋe wâc qanaŋ ba esâic ejarezo” eme fuŋne-jeŋic hone manac epie sâckeme gie jarezo.
Ŋonâŋfâc-jeŋic jaŋe iŋuc jaha metâne junšepieŋ, gupe micko âkec mi enšepieŋ, maŋsowa juhuc wiac sasawa mu bac epie fâri fideteŋ efârezejec.
Babafic moc e ŋokac mocjahahec juzejec. Naru motecfâc-ticne â wiacfâc-ticne sâcne soŋaŋ-jopazejec.
Eme babafic moc e gie-ticne bame biaŋkeme maŋte juju šae biaŋne bâfuaocmu â Kristo Jesurao qohotahuc giere afecke-hâmoocmu.
No gorao biac fâpemurâ manasuhuc sifu kecšiŋucte dâŋ ši qâreŋke-garekopac:
Wiac moczi niŋgiŋnume jupe šorame Anuture ficko ju bac ezore fuŋne kâuc bazic. Anutu jujune ere kikefuŋfâc jaŋe hâcne ficticne erâ wâc dâŋ fâri qizecnere gumi â hobeteŋne juŋgopieŋ.
Miti-nâŋecte fuŋne qame hukicne mutaniŋkeeŋgopeneŋ i qeŋ bipinehec: E sahacko fua tâcnekicne, Mârozi fuŋne bataniŋkekicne, aŋelozi honekicne, qâpucko biŋene mukicne, mâreŋ sâc mana maŋ ekicne, eri tatamacko bafekicne.
Mâro e qanaŋ šiŋuc mujaŋgeŋkerâ muekac: Juku šâhec ŋic tucnezi miti beherâ maŋ bâsifuc bâbâfua jaŋere eeatuc dâŋko â demoŋ jaŋere burecdâŋko qohotaniŋmu.
Ine burecŋiczi maŋjeŋic šukiwic bakicnere ŋic eatuc-jopahuc šiŋuc jazaeŋgopieŋ:
“Ŋokac mi rohuc ŋicšeŋoŋ juzo â nânâ gâcne mi nâhuc irec sowa juzo.” Nânâ i Anutuzi râe-fârewec, erâ mamanasiŋhec juhuc dâŋfâri mana maŋ embeŋzi daŋge âzâcnehuc nanaŋte muwec.
Anuturaonec wiac fuakicne i biaŋne sasawa. Erâ daŋge âzâcnehuc nâ bac eeŋgopeneŋko qaqatarene mi fokac.
I Anuture dâŋzi â nunumuzi jambuŋkekicne hâcne.
Go opâ ruac dâŋ i jaza qâmoc ecmu, ine Jesu Kristore kiŋaŋŋic dâŋ rereŋhec jucmu, ehuc mamanasiŋte dâŋ â mitire dâŋfuŋne fârine mana rereŋ ewaremeŋ izi maŋgere nâqiŋ eha jucmu.
Á qeŋokac qizec dâŋ wose murarane ine qikiŋnezemec. Go Wofuŋ manasiŋkehuc jucmurâ maŋzi aafec bazemec.
Sahacte aafec gie bapa izi fâfârine, â maŋ baafeckehuc Wofuŋ manariŋ qâriŋ eecne ine fârine. Izi šira mâreŋko â juku sambâŋko juju bâfua-nâreocte mukicne.
Dâŋ i fârine jâmbâŋ â mâmâc sâko ro maŋ eenere sâc.
Irec fârine hâcne ronaŋte gie amec fâfâuc baeŋgopeneŋ, ine mumusoriŋzi fai-nâŋecko feipieha Anutu jujune ere mamanacko juhuc eeŋgopeneŋ. E hâcne mâreŋ sâc ŋic jaŋere bâbâpiaŋ juekaczi mamana hec nâŋâcne ejâmbâŋkeekac.
Dâŋ mukopac sasawa i jaza mutâc ezemec.
Go motec ɋâri jukic irec ŋic jaŋe gore manapie wawahane mi ezejec. Go maŋjauŋhec â mamanasiŋhec â maŋɋaɋachec jutec miti mumugezi â juju bapagezi opâ ruac guru hata jowatuzejec.
Woŋec-nane juhuc miti wose qazuc â jaza qâmoc ehuc juzemec.
Micne bapa jaŋe Mâroraonec dâŋ mufuahuc mejeŋic qizecgao râehuc jambuŋgumbiŋ, jambuŋ irec fârine sifucke-garezacte bâiŋ basawec ezemec.
Go irec mana mezac ehuc giege bašihuc batec fârine fuarâ fua ehuc fome hone-fârenšepieŋ.
Gahacne maŋ sahac soŋaŋkehuc mitire dâŋfuŋne furu mimic foŋareocte mâmâc soŋaŋkezemec. Go i hâcne paŋšâic bajuzemec. Iŋuc ecmuo ine dâŋge manaeŋgopieŋ jaŋe mecne â go gahacne mâmâc juju biaŋko fisiniŋmu.
Ŋicqizec moc dâŋ âzâcnemurâ fâfâcnehec mi ecnezemec, mamac-nane muhuc urucko mu tutuc ecnezemec, ŋicmotec hahac ɋafâc-nane muhuc sâcjeŋicko jaza bâtiŋ ejarezemec.
Ŋokac qizec neŋgocfâc-nane muhuc iŋuc jaha uruc jauŋdâŋ jazazemec, ŋokac sahac ɋâri seŋfâc-nane muhuc rucge bahuc dâŋ wiac jazazemec.
Hozec sâsec-jopahuc dâŋjeŋic dopeckezemec, hozec jâmbâŋ jaŋere mukopac.
Hozec moc naru motec me ŋosafâcne juniŋmu, ine jaŋe qanaŋ jaŋacne ficko miti gie bahuc ŋic ŋokac qizefâc-jeŋic jauŋ-jopanšepieŋ, ehuc juwicnao wiac ejarekicne irec tofa bazunšepieŋ. Anutu e irec maname sâckeocmu.
Hozec fârine ine e jahackoaŋ juhuc Anuturao roweckeekac, ehuc ŋafe furec nunumu wâwâsic ecneekac.
Á hozec moc sasec gie baocmu ere ine ɋâricnezi hâmocne mucnezo.
Dâŋ i wâc jaza sanaŋketec manarâ bahacmâc junšepieŋ.
Moc e wiacfâcne â soctofafâcne hone jauŋ kime dopec mi ejareocmu e miti beherâ qâpuc sanaŋ ewec mucnezo.
Hozec moc jara-ticne 60 bazuwec, erâ ŋic mocjahahec juwec, iŋucne sawa šâŋe-ticne bâmec papiao râezo.
Erâ eehâmo gie bawec me mâcne, irec fuŋne taniŋkeocte kecšiŋuc mu wioc ezo: Naru motec rocjoparâ gume jowac ejarewec me mâcne? Erao ŋic furune fisipie hezu hewâneŋ ejarewec me mâcne? Mitiŋic bâmec bajarewec me aricne? Jauŋ gie fuŋne fuŋne bawec me mâcne? Fuŋne-jeŋic iŋuc hâcne manazo.
Hozec sahac ɋâri jaŋe šâŋe-jeŋic bâmec papiao feocte mupie ine qatara-jarezemec. Iŋucne jaŋe sasecte ejareme Kristo qâoma ecnerâ ŋicte sahac bapa eeŋgopieŋ.
Erâ mârâc dâŋ mupaŋkembiŋ i qâsuapie bahacnehec eekac.
Erâ wâc gie tâmiricte ficbiri juhuc oma qâoma erâ jueŋgopieŋ, erâ i sawa mâcne, dâŋ jawane â simbiŋne kosa wosepie feekac.
Irec no šiŋuc mukopac: Hozec sahac ɋâri jaŋe ŋic mocwâc rorâ naru motec rocjoparâ dete mamac â ro rikec qâ rikec enšepieŋ. Iŋuc ehuc jupie kisâ jaŋe sâqocnere ojowa baniŋmurâ dâŋ basarâ behenšepieŋ.
Hozec gâcne jaŋe ine biac hata qâsoriembiŋ Sataŋ bâjâpeeŋgopieŋ.
Hozec moc e miti ŋokac mocte ficko juhuc gie bafickeme ine eki bâmec bacnezejec, â qâqâhâc-jeŋickonec mi rozejec, qâqâhâc-jeŋic i hozec waha qaqane jaŋere ezejec.
Soŋaŋzi gie-jeŋic bapie biaŋkeme wiac bafehuc ehâmo-jarezo, ine miti mumu â qaqazu gie paŋšâic baeŋgopieŋ jaŋe hâcne iŋuc ejarezo.
Miti papiao dâŋqâreŋ šiŋuc hâcne fokac: “Bulimakaozi gi bagarehuc sopâc kecɋaŋ nâzo mume mi sakarecnezemec.” Erâ moc šiŋuc: “Gie bapa ŋic e furi fuacneme sâckeocmu.”
Ŋic mocjahazi soŋaŋ moc dâŋko râezo mume mi manacnezemec, ŋic 2 me 3 jaŋe mupie ine manarâ giene bazemec.
Moczi bahac bâfuame âgo guru jaŋere maio mu bâtiŋ ecnetec gâcne jaŋe manahuc hâwic-jopazejec wâc.
No Anutu â Jesu Kristo ere maio â aŋelo bufuŋfâc-ticne jaŋere maio kecšiŋuc mupaŋke-garekopac: Dâŋ gaza qâmoc ekopac i aimuŋ soŋaŋkehaŋ moc mi wahazejec, ehuc maŋgere ŋic ŋokac wiac sâctiri moc mi ejarezemec.
Go ŋic miti giere fâro ehuc biac mi jambuŋ-jopazemec, jaŋere kiŋzi gore faio fezacte. Gahacne maŋ sahac soŋaŋketec ɋaɋacnea fozejec.
Go bukiki â huc šâic gâbâ egareekacte opâ sawa mi nâzemec, waiŋ opâ afecne mac nâzemec wâc.
Ŋic tucne jaŋere sâqocne i fuŋne babataniŋ dameŋ mi maickeha qanaŋ fua taniŋkeekac, tucne jaŋere soŋsoŋ foku šâhec fuaocmu.
Eme eehâmo gie i iŋuc jaha fua taniŋkeekac, â iŋuc mi eekacko soŋsoŋ foku šâhec fua taniŋkeocmu.
Kiŋaŋ qaqa juŋgopieŋ jaŋe sasawa bomboŋfâc-jeŋic sâsec-jopahuc rume-jarenšepieŋ, Anuture šâŋe biŋe babawaha â miti susure fuazacte iŋuc enšepieŋ.
Erâ bomboŋfâc-jeŋic gâcne opâ ruac jaŋe ine šiŋuc mi muhuc bawahac­ jopanšepieŋ: “Mitio sâcnâŋec mocjaha eŋgopeneŋ.” Aricne, “bomboŋfâc-nâŋec jaŋe Wofuŋ manasiŋkepie âgo jauŋ ejareekacte ehâmo-nâreeŋgopieŋ”, iŋuc muhuc kiŋaŋ maŋafec jaha qajarepie sâckeocmu. Go dâŋ i jaza mutâc ehuc faŋ qajarezemec.
Moc e dâŋ i âke sipurâ moc muhuc Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristo ere dâŋbiaŋ qikiŋnehuc miti hatare sâcmutâc râpeckeekac ere šiŋuc muzo:
E maŋgâc erâ sahac-ticne bafehuc dâŋ giŋkeme giŋ bašihuc muraocmu, izi sasec-ticne eocmu hâcne. Eme irec iiŋguuŋ, hehefaric, mumusoriŋ, qoqoric,
erâ wâc mu qaqatarac hati fuaekac. Ŋic iŋucne jaŋe maŋjeŋic sifuckerâ mamana-jeŋic šikeme, moneŋ mafa fua-nârezejec muhuc miti bajuniŋte mueŋgopieŋ.
Miti babajuzi jâmbomac sahacte dope bâbâfua-nârene, mocjaha mukâroŋ tâmiric bajunšepeneŋ.
šiŋuc manasunšepeneŋ: Fuanaŋte mâreŋko metariŋ warembeŋ, juku hâmonaŋte iŋuc jaha metariŋ jaha ranaŋmu.
Eme irec hâcne nânâ wiac â ŋaqi qoruc fonâreme manapene sâckeha junšepeneŋ.
Moneŋ mafa sâko qâhâckezo muniŋmu, jaŋe eesâicte wiwiticko feniŋmu, erâ wiac omane fuŋne fuŋnere sasec bâfuarâ mana utuckehuc sipirickeniŋmu.
Moneŋ mafare andaczi sâqocne gâcnere jâcne hâcne. Ŋic tucnezi irec harac ehuc miti hata qâsorierâ bušâic sâko bâfuambiŋ.
Anuture ŋic go wiac iŋucne geŋkezemec. Ehuc tiŋke biaŋ erâ mitihec â mamanasiŋhec â maŋjauŋhec â sasanaŋhec â buuruchec ecmurâ irec fotac qatariezemec.
Erâ mamanasiŋte juju gie biaŋ bazemec. Baku juju sanaŋte hešakiezemec. Go irec hâcne hefârecgukicne, erâ go gahac iŋuc ecmurâ ŋic tutumaŋko mupaŋketec manambiŋ.
Anutu wiac sasawa juju bâfua-jareekac ere maio â Jesu Kristo kia Pilatorao mumupaŋ fârine muwec ere maio musanaŋke-garekopac:
Go sâcmutâc dâŋ mugarekicne i bâbâsifuc tâmiric â bâbâbiene tâmiric reŋkehuc juhaŋte Wofuŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristo fisizejec.
Irec dameŋ maickeme juju aŋac â tâpiri buc focneekac Anutu hâcne, eki motâc rome fua taniŋkeocmu. E ŋicwofuŋ jaŋere Wofuŋ Sâko â fekicne jaŋere Fekicne.
E bucticne hâhâmo tâmiriczi, tatamac moczi moc mi rarašine irec maŋnao juekac. E ŋic moczi moc mi honekicne erâ mi honezo. Mumumbiaŋ â tâpiri focneweczi focnehuc juocmu sanaŋ. Jâmbomac.
Ŋic mâreŋte moneŋ mafa ɋâfoŋne fojarekac jaŋe jazatec sahac-jeŋic mi bafehuc wiac sisirowenere manapie izi hobeteŋne-jeŋic eme ira mi âtesiŋnenšepieŋ. Anutu e mâriri bâfua-nâreme nâ bac ehuc jueŋgopeneŋ erao âtesiŋnenšepieŋ.
Erâ mu jaretec buafec â bokifac erâ eehâmo gie bahuc mitire fârine bocjaha bâfuanšepieŋ.
Ehuc hobeteŋne-jeŋic moc fofo sanaŋ i bâfuarâ juju fârine rauckenšepieŋ.
O Timoteo, go merâfâc garekicne i soŋaŋkehuc bajuzemec. Erâ dâŋ jawane â fârimâc, ŋic gâcnezi bajuhuc šâŋene “dâŋ qame hukicne” mueŋgopieŋ, i qikiŋnezemec.
Ŋic tucnezi dâŋ ira hâcne qohotahuc mamanasiŋte hata qâsoriembiŋ. Aki anonoczi ŋoŋerao fozejec.
Paulo no Anuture micte, Kristo Jesuzi juju bâfuawec irec biŋedâŋ muiŋnepemurâ Kristo Jesure aposolo epozi
Timoteo motec biaŋ-nane gore papia ši qâreŋkekopac. Anutu Mamac â Wofuŋ-nâŋec Kristo Jesu eraonec aki anonoc, uruc jauŋ â wama gorao fotâcnerâ fozejec.
Mamac ŋosafâc-nane jaŋe maŋfâsâc juhuc tuczi tuc Anuture kiŋaŋ qawarekupie ɋâric-jeŋic noni iŋuc jaha eekopaczi daŋge âzâcnehuc nunumuo šušuhuc ŋafe furec manasucguhuc juekopac.
Nore ki busâqoc emeŋ, irec manasurâ honecguhuc bubiaŋ sâko manapemurâ enareekac.
Erâ mamanasiŋ fârine fogarekac, irec wâc manasuekopac, mamanasiŋ i hâcne mimige Loisi â neŋgocge Eunike jaherao foweczi gorao wâc fotâcnewec fokac i manakopac.
Eme no irec hâcne manasu-gararâ mupe: No menane qizecgao râepe Anutuzi jambuŋ tahacguwec i hehâroŋketec šocne fuazejec.
Ehuc šiŋuc manasuzemec: Anutu e hâbi-nâŋec goroŋkeocte mâro mi nârewec, tâpirihec â maŋ jauŋhec â maŋsowahec enaŋte nârewec.
Irec go Wofuŋ-nâŋecte biŋe mutaniŋkecmurâ mimi gaŋgaŋ mi ezemec, erâ kâpâcwâru ŋicticne nore dâŋ mucmurâ acmeruŋ wâc mi ezemec. Go Anutuzi tâpiri gareme sâc no qâsuecnurâ Biŋebiaŋte erâ šârâ hâriŋ faio juzemec.
Eki hâcne bâpiaŋ-nâporâ tiridâŋ-ticnezi hefârec-nâpowec. I biaŋ-nâŋecte mâcne, e jahac maname fowecte aki anonoc-ticnere erâ iŋuc enârewec. I mârâc jaha jâmbâŋ Kristo Jesure erâ biŋe qanârekicne.
Eme fârine fufua ine dameŋ ši bâbâpiaŋ-nâŋec Kristo Jesu wahame fua tâcnewec. Eki hâcne hâmoc qâmizierâ juju â wiac fofo sanaŋ Biŋebiaŋko bajaŋgeŋke-nârewec.
Eme no irec biŋe mumu â aposolo â qaqazu jupemurâ munarekicne.
No irec hâcne šârâ hâriŋ faio juekopac, ehuc mi mimieekopac. No manasiŋkeekopac ere maŋjahec mi eekopac, aricne, no šiŋuc manapaŋkeekopac, e tâpiriheczi šeŋaŋ-nane sâcne soŋaŋke-narehame dameŋ sâko maickezokac.
Dâŋ fârine irec biri-ticne qazu-garepo ijaha bâjâpezemec, i Kristo Jesu manasiŋkehuc â maŋzi jauŋkehuc iŋuc ezemec.
Tiri Mâro maŋnâŋecko juekac eki neŋgoc ŋegarehame miti kâdoc qârârie-garekicne, i aimuŋ soŋaŋketec fogarezejec.
Asia mâreŋko behecnu-fârembiŋ i manameŋ, Figelo â Hemogene jahe mâmâc.
Wofuŋ e Onesiforo ere wiacfâc maŋuruc qajarezejec. Mamac-jeŋiczi kâpâcwâru ŋic nore mi takickeha bubiaŋ hati qanarehuc juwec.
E Roma haeo fisirâ šoɋac basacnuku bâfuacnuwec.
Wofuŋzi manaha dameŋ sâko Wofuŋtao uruc jauŋ bâfuazejec. E Efesoo wâc kiŋaŋ qaqa gie wemo afecne bawec i go gahac hone manac emeŋ.
Kristo Jesuzi aki anonoc tahacguwec i go motec-nanezi bajuhuc qabocge qame huzejec
Ŋic bocjahazi hone manac ehapie gie gaza gowatuc epo, gie i hâcne ŋic tucne Wofuŋte hatao jueŋgopieŋ â miti munusuŋkeniŋte tâpiri fojarekac iŋucne jaŋe qazu-jaretec banšepieŋ wâc
Go Kristo Jesure momori ŋic sanaŋne juhuc irec šârâ hâriŋ kâdocge rocmurâ mi takicguzejec.
Moc e momori gie baocmuzi wemocko sahackopec gie fuŋne fuŋne ameckeocmu. E momori jaŋere birio râeweczi wiac honeme sâckeocmu i sawa eocte muocmu.
Moc e sisiric gie bahuc sâcmutâc qâsuaocmuzi furine mi roocmu.
Moc e he sarac ehuc šâic-ticne manaocmuzi nânâ fârine micne barâ bâsurâ nâme sâckeocmu.
Dâŋ gazakopac i manatâc qâtâc ezemec. Wofuŋ eki maŋge bâwiŋkeme mana tara-fârezemec.
Go Jesu Kristore mamanac juzemec” e Dawidire ɋâriczi hâmockonec ɋârerâ faharewec” Biŋebiaŋ-ticne iŋuc hâcne muekopac.
Biŋebiaŋ irec erâ šâic fâro manaekopac, erâ wâc sâqocne bapa iŋucne niŋgiŋnumbiŋ ŋekopac Anuture dâŋ ine mi niŋgiŋkekicne.
No šâic gie sasawa i Anutu bâwosâefâc-ticne jaŋere erâ ŋetâcneekopac, jaŋe Kristo Jesure bâbâpiaŋzi ŋihe umbiŋ ejareha eri tatamac fofone mâmâc rauckeniŋte iŋuc eekopac hâcne
Dâŋ šiŋuc fokac i jâmbomac: Ere hâmocko šuhuckembeŋko juju-ticnao iŋuc jaha šuhuckenaŋmu,
šâic mana takirenaŋmuo ehec guriŋ bapa gie wâc banaŋmu. E mic banaŋmuo eki iŋuc jaha mic bacnâpoocmu.
Mumupaŋ-nâŋeczi dockeocmuo ere mumupaŋzi sanaŋkeocmu. Moc murâ moc mu i erao mi fokac.
Go dâŋ i heɋâre-jarerâ Anuture maio mujomirehuc jaza sanaŋketec dâŋ racnere mu iigoc mi enšepieŋ. I wiac fârimâc, iŋuc ehuc miti mamana sipiric-jopaniŋmu.
Anutuzi mana-gareme sâckeocte šoɋachec juhuc giege bazemec, ehuc dâŋ fâri qizecne fâretiŋ jaha mujaŋgeŋkehuc jutec mimizi gieŋic gore faio mi fezejec.
Á dâŋ jawanere ojowane bapie mi bafic-jopazemec. Iŋuc eeŋgopieŋzi eraku miti beheniŋmu.
Burecdâŋ-jeŋiczi biac wicbâroŋ iŋucne erâ ŋedâmâreocmu. Ŋic iŋucne jaŋeraonec moc Himenaio â moc Fileto.
Jahe dâŋ fâri beherâ mukopirec, fafahare i biac fuawec. Iŋuc muhuc ŋic gâcne miti ba imac ejarekopirec.
Anutuzi qânâ wâtuŋ râeme huwec ine qiŋ herâ domakac. Maqâreŋ-ticne šiŋuc fokac: Wofuŋzi biŋefâc-ticne šâŋitac-jopaekac Erâ moc šiŋuc “Wofuŋte šâŋe bajuŋgopieŋ jaŋe šeŋgoma bâbâsifuc râpeckenšepieŋ.”
Ufuŋ sâkoo râqâc wiac goì â siliwazi bakicne i sawa mâcne, jâczi â mâreŋzi bakicne i mâmâc ŋekac. Râqâc gâcnao wiac furi sâkozi huocmu. gâcnao wiac omanezi huocmu.
Moc e bâbâsifuc wiac qikiŋneme maŋne ɋaɋackeme râqâc furi sâko eme ufuŋ runezi jambuŋkerâ bajuhuc izi gie biaŋ fuŋne fuŋne baocmu.
Socɋârizi wiac fuŋne fuŋnere andac eeŋgopieŋ i bâec bazemec. Ehuc maŋjeŋic biaŋkekicnezi Wofuŋ mu wâwâsic ecneeŋgopieŋ jaŋe bafic-jopatec tiŋke biaŋ eere â mamanasiŋte â maŋjauŋte â wamare henširiŋnenšepieŋ.
Mugufuc dâŋ mutucne â racne igockezemec, irec fârine mu qaqatarac sawa fuaekac i manakic.
Wofuŋte kiŋaŋŋiczi mu hehefaric mi ezejec, e ŋic sasawa âgo ejarehuc miti micafec qazu-jarezejec, â pepecne ecnepie wiac aaricko mi ejarezejec”
erâ ŋic maŋrâŋgeŋ ine urucko mu bâtiŋ ejareme Anutu e jahac moc bawahac-jopame maŋjeŋic bârisierâ dâŋfâri šâŋitanšepieŋ.
Eme maŋjeŋic uŋtome, Sataŋte dâŋ reŋkeniŋte wiwitic-ticnao kicjopawec i hetaranšepieŋ.
Go šiŋuc manazemec: Dameŋ tarazo eha sâqocnezi sawe mâririackeocmu.
Ŋic kecšiŋucne juniŋmu hâcne: Jaŋe jaŋacnere sawa manoniehuc juju, moneŋ sasec, ruruc bâbâcne, sahac mumuteŋ, musurecne, neŋgoc mamac dâŋ qaqatara, nâme nikecne, araŋ bapa tâmiric,
maŋjauŋ tâmiric, kiŋ babaju, micko âkechec, nâ areŋne, qicqucne, wiac biaŋne qaqaisoc,
docbapa, enšaŋaucne, pepecne, sasecte aŋac kâcɋene bajuhuc Anuture aŋac mi mamana,
sahaczi miti hawari juhuc mitio sasanaŋ tâmiric juju. Iŋucne hâcne jupie honec-joparâ râpec-jopazemec.
Ŋic mukopac jaŋeraonec tucnezi kamierâ ficbiri juhuc ŋokac kosane, bahac fuŋne fuŋne bâfuambiŋ â saseczi ejareme ra qa ware qa eeŋgopieŋ, iŋucnezi jaŋere eniŋte mu bâdoc ejareeŋgopieŋ”
ŋokac dameŋ sâc mamana gie bahuc dâŋ fâri qizecnere fuŋne mi mana taraeŋgopieŋ iŋucne hâcne.
Mârâc jaha Jaŋe â Jambere jahe Mosere dâŋ bawahapic, iŋuc jaha ŋic mukopac jaŋe maŋjeŋic sifuckekicnere mamanasiŋte hata kâuc bahuc mutuc eeŋgopieŋ.
Erâ wiac eejeŋic wemocko boc efeniŋmu. Mutuc-jeŋicte fuŋne taniŋkeme ŋic sasawa hone-fâreniŋmu, Jaŋe Jambere jaherao fuawec iŋuc.
Go jupe juju-nanezi ine miti mumu-nane, juju-nane, giebapa-nane, mamanasiŋ-nane, buuruc-nane, maŋjauŋ-nane, sasanaŋ-nane,
fific guguriŋ-nane â šârâ hâriŋ-nane, irec hatane âtehuc bâjâpecnuekic. Antiokia haeo â Ikonioŋ haeo â Listera haeo fific guguriŋ enarepie šâic serereŋ mo iŋucne manapo¡ Eme Wofuŋzi sifu wiac iŋucnaonec bataracnuwec.
Erâ ŋic gâcne wâc Kristo Jesurao qohotahuc miti hata âteniŋmu jaŋe mâmâc fific guguriŋ fua-jare-fâreocmu.
Ŋic repicne â eeatucne jaŋe ine jaŋacnao â gâcne jaŋerao eeatuc gie bafeku repire sanaŋkeniŋmu.
Go ine dâŋ qazu-garekicne â maŋge ekicne ira qohotahuc juzemec. Dâŋ moraonec romeŋ i kâuc mi bakomec.
Erâ go ɋieocnecteaŋ tiri papia wose manac ewefuhuc juekicte izi maŋge batamaeha Kristo Jesu manasiŋkehuc bâbâpiaŋ sâcne bâfuacmu.
Miti papia i Anutu Mâro-ticnere qafeŋko fua-fârewec, eme irec wose manac epene mitire fuŋne qazu-nâreekac â mu tutuc enâreekac â mu bâtiŋ enâreekac â tiŋne hata nâwotuekac.
Iŋuc enârehuc bašawiec-nâpokume nâŋâc Anuture ŋicfâri erâ eehâmo gie fuŋne fuŋne sâcne bâfuanaŋmu.
No Anuture maio â Kristo Jesu, juku Wofuŋ tâpirihec fisirâ ɋâricne â hâmokicne dâŋnâŋec mutaraocmu, ere maio gazapaŋkepe manac:
Go miti muminširiŋkezemec, ehuc ŋic irec ejareha me mi ejareha ɋicwânšâŋ jaha jazazemec. Erâ ŋic mu tutuc â mu bâtiŋ â mu sawaŋ ejarehuc qaqazu giege uneŋko tatakic tâmiric bazemec.
Juku dameŋ moc maickeme miti riucdâŋ manapie joŋtaweme qikiŋneniŋmu. Qikiŋnerâ miti hazecte nâpene-jeŋic sawa eme qaqazu mana wosâc ejarepie maŋjeŋic sâckeme iŋucnea guruhec rocjopaniŋmu.
Ehuc mitidâŋ fârine râpeckerâ nemu binaŋko qohotaniŋmu.
Go ine dameŋ sâc maŋtiec juzemec, šârâ hâriŋzi faigao feme sanaŋkezemec, Biŋebiaŋ muromackezemec, gie mugarekicne i basarickezemec.
No ine biac due bazo ekopac, rara dameŋ-nane bembeŋkekac.
No juju gie biaŋ batarakopac, hata-nane âte wareku mao fisikopac, mamanasiŋ-nane soŋaŋkehape mi ŋeŋgoroŋkewec.
Eme ši sambâŋte eri hendiŋ biŋe-nane râekicne fokac, i juku dameŋ sâkoo Wofuŋ, mumutara tiŋne eki narezokac, erâ no sawa mâcne, fifisi-ticnere aŋac-jopaha jueŋgopieŋ jaŋe mâmâc jarezokac.
Go fâro barâ norao biac warezemec.
Dema e mâreŋkopec wiac irec mana kikiwerâ behecnurâ Tesalonike haeo fâwec, Kereske e Galatiao rawec, â Tito e Dalimatia mâreŋko fâwec.
Ʒi Lukahec buc jukoperec. Mareko jowatec mâmâc warezepirec. E giere sâcne baficnuocmu.
Tikiko ine sorepe Efeso haeo fâwec.
Warezo ehuc hata ŋaqi-nane Troa haeo Karpo ere ficko hetarapo i bawarezemec, erâ papia-nane qizecne â rehacne mâmâc amecke warezemec.
Aeŋzi wiac bapa ŋic Alesande e sâqocne bocjaha enarewec, irec Wofuŋzi juku okacne bazucneocmu.
Dâŋnâŋec mâretec ro waha âte ewec. Go ere sawaŋge qazemec.
Dâŋgie-nane bâbâni fuawec dameŋ ira âgo moczi dâŋte mi baficnuwec, aricne, jaŋe behecnu-fârembiŋ” kiŋjeŋic mi fojarezejec.
Wofuŋ eki ine miti musawe tarape qâpuc jaŋe mana-fâreniŋte dopecnurâ basanaŋnuwec, ehuc laioŋte mickonec bataracnuwec.
Wofuŋ e sâqocne irec me irec ŋezicnurâ sambâŋ uucmaŋ-ticnao râecnuocmu. Erao eri tatamac forahuc juzejec sanaŋ. Jâmbomac.
No Prisika â Aqila â Onesiforo wiacfâc-ticne mâmâc manasu-jare-fârekopac, i jazazemec.
Erasto e Korinti haeo juwec â Trofimo e huc bame Milete haeo hetarapo.
Go hoemaŋ dameŋ mi maickeha biac warezemec. Eubulozi manasu-garekac, erâ wâc Pudeŋ â Lino â Klaudia â âgo sasawa jaŋe iŋuc jaha manasu-gareŋgopieŋ.
Wofuŋzi maŋ qâqâtâcgehec juzejec. Aki anonoczi ŋoŋerao fozejec.
Paulo, Anuture kiŋaŋŋic â Jesu Kristore aposolo, no gie munarekicne i Anuture bâwosâecfâc jaŋe mamanasiŋhec eniŋte â dâŋ fâri qizecne mitio fokac i mana taraniŋte”
ehuc juju sanaŋte biŋedâŋ, Anutu burec tâmiriczi mârâc jaha dameŋ mi fowecko muwec, i manahuc juju sanaŋ worickehuc juniŋte.
Dâŋticne i hâcne dameŋ-ticnao mufuahuc Anutu bâbâpiaŋ-nâŋeczi noni muromackepemurâ mupaŋke-narewec.
Eme mamanasiŋ wirec fonârekacte motec jâmbâŋ-nane jukomec Tito go hâcne papia ši râe-garekopac. Anutu Mamac â bâbâpiaŋ-nâŋec Kristo Jesu eraonec aki anonoc â wama gorao fotâcnerâ fozejec.
Gie tofane fokac i bataracmurâ Kreta nucko hetaracgupo, irec gazapo iŋuc ehuc hae sâc soŋaŋ râec-jopa razemec.
Ŋic moc bahac fâsâc â ŋokac mocjahahec juocmu, erâ naru motecfâcne mitihec â šaubac tâmiric â pepecne tâmiric juniŋmu, ŋic iŋucne râec-jopazemec.
Micne bapa moc e Anuture gie soŋaŋkeekaczi bahacmâc juzejec, ehuc pepecne tâmiric â šâšâicne tâmiric â waiŋ âmbâŋ mi nânâ â šikare aafec tâmiric â moneŋ mafare sasec tâmiric, iŋuc juzejec.
Erâ jauŋhec â wiac biaŋne sasawa dodopecke â wama ruaine, tiŋne, araŋ bapanehec â sowa bâtâchec juzejec.
Mitidâŋ mu qaqazuc ehuc hatane basanaŋkekicne i paŋnea bajuzejec. Eme izi tâpiri râcneme dâŋ fâri biaŋ ŋic qazu-jarehuc mu sawaŋ ejarezejec â miti âke sipueŋgopieŋ jaŋere dâŋ bawahazejec.
Ŋic bocjahazi râŋgeŋne â dâŋ racne mumu â eeatuc-jeŋichec juŋgopieŋ, Judaŋiczi opâ ruac jaŋerao wemo afecnezi iŋuc juŋgopieŋ.
Ŋic izi hâcne moneŋ mafare erâ, mumusifuc-jeŋic qatarakicne i musawehuc garikiŋ gâcne furu jaha ba sipiric ejareeŋgopieŋ” ŋic iŋucne jaŋere mic qâbâzickezo.
Kreta jaŋacne porofete moczi šiŋuc muwec: “Kreta ŋic jaŋe burec hati, qowi mimicne â wiac âmbâŋ nânâ.”
No dâŋ i manape jâmbomac ekac. Irec go mu bâtiŋ sanaŋne ejaretec mamanasiŋzi bâɋârec-jopame ɋiɋic qanšepieŋ.
Ehuc Judaŋic jaŋere mamana gufuc dâŋ racne â ŋic dâŋfâri râpeckembiŋ jaŋere sâcmutâc dâŋ mi mananšepieŋ.
Maŋɋaɋachec jueŋgopieŋzi wiac sasaware manapie ɋaɋacne eekac. Á sâqocnezi maŋjeŋic bâbiekume mamanasiŋ tâmiric embiŋ jueŋgopieŋ, jaŋe ine mamana â maŋjeŋic mâmâc wâwânâŋhec efârewecte wiac mocte manapie ɋaɋacne mi eekac.
Jaŋe, Anuture fuŋne manaeŋgopeneŋ, miczi iŋuc muhapie eebapa-jeŋiczi ine mickeekac. Jaŋe ŋic mamakâcne â dâŋ qaqatara, â gie biaŋne moc bapanere sâc mâcne.
Go ine miti riucdâŋ fokac irec sâcko jaza mutâc ezemec.
Ehuc mutec ŋic kâcɋene jaŋe sowa bâtâc â metâne â wama ruaine jupie mamanasiŋ â maŋjauŋ â maŋuruc furu fojarezejec.
Erâ ŋokac kâcɋene iŋuc jaha jazatec miti ŋokac fârine erâ gupe micko âkec tâmiric â nârâmbe tâmiric juhuc juju biaŋte qaqazu enšepieŋ.
Ehuc ŋokac socɋâri jaza mutâc epie ŋowe ɋiefâc-jeŋic jauŋ biaŋne ejarenšepieŋ.
Erâ mimihec erâ sasec tâmiric juhuc nâ qofac â wiac bâpiaŋke emasaŋ ehuc ŋowefâc-jeŋic sâsec-jopanšepieŋ. I Anuture dâŋ susure fuazacte iŋuc enšepieŋ.
Ŋicmotec iŋuc jaha esoc-jopatec sowa bâtâc-jeŋichec junšepieŋ.
Ehuc go gahac wiac biaŋne sasawa irec micne bajarehuc eehâmo gie batec honerâ bâjâpecgunšepieŋ. Miti mutiŋnehuc â bâmâckehuc jazazemec.
Erâ hata sanaŋ fokac irec sâcko musaricketec kisâ jaŋere maŋ henšaŋneme jaŋe burec enâreniŋte dâŋ basarâ behenšepieŋ.
Kiŋaŋ qaqa jazatec bomboŋfâc-jeŋic jaŋere dâŋ reŋke-fârehuc kiŋaŋ biaŋne qajarenšepieŋ, ehuc micjeŋicko mi ronšepieŋ.
Erâ fiuc serereŋ tâmiric juhuc wiac-jeŋic hone qâzuc ehâmonšepieŋ. Iŋuc ehuc bâbâpiaŋ-nâŋec Anutu dâŋticne ba eric ecneniŋmu.
Mâreŋ sâc ŋic biaŋkenaŋte Anuture aki anonoczi bâtâcne bâtimuŋ ewec.
Erâ izi bâfiriec-nâpohuc bâtiŋ-nâpohame qâpuc hata â wiac jawanere andac i qikiŋnerâ mâreŋ šira wama ruaine â tiŋne â mitine junšepeneŋ.
Iŋuc juhuc Anutu sâko â bâbâpiaŋ-nâŋec Kristo Jesu ere eri tatamac fua tâcneme juju aŋacko fisinaŋte irec mamanac junšepeneŋ.
Eki hâcne nâŋâcnere due bahuc sindaŋkonec bâhoc-nâpowec, erâ fuŋfuŋfâc-ticne juhuc mitire fârine šoɋac erâ bâfuanaŋte šure bâpiaŋ enârewec.
Go paŋšâic erâ dâŋ i hâcne jazahuc mu sawaŋ â mu bâtiŋ ejarezemec. Ŋic jaŋe go mi hucgunšepieŋ.
Go dâŋ heɋâre-jarehuc jazatec ŋic jaŋe kia gawamaî â fekicne araŋ bajarehuc dâŋjeŋic reŋkenšepieŋ, erâ gie biaŋne fuŋne fuŋne fokac irec afeckerâ banšepieŋ.
Erâ mumusoriŋ â dâŋ mumuc mi enšepieŋ. Aricne, wamane juhuc ŋic maŋuruc ejare-fârenšepieŋ.
Nâŋâc mârâc jaha iŋuc jaha maŋmutuc erâ râŋgeŋne juhuc qac qâsoric ejumbeneŋ. Erâ sasec fuŋne fuŋne irec kiŋaŋ qahuc sindaŋ â iiŋguuŋ bâfuarâ mamakâcne erâ kikisuec ejumbeneŋ.
Izi šâhec ine bâbâpiaŋ-nâŋec Anutu uruc jauŋ â buafec-ticne fua tâcneme
eki nâŋâc tiŋne juhuc gie moc bambeŋte mâcne, buuruc-ticnere erâ juju ɋârire opâzi â Tiri Mâroraonec fufua ɋâricnezi bâpiaŋ-nâpowec.
E bâbâpiaŋ-nâŋec Jesu Kristore erâ Tiri Mâro afecne mi qoŋgiŋke-nârewec.
I nâŋâc Kristore aki anonocte erâ kiŋnâŋec fâsâeme juju sanaŋte mamanac juku rauckenaŋte iŋuc enârewec.
Dâŋ i jâmbomac, eme go ɋicwânšâŋ erâ âkendâŋnetec Anutu manasiŋkeeŋgopieŋzi eehâmo gie baniŋte šoɋac enšepieŋ. I wiac biaŋne, i epie ŋic jauŋ bacjopaocmu.
Á mugufuc dâŋ jawane â fuŋne qaqa dâŋbiri â sâcmutâc dâŋte mu qaqatarac â bac bârisic ine geŋkezemec. I wiac racne â fârimâc.
Ŋic hâme âkefâucne moc uŋdâŋ mocjaha me jajahec âzâcnetecne qikiŋneme behetec buc juzejec.
Go manakic, ŋic iŋucne e qaqaharicne, maŋnezi mumu hehec ecne-bipieha sâqocne baekac.
No Atema me Tikiko sorepe gorao fâ fisime biac Nikopoli haeo ware bâfuacnuzemec, no hae ira hâcne hoemaŋko juzo mukopac.
Sâcmutâc mamana ŋic Ʒena â Apolo jahe miti kiŋaŋ ranicte nânâ mafa wiac bâmocke-jactetec wiac mi basahuc bititiezepirec.
Ŋicfâc-nâŋec jaŋe wâc eehâmo gie baku maŋjeŋic ezejec, eme sahacte dope babasa fuaocmu sâc jauŋ gie bapie miti-jeŋiczi fârinehec ezejec.
Ŋic nohec jueŋgopieŋ jaŋe sasawa go manasu-gareŋgopieŋ. Mitio âgo enâreeŋgopieŋ jaŋe manasu-jareŋgopeneŋ irec wâc jazazemec. Aki anonoczi sâcŋopa-fârezejec.
Paulo, Kristo Jesure kâpâcwâru ŋic no, â âgo-nâŋec Timoteo, nâhe Filemoŋ joroc babafic-nâhec gore papia ši râekoperec”
erâ wâc ŋokac âgo-nâhec Apia â momori âgo-nâhec Akipo, erâ Filemoŋ gore ficko mitire tumaŋneeŋgopieŋ ŋoŋere mâmâc râekoperec.
Mamac-nâŋec Anutu â Wofuŋ Jesu Kristo eraonec aki anonoc â wama ŋoŋerao fotâcnerâ fozejec.
No nunumuo gore manasuhuc sâc Anutu-nane daŋge âzâcneekopac.
Go Wofuŋ Jesurao â mitiŋic jaŋerao maŋge domakac â jaŋere mamanac juekic irec biŋe manakopac hâcne.
Eme go mamanasiŋko nâŋehec maŋ mocjaha emeŋte wiac biaŋne Kristoraonec fua-nârewec fokac i sasawa mana taracmurâ numuekopac.
Âgo-nane,go mitiŋic bubiaŋ qajareekomec, irec no maŋjauŋgere bunane urueme wemo afecne šeri epo.
Go wiac ecmurâ i no Kristore micte mupaŋke-garezo murâ sâcne afeckerâ ezapo,
erâ sifu maŋjauŋte erâ mâc mu hemunaŋ egarehuc mupe” ŋicqizec Paulo no hâcne, erâ dameŋ ši wâc Kristo Jesure kâpâcwâru ŋic epozi,
no motec-mae Onesimo, kâpâcwâru ficko juhape fua-narewec, ere gazakopac.
E mârâcko jugareme mi sâckewec, ši ine no â go mâmâc junâcteme sâckekac.
Buhândâŋ-nane e hâcne sifu bârisie-garepe fakac
No Biŋebiaŋte erâ kâpâcwâru ficko ŋehape gore âkehoc kiŋaŋ qanareocte sakarezo mupo.
Erâ go mi manahaŋtecne sakarepe urucko mâcne, jâiŋko qikiŋne-narezicte manabâc ehuc bârisie-garekopac.
Behecgume e tâmiric piticne jumeŋ, i fuŋne šiŋucte mecne, risie-garerâ gohec jusanaŋkeocte.
Kiŋaŋ qaqage sawa mâcne, mitio âgoge erâ juocte fagarekac. No hâcne iŋucne junarewec, â go ine fehuc jugareocmu i šiŋucte: Sahaczi gore juweczi Wofuŋte erâ bufuŋge ekac.
Go nore manatec âgoge ekopacko ine e hefârockehuc manatec Paulo hefârockekopac ezejec.
Wiac moc sipiricke-garewecko me tofage moc erao fokacko ine nore muzemec.
Paulo no hâcne ši qâreŋke-garekopac, okacne bazu-garepemu. No nahacne tofa wâc gorao kâcɋene fokac, noraonec hâcne fuameŋ i” erâ irec wemocte boc mupemu.
Âgo-nane, go Wofuŋte erâ wiac buafec tahacnucmurâ enarekac. Kristore erâ bubiaŋ qanarezemec.
Go micrereŋge fokac i manahuc dâŋ ši qâreŋke-garekopac. Erâ manakopac, gazakopac i sawa mi ehuc maŋgere gâcne šuhuckecmu.
Ŋoŋe nunumuzi bataracnupie Wofuŋzi no bâriesiecnu-ŋareme fâpemurâ mukopac, eme go irec ŋeŋe hewâneŋke-narezemec.
Kristo Jesure kâpâcwâru ŋic âgo-nane Epafra e manasu-garekac.
Erâ babaficfâc-nane Mareko, Aristako, Dema â Luka jaŋe iŋuc jaha manasu-gareŋgopieŋ.
Wofuŋ Jesu Kristo ere aki anonoczi maŋŋeŋicko fozejec.
Anutu e mârâc jaha porofete ejareme jaŋe mimiŋnefâc-nâŋec dâŋ hawarine fuŋne fuŋne â hatane fuŋne fuŋne jaza warekuhapie
ine šâhec tataranao, dameŋ šira hâcne, Ŋokâ ecneme dâŋ nâzâwec. ŋokâ e wiac sasawa irec rune juocte mucnewec, ehec hâcne wiac bâfua-fârepic.
Anutu eri tatamac-ticnere qâreŋ erao fuawec fokacte â ju ju-ticnere sâc juekacte tâpiri dâŋticnezi wiac sasawa dope siŋsiŋ ecneha foekac. Eki sâqocne šure bataniŋ gie bafârerâ faic fekicne sâko ere fâreo fewec ŋekac.
Aŋelo hucjopa-fârewec jukac, irec sâcko aŋelo šâŋe siricke-fârehuc šâŋe fekicne hotâckewec.
Anutuzi mo aŋelo mo kecšiŋuc moc âzâcnewec: “Go hâcne ŋokâ-nane, no miŋecgac bâfuacgukopac”? Me kecšiŋuc: “Noni Mamac ecnerâ jupemu â eki Ŋokâ enarerâ juzejec”?
Moc ine juku mârâc fufua e mâreŋko râeme wahaocmu irec dâŋ šiŋuc muwec: “Anuture aŋelofâc jaŋe dieŋzi hecne-fârenšepieŋ.”
Aŋelo jaŋere kecšiŋuc mukicne: “E aŋelofâcne hawari-jeŋic bâtikieme mâŋâŋ eeŋgopieŋ, â kiŋaŋ qaqafâcne hawari-jeŋic bâtikieme šocbâruŋ eeŋgopieŋ
Ŋokâre ine šiŋuc mukicne: “Anutu go ŋicwofuŋ ŋeŋege i ŋeŋe sanaŋ ŋerašihuc juocmu, â ŋicwofuŋ gunuge i bâbâtiŋ gunu biaŋ.
Go tiŋnere egareekac â hehesic ine râsi ecneekic. Irec Anutu, gore Anutu, eki šeri wokemaŋ rua-garewec, i âgofâcge jaŋere sâc jâuruhuc rua-garewec.”
Moc šiŋuc mucnekicne: “Wofuŋ go fufuŋkenao mâreŋte hobeteŋ râemeŋ, â sambâŋne sambâŋne jaŋe megere qâreŋ.
Jaŋe siroweniŋmu, go ine jusanaŋkekic, jaŋe ŋaqi iŋucne raŋɋaŋkeniŋmu.
Ŋaqi iŋucne epie goki bataforiec-jopacmu, eme jaŋe hawari moc eniŋmu. Goki ine juekic ijaha juekic, â jara dameŋge i moc mi taraocmu.”
Anutu e mo aŋelo mo šiŋuc moc âzâcnewec: “Ware fâre-naneo ŋehaŋtec râsifâcge guruc-jopape kikegere ââtesiŋ enšepieŋ”?
Aŋelo sasawa jaŋe mârozi kiŋaŋ qaqa, ŋic bâbâpiaŋ rauckeniŋte mukicne jaŋe bafic-jopaniŋte sorec-jopakicne.
Irec nâŋâc ma bâtirinšipeŋte dâŋ manambeŋ i mocwâc paŋšâic mana sakac enšepeneŋ.
Aŋelo mickonec dâŋ mukicne i mupaŋkekicne, eme huhucke â qaqatara fuame okacnehec ejujec,
izi wemocko bâbâpiaŋ dâŋ fekicne qikiŋnepene okacmâc foocmu? I Wofuŋ e jahac qanaŋ mufuawec, eme hazec fâri-jeŋiczi manambiŋ jaŋe muwarekupie sanaŋke-nârewec.
Ehame Anutu e jahac wâc mâsi â tâpiri wiac šâŋe furu bâfuahuc dâŋ i dopeckehuc Tiri Mârore taha biaŋ manawec sâc kâdoc qajarehuc feŋeŋ râecnewec.
Hae mâreŋ šâhec fuaocmu, dâŋne muŋgopeneŋ hâcne, i Anutuzi aŋelo jaŋe guriŋne baniŋte mi muwec.
Mitiŋic moczi irec dâŋ mutaniŋkewec ine šiŋuc: “Go ŋic e wemomac-ticnere manasucneekic, â ŋicte ɋâric e wemo-ticnere hone maiŋ ecneekic?
Go dameŋ ŋondeŋ bembeŋne mac aŋelo jaŋere wahamicnao juocte mucnemeŋ, go tatamac â šâŋe biŋezi erickemeŋ,
ehuc wiac sasawa kike-ticnere rurumaŋko râemeŋ.” Anutu e wiac sasawa ŋicte rurumaŋko râewec, i bâtâc mi bahuc wiac furu jaha qikiŋnecne-fârewec ekac. Dameŋ šiŋuczia ine wiac šeŋgoma ŋicte rurumaŋko guruckekicne i mi honeeŋgopeneŋ.
Jesu ine honeŋgopeneŋ, e dameŋ ŋondeŋ bembeŋne mac aŋelo jaŋere wahamicne juhuc hâmocte šâic manawecte tatamac â šâŋe biŋe tahackekicne hâporâ jukac. E Anutuzi aki anonoc enâreocte mume hâmoc hâtâne ŋic sasawa nâŋâcnere erâ manawec hâcne.
Wiac sasawa irec rune â bâbâfua e naru motecfâcne bocjaha eri tatamac-ticnao jowac-jopaocte manasuhuc bâbâpiaŋ-jeŋicte micne bapa e šâic serereŋ gie baku mao fisiocte mucnewec i sâcke-hâmowec.
Eme maŋfuru bacjopakac e mecne â furu bacjopakicne jaŋe mecne Mamac-jeŋic mocjaha, irec ɋafâc-nane mujareocte maname mi quŋkeekac.
Dâŋticne šiŋuc hâcne fokac: “No šâŋe biŋege ɋafâc-nane muromacke-jarepe, kikefuŋ guruo šeri mumuteŋ egarepe.”
Erâ moc šiŋuc: “No erao roweckehuc jupemu.” Erâ moc šiŋuc: “Ʒi no erâ Anutuzi ɋie guru narewec nâŋe mâmâc juŋgopeneŋ.”
Eme ɋie jaŋe sahac biuchec sasawa jueŋgopieŋte eki ijaha wâc rowec. I e jahacne hâmoczi hâmoc rune Sataŋ hâcne tâpiri-ticne qame goroŋkewecte,
erâ wâc hâmocte hâhâwiczi niŋgiŋ-jopame dameŋ-jeŋic sâc kâpâcwâru ficko ŋejumbieŋ jaŋe batarac-jopaocte iŋuc ewec.
Wiac i aŋelo kime dopec mi ejareekac i, e Abrahamte ɋâricfâc nâŋâc kime dopec enâreekac.
Eme irec hâcne ɋafâc-ticne jaŋehec sâc mocjaha jâmbâŋ eocte mucnekicne, hatane gâcne moc mi fowec. I taha bapa sâko urucne â hazec hâricne erâ Anuture maio taha gie bahuc ŋic ŋokac nâŋâcne sâqocne šure tâmireocte iŋuc ewec jukac hâcne.
E jahac šâic manahuc eesâicko rašiwecte ŋic eesâic fua-nâreha sâcne bafic-nâpoekac.
Mitiŋic âgofâc-nane, sambâŋte mâmâc hefârec-ŋopakicne, ŋoŋe miti kiŋaŋ ŋic â taha bapa sâko Jesu, šâŋene murâ rereŋ eeŋgopeneŋ, erao findendeŋnenšepieŋ.
Eki gie runere mume rereŋ juwec, Mosezi Anuture ficko juwec irec sâc juwec hâcne.
Fic baekac ere šâŋe biŋezi ficte šâŋe biŋe jâuruekac, sâc ijaha Jesu šai šonšoŋ-ticnezi Mosere sirickekac.
Ficne ficne i bâbâfua-ticnehec, wiac sasawa irec bâbâfua ine Anutu.
Mose e Anuture ficko jufârehuc mume rereŋ gie bawec, i dâŋ šâhec fufuanere biŋe muocte kiŋaŋ qaqa juwec.
Kristo e ine ŋokâzi fic rune jukac. Ficticne nâŋâc hâcne. Erâ i mâc mâcne, wiac biŋe qanârekicne irec mamanac paŋšâic â bubiaŋko juhapene taraocmu, ine ficticne eŋgopeneŋ muzo.
Irec Tiri Mârozi dâŋ šiŋuc muwec i nâŋâcne biŋe ekac: “Ŋoŋe miŋecgac dâŋticne manaŋgopieŋko,
tuhuo eesâic fuame aaricko ekicne, maŋsanaŋ iŋuc mi enšepieŋ.
Mimiŋnefâc-ŋeŋic jaŋe ira wiac bapa-nane jara 40 honembiŋ, erâ sifu pepecne enarehuc esâicnumbiŋ.
Eme no irec manape gâpâreme jaŋere šiŋuc mupo: `Jaŋe maŋjeŋiczi raŋɋa raŋɋa qâsorieeŋgopieŋ, jaŋe nore hata moc mi hone manac embiŋ.'
Iŋucte kimbeŋ qajarehuc mumupaŋ dâŋ šiŋuc mupo: `Jaŋe nore jujumana hae mâreŋko moc mi rašinšepieŋ'.”
Âgofâc-nane, ŋoŋeraonec moc e miti qikiŋnehuc maŋ gâgâpâc erâ Anutu jujune râpeckezacte soŋaŋ babac ehuc junšepieŋ.
Erâ šoaŋne šoaŋne miŋecgaczi miŋegac forahuc juocmu sâc faŋ qaqac enšepieŋ, sâqocnere eeatuczi ŋoŋeraonec ŋic moc ecneme maŋbâzic ezackohec.
Nâŋâc Kristore miti kâdoc babaju, ine fuŋkehuc manasiŋkembeŋ mamanasiŋ i paŋnea bajuku mao fisinaŋmuzi eŋgopeneŋ.
Dâŋ šiŋuc fokac: “Ŋoŋe miŋecgac dâŋticne manaŋgopieŋko, aaricko ekicne, maŋsanaŋ iŋuc mi enšepieŋ”,
ine weni jaŋe dâŋticne mana-bipiehuc aaric bâfuambiŋ? I mockoneczi mâcne, Mosezi micne bajareme Aigita mâreŋkonec warembiŋ ŋicguru i sasawa jaŋe hâcne.
Me weni jaŋere Anutuzi maname gâpâreme jara 40 tarawec? I sâqocne bahuc mâreŋ tuhuo hâmo sipiric embiŋ jaŋere hâcne iŋuc ewec.
Erâ weni jaŋere mumupaŋ dâŋ šiŋuc muwec: Nore jujumana hae mâreŋko mi rašinšepieŋ? I dâŋticne qahuc jumbiŋ jaŋere hâcne muwec.
Irec šiŋuc honeŋgopeneŋ: Jaŋe miti qiqikiŋ-jeŋicte quŋkerâ mi rašimbiŋ.
Jujumana hae mâreŋ-ticnao rašinaŋte mukicne. biŋedâŋ i mi hetâtieme omaewec, irec ŋoŋeraonec moczi hatao sifuckezacte mezac-nâpozejec.
Biŋe biaŋ dâŋ jaŋe jazakicne sâc ijaha nâŋâc nazakicne. Jaŋe ine dâŋ i manarâ maŋjeŋicko mi râepie hurâ fowecte jaŋerao fârimâc ewec.
Nâŋâc miti mana šakieeŋgopeneŋzi jujumana hae mâreŋko rašieŋgopeneŋ. E šiŋuc muwec: “No kimbeŋ qajarehuc mumupaŋ dâŋ šiŋuc mupo: Jaŋe nore jujumana hae mâreŋko moc mi rašinšepieŋ”, i mâreŋ hobeteŋne râehuc wiac sasawa bafârerâ sifu iŋuc muwec.
Irec šoaŋ namba 7 irec dâŋ moc šiŋuc muwec: “Anutu e wiac sasawa bafârereâ šoaŋ 7 ira jumanawec.”
Ehame faic honembeneŋ ine šiŋuc muwec: “Jaŋe nore jujumana hae mâreŋko moc mi rašinšepieŋ.”
Eme ši ŋic gâcnezi jujumana hae mâreŋko rarašinere hata fokac jaha, â mârâc rarašire biŋe biaŋ jazakicne jaŋe qikiŋnehuc mi rašimbiŋ”
irec “miŋecgac” šâfo i mocwâc bahuc šâhec Dawidire micko dâŋ mupac i râeme šiŋuc muwec: “Ŋoŋe miŋecgac dâŋticne manaŋgopieŋko maŋbâzic mi junšepieŋ.”
Josuazi jujumana hae mâreŋ fârine bâfua-jareme muzac, Anutuzi šâhec dameŋ mocte mi muzac.
Irec šiŋuc mananšepeneŋ: Anuture ŋicfâc jaŋere jujumana hombaŋ moc fokac.
Anutuzi gie batararâ jumanawec, iŋuc jaha ŋic moc Anuture jujumanao rašiocmuzi gie-ticne hetararâ jumanaocmu.
Eme nâŋâcnaonec moczi docke sâqorec erâ ŋic mârâc qaqatara hata âtembiŋ ijaha âtezacte jujumana hae mâreŋko rašinaŋte šoɋac enšepeneŋ.
Anuture dâŋ i jujuhec â tâpirihec, erâ sâqe moc bune râpene micnehec irec sâc jâuruhuc mictara jâmbâŋ. Izi nâhuku qâqâtâc â maŋ, bibiric â siec wamboŋ šušuhuc-jeŋic nâtâcneekac, ehuc maŋte mamanasu â mamana wosâc irec fuŋne bataniŋkeekac.
Eme wiac bâfuakicne moczi moc Anuture maio soŋsoŋ mi foekac, erao wiac sasawa tâtâc â foŋ tâmiric foekac. Erao hâcne dâŋgie banaŋmu.
Taha bapa sâko hahaŋnehec moc junârekac, e sambâŋ fotâcne-fârerâ fewec jukac, Jesu Anuture Ŋokâ hâcne, eme iŋucne junârekacte šâŋe-ticne murâ rereŋ enšepeneŋ.
Erâ taha bapa sâko-nâŋec e dodocne enâreme hone qâoma mi enâreekac, nâŋâcnao eesâic fuaekac iŋuc jaha wâc erao eesâic fuŋne fuŋne fuawec, eesâicko dodocke mocjaha ine mi ewec.
Irec nâŋâc aki anonoc ŋeŋe rowaŋnao maŋafec jaha fisihuc junšepeneŋ, eme wiac izi me izi maic maic-nâpoha eki buuruc enârehuc aki anonoc-ticnere erâ bafic-nâpozejec.
Mâreŋŋic nâŋâcnaonec taha bapa sâko rowosâec-jopakicne sasawa jaŋe ŋic jaŋere erâ Anutu fuacnehuc kiŋ bahacte taha bâzi rikecne niŋte râec-jopakicne.
Taha bapa iŋucne e jahac ŋic dodocne jukacte ŋic mutucne â qâsoriekicne sâcne urucne ejareekac.
Erâ fuŋne iŋucte ŋic jaŋere kiŋ bahacte mecne â e jahacne mâmâc taha bâzi rikeocte mukicne
Gie fekicne i ŋic moczi maŋticnere mi rorâ bapane, taha bapa ŋic moc e Anutuzi rowosâerâ gie mucneme sâcne baocmu, Aroŋ iŋuc hâcne ecnewec
Eme Kristo e iŋuc jaha e jahacne maname fefene eha taha bapa sâko mi ewec, i Anutuzi šiŋuc muhuc mucnewec: “Go hâcne Ŋokâ-nane, no miŋecgac bâfuacgukopac.”
Erâ dâŋ moc šiŋuc muwec: “Goki Melikisede ere sâcko taha bapa jurašihuc jucmu sanaŋ.”
Jesu e mâreŋko juwec dameŋ ira, hâmockonec bataraocte tâpiri focnewec erao numuhuc kio wâwâsic kâcɋene ecnewec. Ehuc Anutu araŋ bacnewecte manacnewec.
E ŋokâ juwec, erâ sifu šâic gie baku micrereŋte fuŋne mana tarawec.
Erâ wiac emataucke-fârerâ mume rereŋfâc-ticne sasawa jaŋere bâbâpiaŋ tatara tâmiric bâfuawec.
E hâcne taha bapa sâko erâ Melikisede ere sâcko juocte Anutuzi mucnewec.
Irec dâŋ bocjaha fokac, erâ ŋoŋe hazecfâŋ juŋgopieŋte ŋaza mutâc epemurâ manape ŋemâckekac.
Ŋoŋe dameŋ šora miti mana wareeŋgopieŋzi gâcne qazu-jarepie sâckezac” eme iŋucne ŋoŋe miti maine i mocwâc qaqazu-ŋarenere sâc eŋgopieŋ. Ŋoŋe nânâ sanaŋnere sâc aricne, susu nânâre sâc sawa juŋgopieŋ.
Susu nâeŋgopieŋ jaŋe ine ɋiene mujarezo, iŋucnezi dâŋ fârine wemocko mana taraniŋmu?
Nânâ sanaŋne i sokakicne jaŋere biŋe, maŋ mamanasu-jeŋic fua tâcneme biaŋne sâqocne mana wosâeeŋgopieŋ jaŋere biŋe hâcne.
Irec nâŋâc ši Kristore dâŋ maine, fufuŋkeo mumune, i râepene foha dâŋ hukicne, wiac efehuc mumune, i moc šuhuckenaŋ. Wemocte miti hobeteŋne i hâsine râehuc maŋ bâbârisie â juju raŋɋa bebehe â Anutu mamanasiŋ,
â Miti Opâ â qizecko me rârâe â hâmockonec fafahare â bâtâc sanaŋ irec dâŋ mocwâc fuŋkezo?
Anutuzi maname sâckeme dâŋ moc šuhuckenaŋ.
Ŋic mitizi maŋjeŋic batamaeme sambâŋkonec nânâ nâhonembiŋ â Tiri Mârohec embiŋ,
erâ Anuture dâŋbiaŋ â juju sanaŋte tâpiri mana aŋac embiŋ,
ŋic iŋucne jaŋe miti behe sanaŋkehuc Anuture Ŋokâ jaŋacne maŋte mocwâc maripoŋko qahuc mamakâc ecnepie mitio bâbârisiec-jopane mi fokac.
Mâreŋ moc hoezi gâbâ hehuc bâgunuckekume, ŋic sara mamac eeŋgopieŋ jaŋere biŋe nânâ monšaŋ bâfuaekac, i Anutu jambuŋ-ticnere fârine fuacneekac.
Á mâreŋ mocko hofâ qinšiŋ sawa fuaocmu, ine fârimâc ekacte sâwec fâreme juku šoczi šaocmu.
Âgofâc, no dâŋ mukopac i ŋoŋe sipirickeniŋmu manahuc mâcne, mitio biaŋke-hâmoniŋmu, iŋuc manahuc mukopac.
Anutu e eesifucne mâcne” ŋoŋe ere erâ ŋicfâc-ticne hone bafic ejarehuc jauŋ bacjopambiŋ erâ eeŋgopieŋ jaha irec wemocko nikeckeocmu.
Ŋoŋe šiŋuc eniŋte enârekac: ŋoŋe mâmâc sasawa sâc ijaha ɋicwânšâŋ epie sambâŋ šeŋaŋ bâbâfuare buâkec mi omaezejec, fofehame dameŋ tarazejec.
Eme mi rokawehuc, mitiŋic gâcne mamanasiŋ â sasanaŋhec juhuc wiac biŋec-nâpokicne rauckeeŋgopieŋ, jaŋere hata âteniŋmu.
Jaŋeraonec moc Abraham e Anutuzi biŋedâŋ âzâcnerâ femicne mocte maio mupaŋkeocte basarâ e jahacnao râehuc mupaŋkewec.
Ehuc šiŋuc muwec: “No jambuŋgurâ jambuŋgu epemu â basawecgurâ basawecgu epemu.”
Eme Abraham e mumupaŋ dâŋ irec woŋec tatakic tâmiriŋ juku fârine rowec.
Ŋiczi fekicne moc ere maio mumupaŋ dâŋ mupene mu qaqatarac eene mi fuaocmu.
Irec Anutu e ŋic biŋe qajareme maŋjahec enšipiŋte, maŋticnezi sanaŋkeha muwec irec fuŋne bataniŋkehuc biŋedâŋ irec fainao mumupaŋ dâŋ šuhuckewec.
Anutu e burec tâmiriczi dâŋsanaŋ jajahec âkendâŋ-jofahuc nâŋâcnao suru râewec, i ere dapeŋko rašimbeŋzi wiac biŋe qanârekicne irec fârine fotarierâ ronaŋte manasuhuc ewec.
Biŋe qanârekicne irec fârinezi juju-nâŋecte aŋga sanaŋne â tâtâcne tâmiric iŋucne ekac, erâ aŋga izi faic qoruc ââketâc irec râpenao râekicne fokac.
Ââketâc i micne bapa-nâŋec Jesu eki bânie-nârehuc fotâcnerâ maŋnao rašiwec. E Melikisede ere sâcko taha bapa erâ jusanaŋkeekaczi iŋuc ewec hâcne.
Melikisede e hâcne Salem haere ŋicwofuŋ â Anutu femicne sâko ere taha bapa juwec. Eki hâcne Abrahamzi ŋicwofuŋ râsifâc-ticne joparâ risiehame ra hatao bâfuarâ jambuŋkewec.
Erâ e hâcne Abrahamzi mafa mateŋ bâtâc barâ teŋkonec wâŋ irec sâc râcnewec. Melikisede šâŋe-ticne nâŋâcne dâŋko “Tiŋne ŋicwofuŋ”, â Salem ŋicwofuŋ ine “Wama ŋicwofuŋ”.
Melikisede e neŋgoc mamac tâmiric, apa ŋosa fuŋne-ticne qahuc mi mufuakicne, e juju-ticne fufuŋke tâmiric â tatara tâmiric. E Anuture ŋokâ ere sâsâc eocte mukicnezi taha bapa juju hati ewec.
Ʒi honeniŋ, e ŋic fekicne mo iŋucne irec mimiŋne-nâŋec Abrahamzi mafa mateŋ biaŋne sasawa bâwosâerâ teŋkonec wâŋ irec sâc râcnewec
Lewi-e ɋâricfâc gâcne taha gie baniŋte mujarekicne jaŋe ŋic ŋokac âgofâc-jeŋic Abrahamte tofafâc jaha sifu mafa wiac teŋkonec wâŋ irec sâc jowac roniŋte sâcmutâc dâŋqâhâcko mutâcne-jarekicne.
Á Melikisede e jaŋere guruonec mi fuakicnezi ine Abrahamtaonec teŋkonec wâŋ rowec Ehuc miti biŋe qacnekicne e jambuŋkewec.
Á fekicnezi wahakicne jambuŋkeekac i mozi mickeocmu?
Dameŋ ši ŋic sisirowenezi teŋkonec wâŋ roeŋgopieŋ” ira ine juju hati mucnekicnezi rowec.
No manape šiŋuc ekac, Lewi e teŋkonec wâŋ roekaczi Abrahamte bifuŋko fohuc wiac i Melikisede râcnewec”
e mamac-ticnere bifuŋko fohame Melikisedehec bâbâfuac epicte Abrahamzi râcneme Lewizi mâmâc râcnewec ekac.
Lewire ɋâricfâc jaŋere taha bapa gie sâcke-hâmozac muzac, wemocko šâhec taha bapa moc Melikisede ere sâcko fuazac â Aroŋte sâcko aricne? Taha bapa giere erâ ŋic ŋokac sâcmutâc dâŋ jarekicne.
Eme taha bapa gie raŋɋane rârieha ɋâricne moc fuame, raŋɋanere sâcmutâc dâŋ iŋuc jaha râriehame ɋâricne moc fuaocmu.
Findaŋdâŋzi ŋic rokac e taha ufuŋko gie mujarekicne jaŋere guruonec mi fuawec, e guru mockonec.
Wofuŋ-nâŋec e Judare tofafâc jaŋeraonec fuawec, i mana-fâreŋgopeneŋ. Eme ŋicguru i jaŋe taha gie baniŋte Mosezi moc mi muwec.
Erâ irec fuŋne moc taniŋke-hâmokac wâc. Taha bapa moc Melikisedere sâcko fuaocte mukicne,
e sahaczi fuakicnere sâcmutâc râekicne irec sâcko mâcne, juju fofo sanaŋte tâpirio taha bapa erâ juwec jukac.
Ere hâcne dâŋ šiŋuc mutaniŋkekicne: “Goki Melikisede ere sâcko taha bapa jurašihuc jucmu sanaŋ.”
Ine hâcne sâcmutâc dâŋ mârâc mukicne i tâpirimâc â fâri tâmiric ewecte bârâriekicne.
Sâcmutâc dâŋzi wiac moc mi emataucke-fârewec” eme irec okacne woworic fârine bâfuakicne, izi fârec-nâpome Anutu sâcne maickeeŋgopeneŋ.
Ɋâricne fuawec i mumupaŋ dâŋsanaŋ tâmiric mi fuawec raŋɋane jaŋe mumupaŋ tâmiricko taha bapa erâ jumbiŋ.
Ɋâricne ši ine mumupaŋ faio taha bapa ewec jukac. Ere dâŋqâreŋ šiŋuc fokac: “Wofuŋzi mumupaŋ dâŋ muwec i mi beheocmu: `Goki taha bapa jurašihuc jucmu sanaŋ'.”
Fuŋne iŋucte šâšâfic fârinere jâcne ewec, Jesu hâcne.
Raŋɋane jaŋe hâmohuc tuczi tuc juwarembiŋte bocjaha juwarembiŋ.
Ɋâricne e ine juju sanaŋ jukacte taha bapa gie-ticne šušuhuc focnehuc juocmu sanaŋ.
Irec ere ŋesiŋko Anutu maickeeŋgopieŋ jaŋe sâcne bâbâpiaŋko râe basanaŋ ejareekac, e juju sanaŋ jukaczi hâcne dameŋ sâc roroŋ sasape ejareekac.
Taha bapa sâko-nâŋec hâcne e furu, bahacmâc, ɋaɋacne, sâqocne bapa jaŋere sâcko mi juhuc qâtâcnerâ pectâc jujune, erâ sambâŋ hucke-fârewec jukac. Iŋucnezi hâcne junâreme sâcke-hâmokac.
E taha bapa raŋɋane jaŋe iŋucne mâcne, e sindaŋ tâmiriczi wemocko šoaŋne šoaŋne qanaŋ e jahacne sindaŋte erâ taha bâzi rikerâ šâhec ŋic jaŋere rikezac, e jahacne maŋ sahac i taha bâzi-nâŋec mocjaha hâcne râeme tarawec.
Sâcmutâc dâŋko ŋic maŋjeŋiczi dodocne jaŋe taha bapa sâko juniŋte mukicne. Eme šâhec ine sâcmutâc dâŋ faicnao mumupaŋ dâŋsanaŋzi Ŋokâ âkendâŋnewec. Eki hâcne maŋfuru jaha jurašihuc juocmu sanaŋ.
Dâŋ mukicne irec hândâŋne šiŋuc: Taha bapa sâko junârekac e faic sambâŋko femicne sâko ere ŋeŋefuŋko mefârenao fewec ŋeekac.
E furu ufuŋ, mitific fârine hâcne, irec taha bapa jukac. Ufuŋ i ŋiczi mâcne, Wofuŋ e jahac bâfuawec.
Taha bapa sâko sasawa jaŋe nânâ qowi bâzi râe rikec eniŋte mujarekicne, irec taha bapa sâko-nâŋec wemocko taha bâzi tâmiric juzac?
Erâ e mâreŋko juhuc muzac taha bapa mi juzac, mâreŋko sâcmutâc dâŋte sâcko bâzi ririke ŋic sâcne juŋgopieŋ.
Jaŋe gie-jeŋic mitific jabane â sâsâcne ira baeŋgopieŋ, fârine ine sambâŋko ŋekac. Mose e mitire qoruc boze bazo ehame Wofuŋzi šiŋuc âzâcnewec: “Manakic, tikio hawarine gowatukicne irec sâcko wiac sasawa bazemec.”
Ʒi ine Jesuzi šâšâfic fekicnere jâcne juekacte taha gie fekicne jaha baekac. Ʒâšâfic fekicne ine biŋedâŋ fekicnezi hobeteŋ ecneha bâfuakicne.
Mârâc šâšâfic fowec, izi fârinehec eme muzac šâhec moc fuaocte dâŋne mi fuazac.
Anutu eki ine ŋic jaŋere maname mi sâckeme šiŋuc muwec: “Juku dameŋ mocko Israe kikefuŋ â Juda kikefuŋ jaŋehec šâšâfic ɋâricne moc bâfuapemu, Wofuŋzi iŋuc mukac.
Mârâc mimiŋnefâc-jeŋic Aigita mâreŋkonec jowac-jopapere mejeŋicko rohuc jaŋehec šâšâfic epo, šâšâfic iŋucne mâcne; jaŋe šâšâfic irec maŋnao paŋšâic mi jupie noni râpec-jopapo, Wofuŋzi iŋuc mukac.
Á šâhec Israe kikefuŋ jaŋehec šâšâfic epemu ine kecšiŋuc: No mumupaŋ dâŋnane maŋjeŋicko râepe huocmu, erâ buhândâŋ-jeŋicko qâreŋkepe foocmu, eme no Anutu-jeŋic jupemu â jaŋe kikefuŋfâc-nane juniŋmu.
Eme ŋic moczi ŋicâgo-ticne me ŋic moczi qomâ-ticne šiŋuc mi muhuc miti qazucneocmu: Ajoc, go Wofuŋte fuŋne manac â!' Macne, jaŋe wahakicnezi mecne fekicnezi mecne mâmâc manacnu-fâreniŋmu.
Ʒiŋucte manacnuniŋmu: No kiŋjeŋic behe-jarepemu â sindaŋ-jeŋicte mocwâc mi manasupemu, Wofuŋzi iŋuc mukac.”
Eme Wofuŋ e šâšâfic ɋâricnere dâŋ muhuc, mârâc fowec irec “raŋɋaŋkekicne” muwec. Eme wiac raŋɋaŋkekicne â gufekicne izi arictac ezo ekac hâcne.
Ʒâšâfic raŋɋanao Wofuŋ mai eecnere hata fowec â irec tiri qoruc boze mâreŋko ŋewec wâc.
Mitire qoruc boze hâcne kecšiŋuc bambiŋ: Maŋne moc maine, šâŋene Furufic mukicne, ira kendo kikenehec domawec erâ tebo ŋewec fainao poroŋ furu mukicne i fowec.
Eme bumec maŋne moc âke tâcnekicne fowec, šâŋene Furu Dindiŋ mukicne.
Ira hosâc ririke alata golzi bakicne ŋewec, erâ šâšâficte qorac tapa katapa golzi ɋorockekicne i ŋewec, erâ Aroŋte gunu ɋârerâ gitec hekicne i â qorac tapa mâmâc râekicne.
Fainao ine tatamacte kerubim hawari jajahec fakec-jekiczi katapa tapane sâockehuc domapic. Irec dâŋ ninic jaha wemocko mufârezo.
Wiac iŋuc râepie fohame fic maŋne maine ira taha bapa jaŋe dameŋ sâc fec wahac ehuc gie-jeŋic bajumbieŋ.
Fic maŋne moc ira ine taha bapa sâko e bucticne jara moc maŋnao arec mocjaha fejujec. Erâ soc tâmiric aricne, sochec sasawa fehuc e jahacne â ŋic jaŋere bahacte tie jujec.
Wiac irec fuŋne Tiri Mârozi šiŋuc nâwotukac: Maŋne maine izi ŋehame furu ufuŋko rarašire hata mi fua tâcnekac.
Maŋne maine izi dameŋ šiŋuczia mâreŋko juŋgopeneŋ irec sâsâcne ekac. Tiri qoruc bozeo nânâ qowi bâzi râe rikec ee izi wemocko ŋic Anutu mai ecnembiŋ jaŋere maŋ bâpiaŋkezac?
I sahackopec sâcmutâc dâŋ sawa, nânâ opâre â sahac šušurere dâŋ fowec iŋucne, i šâhec fârinezi âkehockeocte jaba fowec.
Kristo eki ine wiac fârine fuaocte mukicne irec taha bapa sâko fuawec, ehuc qoruc boze sâc moc, fârine jâmbâŋ, mezi mi bakicne, mâreŋko mi ŋeŋene, ira rašiwec.
Noniŋ bulimakao sochec mâcne, e jahacne sochec Furuficko arec mocjaha rašihuc kitâc-nâpowec izi fofo sanaŋ foocmu.
Noniŋ bulimakao soc â bulimakao šafe i ŋic wâwânâŋ fua-jarewec jaŋe epie furu bacjopame sahackopec ɋaɋackembiŋ”
Kristo e ine Mâro juweczi jukac eki neŋgoc ŋecneha maŋ sahac-ticne Anutu taha bâzi furu biaŋ ecnewec, eme nâŋâc eebapa aputacnezi maŋnâŋec hegâpârembeŋ i Kristore soczi sâcne šure ɋaɋackeme Anutu jujune kiŋaŋ qacnenaŋmu.
Irec hâcne Kristo e šâšâfic ɋâricnere jâcne ewec, erâ šâšâfic raŋɋanao juhuc kiŋ bâfuakicne i taraocte hâmowec, eme irec biŋefâc-ticne jaŋe juju sanaŋte merâfâc roniŋte mujarekicne i sâcne roniŋmu.
Merâfâcte hata šiŋuc fokac: Runezi hâmome jaha rauckezo.
Ɋâricne juhame merâfâcte dâŋ mukicne i mâc foocmu, hâmome ine dâŋ irec fârine fuaocmu.
Irec hâcne šâšâfic raŋɋane i soc tâmiricko wâc mi fuawec.
Mose e sâcmutâc dâŋqâhâc jâcne jâcne, mutâcnekicnere sâcko ŋic jazaku jaza-fârerâ bulimakao â noniŋsoc opâhec bâsifuckerâ kâcbiŋko lama kanšaŋ bâbâroŋ qâfiserâ izi soc tieme miti papia mecne ŋic ŋokac mecne mâmâc rua -jarewec.
Ehuc šiŋuc jazawec: “Anutuzi šâšâficte dâŋ mupaŋke-ŋarejec irec soc ši hâcne.”
Erâ taha boze â taha giere râqâc wiac i iŋuc jaha soczi ruacne-fârewec.
Ine hâcne, sâcmutâc dâŋko mukicnere wiac šeŋgoma qâririŋ soczi šure ɋaɋackezo, â soc tâmiricko sâqocne bâbâtâmire mi fokac.
Sambâŋko wiac fârine fokac irec sâsâc wiac i soc omanezi šure ɋaɋackeocte mukicne, â wiac fârine e jahacne ine taha furi sâkozi šure ɋaɋackeocte hatane mocjaha fokac.
Irec hâcne Kristo e furu ufuŋ mezi bakicne, fârine irec sâsâcne mac, ira mi rašiwec, e sambâŋ maŋnao rašiwec, eme ira Anuture maio juhuc nâŋâcnere erâ taha gie-ticne baekac.
Erâ e maŋ sahac-ticne hâsi fâri taha-nâŋec qikiŋneocte wâc mi fewec, taha bapa sâkozi jâmbomac jarane jarane feekac, ehuc e jahacne soc mâcne, soc jabane rorâ tiri ufuŋko feekac.
Kristo e iŋucnere sâc erâ muzac mâreŋ fuaweckonecteaŋ wemo afecne hâmo warehuc juzac. E ine iŋuc mi ehuc dameŋ ŋondeŋ tataranao due-nâŋec bahuc kiŋnâŋec bârârieocte fua tâcnewec.
Ŋiczi mocjaha hâmonaŋte munârekicne, eme irec faicnao dâŋnâŋec mumutara fuaocte mukicne”
eme Kristo e iŋuc jaha, ŋic bocjaha kiŋjeŋic âsickehuc mocjaha hâcne hâmoweczi mocwâc sâqocnere gie baocte mâcne, e worickehuc jueŋgopieŋ jaŋe rocjopaocte sawa fua taniŋkeocmu.
Sâcmutâc dâŋko wiac mukicne i mâc šâhec fârine fuaocmu irec mumucne sawa fuakac, fârine jâmbâŋ mâcne. Irec taha bapa jaŋe sâcmutâc dâŋ reŋkehuc jarane jarane taha barâ ba epie ŋic ira Anutu mai ecneeŋgopieŋ jaŋe sâcne maŋfuru mi bacjopaekac.
Iŋuc eme muzac, taha bâzi ririke omaezac i¡ Ira Anutu mai ecneeŋgopieŋ jaŋe kiŋfâsâc enšapiŋ muzac, kiŋjeŋicte manabâc mocwâc mi enšapiŋ.
Taha bâzi izi ine jarane jarane fuame kiŋjeŋicte manasueŋgopieŋ.
Noniŋ bulimakao soczi wemocko kiŋjeŋic bâtâmirezac? I aricne.
Irec hâcne Kristo mâreŋko wahaocte dâŋ šiŋuc muwec: “Taha bâzi fuŋne fuŋnere mi egareekac, sahac ine bâfua-narekomec.
Qowi hâcbuc ririke me sâqocnere taha bapa i fua-gareocte mi muekic.
Eme mupo, `Manakic, no Anutu gore mic reŋkepere fisikopac', miti papiao nore dâŋ qâreŋkekicne irec sâcko.”
Faic dâŋ šiŋuc muwec fokac, “Taha bâzi fuŋne fuŋne â qowi hâcbuc sâqocnere taha irec mi egareekac â irec takicguekac” wiac i sâcmutâc dâŋte sâcko râe rikec ekicne.
Erâ dâŋ šiŋuc šuhuckerâ muwec: “Manakic, gore dâŋ reŋkepere fisikopac”, iŋuc muhuc wiac raŋɋane bârârierâ ɋâricne moc âkendâŋnewec.
Irec Anuture micdâŋte erâ Jesu Kristo e sahac-ticnezi taha bame maŋfuru embeŋ, i arec mocjaha ekicnezi fofo sanaŋ.
Taha bapa sasawa jaŋe šoaŋne šoaŋne gie-jeŋic bahuc bâzi ijaha hati rikerâ rike ehuc jueŋgopieŋ, eme izi kiŋ bahac sâcne moc mi bâtâmireekac.
Kristozi ine sâqocne-nâŋecte taha mocjaha bame tarame faic Anutu mefârenao fewec jukac.
Eme ira râsifâc-ticne dockerâ waha fohuc kike-ticnere ââtesiŋ eniŋte woŋec juekac.
Maŋfuru eere hatao juŋgopieŋ jaŋere taha mocjaha bahuc bâbâpiaŋ-jeŋicte gie batarawec.
Eme Tiri Mârozi irec dâŋ mufua-nârekac wâc. Qanaŋ dâŋ šiŋuc fokac, Wofuŋ e kecšiŋuc mukac:
“Ʒâhec dameŋko jaŋehec šâšâfic epemu ine kecšiŋuc: No mumupaŋ dâŋnane maŋjeŋicko râepe huocmu, erâ buhândâŋ-jeŋicko qâreŋkepe foocmu.”
Erâ šuhuckekac, “No kiŋjeŋic behe-jarepemu â sindaŋ-jeŋicte mocwâc mi manasupemu.”
Sâqocne tâmire-fâreme ine irec taha bapa iŋuc jaha omaeocmu.
Âgofâc, Jesu e socticnezi motâc ronârewecte furu ufuŋko fenaŋte maŋnâŋe. afeckekac.
Irec hatane ɋâricne â jujune ine e jahac bâšâwe-nârewec. Ehuc ââketâc fowec, sahac-ticne hâcne, i fotâcnerâ fewec.
Eme taha bapa fekicne Anuture ufuŋ qizeckerâ junârekac.
Irec nâŋâc mamanasiŋzi maŋnâŋec baafeckeha siocmâc mai ecnehuc junšepeneŋ. Ine qanaŋ maŋnâŋec kiŋzi hegâpârekicne i socticnezi ruacneme taniŋkeha â sahac-nâŋec opâ ɋaɋaczi šureha iŋuc sâcne enaŋmu.
Erâ mume sasanaŋzi wiac biŋe qanârewecte biŋedâŋ i kiki papaŋ jaha bajuhuc muhaŋnenšepeneŋ.
Erâ wâc sosoŋaŋ ehuc maŋjauŋte â eehâmo giere qaqafeŋ enšepeneŋ.
Ehuc mitire tutumaŋko gâcnezi mi fisihuc qâoma eeŋgopieŋ iŋuc mi ezo. Dameŋ sâko bâqiŋ-nâpokac, iŋuc hâcne manahuc šoɋac erâ faŋ qaqac enšepeneŋ.
Nâŋâc dâŋ fâri qizecnezi maŋnâŋec âke tamaehame sâqocne mana jaŋgeŋkehuc bapene mozi irec taha bame tâmireocmu? Aricne, iŋuc mi fokac,
ine okacne hâhâwicne â šocbâruŋ sâko izi sawa woŋec-nâŋec foocmu. Ʒocbâruŋ izi mitire râsifâc šâmiziec-jopaocmu hâcne.
Ŋic moczi Mosere sâcmutâc dâŋ mana suahuc qame ŋic jajahec me jahec â moczi mujaŋgeŋkepie acmâc jaha qapie hâmoekac.
Eme ŋic moc e Anuture Ŋokâ ro waha âte ecnehuc, šâšâficte soc ruarâ maŋfuru ewec i mana suahuc aki anonoc rune Mâro musoriŋkeocmu, e okacne mo iŋucne fisicneocmu muŋgopieŋ?
Nâŋâc dâŋ kecšiŋuc muwec ere fuŋne manaeŋgopeneŋ: “Kiŋ babatara i nore gie, okacne babazu i noni epemu.” Erâ moc šiŋuc fokac: “Wofuŋ e ŋicfâc-ticne jaŋere dâŋ mutara-jareocmu.”
Anutu jujune ere meo fefe i wiac hâhâwicne jâmbâŋ.
Ŋoŋe mârâc wiac ejumbieŋ irec manasunšepieŋ. Dameŋ ira maŋŋeŋiczi hae furehame fific guguriŋ maŋko juju gie sâko bahuc sanaŋkembiŋ.
Eme gâcne ŋoŋe imaŋ gomaŋ â šâic busâqoc fai-ŋeŋicko feme ŋic jaŋere maio mamakâc embiŋ, â gâcne ŋoŋe ine âgofâc-ŋeŋic wiac iŋucne ejarepie šâic-jeŋic mâmâc manambiŋ.
Ŋoŋe âgofâc-ŋeŋic kâpâcwâru ficko fepie jaŋere erâ buheric fua-ŋarewec, â moneŋ mafa ŋowac ropie ine mafa fârine fofone fonârekac muhuc manapie bubiaŋnehec ewec.
Eme ši hâbi-ŋeŋic mi goroŋkezejec, hâbihec juku furine kâcɋene rozo.
Irec ŋoŋe sasanaŋ bâfuarâ Anuture micdâŋkoa juku wiac biŋe qaŋarekicne irec fârine ronšepieŋ.
“Irec dameŋ bembeŋne mac moc fokac i tarame wareocte mukicne e ŋeŋe râqâc mi ehuc biac fisiocmu.
Ŋicnane biaŋkekicnezi ine mamanasiŋte erâ juju hotâckeocmu, â docke pârâc eocmuo maŋnanezi manacnepe mi biaŋkeocmu.”
Nâŋâc ine docke pârâc ehuc sisipiricko rara irec biŋe mâcne, nâŋâc manasiŋkehuc maŋ qâqâtâc ŋeŋezic irec biŋe.
Wiac biŋe qanârekicne i manapaŋkerâ irec woŋec juju, â wiac mi hohonene maŋzi sakarerâ babaju, izi mamanasiŋ ekac.
Mitiŋic raŋɋane jaŋe mamanasiŋ iŋucnehec jupie Anutuzi honec-jopame biaŋkewec hâcne.
Mâreŋ i Anuture micte fuawec, ine mamanasiŋhec juhuc mana taraeŋgopeneŋ. Wiac hohonene i mi honekickonec fuawec hâcne.
Mamanasiŋhec juhuc Abezi Anutu bâzi rikecneme honeme sâckeha Kaiŋte qikiŋnewec. Mamanasiŋ-ticnere hâcne Anutuzi honeme kiŋfâsâc eme bâzi-ticne rohuc fuŋne-ticne bataniŋkewec. E mamanasiŋhec juwecte manapene hâmokicnezi sifu dâŋ nâzâkac ekac.
Enoko e mamanasiŋhec juwec, irec hâmoczi mi bâuaocte Anutuzi ɋâricne bafewec. Iŋuc ecnewecte ŋiczi basambiŋ. Erâ mi feha fuŋne-ticne biac šiŋuc mutaniŋkekicne: Anutuzi e honeme biaŋkewec.
Mamanasiŋ tâmiric jupene Anutuzi honec-nâpome bibiaŋke ine mi fokac. Anutu mâc mai mi ecnezo, jukac i mana šakiezo, â maŋzi hefârepene tahac-nâpoekac dâŋ i mana šakiehuc mai ecnezo.
Noa e mamanasiŋhec juwecte Anutuzi wiac šâhec fuaocmu irec biŋe qanaŋ âzâcnewec. Âzâcneme araŋ bacnehuc wiacfâc-ticne ɋâricne juniŋte murâ woke bawec. Iŋuc ehuc ŋic kiŋjeŋicte fuŋne bataniŋkewec. Erâ mamanasiŋte erâ kiŋfâsâc ee irec fârine rauckewec.
Abraham e mamanasiŋhec juwecte mâreŋ-ticne beherâ moc rauckeocte irec dâŋ erao fuame reŋkewec. Erâ mâreŋ irec me irec mukicne kâuc bahuc sifu rawec.
Mamanasiŋhecte mâreŋ biŋe qacnekicne ira ra fisirâ jaba juwec. Jaba juhuc bozeo sawa ŋeŋerâ juwec. Isaka â Jakobo jahe biŋe mâmâc qajactekicnezi sâc ijaha epic.
Abraham e hae ŋeŋe sanaŋ moc Anutuzi bâfuarâ basarickewec irec mamanacko juwec.
Sara e iŋuc jaha mamanasiŋhecte tâpiri fuacneme ŋokac qizec juipiehuc kiwechec ewec. Ine ɋâricte biŋe qacnewec ere, mume fufuazi mukac, muhuc iŋuc ewec.
Eme irec hâcne ŋic mocjaha, fua sawecte tâpiri-ticne arictac ehame, eraonec ɋâric fua sawec embiŋ jaŋe sambâŋko bâpiŋ ŋerakac irec sâc, erâ hâwecmecko moŋgeŋ forakac, ŋiczi mi wowosene, irec sâc fuambiŋ.
Ŋic izi hâcne mamanasiŋhec juhuc hâmo-fârembiŋ. Wiac biŋe qajarekicne irec fârine ine mi roro mâc taicko fome honerâ worickehuc jumbiŋ. Iŋuc ehuc fuŋne-jeŋic šiŋuc manambiŋ: Nâŋe mâreŋko hotâ â jaba juŋgopeneŋ.
Dâŋ iŋuc muhuc mâreŋ qizec moc bâfuaniŋte maŋjeŋic âeckeba ewec.
Erâ jaŋacne hae mâreŋ râpeckembiŋ irec maŋhâhâŋ mi ejarewec, irec ejareme muzac risiezo murâ sâcne risienšapiŋ.
Jaŋe ine hae mâreŋ biaŋ mocte maŋhâhâŋ ejarewec, sambâŋko fokac irec hâcne. Irec Anutu e jaŋere Anutu, ere iŋuc mupene maname mi sâqoreekac. Wemocte? E jahac hae sâko moc bâfua-jarewec.
Abraham e Anutuzi esâickeme mamanasiŋhec juwecte Isaka taha bâzire qikiŋnewec, e biŋedâŋ roweczi ŋokâ-ticne mocjaha qikiŋnezo ewec hâcne.
Biŋedâŋ šiŋuc âzâcnekicne: “Isakaraonec ɋâricfâcge fua sawec eraniŋmu.”
I kecšiŋuc muhuc ewec: “Anutu e ŋic hâmockonec bâɋârec-jopaocte tâpiri focnekac.” Eme irec hâmockonec tinac bârisiecnewec.
Isaka e mamanasiŋhec juwecte Jakobo â Esau jambuŋ-jofahuc wiac šâhec fuaocmu irec findaŋdâŋ wâc jasawec.
Jakobo e mamanasiŋhec juwecte hâmozo ehuc Josefe ŋokâ jahec-ticne jambuŋ-jofawec, ehuc gunuzi âkesiŋnerâ ŋehuc Anutu dapecnewec.
Josefe e mamanasiŋhec juwecte hâmozo dameŋ-ticne maickeme Israe ŋic jaŋe juku Aigita mâreŋ beherâ raniŋmu irec manasurâ siec-ticnere qanaŋ dâŋ mutâcne-jarewec.
Mose fuame neŋgoc mamacne jahe mamanasiŋhecte motec honebâckerâ ŋicwofuŋ dâŋticnere mi hâwic-jofaha mosa jahec â moc soŋkepic.
Mose e mamanasiŋhec juwecte ine sokarâ Farao otâ-ticne-e ŋokâ mucneniŋte mupie qikiŋnewec.
E sâqocnere aŋac bembeŋne qikiŋnerâ Anuture ŋicfâc jaŋehec šâic busâqoc manaocte wosâewec.
Ehuc Aigita mâreŋkonec moneŋ mafa mâriri irec maname jawane ewec, â Kristore erâ mamakucne juocte ine maname fârine ewec. I juku furine roocte mana suhuc iŋuc ewec.
E mamanasiŋhec juwecte ŋicwofuŋ aaric-ticne qamaserâ Aigita mâreŋ behewec. Erâ Anutu mi hohonene e šâŋezi honehuc tinac erao siŋkewec.
Mose e mamanasiŋhec juwecte mume aakic lama hezurâ socnezi ficmotâc ruacnepie aŋelo momorizi jowaruhuc mârâc ŋokâfâc-jeŋic akic-jopawec.
Eme Israe ŋic jaŋe mamanasiŋhec jumbiŋte Hâwec Bâbâroŋko tiŋko rara tinac rahuc fotâcnembiŋ. Aigita ŋic jaŋe i jaha ezo mupie hâweczi ɋâcjopawec.
Israe ŋic jaŋe mamanasiŋhec jumbiŋte Jeriko haesac orâŋkekuhapie šoaŋ gie bapa 7 eme hericke qawec.
