“Wofuŋ-nâŋec Anutu, eri qaraweŋ â šâŋe biŋe â tâpiri i goki raucketec sâcke-hâmokac, goki hâcne wiac sasawa bâfuameŋ, â gore micte wiac fua-fârewec fokac.”
Eme eri ŋeŋeo ŋeekac e mefâre-ticnezi papia foforiŋ moc baŋeme honepo, papia e bune râpene qâreŋhec jaha fowec, erâ sâfâ 7-zi basanaŋkekicne.
Eme aŋelo sâko honepo, e dâŋ hahaŋnehec šiŋuc muwec: “Mo tiŋnezi papia sâfâ-ticne bâhockerâ bâdâmâreme sâckeocmu?”
Iŋuc mume sambâŋko me mâreŋko me mâreŋ jujuwicnao moczi moc papia sâfâ-ticne bâhockerâ woseocte mi afeckewec.
Eme moczi sâsâcne mi juhuc papia bâdâmârerâ wosewecte bunane sâqoreme boc kiopo.
Iŋuc epe ŋicqizec jaŋeraonec moczi šiŋuc naza muwec: “Mi kioc, manakomec, Judare ɋâricfâc jaŋeraonec laioŋ moc fuawec, Dawidire gitecne hâcne, eki papia sâfâ-ticne 7 bâhockerâ bâdâmâreocte wiac sasawa qamase-fârewec.”
Eme no šâŋe firâ eri ŋeŋe â wiac jujune 4 irec ŋondeŋko ŋicqizec jaŋere birio Lama moc hezukicne hawari domame honepo. šuŋene 7 â šâŋene iŋuc jaha 7. šâŋene 7 i Anuture mâro 7, jaŋe mâreŋ sâc sorec-jopakicne juraŋgopieŋ.
Eme Lamazi rarâ eri ŋeŋeo ŋewec ere mefâreonec papia foforiŋ rowec.
Papia foforiŋ rome wiac jujune 4 â ŋicqizec 24 jaŋe Lamare maŋfuŋko fodapembiŋ. Jaŋe musi-jeŋichec sasawa, â râqâc golzi bakicne i mâmâc barâ fombiŋ. Râqâc maŋkonec hosâc âsu biaŋ wefuwec, i Anuture tiriŋicfâc jaŋere nunumu.
Eme jaŋe gae ɋâricne moc šiŋuc hembiŋ: “Goki papia rorâ sâfâ-ticne bâhocketec sâcke-hâmoocmu. Go gupie socgezi mâreŋ sâc ŋic sahac hawari fuŋne fuŋne â dâŋmarac fuŋne fuŋne kitâc-jopame Anuture biŋe embiŋ.
Erâ qâzuc-jopatec Anutu uucmaŋ-ticnere kikefuŋfâc â taha bapafâc-ticne embiŋ. Eme jaŋe mâreŋte faio guriŋ bapa gie baniŋmu.”
Eme no šâŋe firâ aŋelo bocjaha jâmbâŋ honec-jopahuc micfânâŋ-jeŋic manapo. Jaŋe eri ŋeŋe â wiac jujune â ŋicqizec orâŋ-jopahuc domambiŋ, teŋ tauseŋ gurune gurune â wâŋ tauseŋ gurune gurune domarahuc
dâŋ šiŋuc wiwirao mumbiŋ: “Lama hezukicne eki tâpiri mazuc mâriri â maŋɋârâŋ â sasanaŋ â šâŋe biŋe â eri qaraweŋ â muac baafec rauckeme sâcke-hâmokac.”
Eme sambâŋko â mâreŋko â mâreŋ jujuwicnao â hâwecko jurambiŋ sasawa jaŋe kecšiŋuc mupie manapo: “Eri ŋeŋeo ŋekac e â Lama mâmâc muac baafec â šâŋe biŋe â eri qaraweŋ â tâpiri focnekaczi focnerahuc juzejec sanaŋ.”
Eme wiac jujune 4 jaŋe mumbiŋ: “Jâmbomac.” Á ŋicqizec jaŋe fodapehuc numucnembiŋ
Eme no šâŋe firâ honepo, Lama eki papia sâfâ 7 fowec ine moc bâhockewec. Bâhockeme wiac jujune 4 jaŋeraonec moc e ɋuŋ parandaŋ maracko wirahuc muwec: “Warec.”
Mume mi becâsic qaŋqaŋ moc wareme honezepac i¡ Fainao ŋic moc ŋewec e tepe-ticnehec, eme e eri qoqonaŋ râcnepie momori erâ wiac qamase rahuc juwec.
Eme Lamazi sâfâ namba 2 bâhockeme wiac jujune namba 2-zi wirahuc muwec, “Warec!”
Mume becâsic bâbâroŋ fuawec. Fainao ŋic ŋewec e mâreŋko wama bârârieme ŋic jaŋe qâqâmiziec eniŋte tâpiri râcnekicne. Erâ šika sâko mâmâc râcnekicne.
Eme Lamazi sâfâ namba 3 bâhockeme wiac jujune namba 3-zi wirahuc muwec, “Warec!” Eme no šâŋe firâ honehape mi becâsic gâgâpâc warezejec i¡ Ŋic fainao ŋewec e sigeli baŋewec.
Eme no wiac jujune jaŋere ŋondeŋko ŋicmarac tinac fuarâ šiŋuc mume manapo: “Padi tase 2 furine 1 kina â jacgoŋ 12 iŋuc jaha furine 1 kina. Erâ saŋ hâmeŋ fâric ine akicketec fuazejec.”
Eme Lamazi sâfâ namba 4 bâhockeme wiac jujune namba 4-zi wiwirao muwec, “Warec!”
Eme šâŋe firâ honehape mi becâsic moc sahacne gowaekicne warezejec i¡ Ŋic fainao ŋewec šâŋene hâmoc. Erâ hârâckoneczi bâjâpembiŋ. Eme mâreŋko rukec jahec â moc mâc fohame moc ira mume šikazi â roroczi â huc mimicnezi â kâte qowi momorizi ŋic sipiric-jopaniŋte tâpiri râe-jarekicne.
Eme Lamazi sâfâ namba 5 bâhockewec. Ehame ŋic Anuture dâŋ bajuhuc biŋe-ticne mutaniŋkepie jopakicne jaŋere maŋ qâqâtâc alata maŋfuŋko fopie honec-jopapo.
Jaŋe dâŋ wiwic jaha wirahuc šiŋuc mumbiŋ: “Tiri â mume sasanaŋ Wofuŋ, go wemocte okac dameŋ bâšorahuc socnâŋecte kiŋ ŋic mâreŋko juŋgopieŋ jaŋerao mi batarakic?”
Iŋuc mupie ŋaqi qaŋqaŋ ru sâc jare-fârerâ šiŋuc jazambiŋ: “Kiŋaŋ qaqa âgofâc-ŋeŋic gâcne iŋuc jaha jopa qâhâmoc ejarepie šare-jeŋic qosackeocte woŋec piticne junšepieŋ.”
Eme wiac šiŋuc honepo: Lama e sâfâ namba 6 bâhockeme homeŋ sâko bawec. Ehame šoaŋ gâpârerâ kuši sahacne iŋucne ewec, â mosa e soc iŋucne ewec.
Á bâpiŋ jaŋe mâŋâŋzi nemuja qâmârâŋkeme wahaekac, iŋuc sambâŋkonec mârâŋkerâ wahambiŋ.
Á sambâŋ e ine papia bataforieeŋgopeneŋ iŋuc foforierâ sirowewec. Á tiki â nuc jaŋe.ŋeŋe-jeŋic behembiŋ.
Wiac iŋucne fuame mâreŋ sâc ŋicwofuŋ â ŋicbomboŋ, erâ momori micnefâc-jeŋic â mafa mâririhec â tâpirihec, ŋic fekicne â wahakicne mâmâc sasawa mâreŋ â qânâ hawecko soŋkerâ tiki â hârâc wâsic-jopahuc šiŋuc mumbiŋ:
“Waharâ ŋemac-nâporâ bârârâŋ-nâpopie eri ŋeŋeo ŋekac ere šâŋeo mi henšepeneŋ â Lamare kimbeŋ mi honenšepeneŋ.
Kimbeŋ-jeŋicte dameŋ sâko maickekacte ŋic mozi moc juocmu?”
Eme no šâŋe firâ aŋelo 4 honec-jopapo, jaŋe mâreŋ tuturuŋne 4 ira doma rahuc mâreŋte mâŋâŋ 4 badomambiŋ. Mâreŋko me hâwecko me jâcko mâŋâŋ moc mi qaocte iŋuc embiŋ.
Ehame šoaŋ wewefunaonec aŋelo moc wefume honepo. E Anutu jujune eraonec maqâreŋ bajuwec. Bajuhuc aŋelo 4 mâreŋko â hâwecko ima baniŋte mujarekicne jaŋe wiwic jaha wira-jarehuc šiŋuc muwec:
“Ŋoŋe mâreŋko me hâwecko me jâcko ima biac mi banšepieŋ, nâŋe qanaŋ Anuture ŋicfâc mai-jeŋicko maqâreŋ râenaŋmu.”
Iŋuc mume ŋic maqâreŋhec jaŋere šare kecšiŋuc mupie manapo: “Israe guru sâc jaŋeraonec 144 tauseŋ maqâreŋ râe-jarekicne.
Judare guruonec 12 tauseŋ maqâreŋ-jeŋichec, Rubeŋte guruonec 12 tauseŋ, Gade ere guruonec 12 tauseŋ,
Ase ere guruonec 12 tauseŋ, Naftali ere guruonec 12 tauseŋ, Manase ere guruonec 12 tauseŋ,
Simeoŋ ere guruonec 12 tauseŋ, Lewi ere guruonec 12 tauseŋ, Isasa ere guruonec 12 tauseŋ,
Sebuloŋ ere guruonec 12 tauseŋ, Josefe ere guruonec 12 tauseŋ, Benjamiŋ ere guruonec 12 tauseŋ, ŋic iŋuczi maqâreŋ-jeŋichec embiŋ.”
Wiac i hone manac efârerâ moc honepo, mâreŋ sâc irec ŋic tucne, sahac hawari-jeŋic fuŋne fuŋne â dâŋ marac-jeŋic fuŋne fuŋne, guru sokawec jâmbâŋ, ŋic moczi mi wowosene, jaŋe eri ŋeŋere â Lamare maŋfuŋko domapie honec-jopapo. Jaŋe ŋaqi qaŋqaŋhec sasawa,
erâ mejeŋiczi šariŋ badomahuc dâŋ hahaŋne bahuc šiŋuc mumbiŋ: “Bâbâpiaŋ i Anutu-nâŋec eri ŋeŋeo ŋekac erao â Lamarao fokac.”
Eme aŋelo sasawa eri ŋeŋe â ŋicqizec â wiac jujune 4 orâŋ-jopahuc domambiŋ, jaŋe eri ŋeŋe maŋfuŋnao fodaperâ Anutu nunumu mumuteŋ ecnehuc šiŋuc mumbiŋ:
“Jâmbomac¡ Mumuteŋ â eri qaraweŋ â maŋɋârâŋ â daŋge mumu â šâŋe rara â tâpiri â sasanaŋ i Anutu-nâŋec focnekaczi focne rahuc juzejec sanaŋ. Jâmbomac.”
Eme ŋicqizec jaŋeraonec moczi wio-narerâ muwec: “Ŋaqi qaŋqaŋhec i mo jaŋe? Wenirec warembiŋ?”
Wio-nareme dâŋ šiŋuc bâtikiecnepo: “Ŋicbomboŋ-nane, i goki manakic.” Eme nazawec: “Jaŋe šâic busâqoc maŋnaonec warembiŋ â ŋaqi-jeŋic Lamere soczi šure ɋaɋackembiŋ.
Irec ši Anutu eri ŋeŋe-ticnere maŋfuŋko juhuc ŋafe furec ufuŋ-ticnao kiŋaŋ qacneeŋgopieŋ. Ehame eri ŋeŋeo ŋeekaczi qâtec-jopahuc sâoc-jopaocmu.
Eme nânâ opâre mocwâc mi hâmoniŋmu; šoaŋzi mi rikec-jopaocmu â šâic fâro mi fua-jareocmu. Ŋeŋe šâšâŋiŋko Lama domakac eki hâcne soŋaŋ-jopaocmu, ehuc juju opâ šâkâŋnao amec-jopa rahuc juocmu; erâ Anutuzi šâŋeuc-jeŋic bâkereŋke-fâreocmu.”

Eme Lama e sâfâ namba 7 bâhockeme sambâŋko niniŋ qiririŋ fuarâ fohame haæ aua qâririŋ ewec.
I tarame aŋelo 7 Anuture maŋfuŋko domambiŋ jaŋe honec-jopahape gâcnezi qeŋ 7 jarembiŋ.
Eme aŋelo moczi râqâc golzi bakicne ihec warerâ ra alata maŋfuŋko badomame gâcnezi ira hosâc âsu biaŋ bocjaha râepie huwec. Hume eri ŋeŋe mainao alata golzi bakicne ŋewec irec fainao râehuc mitiŋic jaŋere nunumuo šuhuckewec.
Ehame meticnaonec hosâc âsu biaŋ izi mitiŋic jaŋere nunumu bafickehuc Anuturao fewec.
Aŋelo e iŋuc erâ alataonec šoc kine rorâ râqâc-ticne bâfuserâ mâreŋko hoŋkeme huwec. Hume ɋuŋ parandaŋ â bâbâric â homeŋ fuawec.
Eme aŋelo 7 qeŋ jarekicne jaŋe qeŋ qaniŋte šawiembiŋ.
Ehuc aŋelo namba wâŋ eki qeŋ qame hoe sanaŋ â šoc sochec bâsifuckekicne izi mâreŋko hewec. Heme mâreŋ tucne šoczi šawec â jâc tucne â sopâc kecɋaŋ sasawa šoczi šafârewec.
Eme aŋelo namba 2 eki qeŋ qawec. Qeŋ qame wiac moc tiki sâko iŋucne šocbâruŋnehec hâwecko rucnewec.
Rucneme hâwec tucne soc efârewec. Eme hâwec qowi tucne hâmo-fârembiŋ â woke tucne šaŋke-fârewec.
Eme aŋelo namba 3 eki qeŋ qawec. Qeŋ qame bâpiŋ sâko moc sambâŋkonec tara waharâ ine waha iŋucne bâruŋkehuc opâ gâcnao huwec.
Bâpiŋ šâŋene Hâtâqiŋqiŋ. Eme irec opâ gâcne hâtâ qiŋqiŋne eme ŋic jaŋe nâpie hâtâc-jopame bocjaha hâmombiŋ.
Eme aŋelo namba 4 eki qeŋ qawec. Qeŋ qame šoaŋ mosa â bâpiŋ gâcne ira sâwec fuame tatamac-jeŋic pitiwawec. Tatamac-jeŋic gâkowawecte hae burec burec sawa furewec â ŋafeo iŋuc jaha mosa bâpiŋ buburecne tamaewec.
Eme no šâŋe firâ tucwipe sâko moc honepo. E sawao faic jâmbâŋ juhuc wiwic jaha šiŋuc wirawec: “Jei, jei, jei, aŋelo jahec â moc jaŋere qeŋ fokac, i qapie mâreŋŋic jaŋe weniŋuc eniŋmu!”
Eme aŋelo namba 5 eki qeŋ qawec. Eme noni bâpiŋ moc sambâŋkonec tararâ mâreŋko wahame honepo. E hârâcte tapa roocte irec ki râcnekicne.
Eme hârâcte tapa rome hosâc sâko wefuwec, gie šame hosâc feekac, irec sâc hosâc wefu ferâ šoaŋ â sawa sâocke-fârewec.
Hosâc maŋkonec ine ɋirikiŋ wefurâ mâreŋko wahambiŋ. Micjeŋic ine omeqaqare Sâc.
Erâ jaŋe mâreŋko sopâc nânâ kise me jâcrehac wiac râsi ecneniŋte mi mukicne, ŋic Anuture maqâreŋ mai-jeŋicko mi fowec, jaŋe sawa râsi ejareniŋte mukicne.
Erâ jopapie hâmoniŋte mâcne, mâc mosa 5 kišâic-jopahuc juniŋte mukicne. Ʒâic ine omeqaqare micte sâc iŋuc manazo.
Eme dameŋ ira ŋic jaŋe hâmoniŋte biŋe muniŋmu erâ mi hâmoniŋmu, hâmoc hefâre-bipiepie sifu mi maic-jopaocmu.
Ɋirikiŋ jaŋe ine becâsic hawari, momori jaŋe šikao raniŋte becâsic wiac bâmocke-jareeŋgopieŋ hawari iŋucne hâcne. Qizec-jeŋicko du golzi bakicne tinac ŋewec, šâŋe mai-jeŋic ŋic šâŋe mai tinac.
Kanšaŋ-jeŋic šoricne, ŋokac qizec gere-jeŋicte sâc. Micjeŋic laioŋte mic iŋucne.
Amec-jeŋicko maro wapazi bakicne tinac fowec. Fakec fânâŋ-jeŋic ine keretac fânâŋ iŋucne, becâsic bocjaha jaŋe šikao raniŋte keretac gagasac jaha fâre rapie fânâŋkeekac, iŋucne tinac hâcne.
Gecjeŋic omeqaqare gec iŋucne Micjeŋic i gecjeŋicko hâcne fokac, izi ŋic mosa 5 kišâic-jopahuc juniŋmu.
Erâ hârâckonec aŋelo e ŋicwofuŋ jujarekac, šâŋene Judaŋic jaŋere dâŋko Abadoŋ â Grikŋic jaŋere dâŋko Apolioŋ. ª
Tucwipezi jei jahec â moc wirawec, moc omaekac, ši jajahec fokopirec. Aŋelo namba 6 eki qeŋ qame momori guru hâhâwicne fuambiŋ
Eme aŋelo namba 6 eki qeŋ qawec. Eme alata golzi bakicne, Anuture maio ŋekac, masune 4,
irecnec dâŋ wefurâ aŋelo namba 6 qeŋ badomawec e šiŋuc âzâcnewec: “Eufrata opâ sâkoo aŋelo 4 niŋgiŋ-jopakicne jaŋe bâŋgoroŋ-jopac.”
Eme aŋelo 4 jaŋe jara, mosa, šoaŋ, aua maickeme mâreŋ sâc ŋic tucne qâmiziec-jopaniŋte woŋec jumbiŋ, jaŋe hâcne firuec-jopawec.
Eme momorifâc-jeŋic becâsicko ŋeŋe jaŋere šare 200 million, iŋuc mupie manapo.
Ŋic â becâsic jaŋere hawari ine maŋ šâŋe-nanezi kecšiŋuc honepo: Ŋic jaŋe maruku bâbâroŋ â keda â bâbâŋeŋ iŋuc rojumbiŋ, â becâsic jaŋere qizec laioŋ qizecne iŋucne, micjeŋickonec ine šoc â hosâc â tepe šocne wahawec.
Eme wiac fârone jahec â moc izi ŋic gâcne sipiric-jopa-fârewec, becâsic mickonec šoc â hosâc â tepe šocne wahawec izi hâcne.
Becâsic tâpiri-jeŋic ine micjeŋicko â gecjeŋicko fowec. Gecjeŋic homa iŋucne, qizecnehec, izi hâcne ŋic sipiric-jopaeŋgopieŋ.
Eme ŋic tucne hâmo sipiric ehapie tucne akic-jopakicne jaŋe maŋjeŋic mi bârisiembiŋ â juju bapa-jeŋicte manapie mi sâqorewec. Aricne, jaŋe sifu demoŋ wiac bajumbiŋ. Á nemuɋâŋ golzi â siliwazi â aeŋzi â qânâzi â jâczi bakicne, hone manac eene tâmiric â rarac wawarecne tâmiric, i numu-jarehuc jumbiŋ.
Ehuc šika â qaŋgec â sasec â fiuc i mi behembiŋ.
Eme aŋelo sâko moc sambâŋkonec wahame honepo. E karoraczi rufacnekicne, qizec botâŋnao huriri somâckerâ domawec, šâŋe maine šoaŋ iŋucne, kike jahecne šocbâruŋhec.
Meticnezi papia piticne moc bâdâmârekicne i badomawec. Erâ kike fâre-ticnezi hâwec faio â kike qanazi mâreŋko âterâ domawec.
Domahuc dâŋ wiwira kâcɋene, laioŋte dâŋ sâcko ewec. Wirame ɋuŋ 7 jaŋe dâŋembiŋ.
Dâŋehuc mupie manarâ qâreŋke 20 ehape sambâŋkonec wiwira norao šiŋuc wahawec: “Ɋuŋ 7 dâŋ mumbieŋ i mi qâreŋkec, mâc tapa batec fooc.”
Eme aŋelo hâwecko â mâreŋko âterâ domawec, eki mefâre-ticne sambâŋkopec sicnehuc dâŋ mupaŋkewec.
Ehuc jurašihuc juocmu sanaŋzi wiac bâfua-fârewec, sambâŋ â irec wiac-ticne, mâreŋ 3 irec wiac-ticne, hâwec â irec wiac-ticne, erao hâcne ɋetickehuc šiŋuc mupaŋkewec: “Dameŋ mocwâc mi fokac.
Aŋelo namba 7 qeŋticne qame fânâŋ fuaocmu, dameŋ ira Anuture dâŋsoŋ, ŋicfâc-ticne porofete biŋene jazawec, irec fârine fua taraocmu.”
Eme sambâŋkonec dâŋ manapo ijaha mocwâc fuarâ šiŋuc nazawec: “Go rarâ aŋelo hâwecko â mâreŋko âterâ domahuc papia bâdâmârekicne badomakac i roc.”
Mume no aŋelorao rarâ papia nareocte âzâcnepe šiŋuc nazawec: “Rorâ nâc. Nâtecne bugao hâtâcguocmu â micgao baŋac iŋucne erâ aŋacguocmu.”
Iŋuc murâ papia nareme nâpo. Nârâ micnaneo baŋac iŋucne erâ aŋacnuwec, izi nâkâcnepe ine bunaneo hâtâcnuwec.
Eme šiŋuc nazambiŋ: “Go ŋicguru bocjaha, sahac hawari-jeŋic â dâŋmarac-jeŋic fuŋne fuŋne erâ ŋicwofuŋfâc-jeŋic jaŋere findaŋdâŋ mocwâc muzemec.” Kâtedâŋko: Sisipiric rune.
Eme moczi gunusâc narehuc šiŋuc nazawec: “Go fahare Anuture ufuŋ â alata sâc barâ maŋnao numuhuc jueŋgopieŋ jaŋe wosec-jopazemec.
Ufuŋte hae šoŋa ine sâc mi bahuc mâc behetec fooc, i qâpuc jaŋere qikiŋnekicne. Jaŋe hâcne miti hae mosa 42 ima bahuc juniŋmu.
“Eme no mumutaniŋ ŋicjahec-nane ejactepe mateŋ barâ ŋic findaŋdâŋ jazahuc juhapire šoaŋ gie bapa 1 tauseŋ â 260 tarazejec.”
Jahe oliwa jâc â lambe iŋucne, jahe mâreŋte Wofuŋ ere maio domakopirec.
Ŋic moc e râsi ejactezo mume micjekickonec šoc waharâ šaocmu. Irec ŋic moczi râsi ejacterâ sipirickeocmu.
Ŋic jahe hoere motâc henicte tâpiri jactekicne, irec mupire hoe mi hehe mâc fohame findaŋdâŋ muhuc junicmu. Erâ mupire opâzi soc eocte irec tâpiri fojacteocmu, erâ mâreŋko wiac micne momori fuaocte mupire sâc fuaocmu.
Eme miti mumutaniŋ dameŋ-jekic tarame hârâckonec qowi mimicnezi wefurâ râsi ejacterâ jofame hâmonicmu.
Hâmopire ŋic jaŋe qâŋɋâŋ-jekic behec-jofapie hae sâkore hae šoŋao fonicmu. Hae irec šâŋe herâriehuc Sodom â Aigita mukicne, Wofuŋ-jekic hae ijaha maripoŋko qapie hâmowec.
Eme mâreŋ sâc ŋic gâcne, sahac hawari-jeŋic fuŋne fuŋne â dâŋmarac-jeŋic fuŋne fuŋne, izi qâŋɋâŋ-jekic šoaŋ gie bapa jahec â moc â moc nâfocne honec-jofahuc juniŋmu, erâ gâcnezi ducjofazo mupie qatara-jareniŋmu.
Eme porofete jahe ŋic boc bâšâic-jopapicte mâreŋne mâreŋne ŋic šeri bubiaŋ ehuc boreŋ nareŋ gareŋ eniŋmu.
Eme šoaŋ gie bapa jahec â moc â moc nâfocne tarame Anuturaonec juju bâbâfua mâro qâŋɋâŋ-jekicko rašime ɋârerâ faharepic. Faharepire ŋic jaŋe honerâ bipic-jeŋic tarawec.
Ehame sambâŋkonec wiwira kâcɋene jaherao šiŋuc wahawec: “Ŋohe šira wefunic.” Eme râsifâc-jekic honec-jofahapie karorac maŋko sambâŋko fepic.
Eme dameŋ ijaha sambâŋko fepire izia homeŋ sâko bawec. Bame hae sâkoo fic gâcne, teŋkonec wâŋ irec sâc, herickehuc ŋic 7 tauseŋ jopame hâmombiŋ. Eme ɋâricne jumbiŋ jaŋe hâwic-jopame Anutu sambâŋ rune muteŋkembiŋ.
Tucwipezi jei jahec â moc wirawec, ine jajahecte fârine fuawec, mocjahare fokac ine biac fuaocmu.
Eme aŋelo namba 7 eki qeŋ qawec. Qeŋ qame sambâŋko micfânâŋ sâko embiŋ, ehuc šiŋuc mumbiŋ: “Ʒi mâreŋ sâko mâreŋ irec Wofuŋ jujure tâpiri i Wofuŋ-nâŋec â Kristo-ticne ere meo fekac, eme e guriŋ bapa gie barašihuc juocmu sanaŋ.”
Eme ŋicqizec 24 Anuture maio eri ŋeŋe-jeŋicko ŋembiŋzi waha fodaperâ Anutu šiŋuc muhuc daŋge nunumu ecnembiŋ:
“Wofuŋ Anutu bapafâre, jumeŋzi juekic, nâŋe go daŋge mumuteŋ egareŋgopeneŋ. Go tâpiri sâkoge qaratietec fuakac, ehuc Wofuŋ giege fuŋkerâ bataniŋkekic.
Ŋicne ŋicne kimbeŋ qapie gore kimbeŋzi fuakac. Erâ hâmokicne jaŋere dâŋ mutaracmurâ dameŋ maickekac. Erâ kiŋaŋ qaqafâcge, porofete â mitiŋic, â araŋ bagareeŋgopieŋ fekicne wahakicne, jaŋe furine jarecmurâ dameŋne maickekac, â mâreŋ sipirickeeŋgopieŋ jaŋe sipiric-jopacmurâ irec dameŋ mâmâc maickekac.”
Jaŋe iŋuc epie sambâŋko Anuture ufuŋ aŋkeme qorac tapa katapa ufuŋmaŋko tâtâc fuawec. Eme izia bâbâric â micfânâŋ â ɋuŋ parandaŋ â homeŋ â hoe sanaŋ hâhâwicne fuawec.
Eme sambâŋko mâsi qâreŋ kecšiŋuc fuawec: Ŋokac moc domawec, e šoaŋzi rufacnekicne, kike jujuwicnao mosa ŋewec, qizecnao bâpiŋ 12 izi hendiŋ ecnembiŋ.
Erâ e kiwechec, eme motec roocte gozi kime kio owa ewec.
E iŋuc ehuc domahame mâsi qâreŋ moc sambâŋkoa fuawec. Ine oâ sâko moc fowec, hawarine bâbâroŋ jâmbâŋ, qizecne 7 â šuŋene 10, â qizec-ticne sâc ŋicwofuŋ du jaha ŋerawec.
Eme gecnezi sambâŋko bâpiŋ gâcne qatarac-joparâ mâreŋko sâroc-jopame wahambiŋ. Oâ e iŋuc erâ, ŋokac motec rozo ehame šiŋuc manasuhuc ra maŋfuŋnao fowec: Motec rome ɋâckezepac.
Eme motec rowec, e mâreŋ sâc ŋicne ŋicne aeŋ gunuzi soŋaŋ-jopaocte mucnekicne. Erâ motec fuame ine Anuturao baferâ eri ŋeŋe-ticnere maŋfuŋko râekicne.
Á ŋokac e ine mâreŋ tuhuo wiserâ rawec, ira šoaŋ gie bapa 1 tauseŋ â 260 gume jauŋ ecneniŋte Anutuzi ŋeŋe hae moc bâfuacnewec.
Eme sambâŋko šika fuawec. Mikae â aŋelofâc-ticne jaŋe oâ qa jâpec ecneniŋte râsi roroc embiŋ, â ŋifec oâ â aŋelofâcne jaŋe iŋuc jaha râsi roroc embiŋ.
Erâ mi sanaŋkembiŋ. Dockepie sambâŋ sakare-jarembiŋ.
Ehuc oâ sâko, homa raŋɋa, demoŋ micne sâko Sataŋ hâcne, mâreŋ sâc ŋic maŋ bâsifuc ejareekac, e hâcne tuŋkepie mâreŋko wahawec. E jahacne tuŋkehuc aŋelofâcne mâmâc tuŋjopapie wahambiŋ.
Eme sambâŋko dâŋ wiwira šiŋuc fuame manapo: “Anutu-nâŋecte bâbâpiaŋ â tâpiri â guriŋ bapa gie â Kristo-ticnere Wofuŋ qâreŋ ši fua taniŋkekac. Âgofâc-nâŋec jaŋere râsi, Anuturao ŋafe furec qoric-jopaekac, e tuŋkeŋgopieŋ hâcne.
Jaŋe Lamare socko ŋesiŋnehuc miti hâwicmâc mutaniŋkembiŋte sanaŋkembiŋ, ehuc juju-jeŋic mi sakarehuc hâmocte qikiŋnembiŋ.
Irec sambâŋ maŋne maŋne â ira juŋgopieŋzi šeri enšepieŋ. Á mâreŋ â hâwec, jei, ŋohe weniŋuc enicmu¡ Ʒi Sataŋzi ŋoŋerao hufakac, erâ dameŋ-ticne biac taraocmu, i manahuc aaric sâkohec jukac hâcne.”
Eme oâ e mâreŋko behepie waharâ, ŋokac motec rowec e râsi ecnewec.
Eme ŋokac e tucwipe sâkore fakec jahecne râcnepie mâreŋ tuhuo ŋeŋe hae-ticnao wiserâ homare hâhâwic soŋkewec, ira gume jauŋ ecnehuc juhapie jara jahec â moc â moc nâfocne taraocmu.
Eme ŋokac wisehame homa e râpefuŋnao opâ maŋume micticnaonec waharâ rumi sâko ewec, i ŋokac jowaocte iŋuc ewec.
Eme mâreŋzi ŋokac ŋezickehuc micne aŋkeme oâzi opâ maŋuwec i ira hufârewec.
Eme oâ e ŋokacte mana gâpârerâ kikefuŋfâc-ticne jopaocte rawec. Anuture sâcmutâc dâŋ reŋkehuc Jesu mutaniŋkeeŋgopieŋ jaŋe hâcne jopaocte rawec.
Ehuc hâwec moŋgeŋko hurâ domawec.
Eme no honehape hâwecmaŋkonec qowi mimicne moczi wefuwec. E šuŋene 10 â qizecne 7, erâ šuŋene sâc ira ŋicwofuŋ du 10 ŋerawec. Erâ qizec-ticnao šâŋe qâreŋ simbiŋne forawec.
Qowi mimicne honepo e hawarine qâto iŋucne, menezi pusime iŋucne, â micnezi laioŋ mic iŋucne. Eme oâ e šoɋac sasanaŋ-ticne â ŋicwofuŋ ŋeŋe-ticne â tâpiri sâko qikiŋnecnewec.
Qowi qizecne moc qâhâmokicne tinac honepo. Eme izi wicticne somieme biaŋkewec. Eme irec mâreŋ sâc ŋic jaŋe qowi hone warec boc ecnehuc râpefuŋnao jumbiŋ.
Erâ oâ e qowi tâpiri râcnewecte muteŋ bâteŋ ecnembiŋ. Ehuc qowi iŋuc jaha fenšoŋkehuc šiŋuc mumbiŋ: “Qowi e iŋucne mozi jukac? Erâ mozi moc wemo ecneocmu?”
Eme sahac mumuteŋ dâŋ â dâŋ gâgâpâcne muocte irec micne heteckekicne. Erâ gie-ticne i mosa 42 bahuc juocte dameŋ bacnekicne.
Eme irec Anutu e jahacne mecne â šâŋe biŋe-ticne mecne â sambâŋko ŋeŋe juju eeŋgopieŋ jaŋe mecne musoc qâsoriŋ ejarehuc juwec.
Erâ Anuture tiriŋicfâc râsi ejarehuc jopa sipiric ejareocte mana fâsâecnekicne, erâ wâc mâreŋne mâreŋne ŋic sahac hawari-jeŋic â dâŋmarac-jeŋic fuŋne fuŋne jaŋe ŋicbomboŋ ejare-fâreocte tâpiri râcnekicne.
Eme mâreŋŋic sasawa jaŋe mu šeri ecneniŋmu, ŋic šâŋe-jeŋic Lama qa hezuc ekicne ere juju papiao mârâc jaha mâreŋ fufuaonecteaŋ mi qâreŋkekicne jaŋe hâcne qowi iŋuc ecne-fâreniŋmu.
Hazecneheczi dâŋ kecši manazejec:
“Moc e kâpâcwârure biŋe eweczi kâpâcwâru ficko fezejec. Moc e šikare biŋe eweczi šika kizejec.” Tiriŋic jaŋe dameŋ ira hâcne sasanaŋhec â mamanasiŋhec junšepieŋ.
Eme mâreŋmaŋkonec qowi mimicne moc wefume honepo, e lama iŋucne šuŋene jajahec sawa fowec. Dâŋticnezi ine oâdâŋ.
Eme qowi izi qowi mârâc wefuwec ere maio ere tâpiri gie jaha bahuc jukac. Ehuc mâreŋŋic ejareme mârâc qowi, hâmocne tinac erâ ɋârewec, e dieŋzi hecneeŋgopieŋ.
Erâ mâsi kâcɋene baekac, ehuc mume mâreŋŋic honehapie sambâŋkonec šoc wahaekac.
Mâsi iŋucne hâcne baocte manacnekicnere mârâc qowi ere maio bahuc mâreŋŋic maŋ bâsifuc ejareekac. Ehuc mume qowi hâmokicne tinac erâ ɋârewec ere hawari baeŋgopieŋ.
Hawari i barâ râepie domaha šâhec qowi e manacnekicnere bâɋâreme dâŋ dâŋ eekac. Dâŋ dâŋ ehuc mume ŋic, e dieŋzi mi hecneeŋgopieŋ jaŋe qâhâmoc-jopaeŋgopieŋ.
Erâ wâc fekicne â wahakicne, mafahec â hapetac, ŋicbomboŋ â kiŋaŋ qaqa, ŋic i mâmâc sasawa ejareme mefâre-jeŋicko â mai-jeŋicko maqâreŋ bafâreeŋgopieŋ.
Eme qowire šâŋe qâreŋ â šare mi bajueŋgopieŋ, jaŋe wiac furi bapare aka hejareeŋgopieŋ.
Maŋɋârâŋ šira fokac: Ŋic moc e mamana focnekacko qowi šare-ticnere fuŋne bâfuazejec. Ʒare i ŋic mocte šâŋe. Ʒare hâcne i 666.
Eme no šâŋe firâ mi Lama Zioŋ tikio domame honezepac i¡ Erâ ehec ŋic 144 tauseŋ mâmâc domambiŋ. Mai-jeŋicko e jahacne šâŋe qâreŋ â Mamac-ticnere šâŋe qâreŋ fowec.
Eme sambâŋkonec dâŋfânâŋ manapo, i opâ sâro fânâŋ iŋucne â ɋuŋ fânâŋ sâko iŋucne. Erâ dâŋfânâŋ i manape musi tinac ewec, ŋic bocjaha musi bapie fânâŋkeekac iŋuc tinac manapo.
Jaŋe eri ŋeŋere maŋfuŋko â wiac jujune 4 â ŋicqizec jaŋere maio gae ɋâricne moc heeŋgopieŋ. Gae i ŋic gâcnezi he manac eene mi ewec, ŋic 144 tauseŋ, mâreŋŋic gâcne jaŋeraonec furi bacjopakicne, jaŋe sawa mamanane.
Jaŋe hâcne ŋokacko mi sâqorehuc maŋɋaɋac jaha jumbiŋ” jaŋe hâcne Lama jume ju ecneeŋgopieŋ” jaŋe hâcne mâreŋŋic gâcne jaŋeraonec Anuture â Lamare qaqasune bâbâni rocjopakicne.
Erâ micjeŋickonec burecdâŋ moc mi wahawec, jaŋe bahacmâc.
Eme no aŋelo moc honepo, e faic sawao fotâcnehuc rawec. E mâreŋŋic jaŋere Biŋebiaŋ fofo sanaŋ, mâreŋ sâc ŋic sahac hawari-jeŋic â dâŋmarac-jeŋic fuŋne fuŋne, jaŋere bajuwec.
Eki wiwic jaha wirahuc šiŋuc muwec: “Ŋoŋe Anutu araŋ bacnehuc sâsenšepieŋ, okac dameŋ-ticne maickekac hâcne. Sambaŋ â mâreŋ, hâwec â opâ šâŋe bâfuawec e mu wâwâsic ecnenšepieŋ.”
Iŋuc murâ rame râpefuŋnao aŋelo moczi warerâ šiŋuc wirawec: “Babe hae sâko tâtiekac, tâtie-jâmbâŋkekac, hae irec rune mâreŋ sâc ŋicne sasecte waiŋ opâ momori gumec-jopahuc jumbiŋ hâcne.”
Eme râpefuŋnao aŋelo âgo-ticne moczi warerâ dâŋ hahaŋne bahuc šiŋuc muwec: “Moc e qowi mimicne e jahacne me hawari-ticne dieŋzi hecneocmu â mai-ticnao me meticnao maqâreŋ roocmu,
e Anutuzi kimbeŋ-ticnere waiŋ opâ momori jâmbâŋ, opâ jâmbâŋhec mi bâsifuckekicne, i râqâc-ticnaonec gumeme tiri aŋelo â Lama jaŋere maio šocbâruŋko hurâ šâic serereŋ mana rahuc juocmu.
Eme šoczi ŋic iŋucne šâfitac-jopame irec hosâcne ŋezume ŋezu fehuc foocmu sanaŋ. Irec ŋic qowi mimicne â hawari-ticne dieŋzi hecnembiŋ jaŋe mecne, â šâŋe qâreŋ-ticne bajumbiŋ jaŋe mâmâc šâiczi mi behec-jopame ŋeŋe mana tâmiric ŋafe furec šušuhuc jaha mana rahuc juniŋmu.”
Dameŋ ira hâcne Anuture sâcmutâc dâŋ reŋkehuc Jesure miti hâwicmâc bajueŋgopieŋ tiriŋic i jaŋe sasanaŋ bâfuanšepieŋ.
Eme sambâŋkonec dâŋ moc šiŋuc wahame manapo: “Go dâŋ ši qâreŋkec: Dameŋ ši fuŋkerâ, Wofuŋtao qohotahuc hâmoniŋmu jaŋere bubiaŋ manazo. Mârozi mukac, jâmbomac, jaŋe neneŋ gie-jeŋic hetararâ ŋemanahuc biaŋ-jopaocmu. Erâ juju bapa-jeŋicte fârinezi rapie raocmu.”
Eme no fipe feme karorac qaŋqaŋ ututuŋ fuame honepo. Erâ karorac faio moc ŋewec, e hawari-ticne ŋic iŋucne. Qizec-ticnao ŋicwofuŋ du golzi bakicne roŋewec â meticnezi sâqe mictara baŋewec.
Ehame ufuŋkonec aŋelo moczi waharâ karorac faio ŋewec, e šiŋuc wiracnewec: “Go sâqegezi gie fârine qa roro ec, mâreŋko giere fârine woze-fârewecte qa roro ezore dameŋne maickekac hâcne.”
Iŋuc mume karorac faio ŋeweczi sâqe-ticne wickeme mâreŋko fârine qafârewec.
Eme aŋelo moczi sambâŋko ufuŋkonec wahawec, e iŋuc jaha sâqe mictara bajuwec.
Warehame âgo-ticne moczi alata ŋeweckonec warewec. E šocte soŋaŋzi âgo-ticne sâqe mictara bajuwec e šiŋuc wiracnewec: “Go sâqege mictara mâreŋko waiŋ fârine qâtâcne-fârec, hândâŋne qeue-fârekac hâcne”
Mume aŋelo âgo-ticnezi sâqe wickeme mâreŋko waiŋ hândâŋne nâtâcneme Anutu kimbeŋ-ticnere katapa sâko irec maŋko beheme hufârewec.
Erâ hae râpeo âte pisickepie katapa maŋkonec socsâko wahahuc fowec. Wahaku šâkâŋne fuarâ becâsic mecqaŋeŋ-jeŋicko qawec. Á šâkâŋ rereŋ šoric-ticnere sâc ine 300 kilometa iŋuc ŋerawec.
Eme sambâŋko mâsi qâreŋ sâko bipinehec moc honepo. Aŋelo 7 jaŋe wiac micne momori 7 badomambiŋ. Wiac i mimic fuahame Anuturaonec okacne fisi taraocte mukicne.
Erâ hâwec moc honepo, i kiruŋzi barâ šocbâruŋhec bâbâsifuc ekicne tinac fome honepo. Erâ qowi mimicne ere dâŋ â hawari â šare qâreŋ i sanaŋkerâ qikiŋnembiŋ ŋic i jaŋe kiruŋzi hâwec irec mecnao Anuturaonec musi badomapie honec-jopapo.
Jaŋe Anuture kiŋaŋŋic Mose â Lamare gae kecšiŋuc muhuc heeŋgopieŋ: “O Wofuŋ Anutu bapafâre, go gie fekicne â bipinehec baekic. Ŋicne ŋicne jaŋere Wofuŋ Sâko, go hatage tiŋne â fâri fideteŋ.
Wofuŋ go mozi araŋ mi bagareocmu â mozi šâŋege mi mumbiaŋkeocmu? Go mocjahazi tiri hâcne. Irec ŋicne ŋicne gorao warerâ dieŋzi hegareniŋmu. Go bâbâtiŋ gie fârine batec fuŋne taniŋkekac hâcne.”
Eme no šâŋe firâ honehape sambâŋko ufuŋ qoruc boze-ticnehec irec motâc aŋkewec.
Aŋkeme aŋelo 7 wiac micne momori 7 bajumbiŋ, jaŋe ufuŋkonec wahambiŋ. Jaŋe ŋaqi ɋaɋacne qaŋqaŋ rojumbiŋ, â amec-jeŋicko umbika golzi bakicne fowec.
Eme wiac jujune 4 domambiŋ jaŋeraonec moczi aŋelo 7 râqâc 7 golzi bakicne jare-fârewec. Râqâcmaŋko ine Anutu juju sanaŋ runere kimbeŋ fusucmarâ fowec.
Eme ufuŋmaŋko Anutu tatamac-ticnere â tâpiri-ticnere hosâc fuarâ fusucma-fârewec. Eme aŋelo 7 jaŋe wiac micne momori 7 mi bâfua tarahapie ufuŋko fefere hata mi fuawec.
Eme ufuŋmaŋkonec dâŋ wiwira sâko wahame manapo. I aŋelo 7 šiŋuc jazawec: “Ŋoŋe rarâ râqâc 7 hoŋkepie Anuture kimbeŋzi mâreŋko huzejec.”
Eme aŋelo namba 1 eki rarâ râqâc-ticnaonec wiac hoŋkeme mâreŋko huwec. Hume ŋic qowi mimicnere šâŋe qâreŋ bajumbiŋ â hawari-ticne dieŋzi hecnembiŋ jaŋe wicšâhâc šâic sisiac-ticnehec mâretec fua-jarewec.
Eme aŋelo namba 2 eki râqâc-ticnaonec wiac hâwecko hoŋkeme huwec. Hume hâweczi soc tânipu tinac ewec. Eme irec hâwecko qowi hâmo-fârembiŋ.
Eme aŋelo namba 3 eki râqâc-ticnaonec wiac hoŋkeme opâo â riqicko hume soc efârewec.
Eme aŋelo opâ soŋaŋ râekicne eki šiŋuc mume manapo: “Tiŋne â tiri, jumeŋzi juekic, okac babazuge bâbâsifuc tâmiric.
Jaŋe mitiŋic â porofetefâcge jaŋere soc sipirickembiŋte soc jaha gumec-jopatec nâŋgopieŋ. Eme i sâcke-jarekac.”
Eme alatazi dâŋ šiŋuc mume manapo: “Jâmbomac, Wofuŋ Anutu bapafâre, okac babazuge tiŋne â fâri fideteŋ.”
Eme aŋelo namba 4 eki râqâc-ticnaonec wiac hoŋkeme šoaŋko huwec. Ira hume šoaŋ šocne bâruŋke-jâmbâŋkerâ ŋic mâretec šacjopawec.
Eme ŋic jaŋe šoaŋ fâroroc-ticnezi boc rikec-jopame Anutu, micticnere wiac micne momori iŋuc fuawec, e šâŋe biŋe-ticne musâqorembiŋ. Erâ maŋjeŋic sifu mi bârisierâ Anutu mi sâsembiŋ.
Eme aŋelo namba 5 eki râqâc-ticnaonec wiac qowi mimicnere ŋicwofuŋ ŋeŋeo hoŋkeme wahawec. Wahame hae mâreŋ-ticne dapâc efârewec. Eme ŋic jaŋe šâic serereŋ manahuc nameŋ-jeŋic kitâcnembiŋ.
Eme šâic-jeŋicte â wicšâhâc-jeŋicte Anutu sambâŋ rune musoriŋkembiŋ. Ehuc maŋjeŋic mi bârisierâ juju bapa-jeŋic mi qikiŋnembiŋ.
Eme aŋelo namba 6 eki râqâc-ticnaonec wiac hoŋkeme Eufrata opâ sâkoo huwec. Hume opâ šickewec. I hata fuame šoaŋ wewefunaonec ŋicwofuŋ fisiniŋte iŋuc fuawec.
Eme no honehape oâre mickonec â qowi mimicnere mickonec â porofete burecne ere mickonec demoŋ repicne jahec â moc qaqec hawari tinac wefumbiŋ.
I jaŋe demoŋ fârine, mâsi wiac baniŋte tâpiri fojarekac. Jaŋe hâcne mâreŋ sâc irec ŋicwofuŋ qafeŋ-jopapie Anutu bapafâre ere dameŋ sâkoo râsi roroc erâ fisirâ qaqac eniŋmu.
“Manaŋgopieŋ, no šika qaqa jaŋe iŋucne ututuŋ fisipemu. Irec moc e biuctac jume mimi-ticne fuazacte maŋɋâri juhuc ŋaqi-ticne soŋaŋkezejec. Iŋuc eocmu ere manape šerine ekac.”
Eme demoŋ jaŋe mâreŋ moc šâŋene Judadâŋko Hamagedoŋ mukicne, ira ŋicwofuŋ hetumaŋ-jopa-fârembiŋ.
Eme aŋelo namba 7 eki râqâc-ticnaonec wiac sawao hoŋkeme huwec. Eme ufuŋko eri ŋeŋe ŋeweckonec dâŋ wiwira moc šiŋuc wahawec: “Efârekicne.”
Eme bâbâric â ɋuŋ parandaŋ â micfânâŋ fuawec â homeŋ kâcɋene sâko jâmbâŋ bawec, sâc iŋucne moc ŋic fuarâ juwarembiŋko mi bawec.
Eme hae sâko fâuckeme jahec â moc ewec. Erâ mâreŋ sâc ŋic jaŋere hae tâtie-fârewec, â Babe hae sâkore rufâc jaŋere Anutuzi iŋuc jaha manasurâ kimbeŋ-ticnere waiŋ opâ gumec-jopawec.
Erâ wâc nuc â tiki mâmâc sirowe-fârembiŋ.
Á sambâŋkonec hoe sanaŋ hewec, hândâŋne buse iŋucne, izi ŋic hecjopame Anutu musoriŋkembiŋ. Hoe i hâhâwicne jâmbâŋ, ima-ticnehec.
Eme aŋelo 7 râqâc 7 bajumbiŋ jaŋeraonec moczi norao warerâ šiŋuc nazawec: “Sasec ŋokac sâko opâ kâcɋenao ŋeekac e okacne fisicneocmu, i waretec gowatupe.
Mâreŋne mâreŋne ŋic jaŋe ehec sasec eec eeŋgopieŋ â mâreŋ sâc ŋicwofuŋ jaŋe eraonec hâcne sasec-ticnere waiŋ opâ nârâ maŋsifuc ejareekac.”
Iŋuc nazame maŋnane ŋerisieme mâreŋ tuhuo jowacnu rawec. Eme ira ŋokac moc honepo, e qowi mimicne bâbâroŋ moc ere faio ŋewec. Qowi sahac-ticnao šâŋe qâreŋ simbiŋne fuŋne fuŋne sâcke-fârerâ fowec. Erâ qowi hâcne e qizec-ticne 7 â šuŋene 10.
Á ŋokac e ŋaqi bâbâroŋ â âmuc âmucne rojuwec, erâ erizi kiseŋ qâseŋ kiwec. Meticnezi râqâc moc golzi bakicne badomawec, i sasec-ticnere sohoŋ mamakâczi fusewec.
Mai-ticnao šâŋesoŋ-ticne kecšiŋuc qâreŋkekicne fowec: “Babe hae sâko, mâreŋ sâc sasec mamakâc wiac irec neŋgocne no hâcne.”
Eme ŋokac e tiriŋic â Jesure mumutaniŋfâc jaŋere soc nâku maŋne bibiriwame honepo. Honerâ bipic tatara enarewec.
Eme aŋelozi šiŋuc muhuc wio-narewec: “Wemocte bipic tatara egarekac? No ŋokacte fuŋne â qowizi âsickekac ere fuŋne â qowi qizecne 7 â šuŋene 10 irec fuŋne mâmâc gazape manac.
Go qowi mimicne honemec i mârâc jaha juwec, ši mi jukac, šâhec ine hârâckonec risie wefurâ sisipiric sanaŋko huocmu. Eme qowi mârâc juwec, ši mi jukac, juku ine risieocmu, i mâreŋko ŋic jaŋe honerâ mu warec ecneniŋmu. Ʒâŋe-jeŋic mâreŋ fufuaonecteaŋ juju sanaŋte papiao mi qâreŋkekicne, ŋic i jaŋe hâcne iŋuc eniŋmu.
Ʒi maŋɋârâŋheczi mamanane fokac: Qizecne 7 i tiki 7, ŋokaczi ŋefackekac hâcne.
Eme tiki 7 izi ŋicwofuŋ 7. Ŋicwofuŋ 5 arictac embiŋ, moc ši jukac â moc juku fuaocmu. Fuarâ dameŋ bembeŋne mac juocte mucnekicne.
Qowi mârâc juwec, ši ine mi jukac, izi ŋicwofuŋ 7 jaŋere birio zuhuckehuc namba 8 eocmu, erâ sisipiricko huocmu.
“Ʒuŋene 10 honemec i ŋicwofuŋ 10 jaha wâc, erâ jaŋe gie-jeŋic dameŋ šiŋuczia mi fuŋkembiŋ. Ŋicwofuŋ gie-jeŋic fuŋkerâ qowi mimicnehec dameŋ bembeŋne mac baniŋmu.
Jaŋe maŋ mamanasu-jeŋic mocjaha fome qowi mimicnere kiŋaŋ šoɋachec qaniŋmu.
Ehuc Lamahec šika gie baniŋmu. Eme Lama eki ine sanaŋkerâ jopaocmu. Eki hâcne fekicne jaŋere Fekicne â ŋicwofuŋ jaŋere Wofuŋ Sâko. Á jume jujufâc-ticne rowosâec-joparâ rocjoparâ bufuŋfâc-ticne bacjopakicne hâcne.”
Iŋuc murâ šiŋuc šuhuckerâ nazawec: “Sasec ŋokac e opâ sâko irec mecnao ŋeme honemec, opâ izi ŋicne ŋicne, sahac hawari â dâŋmarac fuŋne fuŋnehec.
Erâ šuŋene 10 honemec, jaŋe mecne â qowi e mâmâc qaisockerâ ŋaqi wiac jâoc rofârerâ biucne nârâ siec sahacne šocko rikeniŋmu.
Erâ i mâc mi eniŋmu, Anutuzi maŋ jeŋicko mu qafeŋ râeme jaŋe dâŋticne reŋkehuc maŋ mocjaha efârerâ qowi kiŋaŋ qacneniŋmu. Qacnehuc juhapie Anuture dâŋ hâcne sanaŋke-fâreocmu.
Erâ go ŋokac honemec i hae sâko, e hâcne mâreŋ sâc ŋicwofuŋ ejareme kiŋaŋ qacneniŋte tâpiri focnekac.”













































Eme no sambâŋkonec aŋelo moczi wahame honepo. E hârâcte ki â kâpâcwâru sâko moc bajuwec.
Erâ e oâ, homa raŋɋa, demoŋ micne Sataŋ hâcne, e rorâ kâpâcwâruzi bândeŋnerâ jara 1 tauseŋ niŋgiŋhec foocte mucnerâ
hârâcko tuŋkeme huwec. Hume motâcne kizi basanaŋkerâ sâfâzi bâbâzickewec. Eme ŋicne ŋicne maŋ bâsifuc mocwâc mi ejarehuc mâc fohame jara 1 tauseŋ taraocte mukicne. Tarame firuepie wefurâ dameŋ bembeŋne mac juocmu.
Eme no eri ŋeŋe ŋerame honepo. Honehape ŋic fisirâ fainao ŋembiŋ jaŋe mumutara gie baniŋte mujarekicne. Eme Jesu mutaniŋkehuc Anuture dâŋ hâwicmâc bajuhapie upe-jeŋic qâtâcnekicne jaŋere maŋ qâqâtâc honec-jopapo, erâ qowi mimicne e jahacne â hawari-ticne dieŋzi mi hecnembiŋ â šâŋe qâreŋ-ticne mai-jeŋicko â mejeŋicko mi bajumbiŋ, jaŋere maŋ qâqâtâc mâmâc honec-jopapo. Eme ŋic i jaŋe sahac-jeŋic ɋâreme honec-jopapo. Eme jaŋe Kristohec ŋicwofuŋ gie bahapie jara 1 tauseŋ tarawec.
Hâmokicne gâcne sâko jaŋe ine mi ɋârehuc jara 1 tauseŋ taraocte irec woŋec fombiŋ. Fafahare honepo i fafahare namba wâŋ.
Fafahare namba wâŋko šuhuckeŋgopieŋ jaŋe šeri bubiaŋ faio tiri juŋgopieŋ. Ŋic iŋucne hâmoc namba tuzi bâsowariec-jopaocmu. Jaŋe Anuture â Kristore taha bapafâc erâ juniŋmu, ehuc ehec ŋicwofuŋ gie bahuc juhapie jara 1 tauseŋ taraocmu.
Eme jara 1 tauseŋ tarame Sataŋ firuepie kâpâcwâru fickonec mocwâc wefuocmu.
Wefurâ ŋicne ŋicne mâreŋ ŋifec â ŋifec, faic â juwic juŋgopieŋ maŋjeŋic bâsifuckerâ Gogo â Magogo ŋic qafeŋ-jopame râsi roroc erâ fisiniŋmu, jaŋe šare-jeŋic hâwec moŋgeŋ iŋucne, wowosene tâmiric.
Fisirâ mâreŋ wâneŋ sâko ira raferâ tiriŋic toma âterâ fohapie somâc-jopambiŋ. Somâc-jopahuc hae biaŋ i mâmâc orâŋkembiŋ. Iŋuc ehapie sambâŋkonec šoc waharâ šâhâmoc-jopa-fârewec.
Á Sataŋ, maŋ bâsifuc ejarehuc juwec, e lambe opâre riqiczi šoc šahuc foekac ira behepie huwec. Qowi mimicne â porofete-ticne burecne jahe ijaha mâmâc jupic. Eme jahe ira ŋafe šoaŋ qâqâtiri šâic fâro mana rahuc junicmu sanaŋ.
Eme no eri ŋeŋe kâcɋene qaŋqaŋ moc honepo. Fainao ŋewec ere maionec sambâŋ â mâreŋ wise tâmirepic.
Ehame hâmokicne fekicne wahakicne jaŋe mâmâc sasawa eri ŋeŋe fuŋnao domapie honec-jopapo. Domahapie papiane papiane qaratiembiŋ. Erâ moc qaratiembiŋ i juju sanaŋte papia. Eme hâmokicne jaŋe juju bapa-jeŋicte dâŋ papiao qâreŋkekicne i honehuc dâŋjeŋic mutarambiŋ.
Eme dameŋ ira hâweczi maŋnao hâmokicne fombiŋ jaŋe bârisiec-jopawec â hâmoczi ŋic hâmocne bârisiec-jopawec â hârâczi ŋic hâmocne bârisiec-jopawec wâc. Eme hâmokicne sasawa jaŋe ju ju bapa-jeŋicte fuŋne rituhuc tofa bazu-jarekicne.
Eme hâmoc â hârâc i šocriqicko behepie huwec. Izi hâmoc namba tu ekac, šocriqic hâcne.
Eme ŋic moc e šâŋene juju sanaŋte papiao basarâ šocriqicko behepie huwec.
Eme no sambâŋ ɋâricne â mâreŋ ɋâricne honec-jofapo. Sambâŋ raŋɋane â mâreŋ raŋɋane jahe ine sirowepic. Erâ hâwec iŋuc jaha arictac ewec.
Eme tiri hae, Jerusalem ɋâricne hâcne, sambâŋkonec Anuturaonec wahame honepo, ŋokac biŋe moc ŋicko râeniŋte erickeeŋgopieŋ iŋuc tinac ericke emasaŋ ekicne honepo.
Eme eri ŋeŋeonec dâŋ kâcɋene šiŋuc wareme manapo: “Honekic, Anuture ŋeŋe hae ŋic jaŋerao fuakac hâcne. Eki ŋondeŋ-jeŋicko ŋeŋe juju ehame jaŋe ŋicfâc-ticne erâ juniŋmu.
Anutu e jahac jaŋerao juhuc šâŋeuc-jeŋic bâkereŋke-fâreocmu. Hâmoc me busâqoc me ki oowa me huc šâic ira mi fuaocmu. Wiac raŋɋanezi omae-fârewec hâcne.”
Eme eri ŋeŋeo ŋeweczi šiŋuc nazawec: “Manakic, no wiac sasawa ɋâricne bâfuakopac.” Iŋuc murâ muwec: “Go qâreŋkec, dâŋ i fâri hândâŋne jâmbâŋ.”
Erâ šiŋuc nazawec: “Wiac efârekicne, no bâbâni â šâhec, wiac fufuŋke â babatara. Moc e opâre hâmome no juju opâ šâkâŋkonec fiarâ katucmâc gumepemu.
Moc e sasanaŋte gie baku batararâ wiac ši raucke-fâreocmu, eme noni Anutu-ticne erâ juhape eki motec-nane erâ juocmu.
Hâwic bâroŋ â miti qiqikiŋ â wâwânâŋhec â šika qaqa â sasecŋic â hafec qaŋgec ŋic â nemuɋâî babaju â siocdâŋ babaju sasawa, ŋic i jaŋere ŋeŋe lambe opâre riqiczi šoc šahuc foekac ira mukicne. Izi hâmoc namba tu.”
Eme aŋelo 7 râqâc-jeŋic sâc wiac micne momorizi fuseme badomambiŋ, jaŋeraonec moczi norao warerâ šiŋuc nazawec: “Waretec Lamare ŋokac biŋe gowatupe.”
Iŋuc murâ enareme maŋnane ŋerisieme tiki sâko šoricne moc ŋewec ira jowacnu ferâ tiri hae Jerusalem i sambâŋkonec Anuturaonec wahame nowatume kecšiŋuc honepo:
Anuture eri tatamaczi geroŋke-fârekicne. Hae irec tatamacnezi qânâ furi sâko jawa ririŋ kikicne iŋucne erâ bâric bâricneekac.
Qânâsac sâko šoricnezi hae râreckekac. Sac i motâc-ticne 12, erâ motâc botâŋnao aŋelo moc moc doma rapie 12 jaha ekac, erâ wâc motâc sâc Israe ŋicguru 12 jaŋere šâŋe qâreŋ forakac.
Ʒoaŋ wewefunaopec motâc jahec â moc domakac, mâreŋ juwicpec motâc jahec â moc domakac, mâreŋ faicpec motâc jahec â moc domakac, â šoaŋ huhunaopec iŋuc jaha motâc jahec â moc domakac.
Haesac irec qânâ wâtuŋ 12 doma rakac, eme wâtuŋ 12 irec ombâŋnao Lamare aposolofâc 12 jaŋere šâŋe qâreŋ 12 jaha forakac.
Aŋelo dâŋ nazawec eki gunusâc moc golzi bakicne badomawec, izi hae â motâc-ticne â sâcticne sâc bawec.
Hae i tuturuŋne jahec â jahec, hâŋne otecne sâckoa. Eme aŋelozi hae rârec rârec gunusâc-ticnezi sâc bame kilometa 2 tauseŋ ewec. Hâŋne otecne â šoricne sâckoa sasawa.
Eme haesac ɋâfoŋ-ticnere sâc bame 70 meta ewec, ŋiczi sâc bajueŋgopeneŋ ijaha aŋelozi bajuhuc hae sâc bawec.
Haesac i qânâ ɋaɋacne, huririnehec izi bakicne, â hae ine goì fifimârâŋne kiruŋ ɋaɋacne iŋucne izi bakicne.
Haesac irec qânâ wâtuŋ i qânâ furi sâko fuŋne fuŋne findowakicne sasawa izi bakicne. Wâtuŋ namba 1 i qânâ ɋaɋacne kiruŋ tinac izi bakicne, wâtuŋ namba 2 i qânâ keŋkeŋne izi bakicne, wâtuŋ namba 3 i qânâ kedazi bakicne, wâtuŋ namba 4 i qânâ ârâŋ ɋâri izi bakicne,
wâtuŋ namba 5 i qânâ birâ birâ izi bakicne, wâtuŋ namba 6 i qânâ bâbâroŋzi bakicne, wâtuŋ namba 7 i qânâ âmuc âmucnezi bakicne, wâtuŋ namba 8 i qânâ buge tinac weweaŋne izi bakicne, wâtuŋ namba 9 i qânâ bâbâŋeŋzi bakicne, wâtuŋ namba 10 i qânâ râweckekicnezi bakicne, wâtuŋ namba 11 i qânâ soc tinac gogowacne izi bakicne, wâtuŋ namba 12 i qânâ qondaŋ horiki tinac izi bakicne.
Sacmotâc 12 i kubu furi sâko 12 izi bakicne, motâc moc i kubi moczi bakicne, motâc moc i kubu moczi, iŋuc sasawa. Hae hata i goì ɋaɋacnezi bakicne, kiruŋ iŋucne fifimârâŋne.
Ufuŋ ine haeo moc mi ŋeme honepo, Wofuŋ Anutu bapafâre eki ufuŋ ejareekac â Lamazi mâmâc.
Erâ hae i mosa šoaŋzi mi âke tamaeekac, Anuture eri tatamaczi batamaeekac â Lamazi šoc tatamac-ticne eekac.
Mâreŋ sâc ŋicne ŋicne jaŋe hae irec tatamackoa jufâreniŋmu, â mâreŋ sâc ŋicwofuŋ jaŋe eri boreŋ wiac-jeŋic hae ira bara-fâreniŋmu.
Hae i moc mi ŋafeocmu, irec sac motâcne i šoaŋkore aaŋ sasawa doma-fâreocmu.
ŋicne ŋicne jaŋere wiac furi sâko qame hukicne, aŋac šizine i hae ira bara-fâreniŋmu.
Wiac wâwânâŋhec ine moc mi raši-jâmbâŋkeocmu. Á ŋic moczi wiac mamakâcne me burec bajuocmu, e hae ira wâc mi rašiocmu. šâŋe-jeŋic Lamare juju sanaŋ papiao qâreŋkekicne jaŋe sawa rašiniŋmu.
Eme aŋelozi juju opâ sâko moc nowatume honepo, ɋaɋacne, jawa ririŋ kikicne. I Anutu â Lama ere eri ŋeŋe fuŋkonec wahakac.
Waharâ hae hata šâšâŋiŋnao rakac. Opâ mecnao ŋifec â ŋifec jujujâc doma rakac. Jâc irec fârine hawarine fuŋne fuŋne 12 izi mosa sâc fua qeuc eekac. Eme mâreŋ sâc ŋic jaŋe jâc irec rehacne nâhuc biaŋkeniŋmu.
Hae ira wiac sâwechec mi foocmu. Anutu â Lama ere ŋeŋe hae ira hâcne fuame ŋicfâc-ticne jaŋe kiŋaŋ qacnehuc juniŋmu.
Erâ hawari-ticne honehuc juniŋmu, â šâŋe qâreŋ-ticne mai-jeŋicko fuarâ foocmu.
Hae i mi ŋafeocmu, erâ lambe me šoaŋ tatamacnere mi muniŋmu, Wofuŋ Anutu e jahac šoaŋ ejareocmu. Eme hae rune jaŋe ŋicwofuŋ gie barahuc juniŋmu sanaŋ.
Eme aŋelozi šiŋuc nazawec: “Dâŋ i fâri hândâŋne jâmbâŋ. Wofuŋ Anutu porofete ejareme maŋjeŋic ŋerisieekac, eki hâcne aŋelo-ticne soreme kiŋaŋ qaqafâc-ticne ŋoŋe wiac, mi šoraha fuaocte mukicne i ŋaza ŋowatuc ewec.
Manakic, no biac fâpemu, eme moc e papia kecšira findaŋdâŋ qâreŋkekicne i sisirombe faio bajuocmu e šeri bubiaŋ manacnezo.”
Eme Johane no hâcne wiac i hone manac efârepo. Hone manac efârerâ aŋelo wiac nowatuwec ere maŋfuŋko fodaperâ numucnezo ehape
qatara-narerâ muwec: “Misac mac, no kiŋaŋ qaqa âgoge, erâ porofete qomâfâcge jaŋere âgo, â papia širec dâŋ aimuŋ bajuniŋmu jaŋere âgo jaha. Go Anutu e jahacne sawa daŋge nunumu ecnec.”
Iŋuc murâ šiŋuc nazawec: “Go papia širec findaŋdâŋ fâzâ mi bazemec. Dâŋ i fârinehec eocte dameŋne bembeŋkekac hâcne.
Irec sâqocne bapa e sâqocne bazo murâ bazejec, â maŋwânâŋheczi maŋwânâŋhec juzo murâ juzejec, â mitio juekaczi ine mitioa juzejec, â maŋfuru juekaczi maŋfuru jaha juzejec.”
“Manakic, no biac fâpemu. Okacnehec fâ fisirâ ŋic juju bapa-ŋeŋicte tofa sâckoa bazu-ŋarepemu.
No bâbâni â šâhec, fuŋne â botâŋne, wiac fufuŋke â babatara.
Ŋaqi-jeŋic šure ɋaɋackeeŋgopieŋ jaŋere manape šerine ekac. Jaŋe hâcne mujarepe jujujâckonec fârine nânšepieŋ â hae irec maŋnao rašinšepieŋ.
Hae râpenao juniŋmu ine qâto â hafec qaŋgec bapa â sasecŋic â šika qaqa â nemuɋâŋ babaju erâ burec bajuhuc irec aŋac-jopaekac.
“Jesu no hâcne aŋelo-nane sorepe eki kikefuŋ gurufâc-nane ŋoŋe mumutaniŋ dâŋ i mufua-ŋarewec. No hâcne Dawidire fuŋqizecne â oso gitecne, erâ bâpiŋ sâko tatamachec.”
Mâro â Jesure biŋefâc jaŋe šiŋuc mueŋgop ieŋ: “Go warezemec.” Á moc e dâŋ ši manarâ iŋuc jaha muzejec: “Go warezemec.” Moc e opâre hâmorâ šira fisizejec. Á moc e irec ecnekacko ware juju opâ furimâc nâzejec.
Papia kecšira findaŋdâŋ qâreŋkekicne i wose manac eniŋmu ŋoŋe uŋ ŋazape mananiŋ: Moc e maŋticnere dâŋ moc šuhuckeocmu, ŋic e Anutuzi wiac micne momori papia kecšira qâreŋkekicne i šuhuckecneocmu wâc,
â moc e findaŋdâŋ ši âke sipuocmu, ŋic erao Anutuzi jujujâcte dâŋ â tiri haere dâŋ ši qâreŋkekicne iŋuc jaha âke sipuocmu.
Dâŋ mufuakicne ši dopeckekaczi šiŋuc mukac: “Jâmbomac, no biac fâpemu.” Jâmbomac, Wofuŋ Jesu go warezemec.
Wofuŋ Jesure aki anonoczi ŋoŋerao fofârezejec. Jâmbomac.
